1.1 Wunaumau missinnin noh matta aonk wuttuwonganit matchetou, asuh matta neepauꝏ̄k, ummáyeuout matchese[a]enuog, asuh matta ápegk wutappuonganit mamanowontamwaénin.
1.2 Qut wuttinnꝏ̄waonganit Jehovah wuttapeneaumꝏ̄onk, kah wuttinnꝏ̄waonk missantam kesukodtaeu kah nukkonáeu.
1.3 Kah ogqueneunkqussu mehtugqut ahketeámuk ut kishke sepupogqut, noh ummeechummuonk uppaudtunk nehenwonche uttꝏ̄wutchu: kah ꝏ̄neepog matta pish nꝏ̄kshaunꝏ̄h, kah wame uttoh ásit pish misségen.
1.4 Matta neane matchetukeg: ut ogqueneunkqussuog wossadtea[u]munit, uttiyeu tꝏ̄[u]nontog waban.
1.5 Newutche matta neepauóog matcheetupanatogig wussittumꝏ̄onganit; asuh matcheussecheg ut ummukkinneonganit wunnomwaeussecheg.
1.6 Newutche ꝏ̄wahteóun Jehovah ummayash sampwesecheg: qut ummayou matcheetupanatogig pish awakompanómꝏ̄.
2.1 Tohwutch penuohteáog musquantamohettit, kah missinninnuog unnantamo[h]ettit tahnꝏ̄che teaguas.
2.2 Ketassꝏ̄tamwog ohkeit chipaphéaog wuhhogkauh, & n[a]nánuácheg kenꝏ̄nittuog ayeuuhkonittue Godut, kah ayeuuhkonittue sasequnónche, nꝏ̄waog.
2.3 Paskuhkommuttuh wutahtagkupsꝏ̄ongash, amauhteátuh uppémunohteanꝏ̄ash, wutch kuhhogkanónut.
2.4 Noh apit kesukqut [h]ahánou: Manit ummómontauoh.
2.5 Onk pish nahhoh kenꝏ̄[n]uh musquantog: pish wutchepheuh mꝏ̄cheke musquantog.
2.6 Qut onch nuppon nukketassꝏ̄tamom nꝏ̄netupanatamwe ut wadchumut Sion.
2.7 Nꝏ̄wahteauwáhuwam k[e]santamóonk Jehovah nuttugkup, ken nunnaumon, yeu kesukok kꝏ̄naumóniyeu[m]sh.
2.8 Wehquetumah, onk kittinnumoush penowohte[á]og wutche kꝏ̄kompuhchasuash, kah aongkóe anohk[e]ꝏ̄g wutche kutahtóonk.
2.9 Pish kussukquttahwhôog nashpe móohshogque a[n]wohhou, pish kussꝏ̄kquohkonot onatuh ahkuhqutteaénin ꝏ̄wisquadt.
2.10 Waantamꝏ̄k yowutche, woi ketassꝏ̄tamwog, netuhtauꝏ̄k kenaau wussittamwaenuog yeu ut ohkeit.
2.11 Waussumꝏ̄k Jehovah nashpe wabesuonk, weekontamꝏ̄k nashpe nunnuksh[u]onk.
2.12 Chipwuttꝏ̄unápꝏ̄k wunnaumónain, ishkont musquantog, kah kuppaguanimwꝏ̄ wutche mayut: ummꝏ̄squantamꝏ̄onk nashqunak webe oggu[h]se[?]ese, ꝏ̄nanumó[ȯ]g n[]nag paubuhtanumoncheg.
3.0 {Ukketeohhomaonk} David, to[m]wutauont wutch anaquabit} Absolomwoh {wunnaumonuh.}
3.1 Jehovah, toh nuttin kꝏ̄hkꝏ̄tne neg wadtaméhitcheg monaog neg ayeuohkôsitcheg.
3.2 Monaog weatimoncheg nukketeahogkonuh: matta ahtôou aninnummoadtuonk ut Godut. Selah.
3.3 Qut ken woi Jehovah, nutógquneg, nussohsumôonk, kah noh tohshinuk nuppuhkuk.
3.4 Nummauunitteau God nashpe nummishontowáonk, onk nunnꝏ̄tunk wutch ꝏ̄netupantamwe wadchumut. Selah.
3.5 Nussepsinup, kah nukkoueep, nuttꝏ̄kep, newutche Jehovah n[a]naihuk.
3.6 Matta woh nꝏ̄wabesuónuh piogqut muttanonganogkussuog missinninnuog, weenuhkoi[e]hettit.
3.7 Neepaush Jehovah, wadcháneh woi num-Manittꝏ̄m, newutche ken kuttógkom wame nummatwomog ut wutompikkonnꝏ̄w[ó]ut: kuppohquetahham weepittash matcheetou.
3.8 Wadchanittuonk wutchaiyeumꝏ̄ Godut: kꝏ̄naneteáonk ut kummissinninnu[m]tu. Selah.
4.0 {Nohtumuhpequodt ut} Neginoth, {ketohhomaonk} David.
4.1 NOOtah nanompussumunon, woi num-Manittꝏ̄m nꝏ̄nomwaeusseonk, kussohwhuneup, kobhóseon, kitteamonteanum[e]h, kah nꝏ̄tash nuppeantam[ó]wonk.
4.2 Woi kenaau wunnaumonoh wosketompaog, toh uttꝏ̄che kukquinnuppémwꝏ̄ nussohsumówonk en akodchinat? kah kꝏ̄womantamumwꝏ̄ tohnꝏ̄che usseonk, kah kenátinnehamwꝏ̄ pannꝏ̄waonk? Selah.
4.3 Qut wahteauꝏ̄k, Jehovah wutchippeponamonuh wáneetupanatamunutcheh, Jehovah nunnꝏ̄[t]unk wehquetumauog.
4.4 Wabesek, kah hque matchesek, nꝏ̄wagk nehenwonche ketahhꝏ̄wóut ut kutappinneôut, kah chequnussinꝏ̄k. Selah.
4.5 Sephamók God wunnomwausseae sephauseonk, kah ꝏ̄namptók Jehovah.
4.6 Monaog nꝏ̄waog howan nahtinukqueog wanegik? Jehovah tohshinumaiinnean ꝏ̄wequ[á]ꝏ̄m kuskesuk.
4.7 Kummagun weekontamowonk ut nuttahhut, mꝏ̄cheke onk mônakish ꝏ̄weatchiminneoash kah ꝏ̄ske[n] winneumꝏ̄.
4.8 Na neese wunnohteáe nusseepsin kah nukkouem, newutche webe ken Jehovah, kutáyimah nánauwantamóe wunáyeuonk.
5.0 {Nahtompuhpequodt}, Nehiloth: {Ukketoohhamaonk} David.
5.1 NOOtash nukkuttꝏ̄wonganash, woi Jehovah, natwontash nunnatwontamowonk.
5.2 Kukkeihtash nꝏ̄wadtauatonkqussumauwonk, nuk-Ketassꝏ̄tomꝏ̄m, kah num-Manittꝏ̄m, newutche ken kuppeantamoush.
5.3 Nꝏ̄wodtauatonkqussuonk woh kenꝏ̄tam nompoáeu, woi Jehovah: nompoáeu kussampwunnumauunun nuppeantamóonk, kah nuttushpoquáim.
5.4 Newutche ken Manit, matta kuttapeneaumꝏ̄h matcheseonk, onk matta kꝏ̄weetomukꝏ̄h matcheseonk.
5.5 Mattammag[u]og matta pish neepauꝏ̄og anaquabea[n], kussekeneau wame anakausitcheg matcheseonk.
5.6 Pish kuppaguanóog nag pannꝏ̄wacheg: Jehovah ukkogkoánum[a]u sheuteaén[ú]h kah asꝏ̄kekodteanúh.
5.7 Qut neen nuppetutteam keekit, newutche mónatasah kummonaneteaonganash: kah kꝏ̄wabissuónitteonganit kꝏ̄wôwussumush, en nogque kꝏ̄netupanatámukkomukqut.
5.8 Sagkompaguneh, woi Jehovah, en kꝏ̄nomwausseonganit, newutche nummatwomog: sampweteaush kummay ut anaquabeh.
5.9 Newutche matta wunnomwayeuonganinno ut wuttꝏ̄nꝏ̄wóut, wuttinnomaiyeú[m]ꝏ̄wóut matcheseongash: ukquttunganꝏ̄ wôshwi weenohkeyeuꝏ̄, nanwonyeumꝏ̄wog ut weenannꝏ̄w[ó]ut.
5.10 Páguas naghog woi God, penushahettich nashpe nehenwonche ukkenꝏ̄nittuonganuwóut: pogkenok newutche monakish ummatcheseonganꝏ̄óash, newutche kukkeitohteanánittuwáhukquog.
5.11 Qut wame yeug paubuhtanumukqueaneg, weekontamohettich, nagwutteáeu weekontamóe mishontꝏ̄wahettich, newutche nag kukkinhamauog: onk nag womontogig kꝏ̄wesuonk weekontamowónukqush.
5.12 Newutche ken Jehovah kꝏ̄nanum wanomwae ussecheg: nashpe kꝏ̄womóussúonk kꝏ̄weenuhkau, onatuh ogqunneg.
6.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt} Neginoth, {ut} Sheminith: {Ukketoohhamaonk} David.
6.1 Woi Jehovah ahque áuskomeh ut kummusquantamowonganit, onk ahue sasamakoúheh ut kussópetáe kummusquanetamꝏ̄wonganit.
6.2 Monanumeh, woi Jehovah, newutche nꝏ̄chumwes: woi Jehovah, neetskeheh, newutche nussaúꝏ̄kon.
6.3 Nukketeahogkou wonk mꝏ̄cheke onkuppunnau: qut ken, woi Jehovah, aquompak.
6.4 Quinnuppish, woi Jehovah, pohquahwus nukketeahogkou: woi wadchaneh, newutche kummonaneteaonk.
6.5 Newutche nápumukish matta kummequanumitteoh: ut weenohket howan tabuttantamunkquean.
6.6 Nussauanum nutáiukkóntowáonk, qunnenuhkon nutaiyum nutappen pomonsꝏ̄wémou, ut nashpe nussuppequash nutogquehchippadtóh nutappin.
6.7 Nuskesukquash mohtupaemoash wutch mauonk: nano wussesekshau newutche wame nummatwomog.
6.8 Amaeitaegk wame anakauseógish matcheseonk: newutche Jehovah nꝏ̄tam nummauongane wadtauatongqussuonk.
6.9 Jehovah nꝏ̄tam nꝏ̄weehquetumowonk, Jehovah neemunnum nuppeantamowonk.
6.10 Nummatwomog wame akodchehettich, kah onkapunahettich: quinnuppehettich, kah akodchhettich teanuk.
7.0 Shiggaion David, {yeush ketoohomauau Jehovah papaume ukkuttoowongash} Cush {up-Benjamite}.
7.1 Woi Jehovah num-Manittꝏ̄m, nen kupbaubuhtánumoush, wadchaneh wutch wame neg kodwoskhukqueoneg, kah pohquahwusseh.
7.2 Ishkont sóhkwushônau nukketeahogkonuh, onatuh qunônou sohqshadtunk, matta woh toh adt wodchanutteumukish.
7.3 Woi Jehovah num-Manittꝏ̄m, yeu usséon, matcheseonganꝏ̄ꝏ̄uk nunnutcheganit.
7.4 Onkquodtaúogis matcheseonk wonohk[â]sit (nux, nuppohquohwhunop noh tahnꝏ̄che ayeuohkáusit.)
7.5 Matwau wunnômattuhkauonch nukketeahogkonuh, kah tohqunonch, nux, taskuhkodch nukketeaonk ohkekontu, kah ayeuw[á]hitch nukquehtiánumitteaonk puppissiyeuut. Selah.
7.6 Waapish, woi Jehovah, musquantaman waabin kuhhog, newutche ukkogkeeuwaonganꝏ̄ nummatwomog: kah tꝏ̄nhkanumwansheh en ne wussittummꝏ̄onganit, ne anꝏ̄w[á]up.
7.7 Nemehkuh mukkinneonkane missinninnuog pish kꝏ̄weenohkongquog, newutche nag wutch qunnunkquappúe qushkish.
7.8 Jehovah pish wussumau missinninnuh; wussummeh, woi Jehovah, neaunag nꝏ̄nomwausseonk, kah neaunag nussampweusseonk nen ut nuhhogkaut.
7.9 Woi matcheetowog ummatcheetowonganꝏ̄ wohkukqu[t]hsitch, qut menehkeh sampwesecheg: newutche wunnomwáe God qutchehtau metahhash, kah muttꝏ̄nussoh.
7.10 Nuttongkꝏ̄ogqussꝏ̄ God: noh wadchanont sampwuttahonutcheh.
7.11 God wussumau wunnomwausseaenuh: God musquanumau matcheetowoh asekesukokish.
7.12 Matta quinnuppekompauuk, kéhtadtau wuttogkodteg, ónchippinnau wutohtompe kah ukquoshwunuh.
7.13 Kah wonk ukquóshwunnumau tôh woh ánuppinnit: kah wussantequohwoh ukk[ô]unkquodtash noshteanutcheh.
7.14 Kusseh, wutonkquomome paudtaun matcheseonk, wompequaou woskehuwáonk, kah pannꝏ̄wayeuonk neechau.
7.15 Wônteaúh, kah ukkuthámun, onk petshau wônogqut ne kezteunk.
7.16 OOwoskhuwáonk pish quinnuppemꝏ̄ en nehenwonche uppuhkukqut, kah wutcheke usseonk pish pogkishin nehenwonche uppuhkukqut.
7.17 Nuttabuttantamau Jehovah neaunag ꝏ̄[n]omwausséonk: kah nuttinnꝏ̄hhomom tabuttantamóonk, ꝏ̄wesuonganit Jehovah noh quanunkquappit.
8.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut} Gittith: {Ketoohhomaonk} David.
8.1 Woi Jehovah num-Manittꝏ̄m, uttoh nukkukque wunnegen kꝏ̄wes[u]onk wame muttaohket! kupponam kussohsumóonk ongkouwe kesukqut.
8.2 Wutch wuttꝏ̄nꝏ̄wóut mukkiesog, kah nꝏ̄nukeg kuhkuhquttum menuhkesuonk, newutche kummatwomog, onk woh kummanunnisseh matwau onk anꝏ̄tont.
8.3 Natwontamon kukkesukkumash kuppuhkukqu[á]nutchée anakausuonganash, nahnepaúshadt, kah anogqsog kukkeihtimopanneg.
8.4 Howan wosketomp woh mehquânumadt? kah wosketomp wunnaumonuh woh nadtuahheadt?
8.5 Newutche kukkezheop ut agwésu Angelsog: onk kutcheetuhquabin nashpe sohsumóonk kah quttiánittuonk.
8.6 Kittinnunnumain nánaánumun kenutchegane anakausuongash, kupponam wame teanteaquassinash agwe wusseetit.
8.7 Wame sheepsog kah oxenog, nux, kah puppinashimwog ut ohte[a]konit.
8.8 Puppinushaog mamahchekesukqut, kah namóhsog ketahhannit, kah nishnoh pomushomꝏ̄ mayash ketahhannit.
8.9 Woi Jehovah num-Manittꝏ̄moh uttoh en muttae wunnegen kꝏ̄wesuonk wame muttaohket.
9.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt [a]t} Muth-Labben: {Ketoohhomaonk} David.
9.1 Kuttabuttantamoush, woi Jehovah, nashpe mámusse nuttahhut: nunnáhtutteam wame kummonchanatamwu anakausuwongash.
9.2 Nꝏ̄weekontam káh kumm[u]skouanatamꝏ̄woush nuttinnꝏ̄homom tabuttantamꝏ̄wongash kꝏ̄wesuonganit, woi ken quanunkquappean.
9.3 Nummatwomog quaskehettit, nag pish penushaog, kah paguanúog ut anaquabean.
9.4 Newutche kuta[n]umwontamah nussampwusseonk, kah noo[t]s[i]nnꝏ̄wonganit, kutapip ꝏ̄sittamꝏ̄ongane appuonganit, sampwe wussittumunat.
9.5 Kuttaushkomomp penuwohteaog, kuppáguanomp matcheetoweg, kutjiskhomup ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄ micheme.
9.6 Woi ken matwau, pagwanꝏ̄onganash wohkukquôshinneash yauyatcheh: kah kuppapâgodtoh otanash, mehquanumaonganꝏ̄ nashpu nuppók.
9.7 Qut Jehovah pish michemeyeuꝏ̄, quaquashwe[e]htomup wutappuonk wutch wussittumꝏ̄wonk.
9.8 Kah pish sampwe wussittum muttaohke, pish wussumau missinninnúh ut sampwiyeuut.
9.9 Jehovah pajeh spúhhꝏ̄wáonkánuꝏ̄ mukkꝏ̄kinutcheg, pajeh sp[ú]hhꝏ̄wónganuꝏ̄ wuttammepunáumuk.
9.10 Kah nag wahteunkig kꝏ̄wesuonk kꝏ̄namptunkquog: newutche ken Jehovah matta kenukkonóog neg natinneahhukquéaneg.
9.11 Ketꝏ̄hhomok Jehovahut, noh ápit Sion: pahketeauꝏ̄k kenugke missinninnutu wutusseonganꝏ̄.
9.12 Natꝏ̄tomuhteadt nushehteáonk, ꝏ̄wâanumoh nahog: matta wunánatámou ummauonganꝏ̄ ohhohpánutcheh.
9.13 Monanumeh, woi Jehovah, natauwompadtash nꝏ̄tamehpunáonk nashpe nag sekeneunkqueaneg, ken tahshinnea[n] wutch nuppꝏ̄wongane squontamut.
9.14 Woh nahtitteam wame kuttabuttantamonteaongash ꝏ̄squontamut wuttaunésoh Sion: nꝏ̄wekontam kꝏ̄wadchanuaonganit.
9.15 Penuwóhteaog quttauwéog ut wônahteahéganit ne kesteauhetteup: wonâshahettit appéhonuh, ut upputhugkouoh ut nehenwonche wusseetuóut.
9.16 Nꝏ̄wahêoun Goduh nashpe ꝏ̄sittamꝏ̄ongash nish aseche, matchetou puttuhhuk ut nehenwonche wunnutchegane usseonganit Higgaion. Selah.
9.17 Matchetoog pish no[h]kónog chepiohkomukqut, kah wame wutóhtimonneash wananumoncheg Goduh.
9.18 Newutche matta nagwutteáeu wunánuma[ú]ou matchekuoh wutanno[ó]suonk matcheku, matta pish ꝏ̄wánteauun micheme.
9.19 Omohkish, woi Jehovah, ahque sohkoiitch missinnin, penuwohteaog wussumunaj ut anaquabean.
9.20 Wâbesuah, woi Jehovah: onk woh wutohtimóneash, nehenwonche wahteauog webe wosketompaog. Selah.
10.1 Tohwutch neepaiyean nꝏ̄adtit, woi Jehovah? tohwutch puttogquéan ne adt wuttammepunni?
10.2 Matcheetou pitchu[à]numwudt kodwoskéhheau matchékuoh: tohqunukquehettich uppuhchúteaonganꝏ̄ ne unnantamohettit.
10.3 Newutche matcheetou muskóau toh ânahtág wuttah ne nnih: kah wunnanumau i[á]hchewontamwoh uttiyeuh Jehovah óhquanumonche.
10.4 Matcheetou pitchuánumweenongqussit, matta natinneahwóou Goduh, wame wuttinanatamꝏ̄wonganit matta Godunnꝏ̄.
10.5 Wutusseongash nagwutteáeu unkqunneonkquodtash: kussittamꝏ̄wonganash wohqut ahtáash wunnꝏ̄nomputtamunash: kah wame ummatwomoh ummámeshanimuh.
10.6 Nꝏ̄wau ut wuttahhut, matta pish nuttóntsappu; newutche matta woh toh nuttit wuttammehpunóh.
10.7 Wuttꝏ̄nit numwohteau matchenánutteáonk, k[á]h asꝏ̄kekodtea[o]muwonk kah p[ù]hchuteáonk: agwu weenann[ú]uh na wosk[e]huwáonk kah tohnꝏ̄cheyeuꝏ̄uk.
10.8 Appu ónkaumpamúkquodtit otanáemesittu, assampamukquodtit, wuttit nushon m[at]ta woskhuánutche: wuskesukquash kemompamáuh matchekuoh.
10.9 Askuhwheteau matta na[û]ou onatuh qunônou, ne seepsuk: askuhwhau matchekuoh noh wuttin tohqunóneat: tohqunau matchekuoh pasꝏ̄ont wuthashabut.
10.10 Ohtáeu & hohpaheau wuhhogk[u]h, matchekuoh woh penushau nashpe ummenuhkeseumoh.
10.11 Nꝏ̄wau ut wuttahhut, God ꝏ̄wánanatumun: putt[a]ghom wuskesuk, matta woh nunnukqut naumꝏ̄.
10.12 Omohkish, woi Jehovah, woi God tohshinush kenutcheg: ahque wananum hohhohpacheg.
10.13 Tohwutch matcheetou mamànowánumónt Goduh? nꝏ̄wau ut wuttahhut matta kꝏ̄nompagunnumiéin.
10.14 Kenaumunáp, newutche kenaumun wosk[e]huwaonk, kah wutjishanumowonk, onk nashpe kenutcheg woh wuttinheun: matcheku kuppaubuht[á]numuk wuhhogkuh, ken aninnumauadt nag mat wadꝏ̄shꝏ̄gig.
10.15 Pokshadtash wôhpit matcheetou kah woskehuaénin, natinnehash ummatcheseonganash n[ô] pajeh monteag kummi[s]komꝏ̄unat.
10.16 Jehovah keihtasꝏ̄tamꝏ̄ꝏ̄ micheme kah micheme: penuwohteaog paguanóog wutch wutohtuwóut.
10.17 Jehovah kenꝏ̄tam hohpou ukkodtantamóonk: kukquoshaeihtam wuttahhou, kutáyum kuhtaúog wutch nꝏ̄tamunat.
10.18 Wussumónat mat wadꝏ̄shꝏ̄gig, kah woskhetcheg, onk wosketomp yeu muttaohket matta wonk woh woskehuwóou.
11.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ketohhomaonk} David.
11.1 Nuppaubuhtanum ut Jehovah, ut [t]oh woh unnók nukketeuhogkou [p]tꝏ̄wej onatuh psuksesit en kꝏ̄wadchumꝏ̄wóut?
11.2 Newutche kusseh, matcheetowog anchepunuhtaog: quashinumwog úkkôunkquodtou, ut wutahtumanꝏ̄óut: woh kemu pumwôog sampw[ú]tteah[ó]nutche.
11.3 Quenohtáe agweóhteagish matchehteaumuk, toh woh wutusseneau sampweusseaenúog?
11.4 Jehovah appu wunnetupanatamwe templeut, Jehovah wutappuonk kesukqut: wuskesukquash náꝏ̄omꝏ̄oash, wanadteaskesukquash qutcheheau wunnaumonáoh wosketompaog.
11.5 Jehovah qutchéheau sampweussaénuh, qut ukketeahogkóunoh sekeneauau matchetowoh, kah [n]eh womantamunutcheh chenauausuonk.
11.6 Matcheetowoh pish wussokanummaoh ahpehhanoh, nꝏ̄htau kah brimstone nashquttin: yeu wutchippiyeumꝏ̄ wuttattamꝏ̄ongkanꝏ̄óut.
11.7 Newutche sampweusseae Jehovah womantam sampweusseonk, wuttinnussuonk moneaúau sampwusseaeneuh.
12.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut} Sheminith: {ketoohhomaonk} David.
12.1 Aninnumaiinnean Jehovah, newutche wanne manittowompaenúunꝏ̄h: newutche paubuhtanumwaenuog oggushéoog kenugku wunnaumonaohut wosketompaog.
12.2 Tahnꝏ̄che keketꝏ̄hkaâog, nish noh weetatteamonganꝏ̄ꝏ̄ nashpe wunanakꝏ̄wáe wussissittꝏ̄nꝏ̄woash, kah neesi[nn]úꝏ̄ wuttahhꝏ̄woash keketꝏ̄kaóg.
12.3 Jehovah pish tummessum wunánakꝏ̄wáe mussissittꝏ̄nash, kah meenan noh nꝏ̄wadt mishꝏ̄waonk.
12.4 Nꝏ̄wâhettit neenannúu[n]nonash pish nutomskausuwohtómun, nussissittꝏ̄nonash nehenwonche, howan w[ȧ]santimámeog?
12.5 Newutche matchekuoh woskeheaog kah nꝏ̄nunnúkeg ummishonnomꝏ̄ónganꝏ̄, yeuyeu nutomohkem (nꝏ̄wau Jehovah) nuppon nanauwinnuat wutche noh mamashanimont.
12.6 Ukkuttꝏ̄wongash Jehovah pahke kuttꝏ̄wongash onatuh silver sabassumuk kutohk[o]esabassohsuonganit nesausuk[t]ahshit pahketeaumuk.
12.7 Woh kꝏ̄wadchanóog, woi Jehovah, kenánaihéaog yeu wutch pometuonganit micheme.
12.8 Matcheetoog popomsháog nish noh ut, uhque matchetowog ut kenugke wunnaumonuh wosketompaog nananuwahettit.
13.0 {Nohtompuhpequ[a]dt ukketoohomaonk} David,
13.1 Tohuttꝏ̄che pish kꝏ̄wannumeh (woi Jehovah) nagwutteaeu? tohuttꝏ̄che pish kupputtogkuhhum kuskesuk wutche neen.
13.2 Tohuttꝏ̄che woh nukkinnꝏ̄n nukketeahogkou; neuanatamunish ut nuttahhut asekesukokish: toh uttꝏ̄che pish nummatwomog mishshehheaog anue onk neen.
13.3 Nawontash kah nꝏ̄tah, woi Jehovah num-Monittꝏ̄m, wussompuwahteoush nuskesukquash; iskont nukkouem nuppꝏ̄e koueonk.
13.4 Iskont nummatwom nꝏ̄wau, nutomska[û]óp, kah yeug wadtamméhukquéaneg woh muskouanatamwog ontsappeon.
13.5 Qut nuppaubuhtantam kummonaneteaonk, nuttah muskouanatamꝏ̄wontam kꝏ̄wadchanꝏ̄waonk.
13.6 Nukketꝏ̄hhomau Jehovah, newutche nummꝏ̄cheke aninnumunk.
14.0 {Nohtompohpequodt ketohhomaonk} David.
14.1 Mattamog nꝏ̄wau ut wuttahhut, wanne God[u]nꝏ̄, aninwog, niskanakausuongash wuttussenáoash, wanne howan wunnesu.
14.2 Jehovah womómpu wutche kesukqut monneáuau wosketomp wunnaumonuh, kodnaum uttoh wuttin wohtamunneau, kah natinnewhon God.
14.3 Wàme amaeog, moeu niskeneonkqussuog matta howan wunnesu, matta pasuk.
14.4 Wame matanakausuog, wanne wahteauꝏ̄og? mꝏ̄whôog nummissinninnumoh, mechumuk petukqunneg kah matta wehquetumáauóog Goduh
14.5 Naut mꝏ̄cheke wabesu[m]og, néwutche God ut uppometuonganit wunnomwausseaénu appu.
14.6 Kutákodchehteomwꝏ̄ ukkenꝏ̄nꝏ̄waonk matcheku, newutche Jehovah wutushpuhhꝏ̄waonguh.
14.7 Woi ꝏ̄wadchanuonganꝏ̄ Israel waj sohhomꝏ̄ꝏ̄uk wutch Syon: Jehovah sohhꝏ̄wunont wutch missinnainneat ummissinninnumoh, Jakob pish muskauanatam, kah Israel pish wekontam.
15.0 {Ketoohhomaonk} David.
15.1 Jehovah, hówan woh apit keekit? howan woh wadohket kꝏ̄neetupanatamwe wadchumut?
15.2 Noh sompwshadt, kah anakausit Sampweusseonk, kah nꝏ̄wadt wanamuhkutéyuonk ut wuttahhut.
15.3 Noh matta nꝏ̄numimonk ut weenañóut: asa mat matchenehheunk weetatteamunguh kah matta wunnamptamaoou kehkontuonk weetatteamunguh.
15.4 Wuskesukquash jishánumau matcheetowoh: qut quttianumau wabesuonóncheg Jehovah: quashómuadt matta qús[h]kꝏ̄áu tohk[ô]nogque wannéhteunk.
15.5 Noh matta nogohkouhuog wutteaguas wutch anuwu aninnumauwó[n]ah, matta onk quatusseg wutch paummꝏ̄waonk ayeuuhkonittue noh matta tamhóuog, howan ásit yeush, matta pish ontsappu.
16.0 {Um-Michtam} David.
16.1 Wadchaneh, woi God: newutche kuppaubahtanumush.
16.2 Nuttah kuttinnomp Jehovah, ken num-Manittꝏ̄m: nꝏ̄neetowonk matta kꝏ̄nehhukkꝏ̄un.
16.3 Qut waneetupanatogig yeuut ohkeit, kah wanekitcheg, yeug wame nuttappenea[uo]og.
16.4 Pish monatash wutôhquanumꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash natinneohwáhettit onkatoge manittꝏ̄h: ꝏ̄tattamóe wsquehheonkane sephamaonk matta nussephamaôh, asa mat neemunnumꝏ̄h ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄h ut nussissetꝏ̄nut.
16.5 Jehovah wutchippiyeum nutahtaúonk, kah nꝏ̄tattamwáitch: kenanaáihteóh nuttittanohtôadtúonk.
16.6 Nukhuhkinónghash ut wunnegen ohkéit, nux wunnegen nutahtauonk.
16.7 Nuttabuttantamau Jehovah wutch nukkinnꝏ̄nukꝏ̄onk, onk nuttꝏ̄unissog nukkuhkꝏ̄tomunkquog nukkonaeu.
16.8 Nagwutteaeu nuppon Jehovah anaquabeh: newutche appu nuttinnohkôunit, matta pish nutontsappu.
16.9 Newutche nuttah weekontam, kah nussohsumóonk weekontamꝏ̄mꝏ̄: kah nꝏ̄weyaus pish anwôsinꝏ̄mꝏ̄ ut anꝏ̄ôsinneat.
16.10 Newutche matta kenukkonôh nukketeahogkou ut cheppiohkomukqut, asa mat kuttinnanumoh kꝏ̄neetupanatamwaénin náish aninnowonk.
16.11 Pish kꝏ̄wahteauwahe may en keteaonganit: anaquabean wâmut weekontam[ó]onk, kuttinohkôonit weekontamóonk micheme kah micheme.
17.0 {Peantamowonk} David.
17.1 Nootash sampweusseonk, woi Jehovah, kuhkeitash nummauonk, nꝏ̄tash nuppeantamowonk, mo waj sohhamꝏ̄unꝏ̄g eiantogkieue mussissitꝏ̄nut.
17.2 Kꝏ̄sum̃uonk ꝏ̄mꝏ̄utch wutch anaquabean: kuskesukquash naj wunnomwausseonk.
17.3 Kukqutchteop nuttah, kenátaaheup nukkonaeu: kukqutchheup, kah pish monteag kummiskomꝏ̄, nutahchuwéussen, nuttꝏ̄n mat pish matcheyeu.
17.4 Papaume wutanakausuongash wosketompaog nashpe kukkuttꝏ̄wongash, ut kussissetꝏ̄nut nunnaanôweh wutch mayut pagúanaucheg.
17.5 Kenunnush nuppomushaongash kummayut, onk mat woh nusseetash tꝏ̄nequssinunꝏ̄h.
17.6 Kꝏ̄wehquetummaunup, newutche kenꝏ̄tah, woi God, equóhtuhquaeihtah, kah nꝏ̄tash nukkuttꝏ̄wonganash.
17.7 Nait[u]ttꝏ̄sh monchanatamwe kukkitteamonte[á]nutteaonk, woi ken pohquóhwussꝏ̄waen nashpe kuttinohkôu, nag paubuhtanumukqueaneg, wutch nag auꝏ̄hkon[ó]ncheg.
17.8 Unnꝏ̄wadchaneh neane mꝏ̄eskesuk: puttógwheh wutonkôuhtomut, kenuppawhúnash.
17.9 Nag wutch matchetowog woskhukqueaneg: kodnushhukkowoneg nummatwomog, wéenuhkaitcheg.
17.10 Nuppꝏ̄kómꝏ̄wog nehenwonche ꝏ̄weesu: wuttꝏ̄nꝏ̄ pittuánumweyeú[u]ꝏ̄.
17.11 Yeuyeu nukquiñupuhkóngqunonog nuppomshaonganonut: wuskesukꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash ussukkompadtaoash ohkekontu.
17.12 Onatuh qunônou paskonóntog neh kodtohqunoncheh: kah onatuh wushkoshimꝏ̄m qunónou keemohteadt ut onkâompamukquodtut.
17.13 Omkish woi Jehovah wuttameh n[]noh, penuhteash, pohquohwhin nukketeahogkou wutch matchetowog, neg kuttogkodtegannog.
17.14 Wutch wosketompaog kenutcheganog woi Jehovah, wutch wosketompaog yeu muttaohket, nag wuttahtauonganꝏ̄ yeuut keteaonganit: kah kenumwóhtinash wunnogkusséont kutadtahtouongash nag numwápuohwunneechánowoh, chaubohkish um̃[?]úmachiyeumoash wunnukkodtumaooh uppeissesimo[?]oh.
17.15 Qut neen, pish nunnaum kuskesuk ut wunnomwausseonganit: pish nummꝏ̄chekohtóh, tꝏ̄keon, nussean neánussean.
18.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ukketoohomaonk muttinneu Jehovah} David, {kenoonau Jehovah yeush ketoohomae kuttoo[m]ongash, nekesukok Jehovah wame pohquohwhunont, wutch wunnutcheganooont matwomoh, kah wutch w[u]nnutcheganit Saul, kah noowau}.
18.1 Kꝏ̄womonsh woi Jehovah nummenuhkesuonk.
18.2 Jehovah nukqussukquánum, kah nꝏ̄wonkônous, nuppohquohwussuaenum, num-Manittꝏ̄m, nukqussukquanum noh paubuhtanumog nutonkꝏ̄ohqossꝏ̄, kah askon wadchanukqueh, kah nukqunohque wonkônous.
18.3 Nꝏ̄weequetumau Jehovah tapenuk tabuttantamauónat: nemehkuh woh nuppohquohwhunit wutch nummatwomut.
18.4 Nuppꝏ̄wonk wutonkquomomhuaongah nꝏ̄wéinuhkongqunash: wuttomogka[n]ꝏ̄mꝏ̄ matta peantamꝏ̄gig nꝏ̄wabuwunukquog.
18.5 Wutonkquomomhúaongash chepiohkomuk nukquinupuhkongqunash: wutahpehunah nuppꝏ̄onk nukoshkóme tohqunukquog.
18.6 Onkupinnaon nꝏ̄weehquetumau Jehovah, nummaúonitteau num-Manittꝏ̄m, nꝏ̄tamup nꝏ̄wadtauatongqussuonk wutch wuttempleumut, nummauonk peyaumꝏ̄ anaquabit, en wohtaúogut.
18.7 Neit ohke nukkeemꝏ̄ kah quéquan: onk agwu ohtagish wadchuash ontahtaash, kah nukkemꝏ̄ash newutche musquantamup.
18.8 Sohweemꝏ̄ pukit wutch wutchonit, kah nꝏ̄tau wutch wuttꝏ̄nut unnunau, mohkohsaash ne nashpe chikohtaash.
18.9 Quanábuhkam kesuk, kah nꝏ̄keu, kah pohkenái ut agwu wusseetit.
18.10 Kah nayeumugk cherub, kah ptꝏ̄wu: nux, ptꝏ̄wu wutch wuñuppawhuno[h] waban.
18.11 Pohkinteau wutassampamugquodtꝏ̄m: week wueenuhkunk, pohkinnuppog, kuhpógke matohqs póhkahqut.
18.12 Kodshaumwushont ut anaquabit, kuppogki matokqs pamémꝏ̄, mussegan kah nꝏ̄tae mohkohsaash.
18.13 Kah Jehovah padtaquóhhunnéhtea[n] ut kesukqut, kah nôahpit wuttauatonkquísu, mussegon kah nꝏ̄tae mohkohsaash.
18.14 Nux, pummu ukkôunkquodtah, kah wusseauhkonuh nahoh, kah pepummu ukkutshánum, kah wutomskauoh.
18.15 Neit passéhtannash nippekontu nógquadtash, kah muttaohke quenohtagish puhkônumunash, aushkòáan, woi Jehovah, kutchân nashaumꝏ̄ug.
18.16 Anꝏ̄teamꝏ̄ wutch wohqudt, nunneemunuk: nukkuhpunuk wutch nippekontu missi.
18.17 Nuppohquohwhunuk wutch menuhkesu nummatwom, kah wutch nag sekenáitcheg: newutche nag [á]nue menuhkesuog onk neen.
18.18 Nukkinhomunkquog onkapunnáon: qut Jehovah nuttannumunkou.
18.19 Onk nussohhꝏ̄wunuk en mummishke ayeuonganit: nuppohquohwhunuk, newutche nꝏ̄weeteánumuk.
18.20 Jehovah nutunkquatunk neaunag nꝏ̄nomwausseonk: neane pohkág nunnutcheganash nuttinunkquatunkqun.
18.21 Newutche nussampwushám ummayash Jehovah, kah matta nummatcheseáeu nutámaéhtâóh wutch num-Manittꝏ̄mut.
18.22 Newutche wame ꝏ̄sittamꝏ̄ongash ohtaash anaquabeh: kah matta nuppogketamꝏ̄h ukkuhkꝏ̄waongash.
18.23 Neen wonk nussampwes ut anaquabit: kah nꝏ̄wadchan nuhhog wutch nehenwonche nummatcheseongash.
18.24 Yowutche Jehovah nutunkquatunk neane nꝏ̄nomwausseonk, neane pohkág nunnutcheganash ut anaquabit.
18.25 Monaneteáhettit, kummonânumóog: sampwésit, kah ken kussampwes.
18.26 Pahkezhettit, kah ken kuppahkes: kah chenouaushettit nánuk kuchénoaus.
18.27 Newutche kꝏ̄wadchan kuttamunge onkapunácheg missinninnuog, qut kuppenuhteam pahtuánummonugqussitcheg.
18.28 Newutche ken kenashqussum nꝏ̄weequanánteg: Jehovah num-Manittꝏ̄m wequanantam nuppohkenáꝏ̄m.
18.29 Newutche nashpe ken nuppanupwusham, chppanꝏ̄og, kah nashpe num-Manittꝏ̄m nukqueishontam pummeneutunk.
18.30 Qut Jehovah ummay pannuppu wunnegen: wuttinnꝏ̄waonk God pahketeáuun: wuttonkkꝏ̄woquossꝏ̄unnꝏ̄wôh neg wame pabuhtanumoncheg.
18.31 Newutche howan Manittꝏ̄it webe Jehovah, kah howan quasukquânuit webe num-Manittꝏ̄m.
18.32 God nupputtukquábunuk menuhkesuonk, kah uppahketeoun nummay.
18.33 Nusseetash ogquéhteau ahtúhqusseetit, kah nuppónuk nukkussôhkôóoumut.
18.34 Kuhkꝏ̄tomauau nunnutcheganoh ayeuhkonat: nemehkuh nashpe nuhpin pôhqunau mooshagquohtomp.
18.35 Kah wonk kittinnumaiip kꝏ̄wadchanuáe ogqunneg kah kuttinnohkou nutashinuk, kah kummanunnissuonk nummishúkqun.
18.36 Kummissigskéhteau nuttóntahnehtuonganash ut agwu neen, onkummat nuttꝏ̄nukqussinꝏ̄h.
18.37 Nꝏ̄nômahtúhkôomp nummatwóog, kah nummátamóog, onk matta wonk nukqushkꝏ̄h nô pajeh nuppaguanónat.
18.38 Nutchadchéuhtahwhóog onk ummatta tapenumóog ompken, penusháog ut nusseetit.
18.39 Newutche kupputtukquôbussup kummenuhkesuonk ayeuwuttinneat: kenáuwôsikkómpaihéaog yeug neepaiitunkqueaneg.
18.40 Wonk kittinninnumah wussittippukánoóash nummatwomog: onk woh nuppaguanóog sekeneáitcheg.
18.41 Mauwog, matta howan uppohquohwhunoh: nux, Jehovah[]ut, qut matta wunnampꝏ̄hamaúoh nahog.
18.42 Neit nussukquttahwhôog onatuh puppissai tohtꝏ̄anontog: nussohwhôkonunk onatuh pusseog mayut.
18.43 Kuppohquohwussup ummusquánitteaonganóont missinninnúog, kah kutayeuweh ꝏ̄puhkúhqunneaóont penuwohteaog: missinninnúog matta wahhéaogig, pish nꝏ̄wówussumukquog.
18.44 Quéna nꝏ̄taehettit, pish nosweetunkquog, penuohteáog pish nꝏ̄wonkkumukquog.
18.45 Penuwohteaog pish mahchéog, pish wabesuog ut assompamukquodtit.
18.46 Jehovah pomantam, kah ꝏ̄nantaj nukqussukquánum: kah wadchánꝏ̄wáe num-Manittꝏ̄m mishehhenaj.
18.47 N noh God anꝏ̄tauanshikqueh, kah naôhsikómpaaiheunk missinninnúh ut agwu neen.
18.48 Nuppohquohwhunuk wutch nummatwâut: nux, kutahshineh waabe yeug neepaiittunkqueaneg; kuppohquohwussup wutch musquantamuoenúut.
18.49 Newutche kuttabuttantamoush, woi Jehovah, kenugku penuwohteáog, kah nukketꝏ̄homom tabuttantamꝏ̄wonganash ut kꝏ̄wesuwonganit.
18.50 Missiyeuash uppohquohwussuáonkanash wuttinumaon ukketassꝏ̄tomómoh: kah ummonánumoh saséqunoncheh, Davidoh, kah wuskannemunneoh micheme.
19.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt: Ukketoohhomaonk} David.
19.1 Kesukquash wunnáhtuhkóneau wussohsumóonk God, kah mamachekesuk kuhkꝏ̄tomuhteaumꝏ̄ wunnetchegane anakausuonk.
19.2 Hóhsekôeu kesukodash keketꝏ̄hkon: kah hóhsekôeu nukonash náhteteauog wahteauonk.
19.3 Wanne unnóntꝏ̄wáonkanunnꝏ̄ asa mat penꝏ̄wontꝏ̄waonkanunnꝏ̄; adt mo nꝏ̄tamómuk ukkuttꝏ̄wonganꝏ̄.
19.4 Uppemunneohtónꝏ̄ pannu[p]shaumꝏ̄ wame ohket, kah ukkuttꝏ̄wonganꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash aongkoue muttaok: na upponamun wetu wutch nepâuzoh.
19.5 N noh onatuh weseentamwaen sohhog wutch weetu: kah weekontam onatuh menuhkesuwen, nanôahteadt.
19.6 Ummoncheonk[]au weekqshik kesuk, kah uppogkudtuhkomóonk na weekqshik: kah wanne teag asómpamukquodtinoꝏ̄ woh mo kôssopitánꝏ̄g.
19.7 Wuttinnaumatuonk Jehovah pannuppu wunnetuoh, quanuppinónt keteahogkôunoh, ꝏ̄wauwáonk Jehovah wunnamuhkuteyeúꝏ̄, waantamwehheunt asꝏ̄tuoh.
19.8 Ukkúhkwaꝏ̄onganash Jehovah sampao[ù]ash, weekontamwahteunk metah: wutanꝏ̄hteamꝏ̄wonk Jehovah pohkoi, wôshwunnumꝏ̄mꝏ̄ug muskesukquash.
19.9 Qusháonk Jehovah pohkoi, machemohtag: ꝏ̄sittumꝏ̄ongash Jehovah wunnamuhkutêyeuꝏ̄ash, kah wame sampweyeuꝏ̄ash moáeu.
19.10 Mꝏ̄cheke kodtantamunash onk ne gold, nux, onk ne mꝏ̄cheke wanegik gold: onk ánue weekon onk ne hony, kah honycombe.
19.11 Kah wonk amômáog kittinninnúmoh: kah usséog nishog, missi kutongquatunkanun.
19.12 Howan ꝏ̄wahteoúnash uppéhchummaauongash? pahkhe wutch kéme matcheseongash.
19.13 Wonk assón kittinneum wutch mat qushe matcheseongash, ahque piahtimehhettich: neit woh nussumpwes, kah nummꝏ̄ses wutch mishe matcheseonk.
19.14 Nukkuttꝏ̄wonganash wutch nuttꝏ̄nut, káh nunnatwontamꝏ̄wongash ut nuttahhut, tapeneaúmunach ut anaquabean, woi Jehovah, nukqussukquanum, kah nuppohquohwussuaénin.
20.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt: Ukket[oo]khomaonk} David.
20.1 NOOtunkquash Jehovah wuttammepunnáan: ꝏ̄wesuonk um-Manittꝏ̄moh Jakob wadchanukqush.
20.2 Anꝏ̄nonch aninnummoadtuonguh wutch peantamwakomukqut: kah menuhkhukqush wutch Sion.
20.3 Mehquantaj wame kummagꝏ̄onkanash: tapeneaj chikohtáeu sephauseongash. Selah.
20.4 Uninnumungqush neane kodtantog kuttah: kah wame n naj kukkinnꝏ̄sꝏ̄waongash.
20.5 Nꝏ̄wekontamumun kꝏ̄adchanꝏ̄onganit, kah ꝏ̄wesuonganit num-Manittꝏ̄mun nupponamunnan nummuttáagunun: Jehovah ussitch wame kuppeantamꝏ̄wonganash.
20.6 Yeuyeu nꝏ̄wahteóun, Jehovah wadchanau sasequnutche, wunnꝏ̄taoh wutch ꝏ̄netupanatamwe kesukquiꝏ̄mut nashpe kꝏ̄wadchánꝏ̄wáe kuttinohkóunne menuhkesuonk.
20.7 Nawhutch pabahtánittamwog chariotsash, nawhutch horsesoh: qut nummequontamumun ꝏ̄wesuonk Jehovah num-Manittꝏ̄m.
20.8 Nꝏ̄keahheóog kah penusháog: qut nutomohkémun kah nussampokompaúun.
20.9 Wadchanean Jehovah, ketassꝏ̄t nꝏ̄tunkqutteuh weekquetumáogkut.
21.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt, ukketoohhomaonk} David.
21.1 Ketassꝏ̄t muskouantam ut kummenuhkesuonganit, woi Jehovah: kah kꝏ̄wadchanꝏ̄wonganit, woi Jehovah: kah kꝏ̄wadchanꝏ̄wonganit ut toh nukkukqun ummuskouanatamꝏ̄wonk?
21.2 Kuttinnumauop neane kodtantamunit wuttahhoh, kah matta kukkogkaanumaoun nohhan wehquetumunkqueanish wussissetꝏ̄nit. Selah.
21.3 Newutche aspapeantamungkꝏ̄up kuttinnumau wunnaiyeue kꝏ̄naneteaonk, kupponumau pahke gold chetuhquab uppuhkuhqut.
21.4 Kꝏ̄wehquetumunk keteaonk,, kah kittinnumauau sepepomantamowonk micheme kah micheme.
21.5 Wussohsumowonk missi ut kꝏ̄wadchanitteaonganit, quttianittuonk kah wohquanittuonk kupponamau.
21.6 Newutche kutayimau mꝏ̄cheke wunanumaonk micheme: kuttinsuonk ummuskouanatamheuh mꝏ̄cheke.
21.7 Newutche ketassꝏ̄t pabahtanumau Jehovah, kah kesukqut apit monanumont, matta pish ontsappeoh.
21.8 Kenutcheg pish namehheau wame kummatwomoh: kuttinohkou pish namehheau yeug sekeneanukqueaneg.
21.9 Pish kutayeuꝏ̄g onatuh kesomsquttag musquanumadt naghog: Jehovah pish ummishashqunneuh musquantog, kah pish mahchekussuog nashpe nꝏ̄teau.
21.10 Wutontsetuonganꝏ̄ pish kuppagquodtoh wutch ohket, kah ꝏ̄skannemunnoh wutch kenugke wosketompaog wunnaumonaout.
21.11 Newutche kukkodmatchenehukquog: natwontamwog missi matchenehhuwaonk, ne mat tapenumunhetteg ussen.
21.12 Yowutche pish anummekompoog: quoshonkqunnumauadt nagoh ut wushkesukkouwout
21.13 Mishehhenunaj Jehovah, nehenwonche kumenuhkesuonkanit: nemehkuh nukketꝏ̄hhomomun, kah nꝏ̄wawussittumun kummenuhkesuonk.
22.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut Ajeleth Shaharukketoohhomaonk} David.
22.1 Nummanittꝏ̄m num-Manittꝏ̄m, tohwutch ahquanumean tohwutch nauꝏ̄ssuhkáuwean wutch kuttannumiyeuonk: wutch nummaue kuttꝏ̄wonganash.
22.2 Woi num-Manittꝏ̄m kesukodtae nanompanwam, qut matta kenꝏ̄tiyeuh, kah nukkonaeu, kah matta nutchequnappu.
22.3 Qut kꝏ̄neetupanatam, woi ken wadohtean wutabuttantam̃ꝏ̄onganꝏ̄out Israel
22.4 Nꝏ̄shunnonog kuppabahtanumukquog: kuppabahtanumukquog, onk kuppohquohhunnopanneg.
22.5 Kummauunnitteonkapanneg, onk kuppohquohwhunopanneg, kuppabahtanumukquog, kah matta akodchuog.
22.6 Qut neen askꝏ̄k kah mat nꝏ̄wosketompóou; nukkekomukquog wosketompaog, kah nummishananumukquog missinninnuog.
22.7 Wame neg náaitcheg nutâhanetunkquog, mamuskéog, nunnukukquoshôog nꝏ̄waog.
22.8 Pabahtánumop Jehovah, woh uppohquohwhunnuh: pohquohwhunonch, tapeneaúont.
22.9 Qut len neemunnéap wutch ôontomuk kutáyimaiup ánoósuonk nꝏ̄nont ut wussogkodtunganit nokas.
22.10 Kuppadchippuhhouwónup wutch ôontomuk, ken num-Manittꝏ̄m wutch nokas wunnogkussit.
22.11 Ahque nôꝏ̄sukah, newutche wuttammepunnáonk paswohteau: newutche wanne howan nuttannumungkou.
22.12 Monáog bulsog nꝏ̄weenuhkongquog menuhkesuog Bashane bulsog nꝏ̄weenuhkongquog
22.13 Nuttôunnehtongquog onatuh qunnônou mꝏ̄hmꝏ̄skupwit, kah neeneehteadt.
22.14 Nussókem onatuh nippeh, kah wame nuskonash nꝏ̄hnꝏ̄htahshineash: nuttah onatuh wasôbôhteau ut nôeu nunnogkussit.
22.15 Nummenuhkesuonk nunnohteau ónatuh kodchuhkwishquadt, kah neenan pissogquemꝏ̄ nutó[m]peuhkô[n]it, onk kuppásꝏ̄weh uppuppissaiyeumut nuppꝏ̄wonk.
22.16 Newutche anumwog nꝏ̄weenuhkunk: matchetowog ummukkinneonganꝏ̄ nꝏ̄weenuhkongquog, kanittequómwog nunautcheash kah nusseetash.
22.17 Woh nutapogkétam wame nuskonash: nukkehkinneungquog, kah nummosompámukquog.
22.18 Chadchapenumoadtuog nuthogkꝏ̄unash, kah tanahtóadtuog nuppetashqushaonk.
22.19 Qut ahque nôꝏ̄sukah woi Jehovah, woi nummenuhkesuonk teanuk aninnumah!
22.20 Pohquahwhas nukketeahogkou wutch togkodteganit: nunnegonnꝏ̄womoneg wutch ummenuhkesuonganit anum.
22.21 Pohquohwusseh wutch qunonou wuttꝏ̄nut: newutche kenꝏ̄taup wutch wutaskonat nequtyeuun.
22.22 Nukkuhkꝏ̄tomau neematog kꝏ̄wesuonk: ut noeu mukkinneonganit kuttabuttantamoush.
22.23 Kenaa[n] quoshogish Jehovah, tabuttantamꝏ̄k: wame kenaau wuskannemu[n]neoh Jakob sohsumꝏ̄onꝏ̄k kah qushꝏ̄k wame kenaau ꝏ̄skannemunneoh Israel.
22.24 Newutche matta wutchadchepantamꝏ̄un asa wutjishontamꝏ̄un wuttammepunaonk wuttammepunahettit: asa matta puttoghomꝏ̄ wuskesuk noh whutch, qut mau[n]nitteaonk wu[u]nꝏ̄taoh.
22.25 Nuttabuttantamꝏ̄onk pish papaume ken ut mishemukkinneonganit, pish nuttussen nukquoshaumuwaongash anaquabhettit nag qushoncheg.
22.26 Manunnissuog pish meetsuog kah tabepꝏ̄og: nag tabuttantamauaog Jehovah, nag natinnewhoncheg, kuttahhꝏ̄oash micheme pomantamꝏ̄ash.
22.27 Wame aongkoue muttaôhket pish mehquoantamwog, kah quinnuppeôg en Jehovah[]ut: kah wame unnauadtuongash wuttahtimoneat pish wowussummuwaog ut anaquabean.
22.28 Newutche ketassꝏ̄tamowônk wuttaihe Jehovah: kah nagum nanaunnuwaenin kenugke wutahtimoneash.
22.29 Wame wónogqutcheg ohket pish meetsuog, kah waussumóog: wame aoncheg puppissiyeuut pish nauwaeog ut anaquabit, kah matta woh howan pomantamwaheoou, nehenwonche ukketeahogkouunuh.
22.30 Wuskannemunwog ꝏ̄wowussumouh, ne pish ogquontamun ut Jéhovah newutche pometeunk.
22.31 Nag pish peyauog, kah pish wahteauwahuwaog wussampweusseonk missinninnuh nag woh nekitcheg, yeuoh yeu mahche ussit.
23.0 {Ukketohhhomáonk} David.
23.1 Jehovah nussohkommꝏ̄nukꝏ̄waeneum, wanne teag woh nukquenaahikꝏ̄.
23.2 Nuseepsumwahik ashkoskuhkontu nutassꝏ̄wunuk ahtou pagodtut.
23.3 Wonk omohkinau nukketeahogkounoh nutussꝏ̄wunuk wunnomwausseongane mayut newutche ꝏ̄wesu[ó]nk.
23.4 Nux, pumusháon wutonkauhtómut ꝏ̄náunkôáe nuppꝏ̄onk, matta woh nukquehtamꝏ̄ woskehittúonk: newutche kꝏ̄weetomeh, kuppogkomunk, kah kutanwôhhou nꝏ̄nenehukquog.
23.5 Kꝏ̄nechꝏ̄hkah ut anaquabeh, anaquabhettit nummatwomog: kussisséqunum nuppuhkuh nashpe pummee, nꝏ̄tattámwáitch pomponeetupóhshau.
23.6 Wunnamuhkut ꝏ̄náyeuonk kah monaneteaonk pish nutásukkonkqúnash tohsohkepomantam: kah pish nutta[i]h weekit Jehovah micheme.
24.0 {Ukketohhomaonk} David.
24.1 Ohke wuttaihe Jehovah, kah neadtahshimméchimik: muttaok kah neg na wa[d]ohkitcheg.
24.2 Newutche ukquenuhtauunah kehtahhannit, kah umménuhkehtin woskeche sepuut.
24.3 Howan kóhkuhquidt ꝏ̄wadchúmut Jehovah? kah howan neepau ut ꝏ̄netupanatamwe ayeuonganit?
24.4 N$noh po[h]pohkenutchont, kah pahketeahont, noh matta tohshinunk ukketeahogkonuh tahnꝏ̄che, matta asꝏ̄kekodteaumowu chadchekeyeuog.
24.5 Noh pish attumunum ꝏ̄nanetuonk wutch Jehovah, & wunnomwausseonk wutch ꝏ̄wadchanuáe Manittꝏ̄mut.
24.6 Yeu pometeonganꝏ̄ nag natinneawhoncheg, nátinneahogig kuskesuk, woi Jakob. Selah.
24.7 Tahshinumꝏ̄k kuppuhkukꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash, woi kenaau squontamog: tahshinnutteagk micheme squontamog, kah sohsumóe ketassꝏ̄t pish petutteau.
24.8 Howan sohsumóe ketassꝏ̄t? Jehovah menuhkesu kah mishimmenuhkesu, Jehovah menuhkesu ayeúwuttuonganit.
24.9 Tohshinumꝏ̄k kuppuhkukꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash, woi kenaau squontamog: kah tohsheg michemohtáe squontamog, kah sohsumóe ketassꝏ̄t, pish petutteau.
24.10 Howan sohsumóe ketassꝏ̄t? Jehovah wutayeuwehteomuh, n noh sohsumóe ketassꝏ̄t. Selah.
25.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David.
25.1 Kutahshinnumaush, woi Jehovah, nukketeahogkou.
25.2 Woi num-Manittꝏ̄m, kuppabuhtanumoush, ahque akodchitti, nummatwomog ahque wunnantammꝏ̄wôshéttich.
25.3 Nux, ahque akodjhettich nag anoónukqueáneg: nag akodjhettich tahnꝏ̄che matchesecheg.
25.4 Kah nahtusseh kummayash, woi Jehovah, kuhkꝏ̄tomah kuttáongash,
25.5 Sagkompaguneh en kꝏ̄nomwaonganit, kah kuhkꝏ̄tomah: newutche ken nꝏ̄wadchánitteáe Manit, ken kutânóonsh qunni kesuk.
25.6 Mehquoantash, woi Jehovah, kꝏ̄womoausuwáe kitteamonteaneteaongash: kah womoausuwáe kꝏ̄nesuongash, newutche nôadt unniyeupash.
25.7 Ahque mehquontash nummatcheseonganash waskénuean, asa nuppanneseonganash: neaunag kummonaneteaonganash ne nummequanumeh, newutche kꝏ̄neseonk, woi Jehovah.
25.8 Wunneetou, kah sampwésu Jehovah: yowutche kuhkꝏ̄tomauau matcheseaenùh en mayut.
25.9 Sampꝏ̄wunnau má[n]unnissuoh en wussittumꝏ̄wonganit: kah kuhkꝏ̄tomauau mánunnissuoh en ummayut.
25.10 Wame ummayash Jehovah monaneteaonganúꝏ̄ash kah wunnomwaonganúꝏ̄ash: nah nanaihteánutche ꝏ̄nꝏ̄waonk kah ꝏ̄wauwaongash.
25.11 Newutche kꝏ̄wesuonk, woi Jehovah, ahquoantamah nummatcheseonk, newutche missi.
25.12 Howan noh quoshont Jehovah? woh ukkuhkꝏ̄tomauoh én mayut uttiyeu pepénog.
25.13 Ukketeahogkôunoh pish ayeuoh wunáyeuonganit: kah ꝏ̄skannemuneoh pish wutahtaunin ohke.
25.14 Jehovah ukkemeseongash ꝏ̄wahteauwun[á]oash nag quoshoncheg: kah pish wunnahtinoh wunnꝏ̄waonk.
25.15 Nuskesukquash nagwutteáeu unnogque Jehovahut: newutche pish kôdtinnum nusseetash wutch hashabpit.
25.16 Qunnupish en nuhhogkáeiyeu, & monanumeh: newutche nonsiyeu & nꝏ̄tamehpunám.
25.17 OOtaméhpunaongash nuttah mogkiyeuash: woi sohhꝏ̄wunneh wutch nánakompanaonganit.
25.18 Móninneash nutonkapunaonk, kah nutonkquomomꝏ̄wonk: onk ahquoantamah wame nummatcheseonganash.
25.19 Natwánum nummatwômog newutch mꝏ̄naog: kah nag nutjishanumukquog nashpe mishe jishánittuonk.
25.20 Woin nanâih nukketeahogkou, kah pohquahwusseh, ahque akodchitti newutche kuppabatanumoush.
25.21 Pannuppu wunneetowonk, kah sampweseo[n]k wadchanhettich: newutche kuttannóonsh.
25.22 Pohquahwhus Israel, woi God, wutche wame ꝏ̄tamehpunnaonganꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash.
26.0 {Ukketoohhomaonk} David.
26.1 Wussumeh, woi Jehovah, newutche nuppompomusham ut nuppannuppe wunneetowonganit: kah nuppabuhtanum Jehovah, newutche matta woh nuttꝏ̄nequssinꝏ̄h.
26.2 Natꝏ̄tomah, woi Jehovah, kah qutcheheh, qutcheh nuttꝏ̄unnussog, kah nuttah.
26.3 Newutche kꝏ̄womoausuonk anaquabe, kah nuppompomushap kꝏ̄nomwayeuonganit.
26.4 Matta nꝏ̄weetapemo tahnꝏ̄cheyeuwutcheg, asa matta pish nuppetukauóog eiantukeiyeuog.
26.5 Nussekenam ummukkinneonganꝏ̄ matchesecheg: kah matta nꝏ̄weetappemꝏ̄ matcheetowog.
26.6 Nukkutshitto nunnutchegash en pahketeahónat: nemehkuh nukquinnuppuhkom kut-Altarꝏ̄m, woi Jehovah.
26.7 Onk woh nꝏ̄wahshadtóh nashpe wuttanatongqussue tabuttantamóonk, onk woh nussinneash wame kummonchanatamwe anakausuongash.
26.8 Jehovah nꝏ̄womantam ayinneat keekit: kah ayeuonk uttoh ohtag kukquttianumutteaonk.
26.9 Ahque mukkin nukketeahogkou kenugku matcheseaenúut, asa nukkuteaonk kenugku shehteaenúut.
26.10 Wunnutcheganꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash woskêhuwómꝏ̄ash, kah wuttinnohkôunnꝏ̄ numwohteau matcheseonkquatunkash.
26.11 Qut neen nuppompomusham nuppannuppu wunneetuwonganit, pohquohwhunch kah monanumeh.
26.12 Nusset ohteau mꝏ̄saiyeuut, mukkinneonganit nuttabuttantamau Jehovah.
27.0 {Ukketoohhomaonk} David.
27.1 Jehovah nꝏ̄wequáꝏ̄m, kah nꝏ̄wadchanitteaonk, howan quóshog?
27.2 Matchetowog nummatwomog kah ayeuuhkausitcheg nohkuhkoihettit en meechinat nꝏ̄weyaus, togkussittassunwóg kah mishnkoúushsinwog.
27.3 Tohkônogque ayeuhteaog waéenuhki[e]hettit, nuttah matta wabesu: tohkônogque ayeuwuttuonk waabehtúnkquea[n], neit pish nꝏ̄tꝏ̄anatam.
27.4 Pasuk nukkodtanatamau Jehovah, ne nunnatinnehamun: onk woh nuttai weekit Jehovah tosohkepomantam, naumunat ꝏ̄nesuonk Jehovah, kah nuppeantamunat ut wut[-]templeumut.
27.5 Newutche wuttammepunnáon, pish nutáudtashuk ut weekit, ut asampâmukquodtut uppeantamwakomukqut, pish nutadtashúk, pish nukquenashhuk qussukquanit.
27.6 Onk yeuyeu nuppuhkuk tahshémꝏ̄ ánue nummatwomog qunnuppekoihettit: newutche nuttininnumau ut weekit weekontamóe sephausuongash, nukketꝏ̄hhomo[m], nux nuttinnꝏ̄homom tabuttantamꝏ̄wongash Jehovahut.
27.7 Nꝏ̄tah Jehovah mauunnitteauunon nashpe nꝏ̄wadtauatongqussuonk: onk monánumeh, kah nampꝏ̄hamah.
27.8 Nꝏ̄waan natinnehamꝏ̄k nuskesuk, nuttah kuttinuk kuskesuk, woi Jehovah, nunnadtinneóhham.
27.9 Ahque puttogwhush kuskesuk ut nóadtit wutche nen ahque kuttinninneum musquanittamwe pogkes: kuttannumaiip, a[h]que nukkósseh, asa ohqu[ȧ]numeh, woi nꝏ̄wadchanitteae Manit.
27.10 Nꝏ̄sh kah nokas ahquánuméhettit: neit Jehovah nunneemunuk.
27.11 Kuhkꝏ̄tomash kummay, woi Jehovah: kah ussꝏ̄wusseh mꝏ̄siyeuut may, newutche nummatwomog.
27.12 Ahque aninnaumau nuhhog ut wuttenantamꝏ̄onganꝏ̄óut nummatwomog: newutche pannꝏ̄wáe wauwacheg nꝏ̄waábetunkquog, kah neg nashontogig woskehuwaonk.
27.13 Woh nussauunumup, matta wunnamptamꝏ̄wóus, woh nunnaumunat ꝏ̄neséonk Jehovah kenugku neg pamontogig.
27.14 Annoôs Jehovah, wuttꝏ̄ántash, onk pish menuhkitteau kuttah: annoôs nussim Jehovah.
28.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David.
28.1 Kummauunnitteaush, woi Jehovah, nukqussukquanum, ahque cheequnappehtah, iskont chequnapehtiyean, woh nutogqunneunkqus neg womussitcheg en passohtheganit.
28.2 Nꝏ̄tash nꝏ̄wadtauatonkqussue peantamoongash, mauunnitteaunnon, spunnumon nunnutchegash ennogqueu wunneétupanatamwu kut-orackleumut.
28.3 Ahque sꝏ̄wusseh matcheetowehtu, kah kꝏ̄wutche anakausitcheg matcheseonk nnag manunne kenꝏ̄nahettit weetatteamunganꝏ̄oh, qut woskehuwaonk wuttahhꝏ̄wout.
28.4 Aninnumau naghog neaunag wutanakausuonganꝏ̄oash, kah neaunag wutussenitteaonganꝏ̄oash: aninnumau naghog neaunag wunnutcheganne anakausuonganꝏ̄oash aninnumau naghog wutonkatonganꝏ̄oash.
28.5 Newutche wanne tohhentupantamoog wutanakausuong[á]nash God, asa wunnutchegane kesteauongash, pish uppaguanuh kah matta pish ꝏ̄wekuhkonuh.
28.6 Tabuttantamauunach Jehovah, newutche nꝏ̄tam nꝏ̄wadtau[a]tonkqussuonkane peantamoonk.
28.7 Jehovah nummenuhkesuonk, kah nuttogqunneg nuttah uppabuhtanumopuh, kah nuttánumungkup: newutche nuttah misheweekontam, kah nashpe nukkeꝏ̄hhamaonk nuttabuttantamau:
28.8 Jehovah ummenuhkesuwonganouh: & sasequnoncheꝏ̄ wadchanuwae menuhkesuonk.
28.9 Woi wadcha[n] kummissinninnumog, kah wunnantash kutahtoonk: sohkomꝏ̄us wonk kah tahshin micheme.
29.0 {Ukketꝏ̄homaonk} David.
29.1 Aninnumok Jehovah, (woi magassꝏ̄tamogish) aninnumok Jehovah sohsumoonk kah menuhkesuonk.
29.2 Aninnumok Jehovah ne wussohsumoonk neaunag ꝏ̄wesuonk: woussumꝏ̄k Jehovah ut wussohsumꝏ̄ongane wunneetupanatamwé weekit.
29.3 OOwadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah ohteau woskeche nippekontu: wussohsumoe God padaquohha[n]uꝏ̄: Jehovah woskeche mishinnippekontu.
29.4 OOwadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah menuhkoi, ꝏ̄wadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah numwahteau wohquanittuonk.
29.5 OOwadtauatongqussuonk Jehovah pokshanau chikkuppemusse, nux Jehovah pokshadtou utchikkuppemussee ut Lebanon.
29.6 Onk wutayimunash quequeshaut onatuh cowashinuemesit: Lebanon, kah Syrion onatuh wushkoshimwemesu nequtyeuun.
29.7 Wadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah, chadchápenum nꝏ̄nꝏ̄náeu nꝏ̄htau.
29.8 OOwadtauatongqussuonk Jehovah ayeúau wunnechonaóont ahtuhquog: kah ꝏ̄wôshwunoh ut touohkomuk, kah ut weekit nish noh pasuk unnꝏ̄wau wussohsumowonk.
29.9 OOwadtauatongqussuonk Jehovah ayeúau wunnechonaóont ahtuhquog: kah ꝏ̄wôshwunoh ut touohkomuk, kah ut weekit nish noh pasuk unnꝏ̄wau wussohsumowonk.
29.10 Jehovah appu tomogkonehtu: nux, Jehovah michemappu ketassꝏ̄t.
29.11 Jehovah aninnumauau menuhkesuonk ummissinninneumoh: Jehovah ꝏ̄nanum[à]u ummissinninneumoh nashpe wunohteaonk.
30.0 {Ketoohhoma<e>nk, kah unno[o]hhomaonk} David, {anumaont week Goduh.}
30.1 Kutashinush, woi Jehovah, newutche kutashinip: kah matta kuttinánumop nummatwomog nutahánetunkqunnaóut.
30.2 Woi Jehovah num-Manittꝏ̄m, kummauunnitteánup, kah kenetskeheup.
30.3 Woi Jehovah, kutashin nukketeahogkou wutch weenohkeet: kuppompomantamwáheh, woh mat nuttónat weenohket.
30.4 Ketꝏ̄homók Jehovah (woi kenaau ꝏ̄neetupanatamꝏ̄moh) kah tabuttantamꝏ̄k, mehquantamóg ꝏ̄neetupanatamꝏ̄onk.
30.5 Newutche ummusquantamꝏ̄onk tiohqui: kitteamonteanumugquéog ne keteaonk: woh kummau pasuk nukon, qut nompoáeu pish kꝏ̄weekontam.
30.6 Kah wânáéon, nussip, matta pish nummicheme ontsappu.
30.7 Jehovah newutche kitteamonteanumeup, kummenuhkehteóh nꝏ̄wadchúm, kupputtagkuhhumup kuskesuk neit nꝏ̄tamehpunap.
30.8 Kummauunnitteánup, woi Jehovah: kah nuppeantamauop Jehovah.
30.9 Toh kittinanúhhumont wutche nꝏ̄sqhéonk posekinimuk: sun woh puppissai kꝏ̄waeenomuk? sun woh kuhkꝏ̄tomuhtean kꝏ̄nomwausseonk.
30.10 Nꝏ̄tah Jehovah, kah monánumeh, Jehovah aninnumah.
30.11 Kukquinnuppinnum[á]h nummauonk en pummukkônat: kutamaunumaiip nummauongane hogkꝏ̄onk, kah kupputtukquóbsip m[s]koúanatamꝏ̄ónk.
30.12 Onk woh nussohsumóonk kꝏ̄waeenomuk, kah woh matta nutchequnappu, woi Jehovah num-Manittꝏ̄m kuttabuttantamoush micheme.
31.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt: Ukketoohhomaonk} David.
31.1 Ken, woi Jehovah, kuppabuhtanumóush, ahque akodchitti: pohquahwusseh en kꝏ̄nomwausseonganit.
31.2 Ehquóhtuhquaehtuh, teanuk pohquohwusseh: ken menuhkaj nukqussukquanum, wutch nutushpuhhꝏ̄wae-komuk nꝏ̄wadchanukqunat.
31.3 Newutche ken nukqussukquanum, kah nꝏ̄wonkónous: newajeh, newutche kꝏ̄wesuonk sagkompáneh, kah sampwusháseh.
31.4 Kodtinneh na wutch hashabput uttoh ponamihetticheh kemeu, newutche ken nummenuhkesuonk.
31.5 Ut kenutcheganit kutahtôhshinun nunnashauonk: kuppohquáwussip, woi Jehovah, wunnomwáe God.
31.6 Nussekeneauóog n nag wadtꝏ̄wóntogig tahnꝏ̄che pannꝏ̄wáyeuonk: qut nuppábahtanum Jehovah.
31.7 Nꝏ̄weekontam kah nummuskouantam ut kummonaneteaonganit: newutche kenatwontamup nꝏ̄tamehpunáonk: kꝏ̄waheomp nukketeahogkou wadtamehpunáon.
31.8 Kah matta kukkuppuhh[ú]h en wunnutcheganit matwau: kupponum nussetash papahchiyeuut.
31.9 Monanumeh, woi Jehovah, newutche nꝏ̄tamehpunam: nuskesuk mohtupaémo nashpe neuantamꝏ̄wonk: nux, nukketeahogkou, kah nunnogkus.
31.10 Newutche nukketeáonk sánumꝏ̄ꝏ̄ wutch neuanatamꝏ̄wonk, kah nukkodtumꝏ̄mash nashpe mishánumꝏ̄onk: nummenuhkesuonk sánumꝏ̄mꝏ̄ newutche nummatcheseongash, kah nuskonash mohtupaémoash.
31.11 Nummamântunkuppanneg wame nummatwomog: qut nâhnâunne neetatteamunganog: kah netompaog nukqushukkuppanneg: nahetticheh ut poquadchik nꝏ̄sémoteunkquog.
31.12 Nꝏ̄wanánumukquog onatuh nánupuk wanánumit, nutogquñeukqus sukwiwshquadt.
31.13 Newutche nꝏ̄tamau monaog nukkekômukquog, wabesuonk quaquinnuppe ohteau: kânꝏ̄nittehettit moáe ayeuuhkóne neen, nukkodnushúkqunnaóont.
31.14 Qut kuppabahtanumunup, woi Jehovah, nussip, ken num-Manittꝏ̄m.
31.15 Nutaquompayeumash kenutcheganit: pohquahwusseh wutch wunnutcheganóut nummatwomog, kah nag wutch woskhukqueaneg.
31.16 Kuskesuk wôssumwahteauush kittinnumoh, wadcháneh newutch kummonaneteaonk.
31.17 Ahque akodchitti, woi Jehovah, newutche kuppeantamonsh, matcheetowog akodjhettich: kah neetoshuáhettich ut weenohkeet.
31.18 Pannꝏ̄waeu mussissittꝏ̄nash neetashumꝏ̄utch: uttiyeush matcheyeumꝏ̄ugish, p[o]htuánumweyeumꝏ̄ugish mama[n]aantamwu yeumꝏ̄ugish wunnomwaussenutcheh.
31.19 Woi uttoh nukkukqun kꝏ̄neetꝏ̄onk nish wadchanumauadcheh neg quashukkꝏ̄unneg, neananakausuwéhtauasit neg pabahtanumugqueaneg, ut anaquabhettit wosketompaog[]wunnaumonaoh.
31.20 Nag kutadtashôog wutch uppéhtuánumꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ wosketompaog, asampamukquodtit ut anaquabean: nag kemu kꝏ̄wadchanôog ut asampamukquodtut wutch meenanúe penuanittuonk.
31.21 Wun[á]numunaj Jehovah, newutche [n]ahtinuk monchanatamwu ꝏ̄womoausuonk, ut menuhke otánit.
31.22 Newutche nussip wadtamanatamon, nuttumuttahwhut wutch anaquabean: qut kenꝏ̄tamup nꝏ̄wadtauatongqussúe kenanampassumunowonk, máunnitteáuunon.
31.23 Woi womónok Jehovah, wame kenaau ꝏ̄neetupanatamꝏ̄moh, newutche Jehovah wadchanau pabahchuussenutcheh: kah mishongquttauoh pohtuanumwesenutcheh.
31.24 Wuttꝏ̄anatamꝏ̄k, onk menuhketeaou kuttahhou, wame kenaau ánoânogish Jehovah.
32.0 {Ukketoohhomaonk} David, {Maschil}.
32.1 Wunnanumau noh ummatcheseonk ahquoantamanut, kah ummatcheseonk padtagkuhwhôsik.
32.2 OOnanumau missinnin, Jehovah matta ogquanumunk ummatcheseonk: kah wuttah ut wanne asꝏ̄kekodteaumꝏ̄onk.
32.3 Matta kodtꝏ̄on, nuskonash nukkônekônúꝏ̄ash, newutche nummauonk quinnikesuk.
32.4 Newutche kesukodtáeu kah nukkonáeu kenutcheg nuttuhk[é]kꝏ̄[k]ongqun, nutogkuskesuonk óhsꝏ̄wemꝏ̄ en neepune kunkanit. Selah.
32.5 Kussampꝏ̄wontamauunup nummatcheseonk, kah matta nupputtoguhhumꝏ̄h nummatcheseonk: nussip, nussampꝏ̄am nummatcheseongash Jehovahut, neit kutahquoantamaiip nishkeneungque nummatcheseonk. Selah.
32.6 Newútche yeu, nish noh wunneetupanatamwenin pish kuppeantamunk, uttoh woh adtꝏ̄che namehhikquean: wunnamuhkut mishittomogkog, matta pish uppasꝏ̄sukauouh nnah.
32.7 Ken nutassampamukquodtꝏ̄m, pish kꝏ̄wadchâneh wutch wuttamehpunonat: pish kukquinnupohtah pohquawunnitue ketꝏ̄homaonash. Selah.
32.8 Kukkuhkꝏ̄tomoush, kah kenatinush may ut toh woh aôan: nuskesuk pish kussampshanuk.
32.9 Ahque ohqueneunkussek horsesut, asa muleuut, matta waahtamꝏ̄g: uttiyeu mós wuttꝏ̄nut kashpussik nashpe bridle-bit, ishkont kuppasꝏ̄sukkongquog.
32.10 Mꝏ̄cheke pish onkapunnꝏ̄og matcheetowog, qut n noh pabahtanumont Jéhovah, monaneteaonk pish weenuhkunk.
32.11 Weekontamꝏ̄k ut Jehovahut, muskouantamꝏ̄k kenaau sampweseogish: kah weekontamoé mishontꝏ̄wag, wame sampwutteahheogish.
33.1 Muskouanatamꝏ̄k ut Jehovah, woi sampweusseogish: tabuttantamowonk ꝏ̄nekonkqunau neg sampwesitcheg.
33.2 Wa[u]ssumꝏ̄k Jehovah nashpe harp, kꝏ̄tꝏ̄homꝏ̄k nashpe psaltery, kah puhpequonegh piogquomposik pemunneahtonash.
33.3 Ketꝏ̄hamꝏ̄k wuske ketꝏ̄homaonk: wunnepuhpequagk mishontꝏ̄womꝏ̄ut.
33.4 Newutche wuttinnowaonk Jehovah sampwi kah wame wutanakausuongásh wunnamuhkut-eyeuꝏ̄ash.
33.5 Womantam sampweusseonk, kah wussittamꝏ̄onk: ohke numwohtau ꝏ̄netꝏ̄onk Jehovah.
33.6 Nashpe wuttinnꝏ̄aonk God kesteauunash kesukquash: kah nashpe wunnashauonk wutch wuttꝏ̄nut wame neadtahsheu nag.
33.7 Mohmôunum nuppeh ketahhannet, onatuh nomungquag, ponam monóiyeuash maumachiyeu komukqut.
33.8 Wame ohke qushonch Jehovahuh: wame neg wadohkitcheg muttaohket qushahettich
33.9 Newutche kuttꝏ̄p, onk nnihyeup: wussinneuh onk menuhkahtop.
33.10 Jehovah ukkenꝏ̄nittuonganꝏ̄osh penuohteaog mo teagwunneteauunash: wuttinanatamꝏ̄onganoash missinninnuog wutayimunas[h] monteagwunninnꝏ̄ut.
33.11 Ukkenꝏ̄nittuonk Jehovah michemohteau, wuttinanatamꝏ̄wongash ut wuttahhut en wame pometeonganash.
33.12 Wunnanumau wutahtimôin wáManittꝏ̄mut Jehovah noh: kah missinninnuh, neh pepenóoncheh God nehenwonche ꝏ̄tohtoonganinnuh.
33.13 Jehovah wꝏ̄mompu wutch kesukqut, naau wame wunnaumonaoh wosketompaog.
33.14 Wutch nawadohkit, natauwompamau wame wadohkinutche ohket.
33.15 Tatuppehteau nag wuttahhꝏ̄oash: natwontam wame wutanakausuwonganꝏ̄ash.
33.16 Matta ketassꝏ̄t wadchanau nashpe mꝏ̄chequshae wutayeuwehteomoh: manuhkesit, ummishe menuhkesuonk matta pohquohwhunugkꝏ̄.
33.17 Horse tahnꝏ̄cheyeuꝏ̄ wutch wadchanittuonk: kah nashpe mishemenuhkesuonk matta pohquohwhunugkꝏ̄.
33.18 Kusseh wuskesuk Jehovah náau neh qushhukqutcheh: neg anoôsitcheg ut ummonanitteaonganit.
33.19 Pohquawhus ukketeahogkounouh wutche nuppunat, kah uppomantamwaheuh wutch mohshagqunneoneat.
33.20 Nukketeahogkou anoonau Jéhovah: noh nutannóhsueneumun, kah nutohqunneganun.
33.21 Newutche nuttahhun weekontamꝏ̄onoh, newutche nuppabahtantamumun ꝏ̄neetupanatamwe wesuonk.
33.22 Kummonaneteaonk, woi Jehovah, nuhkuhkongqutteuh, nean anoonog.
34.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David, {osuwunuk wutusseongash anaquabit} Abimelek: {noh monchaoohkauont, kah moncheu.}
34.1 Nuttabuttanamau Jehovah nagwutteaeu: tabuttantamauwaonk pish ohteau nuttꝏ̄nut yeoyatcheh.
34.2 Nukketeahogkou muskouantam Jehovahut: hohpóog pish nꝏ̄tamwog, kah weekontamwog:
34.3 Woi misheheh Jehovah weeche neen, kah môeu tahshinummuttuh ꝏ̄wesuonk.
34.4 Nunnanamptassumomp Jehovah, kah nꝏ̄tunkup: kah nuppohuohwhunukup wutch wame nꝏ̄wabesuonganit.
34.5 Wummóneauouh kah wequaiyeúmꝏ̄og: kah wuskesukꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash matta akodchumunꝏ̄ash.
34.6 Yeuoh kuttummunge wosketomp mauꝏ̄p, kah Jehovah wunnꝏ̄taòpuh, onk uppohquohwhunuh wutch wame wuttammepunnaonganit.
34.7 Wut-angelsumoh God weenuhkauwaog nag nah quoshóncheg: kah uppohquohwhuneh nah.
34.8 Woi qutchehtamꝏ̄k kah naumꝏ̄k Jehovah wunneetou, wunnanumau wosketomp noh pabahtanumont.
34.9 Woi qusheuk Jehovah kenaau ꝏ̄netupanatamꝏ̄moh: newutche neg quoshoncheg matta teag quenahukkꝏ̄og.
34.10 Wushkóshumwu qunnónꝏ̄wog quenáhukquog kah paskanantamwog: qut neg natinnewhoncheg Jehovahnoh, mat quenahukkꝏ̄og ne teag wanegik.
34.11 Peyonk peissesog nꝏ̄tiegk, kukkuhkꝏ̄tomauonumwꝏ̄ qushaonk Jehovah.
34.12 Howan nnoh kodtantog pomantamowonk, kah womantam sepepomantamun, woh wunnaumunat wanegik;
34.13 Nanaaitaash keenan wutch matcheyeuonganit, kah kussissittꝏ̄nash matta éyeumunꝏ̄utch asꝏ̄kekodteamꝏ̄wonk.
34.14 Amaehtash matchetowonk, kah wunnésish: natinnehash wunnohteaonk, kah asuhkash.
34.15 Wuskesukquash Jehovah wunnomwaénutu: kah wéhtauogash wôshweemoash en ummauonganꝏ̄óut.
34.16 Wuskesuk Jehovah ayeuuhkonau matchesenutcheh, wuttummehtahwhónat wutch mehquánumaonganꝏ̄ ohke.
34.17 Wunnomwaen mauunnitteauoh, kah God wunnꝏ̄taoh, kah uppohquohwhunoh wutche wame wuttammepunnaongash.
34.18 Jehovah uppasꝏ̄sukauoh nahog pokshunk wuttahhouwoash, kah ꝏ̄wadchanoh nahog pokshunkish wunnashauonganꝏ̄.
34.19 Monat wutonkapunaongash wunnomwausseaénin: qut Jehovah uppohquohwhunoh nish wutch wame.
34.20 Wunnanaehteau wame wuskonash: matta pasuk pokshaunnꝏ̄ut.
34.21 Matcheseonk pish nushau matcheetꝏ̄oh: kah nag sekeneauoncheg wunnomwausseaenu pish nonsayeuꝏ̄og.
34.22 Jehovah pohquohwhunau ukketeahogkôunnꝏ̄oh wuttinnumoh: kah nag pabahtanumoncheg, matta pish pasuk nonsayeueu.
35.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David
35.1 Ke[n]ꝏ̄tamwansheh woi Jehovah, wutch nag mekausitcheg, ayeúkus nnag ayeukónukque[ó]neg.
35.2 Neemunush ohqunneg kah musonkꝏ̄, kah neepaush aninnumah.
35.3 Kodtunush wonk quonnontuk, kah kuppúhhamau ummayou nag kod woskhukquéaneg: us nukketeahogkou nen kꝏ̄wadchanitteaonk.
35.4 Chepshahettich nnag, kah akodchhettich kodnushhukqueaneg: qushkehettich, kah sohquéhenaj natwontogig nꝏ̄woskhukꝏ̄onganꝏ̄.
35.5 Ogqunneungqussehettit wossadteamunit tꝏ̄unnontog waban: kah wut-angelsumoh God wunnaumatehtáhwhonch.
35.6 Ummayou pohkenaj kah tꝏ̄nequaj: kah wut-angelsumoh God wunnaumahtáhwhonch.
35.7 Newutche wanne mon teag wutch nupponahshabpunkquog ut passahthéganit, ne passahteamóhettit wutch nukketeahogkôunnoh, wanne mon teag wutch.
35.8 Paguanúonk nuhkuhkongqutch asq wâhteoóukup: kah neh ponashabpunkqueumpuh puttuhhukqutch, ne nunneáonk unnenneaj.
35.9 Kah nukketeahogkou pish weekontam Jehovahut: pish nummuskouanatam ut ꝏ̄wadchanꝏ̄waonganit.
35.10 Wame nuskonash pish nꝏ̄waog, Jehovah howan anunkquean, pohquohwhunont matchekuoh noh wutch nꝏ̄nunonche, nux matcheku, kah quenahukqut nàh wutch woskheont.
35.11 Pannꝏ̄wae woacheg nꝏ̄wabetunkquog: nuttinaunchemꝏ̄wónukqunau ne mo wahteauo.
35.12 Nutunkquatunkquog matcheseonk wutch wunneseonk, woskeheonát nukketeahogkou.
35.13 Qut neen, mahchenáhettit, nohtonke nuthogkꝏ̄onk: nutáhohpah nukketeahogkou mátta meetseon, & nuppeantamowonk qushkemꝏ̄ en nuppꝏ̄chenauónut.
35.14 Nutógqueenne neetompaut asa neematuh, naòshikquábip, onatuh maémont okasoh.
35.15 Qut onkapunnaon weekontamwog, kah miyaeog: nux matchetowog miyaeog nutayeuhkonukqunaout, kah matta nꝏ̄wahteauouun: nunnenehkshanukquog, kah matta ahqheog.
35.16 Weeche eiantukeiyeuog kah mômôntuhuénuog mahshadtuppꝏ̄hettit nummaumosketunkquog.
35.17 Jehovah tohuttꝏ̄che kummoneauóog? kenáhamash nukketeahogkou wutch ꝏ̄woskhuaonganuóut, pasukꝏ̄ꝏ̄ nuñaumon wutch qunnónꝏ̄ut.
35.18 Kuttabattantamoush ut mis[h]e mukkinneonganit: kꝏ̄wowussumush kenugku monaog missinninnúog.
35.19 Ahque nummatwomog muskouanatammꝏ̄wóushettich pannꝏ̄waeu, asuh ahque kehkehtequohtohuttehettich tahnꝏ̄che sekeneaiitcheg.
35.20 Newutche matta nꝏ̄waꝏ̄wog wunnohteaonk: qut natwontamwog asꝏ̄kekodteamꝏ̄e ahhunagish nah wutch manunaiinutche ut wuttohtawout.
35.21 Nux mishittꝏ̄naéog ayeuukone neen, nꝏ̄waog, Ho, ho, naumunan nashpe nuskesukqunónat.
35.22 Yeu kenaumun, woi Jehovah ahque chequnapash, woi Jehovah, ahque naꝏ̄sukah.
35.23 Mamonchish, kah tꝏ̄hkish en kꝏ̄sittumwanshuonkanit, kah en nuppissaumatuonganit num-Manittꝏ̄m kah nut-Jehovah.
35.24 OOsummeh, woi Jehovah, num-Manittꝏ̄m, neaunag kꝏ̄nomwausseonk, kah ahque muskouantamwonshettich.
35.25 Ahque nꝏ̄wahettich wuttahhꝏ̄wout, ho ne nukkodnehteauunnan, ahque nꝏ̄wahettich, nummisseasquinnean,
35.26 Akodchuhettich, kah moeu sohquehhenaj muskouantamohettit ut nꝏ̄woskhukqunaont: hogquehhettich akodchuonk kah mishshonanittuonk mashehtunkqueoneg.
35.27 Mishontoe wekontamohettich, muskouantamohettich tapeneagig nussampweusseonk, nux nꝏ̄wahettich nagwutteaeu mishehhunaj Jehovah noh tapeneog ꝏ̄nenehheaonk wuttinnumoh.
35.28 Kah neenan pish yeumꝏ̄ kꝏ̄nomwausseonk kahkꝏ̄wowussumunnꝏ̄wonk neteagu.
36.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ukketoohomaonk} David {wuttinneumoh} Jehovah
36.1 Ummatcheseonk matcheetou nꝏ̄wau anomut nuttah ut, qushaonk God wanne ohtano anaquabit.
36.2 Newutche waeenomou wuhhogkuh ut nehenwonche wuskesukqut nô pajeh ummatcheseonk namehteaumuk woh jishanumukquodtu.
36.3 Ukkuttꝏ̄wongash ut wuttꝏ̄nut, matcheetoash kah asꝏ̄kekodteaumꝏ̄ash: nukkodtum waontamun kah ꝏ̄nesen.
36.4 Natwontam woskehuwaonk ut wuttappinneat, ponau wuhhogkuh matta wanegenunnꝏ̄g may, matta jishantamꝏ̄ matcheseonk.
36.5 Kummonanteaonk, woi Jehovah, kesukqut ohtau, kah kꝏ̄nomwausseonk matokqsit.
36.6 Kussampweusseonk ogqunneunkquodt mogkodchuut: kꝏ̄sittumꝏ̄wongash mꝏ̄nôhshinneash: woi Jehovah kꝏ̄wadchan wosketomp kah puppinashim.
36.7 Toh nukkukque mishoadtu kꝏ̄womoausuonk, woi God, yowutche wunneechanaoh wosketompaog pabahtantamwog kenuppawhunog wutonkauhtomꝏ̄wôut.
36.8 Mꝏ̄cheke wamepꝏ̄og nashpe ꝏ̄nogkꝏ̄onk kek, kah kꝏ̄tattamhéoog kussepue weekontamꝏ̄wongash.
36.9 Newutche tohkekommue pomantamꝏ̄wonk kutahtauun: kꝏ̄weequaioumut woh nꝏ̄che naumunnean wequai.
36.10 Woi nagwutteanumau kꝏ̄womoauseónk neg wahukkꝏ̄aneg: kah kꝏ̄nomwausseonk neg sampwutteahhoncheg.
36.11 Ahque pittuanumwemuseet ayeuuhkonsitch: kah ahque wunnutcheg matcheetou ontsinukquttei.
36.12 Anakausitcheg matcheseonk ne wuttit penushonau: kepuhkonog, kah matta pish tapenumoog neepaun.
37.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David.
37.1 Ahque musquanum kuhhog newutche matchesecheg, onk ahque iskáaus anakausitcheg matcheseonk.
37.2 Newutche pish teanuk: tummehtahwhoog onatuh moskehtuut, kah pish uppꝏ̄pásuog onatuh oshkoshqut.
37.3 Pabuhtanum Jehovah kah wunnesish, neit pish kꝏ̄tohkin yeu ohke, kah wunnamuhkut pish kussohkommꝏ̄nt.
37.4 Wonk tapeneau kuhhog en Jehovahut, kah pish kittinninnumunk kukkodtantamꝏ̄wongash ut kuttahut.
37.5 Ahtuhsh kummay Jehovah, kah pabahtanum, kah pish kittinuhkqun.
37.6 Onk pish wussohwhuttauun kꝏ̄nomwausseonk neane wequai, kah kꝏ̄sittumꝏ̄onk onatuh puhshaquodt.
37.7 Anwohsinous Jehovah, manunne annous ahque musquanum kuhhog newutche noh wónaiit ut ummayut, newutche wosketomp noh kesteunk matanatammóongash.
37.8 Netahshe musquantash, ahqueteaush chenauausuonk, ahque musquanam kuhhog ne teag wutch matchesenat.
37.9 Newutche matchesecheg pish tummehtahwhoog: qut yeug anounoncheg Goduh pish wutahtauunneau ohke.
37.10 Newutche teanuk kah pish mat matcheetowenuunnꝏ̄, nux, menuhke pish kenatwontam wutayeuonk, kah wanne ohtano.
37.11 Qut manunnissuog pish wutahtauuneau ohke, kah pish tapeneaumwog monát wunnohteaonk.
37.12 Matchetou kodwoskéheau sampweusenutcheh, kah ummomoskéetauóuh.
37.13 Jehovah wutáhanehtauoh newutche wunnaumaoh usskesukodtum peyaúmꝏ̄uk.
37.14 Matchetou sohwhunnum wuttogkodteg, kah anchuppinohtau, noh wuttin penohkonát matchekuoh kah quenahukqunutche kah nushonat sampweussecheg.
37.15 Wuttogkodtegano pish aumꝏ̄ nehenwonche wuttahhꝏ̄wóut, wutahtompeyeuoh pish pokshauoh.
37.16 O[h]guhsadchasuadt sampweusseaenin, anúhkâaumonaoh matchetowoh ꝏ̄weenaieetuonganꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash.
37.17 Newutche wôhpittenash matchetou pish poksheau; qut Jehovah tahshinau wunnomwausseaenu.
37.18 Jehovah wahteau ukkesukkodtumash sampwesenutche kah ne ahtaahettit pish michemeyeuꝏ̄.
37.19 Matta pish akodchuog ut matcheetinat kah mashogque kesukodtut pish wamepꝏ̄og.
37.20 Qut matchetou pish onkuppunnau: kah ummatwomoh Jehovah pish onatuh Lambse wanogqut, nag pish mohsepaeog, pish pukutau[ꝏ̄]og.
37.21 Matcheetou nogohkou qut matta wonk wunnompenumꝏ̄un: qut wunnomwausseaenin, monaneteau, kah ummagu[n].
37.22 Newutche neh wánanumoncheh pish wutohtauneau ohke: qut nag matchenanumoncheh pish tummehtahwhoog
37.23 Wutontanehtuongash wunneetou ummenuhkehteunash God kah tapeneam ummay.
37.24 Tokonogque uppenushon matta pish papukquane kepshaꝏ̄; newutche Jehovah wuttahshinoh nashpe wunnutcheg.
37.25 Nꝏ̄skenneuꝏ̄p, yeuyeu nummattauntam, qut asq nuppaje n[aáu]n wunnomwaussu ahquanumon, asa ꝏ̄skannemunneoh weenshau petukqunnunk.
37.26 Micheme mona[n]eteau, kah nogohkaeihhuun: kah ꝏ̄skannemuneoh ꝏ̄nanumoneuh.
37.27 Amaéhtash matcheseonk, kah wunnesish; neit micheme wutohkish.
37.28 Newutche Jehovah womantam wussittumꝏ̄wonk, kah matta ahquanumáou wunneetupanatamwoh: nag micheme wadchanꝏ̄og, qut ꝏ̄skannemunnuoh matcheetowog pish tummehtahwhôog.
37.29 Sampweusseaenuog pish ꝏ̄tohkinneau ne ohke, kah ne pish ꝏ̄tohkinneau micheme.
37.30 Wuttꝏ̄n sampweusseaenin missohham waantamꝏ̄wonk, kah weenan weogquttamꝏ̄mꝏ̄ wussittumꝏ̄wonk.
37.31 Wuttinnaumatuonk um-Manittꝏ̄moh ohteau wuttahut, wanne pasuk wuttóntanehtuonk tꝏ̄nequshininnꝏ̄.
37.32 Matchetou askuhwau wunnomwausseaenu, kah ukkodtinneánuh.
37.33 Jehovah matta pish wunnukkonuh ut wunnutcheganit kah wussumahettit, matꝏ̄sumau.
37.34 Anous Jehovah, kah muttumash ummay, kah pish kutashinuk kutahtaunat ohke: matchetowog tummehtahwhut pish kenaumun.
37.35 Nunnaumup matcheetowog missi uppiohquttumóonganꝏ̄, uppenaekinneat onatuh askuhquâmut nehenwonche neepadtag.
37.36 Qut amaemꝏ̄, kah kusseh matta ohtano: nux nunnatinneawhop qut matta nunnamheuh.
37.37 Tuppanum pannuppu wunneetou, kah náou sampwesit: newutche adwòhkukquosik noh wosketomp wunnohteaonganuꝏ̄.
37.38 Qut matchesecheg pish moeu paguanôog; ꝏ̄wohkukquosinnunnaoont matchetowog, pish tummehtahwhoog.
37.39 Qut wadchanaonganꝏ̄ wunnomwausseaenuog, ꝏ̄mꝏ̄ꝏ̄ Jehovahut: & nag ummenuhkesuonganꝏ̄oh wuttammepunahettit.
37.40 Kah Jehovah pish wuttannunnumaoh, kah pish uppohquohwhunuh; pish uppohquohwhunoh wutch matcheetowut kah wadchanoh, newutche uppabahtanumukquoh.
38.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David {mehquontamwahuon}.
38.1 WOi Jehovah ahque auskomeh musquantaman: asa ahque sasamukouheh kossoppag kummusquantamꝏ̄onk.
38.2 Newutche kóunkquodtash patukshauash nuhhogket: kah kenutcheh mꝏ̄cheke nukkinnequohkunk:
38.3 Wanne pasquanninnꝏ̄ nꝏ̄weyaus newutche kummusquantamꝏ̄onk: kah wanne anwósinninnꝏ̄ash nuskonash newutche nummatcheseonk.
38.4 Newutche nummatcheseonganash wunnuhkukkonkqunash nuppuhkuk: onatuh tuhkequod weanin, naish wussaume tahkekhukqunash.
38.5 Nuttanhukkash matchemungquot, kah anittash newutche nutasꝏ̄tuonk.
38.6 Nꝏ̄tamanatam, mꝏ̄cheke nꝏ̄wonkohkom: pumuhshaon n[u]mmau qunnekesukod.
38.7 Newutche nusseganohtogqut numwohteau neechepunaonk, wanne menuhkano nꝏ̄weyaus
38.8 Nꝏ̄chumwes kah nutchechishqusham, nummauup newutche nꝏ̄tamehpunam nuttahhut.
38.9 Lord wame nukkodtantammoonk ohteau anaquabean, kah nutauwakontꝏ̄waonk mutta assampamukquodtinnꝏ̄ wutch kuhhogkaoo[u].
38.10 Nuttah tetequshin, nummenuhkesuonk sanummꝏ̄mꝏ̄: kah nunnaumꝏ̄wongan ut muskesukqut wonk amaemoi,
38.11 Womonukqueaneg, kah neetompaog nukqushhukkongquog wutch nukkehkechesuonk, kah anunkomogig nuppechohkongquog.
38.12 Kah neg wonk kadtinneanukqueaneg, nupponamungquog apehhunnah, kah kod[-]woskehhukqueanég nummamatchenukquog, kah natwontamwog asꝏ̄kekodteaumꝏ̄wonk quinnikesuk.
38.13 Qut neen, onatuh kókobsont,matta nꝏ̄táoog: kah nutogqunneungqussip mokaketꝏ̄muk, mo waushwunnumꝏ̄g wuttꝏ̄n,
38.14 Nemehkuh nutogqunneungqussip mo nanꝏ̄tamꝏ̄k, kah wanne auskomuwaongash wutꝏ̄nut.
38.15 Newutche ken Jehovah kuttannóonsh pish kenꝏ̄tah woi Jehovah num-Manittꝏ̄m.
38.16 Newutche nussip nꝏ̄tah, iskont nuttoontahkanukquog: nusseet tꝏ̄nukqushik mishehheaog wuhhogkauh nutayeukonukqunnaout.
38.17 Newutche nahen nukkꝏ̄kqunnukshom, káh neuantamꝏ̄onk nagwutteaeu ohteau anaquabeh.
38.18 Newutche nupahketeaun nummatcheseonk: nunneuantam wutche nummatcheseonk.
38.19 Qut nummatwomog wunnetantauneau, kah menuhkesuog kah [n]ag tahnꝏ̄che sekeneunkqueóneg monaog.
38.20 Kah nag wonk onkquatausitcheg matchet wutche wunnegen nutayeuuhkonukquog, newutche nutahsuhkom ne wanegig.
38.21 Ahque ohquanumeh woi Jehovah; woi num-Manittꝏ̄m, ahque naꝏ̄sukah.
38.22 Kenuppe aninnumah woi Jehovah, nꝏ̄wadchanitteaonk.
39.0 {Nohtumpuhpequodt ut Jeduthun: ukketoohomaonk} David.
39.1 Nussip nutahqueteounash nummayash onk woh matta nummatchesu ut neenanut: nunnanaueihteoh nuttꝏ̄n nashpe bridle matcheetowog anaquabeh.
39.2 Mo nukkaketꝏ̄p chequnappean: nutchequnapip wutch wunnegenut, kah nunnuantamꝏ̄onk woggkouemꝏ̄p.
39.3 Nuttah kussoppiyop anomut nuhhogkat, natwontamon nꝏ̄tau chikohtop: neit nukkeketꝏ̄komp neenanuut.
39.4 Jehovah ayimah wahteaun nꝏ̄wohkukquosinꝏ̄wonk; kah quttuhhumun nukkesukkodtumash teagua; onk woh nꝏ̄wahteoun toh anukuhquohtei.
39.5 Kusseh kuttinnukkuhqutteah nukkesukkodtumash menutcheg neanuhkuhque kiskag kah nussepepomantamoonk wanne teag ut anaquabean, wunnamuhkut nish noh wosketomp ut menuhkesit, pannuppu tahnꝏ̄cheyeuꝏ̄. Selah.
39.6 Wunnamuhkut nish noh wosketomp pomushau tahnꝏ̄che onatuh onkauohtaut: wunnamuhkut nag wuttamanatamwog tahnꝏ̄che: numwonkquottou weenauweetuonganash, kah matta wahheoꝏ̄ howane pish mohmounumunit.
39.7 Kah yeuyeu Jehovah, teaguas nutannoantam? kuttannoonsh.
39.8 Pohquáhwusseh wutche wame nummatcheseonganash, ahque ayimah wutuspunamoaonganꝏ̄ asꝏ̄kutcheg.
39.9 Mat nukkaketꝏ̄p, mat nꝏ̄waoshwunnumop nuttꝏ̄n, newutche kutussenap.
39.10 Amaunumah kuttogkomꝏ̄waonk: nummohchikonaip nashpe wuttógkomuaonk kenutcheg.
39.11 Auskomue sasamatahwadcheh wosketomp newutche ummatcheseonk, kutayimun ꝏ̄neetuonk mahchemꝏ̄ onatuh moth: wunnamuhkut nish noh wosketomp tahnꝏ̄cheyeuꝏ̄. Selah.
39.12 Nꝏ̄tash nuppeantamꝏ̄wonk woi Jehovah, kah kuhkeitash nummauonk, ahque chequnapsh ut nussuppequnut, newutche nuppenowohteau ut anaquabean, kah nuppenowohteau neane wame nꝏ̄shunnonog.
39.13 Woi Ahque onk woh nummenuhkes, asquam ne mamonchean, kah matta wonk nutappein.
40.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ukketoohomaonk} David.
40.1 Nummanunne annoónup wutch Jehovah, kah nukkeihketunk, kah nꝏ̄tam nummauonk.
40.2 Kah nukkodtinuk wutch uhqueneungquotte pohshahtheganit, wutch pisseagquane manꝏ̄nskut, kah ponam nusseetash qussukquanit, kah menehketeau nuppomushaonganash.
40.3 Onk ponam wusku ketꝏ̄homaonk nuttꝏ̄nut, wáussumonat num-Manittꝏ̄mun, monaog pish wunnaumunneau, kah pish wabesuog, kah pish pabahtanumꝏ̄og Jehovah.
40.4 OOnanumau noh wosketomp ayig uppabuhtanumaonk Jehovah noh, kah matta tohhentupanumonk pihtuanumꝏ̄oh, asa yeuhoh quashkenutcheh en pannuwayeuonganehtu.
40.5 Monatash, woi Jehovah, num-Manittꝏ̄m, kummonchanatamwe anakausuongásh nish kesteauanish; kah kittinanummewonganinnonash, matta woh kuttápohkeetamonteanâsh: tohneit pahketeawon, kah kenꝏ̄tamon monataash onk woh na adtashogkeetamuk.
40.6 Sephausuonk kah magoonk, matta kukkodtantamꝏ̄unash, nutteauogash kuppohquanumup: chikohtae magꝏ̄ongash, kah matcheseongane sephausuongash matta kussein nash aninnumaiegk.
40.7 Neit nussip, kusseh nuppeyaum, kꝏ̄sukkuhwhonganit tannussukkuhwhosu papaume nen.
40.8 Nꝏ̄wekontam ussen kuttinanatámꝏ̄wonk, woi num-Manittꝏ̄m, nux kuttinnaumatuonk anomut nuttahut.
40.9 Nukkuhkꝏ̄tomwehteam sampweusseonk ut mishemukkinneonganit, kusseh matta nussissetonash chequnohtanoash, woi Jehovah kꝏ̄wahteoun.
40.10 Matta nutadtahtoou kꝏ̄nomwausseonk anomut nuttahhut, nuppahketeounap kussampweusseonk kah kꝏ̄wadchanuwaonk: matta nuputtagg[u]hhumꝏ̄ kꝏ̄womoausuonk kah kꝏ̄nomwayeuonk wutche mishemukkinneonganit.
40.11 Ahque kogkôunumah kukkitteamonteanitteae monaneteaonk, woi God; kukkitteamonteanitteaonk, kah kꝏ̄nomwayeuonk nagwutteaeu wadchanehettich.
40.12 Newutche woh mo tâpogkeetamounash matchetowonganash nꝏ̄weinuhkongqunash nummatcheseongash [n]ukkogkonunuk newaj wanne nuttapenummꝏ̄ ishpuhquain: monatash onk neadtahshik nummeesunk ut nuppuhkuhqut, newaje nuttah sauwunuk.
40.13 Wussikketea[n]ininaj, woi Jehovah, pohquohwusseh, woi Jéhovah, kenuppu aninnumáh.
40.14 Nag akodchhettich, káh moaeu chepshahettich kodnushoncheg nukketeahogkounoh, nag a[sô]ꝏ̄hkaunaj kah akodchhenaj matcheanumukqueaneg,
40.15 Nonsayeuwehhettich, newutche wutonkatonganꝏ̄ akodchuonk, anukqueaneg ho ho:
40.16 Wame nattinneahukqueaneg, wekontamꝏ̄onukqush, muskouanatamonukqush newutche ken: neg womontogig kꝏ̄wadchanꝏ̄waonk, nagwutteaeu nꝏ̄wahettich, Jehôvah mishshehenaj.
40.17 Qut nummatchek kah nukquenanhuk, onch Jehovah nummehquanumuk, ken nuttannosuenu, kah nuppohq[u]awussuénu ahque pitchinw[ô]ish woi num-Manittꝏ̄m.
41.0 {Nohtompuhpequod ukketoohomaonk} David.
41.1 Wunnanumau n noh tatabpanumont mátchekuoh: Jehovah pish uppohquohwhunoh wuttammepunanit.
41.2 Jehovah pish ꝏ̄wadchauôh, pish uppomantamwaheuh, kah pish wunnanumau yeuut ohket: kah matta pish kupponoh wuttinanatamꝏ̄onganout ummatwomoh.
41.3 Jehovah ummenuhkehheuh ut ummahchekonaeyeu appinneat; kꝏ̄nashinnumau wame wuttappinneat mahchinait.
41.4 Nussip Jehovah monanumeh neetskeh nukketeahogkou, newutche kummatchenehhesh.
41.5 Nummatwomog nummatchenukquog, aquompak woh nupuk, kah ꝏ̄wesuonk nuppꝏ̄mꝏ̄?
41.6 Kah natauwahit, tahnꝏ̄che keketꝏ̄kau: wuttahhoh mukkinnumont matcheseonk, sohhog, wuttinnaunchemwin.
41.7 Wame sekeneaitcheg nukkehkemwâ[ô]nukquog, ayeuuhkonittue natwontamwog nꝏ̄woskhukkꝏ̄onganꝏ̄.
41.8 Nꝏ̄waog, matcheepunaonk menuhkodtau wuhhogket: kah yeuyeu seepsik, matta pish wonk omohku.
41.9 Nux nehenwonche neetomp sompwanumog n noh sompwanumog, n noh meechup nupputtukqunnunk, nuttogskunk.
41.10 Qut ken Jehovah monanumeh, kah omohkineh, onk woh nutonkquttau.
41.11 Yeu nashpe nꝏ̄wahteoun kꝏ̄sekitteahe, newutche nummatwom, matta nutahanetunkꝏ̄.
41.12 Qut neen, kutahshineh nussámpwutteahaonganit kah kupponeh anaquabean micheme.
41.13 Waussumunaj Jehováh um-Manittꝏ̄m Israel, wutche micheme yea[n] micheme[.] Amen kah Amen.
42.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt Maschil wutch wunnaumonuh} Korah.
42.1 Onatuh sâakussit aiump ut sepuussit: netatupe nukketeahogkou wuttinsanunumun wutche ken, woi God.
42.2 Nukketeahogkou kuhketꝏ̄n Goduh, pomantamwae Goduh uttoh ahquompe woh peyaon kah woh nunnait ut anaquabit God?
42.3 Nussuppegwunash nummeechinapash kesukodaeu kah nukonaeu, nagwutteaeu nag anukquean uttiyeuwoh kum-Manittꝏ̄m.
42.4 Yeush mehquontamon, nussewoh nukketeahogkou ut nuhhogket: newutche nꝏ̄weechauomp monacheg: nꝏ̄weechauopanneg en wekit God, wadtáuatonkqussue nꝏ̄weekontamoonkanun, kah nꝏ̄wawussumaonganun weeche monacheg nananimohhettit peántamwakesuk.
42.5 Tohwutch penuhteaan woi nukketeahogkou, kah tohwutch wuttamanataman ut nuhhogkat, annóôsish en Godut, newutche pish nꝏ̄wowussum, newutche nuttannunumunk wuttinnissuonk.
42.6 Woi num-Manittꝏ̄m nukketeahogkou penuhkon ut nuhhogkat newutche kꝏ̄wáanumush wutch ohkit Jordan, kah Hermonites, kah wutch wadchu Missar.
42.7 Mahskehtugk weéquetum monoi mashantꝏ̄womꝏ̄ug sokanon, wame kuttugkꝏ̄mog kah kuttontukquog nupaumukongquog.
42.8 Qut Jehovah anꝏ̄nau ꝏ̄womoausuonk kesukodaeu, kah nukkonaeu ukketꝏ̄homaonk nꝏ̄weetomup, kah nuppeantamauaonk pomantamoe num-Manittꝏ̄m.
42.9 Nuttinh God, nukqussukquanum, tohwutch wananumean? tohwutch wutohposeh, newutche ꝏ̄woskhuwaonganꝏ̄ nummatwomog.
42.10 Togkodteg nuskonut ukkekomuwaonganꝏ̄ nummatwomog, ashettit askesukokish, uttiyeuoh kum-Manittꝏ̄m.
42.11 Tohwutch penuhteaán woi nukketeahogkou, kah tohwutch wutamanumea[n] ut nuhhogkat? anoas God; newutche onch nꝏ̄wowussum, noh uppomantamowonk nuttinnissuonk, kah num-Manittꝏ̄m.
43.1 Wussumeh, woi God, keketꝏ̄hkansheh en matcheetowog wutahtuóut: woi pohquohwusseh wutch asꝏ̄kekodteamocheg, kah mat sampweussegig.
43.2 Newutche um-Manittꝏ̄moh nummenuhkesuonk, tohwhutch pogkésean? tohwhutch wutohpôseh newutch ꝏ̄woskhúaonganꝏ̄ nummatwomog?
43.3 Woi annꝏ̄s kꝏ̄wequaiꝏ̄m kah kꝏ̄nomwayeuonk, nag sagkompagunéhhettich: nag pasꝏ̄wéhettich kꝏ̄neetupanatamwe wadchúut kah keekit.
43.4 Neit pish nuttóm wut-altarit God en Godut mussi nꝏ̄weekontamóonk: nux: ut harput kꝏ̄waeenomoush, woi Manit, num-Manittꝏ̄moh.
43.5 Tohwhutch penuhteáan woi nukketeahogkou, kah tohwutch wuttamanuméan ut nuhhogkut, anôas God, newutche onk onch nꝏ̄w[a]wussum, noh uppomantamóonk nuttinnissuonk kah num-Manittꝏ̄m.
44.0 {Nohtompehpequodt wutch wunnaumonuh} Korah.
44.1 NOOtamúmunnónup nashpe nuttaúogunnónut, woi God, nꝏ̄shunnónog nuttugqunnanónup, chagua anakausuonk kukkesteaoun nag ukesukkodtumꝏ̄wóut nꝏ̄adtit.
44.2 Kukquonsꝏ̄kauópanneg penuohteaog nashpe kenutcheganit, kah kuppasuopaneg: kutonkapunnanomp missinninnuog, kah kuppogkenópanneg.
44.3 Newutche matta ꝏ̄tahtauóunneau ne ohke nashpe nehenwonche wuttogkodteg, kah nehenwonche wóhpitténꝏ̄ wadchanukuppanneg, qut kuttinohkou kah kuppit, kah wussohsumoonk kuttinnussúonk newutche ken kukkitteamonteanumópanneg nnag.
44.4 Ken nukketassꝏ̄timom woi God: anꝏ̄hteámꝏ̄ pohquohwussuaongash wutche Jakob.
44.5 Nashpe ken nukkepuhteamun nummatwomunonog: nashpe kꝏ̄wesuonk nutahtaskuhkôunnonog ayeuhkonukqueagig.
44.6 Newutche matta nuppabahtanumoh nutahtomp, asa nuttogkodteg matta pish nuppohquohwhunugkꝏ̄h.
44.7 Qut kꝏ̄wadchannimun wutch nummatwomunonut: kah kutakodchehheoog neg sekeneunkqueagig.
44.8 En Godut mꝏ̄cheke nꝏ̄weekontamumun nehteagu: kah nꝏ̄woeenodtumumun kꝏ̄weesuonk micheme. Selah.
44.9 Qut kuppogkesumun, kah kutakodchehimun, kah matta kꝏ̄weeche sohhammꝏ̄tamꝏ̄ nukkesauwameonganun.
44.10 Kukqushkꝏ̄kayimun wutch matwout: kah nag sekeneunkqueogig mukkꝏ̄kinnuwaog wutch wuhhogkauh
44.11 Kuttinnumauoog nuhhogkanonuh onatuh shepsog mꝏ̄hwhut, kah kussiswahimun ut penuwohteatu.
44.12 Kummag kummissinninnumog wutch monteag, onk matta kꝏ̄chenaetu wuttinnoadtuonganꝏ̄.
44.13 Kutayimaiimun nukkekomukkꝏ̄wonganun neetatteamunganonut, nummamanauwanummitteaonganun kah nutahanehtonteaonganun neg weenuhkongqueogig.
44.14 Nꝏ̄woweenwhomukkꝏ̄onganun kutayimaiimun kenugke penuwohteaog: nununukkuhquohtunkqunanonut missinninnuog.
44.15 Nukquenauanumoonk nagwutteohteau anaquabeh kah nuskesukqu[u]e akodchuonk nunnuhkukko[n]gqun.
44.16 Newutche ꝏ̄wadtauatonkqussuonk nnoh kekomukqueog kah noh blasphemont: newutche matwau kah anꝏ̄toaenin.
44.17 Wame yeush nunnuhkukkongqunnanonash: onk onch matta kꝏ̄wannanumunnꝏ̄mun: asa matta nuppannꝏ̄waussumun wutch kꝏ̄nꝏ̄waonk.
44.18 Nuttahhun matta qushkeu; asa nutôntanehtuonganunnonash matta panneomunꝏ̄ash ut kummayut.
44.19 Tokonogque mꝏ̄cheke kuppokshassunau wutohtuout Dragonsog: kah kupputtagkuhhimun wutonkaohtom nuppꝏ̄onk.
44.20 Wananatamôgis ꝏ̄wesuonk num-Manittꝏ̄mun; asa spu[nnn]umauogit nutcheganunnonash pénowe Manittꝏ̄og.
44.21 Sunnummatta woh God wunnatinneahhamꝏ̄un? newutche wahyeau keme unnantamꝏ̄onk nuttahhut.
44.22 Nux wutche ken nunnashshitteàmun quinnikesuk: nutogquanumu[ttt]eamun onatuh sheep nohshit.
44.23 Tꝏ̄hkish tohwutch kouean woi Jehovah, omkish ahque pogkesinan micheme.
44.24 Tohwutch puttoghuman kuskesuk onk wanantaman nuttonkapunnaongan, kah nꝏ̄woskhetteyaonganan.
44.25 Newutche nukketeahogkôunnun n[ô]áyeu en puppissiyeúut nunnogkussen menuhkohteau ohkekontu.
44.26 Omohkish aninnumaiinnean, onk pohquohwussinnan wutch kummonaneteaonk.
45.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut Shoshannim wutch wunnaumonuh} Korah, {Maschil: womoausuoohomaonk}
45.1 Nuttahhut mohchekomeetau wanegik: nussinneash nutayimmoongash papaume ketassꝏ̄t: neenân ummequnuh kenupsukqwhosu.
45.2 Kummꝏ̄cheke wompes onk wunneechanꝏ̄oh wosketompáog, wunneetupanatamꝏ̄wonk sokanumun kussissetꝏ̄nut: newajeh God wananumukquean micheme.
45.3 Wushpinnaush kuttogkomoneg ut kehquâut woi másugkénan, weeche kussohsumowonk kah kꝏ̄wohquânumꝏ̄onk.
45.4 Kah kꝏ̄wohquanumꝏ̄wonganit, wunnaiyeue náiyeumukqush, newutche wunnomwayeuonk, manunnissuonk kah wunnomwausséonk: kah kuttinnohkou kukkuhkꝏ̄tomunk uhquinneunkquokish.
45.5 Kukkouhquodtash kenaiyéuash ut wuttahhꝏ̄wout Ketassꝏ̄t ummatwomoh: ne nashpe penushahettit missinninnuog ut agwe ken.
45.6 Kutappuonk, woi God, michemohteau kah micheme, kukketassꝏ̄tamoe togkodteg sampwe togkodteg.
45.7 Kꝏ̄womontam sampweusseonk, kah kussekeneam matcheseonk: ne wajeh God kum-Manittꝏ̄m sussequanukquean nashpe weekontamoe pummee mꝏ̄cheke onk neg weechaiyeumukqueaneg.
45.8 Wame kuthogkꝏ̄ongash assumungquodtash myrre, aloes, kah cassia: wutch Ivory weetuomash, uttoh waj muskouanatamhinumuk.
45.9 Ketassꝏ̄tamwog wuttaunꝏ̄oh wee[c]haiyeumaog wuttꝏ̄wuttumwossissoh: kuttinnohkôunit sonksq wunnepaun golde hogkꝏ̄unash wutch Ophir.
45.10 Nꝏ̄tah (nuttaunes) kah natwontash kah kukkeitash: wannanum wonk nehenwonche kummissinninnumog, kah kꝏ̄sh week.
45.11 Neit ketassꝏ̄t mꝏ̄cheke kodtantam kꝏ̄neetuonk newutche noh kum-Manittꝏ̄m kah noh wowussum.
45.12 Kah wuttaunoh Tyre na pish wutappen paudtaun magꝏ̄onk: weenaeetuog kenugke missinninnuut pish kꝏ̄wonkkumukquog.
45.13 Wuttaunoh ketassꝏ̄t pannuppe sohsum anomut, wuthogkꝏ̄ongash assequosu Gold.
45.14 Pish pasꝏ̄au ketassꝏ̄tamwut, wuthogkꝏ̄unit ayinneas ahómogquesuuk, nunksquaog, weechayeumonche asukkonkqutcheh pish kuppaudtonteanunk.
45.15 Pish weekontamwe kah muskouantamwe pasouꝏ̄og: pish petutteaog ketassꝏ̄t weekit.
45.16 Kꝏ̄shuwꝏ̄g keneechánuwôog pish wunnómpekompanean yeug woh kussontimóhkouog wame ohkeit.
45.17 Nutayum kꝏ̄wesuonk mehquantamunat ut wame pometuonganit: newajeh pish missinninnuog kꝏ̄waeenomukquog micheme kah micheme.
46.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt wutch wunnaumonuh} Korah {ketoohomaonk ut Alamoth}
46.1 Jehovah nꝏ̄tusphuaonganun, kah nummenuhkesuonganun: kenupaninnohsu wuttammepunaùmuk.
46.2 Newajeh matta wabeseog tokonogque óntohtag ohke, kah tokonogque wadchuash óntahtag en nôeu ketahhannit.
46.3 Ketahhannuppog mishontowag, kah tukkꝏ̄ꝏ̄ꝏ̄gk, wadchuash quequog muttaontukꝏ̄k. Selah.
46.4 Na seip n ne kussitchuan weekontamwahtunk wutꝏ̄tan God: wunneetupanatamwohke week nôappit.
46.5 God nôeu appu, matta pish ontappu, God pish wuttannunnummaoh nompôaeu.
46.6 Penuwohteaog musquantamwog, asꝏ̄támꝏ̄ongash ontahtaash, mishontowau, ohke mohtupaémo.
46.7 Wut-Jehovahnumꝏ̄oh ayeutoáog kꝏ̄wetomukqun: ummanittꝏ̄moh Jakob kuttusphuaonganun. Selah.
46.8 Peyunk naumꝏ̄k wutanakausuonganash Jehovah, uttoh in paguanuongash wutayimun ut[]ohkeit.
46.9 Sohkom ayeuhteaongash aongkouokhomuk: pohqunau ohtompeh; pohquetahham qunnunktug, chikohsum chariotsash ut nꝏ̄taut.
46.10 Chequnappek, kah wahteauꝏ̄k neen Manit, pish nummishhet ut penuwohteátu: pish nummishhet ohket.
46.11 Wut-Iehovahnumꝏ̄oh ayeuteaog kꝏ̄weetomukqun, um-Manittꝏ̄moh Jakob kuttusphuáonganun. Selah.
47.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ketoohhomaonk wutch wunnaumonuh} Korah.
47.1 Woi puhpunkanitcháhꝏ̄k wame missinninnuog, mishontꝏ̄wag en Godut, nashpe sohkuhsue mishontꝏ̄waonk.
47.2 Newutche Jehovah quanunkquapit [û]hqunneongqussu: nnoh kehchu ketassꝏ̄t wame muttaohket.
47.3 Pish sohkauau missinninnuh kenaan ut agwu; kah wutohtimóneash agwu kusseetinnónut.
47.4 Pish kuppépenamwanshhikqun kutohkein: ꝏ̄neetuonk Jakob neh womononcheh. Selah.
47.5 Manittou spéi nashpe mishontowaonk: Jehovah nashpe kuttꝏ̄wómꝏ̄ monopuhpeg.
47.6 Nꝏ̄homunk waeenomaongash God, nꝏ̄hhomunk waeenomaongash: nꝏ̄hhomunk waeenomaongash kukketassꝏ̄tomomun nꝏ̄homunk waussumaongash.
47.7 Newutche God keitassꝏ̄timꝏ̄ꝏ̄ wame muttaohket, nꝏ̄hhomunk waantamwu waeenomaongash.
47.8 God nánauneau pénuwohteoh: God appu wunneetupanatamwu wutappuonganit.
47.9 Nanaunoncheg missinninnuh moeog, ummissinninnumoh um-Manittꝏ̄moh Abraham: newutche muttaohke ogqunnegash wutchayeuꝏ̄oash Godut: nnoh mꝏ̄cheke mishehheuh.
48.0 {Annoohhomae keto[h]homaonk wutch wunaumonuh} Korah.
48.1 Missugken Jehovah, kah mishewa[e]enomau wuttꝏ̄tanit kum-Manittꝏ̄mun, wunneetupanatamwu wadchumut.
48.2 Wunnohteau, ꝏ̄weekontamꝏ̄wonk wame muttaok ne wadchu Sion, nanummuttinneaou, wutꝏ̄tan mishe ketassꝏ̄t.
48.3 God wahheau weekuwout wuttusphuaonganꝏ̄.
48.4 Newutche kusseh ketassꝏ̄tamwog moieog, môeu paumushaog.
48.5 Wunnamuneau, nemehkuh ummonchanatamunneau, ꝏ̄tamanatamunneau, ꝏ̄semutteamunneau.
48.6 Na ut wabesuonk tohqunukquog, kah onkquammamꝏ̄onk, onatuh mittamwossis [n]eechadt.
48.7 Kuppokshadtoh Tarshishe kuhtꝏ̄nogquosh wutchepwosh.
48.8 Neane nꝏ̄tamog, ne kittinne naumunnan ut wutꝏ̄tanit um-Manittꝏ̄mꝏ̄ ayeuteaog; ut wutꝏ̄tanat kum-Manittꝏ̄mun, God pish ummenuhkehteun micheme. Selah.
