48.9 Nummequantamunnan kꝏ̄womoausue kitteamonteanitteaonk, woi Manit, ut nôeu kuppeantamwakomukqut.
48.10 Néaunag kꝏ̄wesuonk, woi Manit, ne nih kꝏ̄waeenamitteaonk, wehque aongkouohkomuk, kittinnohkounit numwohtau wunnomwausseonk.
48.11 Muskouantaj wadchu Sion, wuttauneunk Judah weekontamwehettich newutche kꝏ̄sittummꝏ̄wongash.
48.12 Papomshak Sion, quinnupwshak, ogkeetamꝏ̄k wonkanꝏ̄sinash.
48.13 Kuhkinneamꝏ̄k naneutungash, natwontamꝏ̄k weetuomash: onk woh kummishamâônash pometuonk p[a]omꝏ̄uk.
48.14 Newutche yeuoh God kum-Manittꝏ̄mun micheme kah micheme: n noh kussampꝏ̄wunuk en nuppunnat.
49.0 {Nohtumpuhpequodt ukketoohomaonkanoo wutch wunnaumonuh} Korah.
49.1 Yeu nꝏ̄tamꝏ̄k wame missinninnuog kuhkeihtamꝏ̄k wame wadohkeogish: muttaohket.
49.2 Wosketompaog, kah nanánuacheg weenaieetuwog kah matchekuog moeu.
49.3 Nuttꝏ̄n missohham waantamꝏ̄wonk: kah nuttahhe natwontamꝏ̄wongash papaume waantamowonk.
49.4 Kukkodnꝏ̄tam kukkinneasuonk: nꝏ̄wóhshinum nunnupwꝏ̄aongash ut harpeut.
49.5 Tohwutch wo[h] wabesee matchesemuk, nagquonne matcheseonk quinnuppekongquean?
49.6 Nag pabahtóntogig ꝏ̄weenaieetuonganꝏ̄, kah maskauacheg ut mꝏ̄natut ummaumacheiyeumꝏ̄ash.
49.7 Matta woh howan ta[h]whꝏ̄ou weemattꝏ̄oh: kah matta woh ummanouhhumauouh nahoh Goduh.
49.8 Newutche manꝏ̄whaonk ukketeahogkonꝏ̄oh mishóadtu, kah chequnappu micheme.
49.9 Onk woh micheme pomantam, kah matta woh naumꝏ̄ anneu weenohke.
49.10 Newutche náau waantamwoh nuppꝏ̄oh kah wonk mattamogquoh, kah puppinashimwe wosketomp awohkompanau, kah pish nukkodtumauwaog ꝏ̄weenaeetuonganꝏ̄ onkatogeh.
49.11 Kemeu wuttinanatamꝏ̄onganꝏ̄, weekꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash pish micheme ohtaash, kah ꝏ̄tahtuonganꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash pannuppu wame pometeonganash: hettamwog wutohkéeuoash neahennit.
49.12 Qut quhtianumit wosketomp, matta ꝏ̄weekohteáun: ohqunneungqussu puppinashimwut noh awakompunneat.
49.13 Yeu wutusseonganꝏ̄ wutassꝏ̄tuonganꝏ̄: onch wunneechánꝏ̄oh wuttapeneaumunun ne anꝏ̄wahettit. Selah.
49.14 Onatuh sheepsoh seepsinwog weenohket, nuppꝏ̄wonk pish ummꝏ̄hwho, kah sampwesitcheg pish ummꝏ̄hwho, kah sampwesitcheg pish wunnanaunouh nahhog nompoaeu: kah ꝏ̄neetuonkanꝏ̄ pish mohtupaemo ut weenohket ne wadohkehettit.
49.15 Qut Manit pish pohquohwhunau nukketeahogkounoh, wutch ummenuhkesuonganit weenohkee, newutche pish nutattumunuk. Selah.
49.16 Ahque wabesish, howan weenauweekit: wussohsumowonk weekuwout nano mishehteaumuk.
49.17 Newutchu nuppuk, matta pish teag ꝏ̄tauoouun[:] wussohumꝏ̄wonk matta pish ássuhkongkóu.
49.18 Tohkonogque pamontog, wunnanumau ukketeahogkounoh: kah wosketompaog kꝏ̄woweenomuk ꝏ̄nenehheádt kuhhog nehenwonche.
49.19 Noh pish au pometuonganꝏ̄ ꝏ̄shuoh: nag matta pish naumꝏ̄og wequai.
49.20 Wosketomp quttiantog, qut matta[]waantog ogqunneunkqussu wutawakompunnae puppinashim.
50.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} Asaph.
50.1 Masugkenuk Manit Jehovah wussinneah, weequetum muttaok waj pashpishont, onk yea pajeh wayont.
50.2 Wutch Sion pannuppu wunneetuonk, God wohsumup.
50.3 Kum-Manittꝏ̄mun pish peyau, pish mat chequnnappu: nꝏ̄htau pish nashqunneau ut anaquabit, onk pish mishehtashin wewenu.
50.4 Wutch wohqut wee[h]quetum kesukquásh, kah ohke, onk woh wussumau ummissinninnumoh.
50.5 Mukinumah nꝏ̄neetupanatamꝏ̄mog: yeug ayimaiutcheg wunnꝏ̄waonk nashpe sephausuonk.
50.6 Kah kesukquash pish nahtitteau ꝏ̄nomwausseonk: newutche nagum nehenwonche wussittum. Selah.
50.7 Nꝏ̄tiek, woi nummissinninnumog kah kukkinnꝏ̄numwꝏ̄ woi Israel, kah kutayeukonittue wauwóonsh, nen Manit kum-Manittꝏ̄m.
50.8 Matta kutaushkômunꝏ̄h newutche kussephausuongash, asa chikohtae kummagꝏ̄onganash, nagwutteohtaash anaquabeh.
50.9 Matta pish neemunoh nomposhim wutch keekitm asa nompshimwe goats wutch kutchipaneutunkanit.
50.10 Newutche nish noh puppinashim touohkomukqut nuttaihe: puppinshimwog nequt mutanunkanogkussuog wadchuukontu.
50.11 Nꝏ̄waeh wame papinshásog ut wadchukontu: kah tauohkomukwe puppinashim nuttaiheog.
50.12 Kodtupwean matta kuttinninnꝏ̄un, newutche muttaohk nuttaihe kah neadtahshimmechumik.
50.13 Sun woh nummeech kꝏ̄washinne weyaus, asuh sun woh nꝏ̄tattam ꝏ̄sqheonk goats?
50.14 Aninnumok God tabuttantamꝏ̄wonk kah ôadtuhkou kukquoshaumaongash God nôappit.
50.15 Kah wehquetumah ne késukok wuttammepunnaa[n] pish kuppohquohwhunush, onk pish kussohsummꝏ̄woneh.
50.16 Qut God unnau matchetowoh, tohwutch ussean nꝏ̄tamwahuwon nukkuhkꝏ̄waongash; asa noh kittin neemunnumunat nꝏ̄[n]ꝏ̄waonk ut kuttꝏ̄nut?
50.17 Sekeneamán kuhkꝏ̄tomuhteaonk, kah unnohteaan nuttinnꝏ̄waongash kuppusquanit.
50.18 Náutcheh kommꝏ̄towaenin, neit kꝏ̄weetowom kah kꝏ̄weetom mamussuenuog.
50.19 Kummamatcheyim ut kuttꝏ̄nut: kah keenan ayim asꝏ̄kekodteamꝏ̄ongash.
50.20 Appean kummamatchein keemat: kukkehkom wunnaumonuh nehenwonche kokas.
50.21 Yeush kuttoussenash, kah matta toh nussu, kuttenantamup nuttinussin neanussean qut kutaushkomush, kah nꝏ̄nehtauunash ut anaquabeân,
50.22 Yeuyeu yeu natwontamꝏ̄k wananumogish God, ishkont kenehneeksháunumwꝏ̄, kah matta howân kuppohquohhunukkꝏ̄mwꝏ̄.
50.23 Howan maguk tabuttantamowonk, nussohsumꝏ̄wonuk: kah noh sampwe wánohtunk wutanakausuongash, nunnohtin ꝏ̄wadchanuwaonk God.
51.0 {No[h]tompuhpequodt ukketohhomaonk} David. {Nathan Manittoowomp paaonont mahch[e] petukauont} Bathshebah.
51.1 Kitteamonteanumah, woi God, neaunag kꝏ̄womoausue kitteamonteanitteaonk: neaunag mattanukish kukkittamunge m[o]naneteaonk jishkhash nummatcheseongash.
51.2 Pannuppu kutchessumeh wutch nummatcheseongash: kah pahke wutch nummatcheseongash.
51.3 Newutche nussampꝏ̄am nummatcheseongash, kah nummatcheseonk nagwutteohteau anaquabeh.
51.4 Ken, ken webe kummatche[n]ehesh, kah yeu nutussen matcheseonk ut anaquabean: onk woh kussampotont ketꝏ̄hkôan, kuppahkesittont wussittuman.
51.5 Kusseh nukkuhkenaihetteap ut matcheetupanatamowonganit: wompoquait nokas, ut matchéseonganit.
51.6 [missing!]
51.7 Pahkhe nashpe hisop, onk pish nuppahkes: kutchessumeh, onk pish nutánue wompeseum kꝏ̄n.
51.8 Nꝏ̄tamwaheh weekontamꝏ̄onk kah muskouanatamꝏ̄onk, nish nuskonash pohquatóhha[m]ahpash kuskesuk wutch nummatcheseongashh, onk jiskhash wame nummatcheseongash.
51.9 Puttogwhush kuskesuk wutch nummatcheseongash, onk jiskhash wame nummatcheseongash.
51.10 Kesteah pahkemetah, woi God: kah nagwutteáe sampwôhteae nashauonk wuskéheh.
51.11 Ahque pohkeseh wutch anaquabean, kah ahque amaunumah kꝏ̄neetupanatamwe nashauonk.
51.12 Nompahtah wonk weekontammꝏ̄wu kꝏ̄wadchanuwaonk kah kenannouwe nashauanit kogkánenitch.
51.13 Neit pish nukkuhkꝏ̄tomau pánesecheg kummayash kah matcheseaenuog pish kukquinnuppekompauwehtunkquog.
51.14 Pohquohwusseh wutch shuhkonat, woi God, ken God wadchanuae num-Manittꝏ̄m: kah neenan pish mishontowáꝏ̄homau kussampweusseonk.
51.15 Woi Lord wóshinish nussissittꝏ̄nash, kah nuttꝏ̄n pish nahtitteau kꝏ̄woweénomitteaonk.
51.16 Newutche matta kukkodtantamo sephausuonk, onk woh kittinnummaunun: matta kꝏ̄wekontamo chikohtae magꝏ̄ongash.
51.17 Sephamauaongash God ne pohquesu nashâuonk, pohqui kah tannogki metah, woi matta kutchadchepantamꝏ̄h.
51.18 Wunnesish weekontaman ut Sion: ayish qussukquaninnutongash ut Jerusalem.
51.19 Neit pish kꝏ̄seketahhuk sampweusseae sephausuongashh, chikohsumwe magꝏ̄ongash kah mumusseu chikohsumꝏ̄ongash: neit pish kussephamungquog oxinoh ut kut-Altarumut.
52.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt Maschil ukketoohomaonk} David, Doeg {Edomite anont} Sauloh, {wuttinuh,} David {peyau weekit} Ahimelech.
52.1 Tohwutch waénómut kuhhog woskehuwônat, woi masugkenan? ꝏ̄netꝏ̄onk God nagwutteohteau.
52.2 Keenan natinneham woskehuwaongah, onatuh kenag chahquog, asꝏ̄kekodteamwanakausin.
52.3 Kummꝏ̄cheke womantam matchit onk ne wanegik: kah pannꝏ̄wayeuonk onk ne sampwayeuonk. {Selah.}
52.4 Kꝏ̄womantam wame shehteae kuttꝏ̄wongash, woi asꝏ̄kekodteamwe meenan.
52.5 God pish ken wonk kenushhuk micheme pish kutamaúnuk kah pish kukkodtunuk wutch kꝏ̄tahtuonganit: kah pish kenꝏ̄swꝏ̄muhhuk wutch pomantamwae ohket. {Selah.}
52.6 Kah sampweusseaénin pish wunnaumun, kah wabesu, kah wutahanehtauoh.
52.7 Kusseh, yeuoh wosketomp matta unnant[à]mꝏ̄ God nummenuhkesuonk; qut pabahtantammꝏ̄nat mishe ꝏ̄weenaieetuonk, menehkheau wuhhogkuh ut ummatcheseonganit.
52.8 Qut nutogqunneunkqus askuhquamut olive mahtug, ut weekit God: nuppabahtantam ummonaneteaonk God micheme kah micheme.
52.9 Kummicheme waeenomush, newutche kummahche ussen; kah nuttannôantam kꝏ̄wesuonk newutche wunnegen ut anaquabhettit kꝏ̄neetupanatamꝏ̄mog.
53.0 {Nohtompuhpequdt ut Mahalath Maschil ukketoohhomaonk} David.
53.1 Mattamog nꝏ̄wau ut wuttahhut, wanne Godunnꝏ̄, anunwog, kah mahche usseog niskeneungquok matcheseonk: nag wanne pasuk wun[n]esu.
53.2 God womámpu wutch kesukqut en wosketompaog wunnaumonaoh, kodnâau howaneh wahwatánumutcheh, kah natinneawhont Goduh.
53.3 Nag nishnoh pasuk qushkeog, nag wàme pannuppu niskeneunkqussuog, wanne howan ꝏ̄nesu, wanne mo pasuk.
53.4 Anakausitcheg matcheseonk wanne ahteauog wahteauonk? mohwhaog nummissinninnumoh meechwog petukqunneg: wanne wehquetumauoog Goduh.
53.5 Naut mishe wabesuog toh woh mat adt wabesúmuk: newutche God seóhham wushkonash nnoh ayeuhkonukquéan, nag kutakodcheheaog, newutche God wutjishânumoh nahog.
53.6 Woi wadchanaonganꝏ̄ Israel, wutch sohhammꝏ̄ꝏ̄utch Sion! God quáhchuwunont wutch missinnáinneat ummissinninnumoh, Jakob weekontam kah Israel pish muskouanatam.
54.0 {Nohtumpuhpequodt ut Neginoth Maschil ukketoohomaonk} David. {Ziphimsog paahettit kah ônahettit} Sauloh: {sun matta} David {puttogqueu w[e]eche nenawun}
54.1 Wadchaneh nashpe kꝏ̄wesuonk, woi God, kah wussumeh naashpe kummenuhkesuonk.
54.2 Nꝏ̄tash nuppeantamꝏ̄wonk woi God: kukkeitash nuttinnꝏ̄waongash nuttꝏ̄nut.
54.3 Newutche penuwohteaog neepaeihtunkquog, kah woskehuacheg nukkodnushúkquog: matta pónauꝏ̄og Goduh anaquabhettit. Selah.
54.4 Kusseh, God nuttannohsuenu: God weetomau nag kogkanoncheg nukketeahogk[ô]unoh.
54.5 Pish matunkquatauau nummatwomoh: tummehah naghoh wutch kꝏ̄nomwayeuonk.
54.6 Nanouwe kussephamoush nꝏ̄woweenodtum kꝏ̄wesuonk woi Jehovah, newutche wunnegen.
54.7 Newutche nuppohquohwhunuk wutche wame wuttammehpunnaonganit: kah nuskesukqut nꝏ̄che naum uttoh en kodtantog wutch nummatwômog.
55.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut Neginoth Maschil ukketoohhomâonk} David.
55.1 NOOtash nuppeantamꝏ̄wonk woi God: kah ahque puttogwehtah wutch nꝏ̄weehquttummꝏ̄wonganit.
55.2 Kukkeitah, kah nꝏ̄tah, nummau nuppeantamꝏ̄wonganit kah nꝏ̄wadtauatongqus.
55.3 Newutche ꝏ̄wadtauatongqussuonk matwau, newutche ꝏ̄woskhuwaonk matcheetou: newutche nuttinnuhkongquog matcheseonk, kah musquantamwe nussekeneungquog.
55.4 Nuttahhut mꝏ̄cheke nutonkquomom, kah mishe wabesuonk newutche nuppꝏ̄wonk nunnuhkukkongquog.
55.5 Wabesuonk kah nukshaonk nunnuhkukkongquog, kah quoshque wabeseuonk nukkepuhkonuk.
55.6 Kah nussip, woi onunnuppohwhunonti wuskuhwhunonáut, onk woh nuttꝏ̄wem, onk woh nutanwohsin.
55.7 Kusseh, onk woh nôadtit nuppomuhsham, woh nutap touohkomuk. Selah.
55.8 Woh nukkenuppisham wutch nuppohquohhamunat wutch mehshétash, kah nashqut.
55.9 Paguóhteash, woi God, chachabuwómꝏ̄utch weenannúwóash, newutche nunnaum mishe musquanetúonk kah penuánittuonk ut otanat.
55.10 Asekesukokish, kah nukonáeu papomshaog qussikquanun[n]eutunkanit; woskehuwaonk wonk, kah uhquanumꝏ̄onk noeu.
55.11 Matcheetowonk nôeu ohtau, asꝏ̄kekodteamꝏ̄onk kah puhchuteaonk matta ámaémunꝏ̄ wutch wuttaumaukqut.
55.12 Newutche matta matwau nukkekómukꝏ̄h, neit woh numm[ã]nunnes: asa matta nnoh sekeneaiop mishshéheop wuhhogkuh áyeuuhkonittue neen, neit woh nutattashômp nuhhog.
55.13 Qut ken wosketomp kuttatuppeyeuꝏ̄mun, ken sampwoshássean, kah neetomp.
55.14 Nꝏ̄ne weetuódtimun, moeu nuppompomushaumun weekit God.
55.15 Nuppꝏ̄onk tohqunonch nahog: kah keteáeu áhettich chepiohkomukqut: newutche matcheseonk ne wodohkéhettit, kah kenugku nagkoh.
55.16 Qut nen nꝏ̄weehquetumau God: kah Jehovah pish nꝏ̄wadchánuk.
55.17 Wanúnkꝏ̄ukish: kah mohtompogkish kah puhshaquadcheh nuppeantam, kah nummishantowae mau: onk pish nꝏ̄tam nꝏ̄wadtauatonkqussuonk.
55.18 Wunohteae pohquohwhunau nukketeahogkounoh wutch ayeuwuttinneat ayeuqueúhpanneg: newutche monaog nꝏ̄weechuhumukup.
55.19 God pish nꝏ̄tam kah pish wutônkapinnanoh: nagum macheemapit, Selah: newutche wanne aûseweog newajeh matta qusháhetteg Goduh.
55.20 Quohshunnummaau wunnutcheash neh wânuhkônukqutche: pohqunum ꝏ̄nꝏ̄waonk.
55.21 Ukkuttꝏ̄wongash wuttꝏ̄nut mꝏ̄siyeuash mꝏ̄cheke onk ne butter; qut ayeuteaonk wuttahhꝏ̄wout: ukkuttꝏ̄ongash anue nꝏ̄hkiyeuash onk ne pummee; qut nish kodtunnumwe togkodtegash.
55.22 Unnuhkou kꝏ̄weanun Jehovah, kah pish kukkogkónuk: matta pish unnanumauꝏ̄ wunnomwaenu ontsapsh.
55.23 Qut ken woi Jehovah pish kuttinohkonog onkapunnae psahtheganit: sheteaenuog kah asꝏ̄kekodteamoenuog matta pish pomantamoog pohshe ne woh sohtepomantamwehhetteup: qut neen kuppabahtanumush.
56.0 {Nohtompuhpequadt ut Jonath-Elim-Rechokem, Michtam} David, {Philistiansog tohqunahettit ut Gath}
56.1 Monanumeh woi God, newutche wosketomp nukkod-misheashquónuk: ayeuwéhteadt nishnoh kesukod, nꝏ̄woskhik.
56.2 Nummatwômog nukkod-missashquónukquog asekesukokish, newutche nag monaog ayeuhkôsutcheg, woi ken nô appéan.
56.3 Wabeseon kuppabahtanumush.
56.4 Ut Godut nꝏ̄woweenodtumau wuttinnꝏ̄waonk: nuppabatanum God, matta nꝏ̄wabissuónoh weyaus toh kodnéhit.
56.5 Asekesukokish wôónkitteauꝏ̄og nuttinnꝏ̄waongash: wame wuttinanatamꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash nutayeuuhkonukqunassh wutche machuk.
56.6 Moeog, puttogwhâog w[u]hhogkâug, askuhhumwog nuttontannehtuongash, askwehettit wutch nukketeahogkou.
56.7 Sun woh pohquohhumwog nashpu ummatcheseonganꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash? kummusquantamunat penuhteash missinninnuog woi God.
56.8 Kutogkeetam nꝏ̄wauwónuongash, ponsh nussuppéguenash kꝏ̄wishquadt: sun matta ohtanoash kꝏ̄sukkuhwhonganit?
56.9 Maunnitteaunnon, neit nummatwomog qushkeog: yeu nꝏ̄wahteou[n], newutche God nꝏ̄weechꝏ̄humuk.
56.10 Godut nꝏ̄woweenodtu[m] wuttinnꝏ̄waonk: ut Jehovah nꝏ̄wowussittum wuttinnꝏ̄waonk.
56.11 God nuppabahtanum matta nꝏ̄wabesu wosketomp toh woh ânhukqueh.
56.12 Kukquoshámuaongash nutapehtunkqunash woi God, kꝏ̄woweenomsh.
56.13 Newutche kuppohquohwhun nukketeahogkou, wutch nuppunat: sun matta kuppohquohwhuttau nusseetash wutch penushó[n]at? woh nuppompomusham anaquabit God ꝏ̄wequaiyeumꝏ̄out pomantogig.
57.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt Al tasehith michtan} David, {waseem[o]teaont} Sauloh {ut hassunnegkut}
57.1 Monanumeh woi God, monanumeh, newutche nukketeahogkou kuppabahtanumuk: nux wutonkaohtomut kenuppahwhunnog nꝏ̄tspuhhꝏ̄aonganinneunk; onk neit yeush onkapunnaongash pamwushaumꝏ̄uk.
57.2 Nummauunnitteau God nôhappit: Godut noh aseau[u]shhikque wame teanteaquassinish.
57.3 Pish anꝏ̄teamꝏ̄ wutch kesukqut, kah nꝏ̄wadchanuk wutch ukkekómuwaonk, noh kodmusseasquonukqueh. Selah. God pish anꝏ̄nau um̃onaneteaonk kah ꝏ̄nomwáonk.
57.4 Nukketeahogkou weetomau qunnónꝏ̄oh, kah nꝏ̄weetappemoog chogaswutcheg: wosketompaog wunnaumonaoh, weputtúꝏ̄ah k[ô]unkquodtúꝏ̄ash, kah qunnuhtugkꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash, kah weenannuꝏ̄ keni[]togkodteg.
57.5 Mishshehununaj woi God ut ongkoue kesukquehtu: kussohsumoonk ongkoue ohtaj wame ohkit.
57.6 Quoshwunnáog wutashhabpꝏ̄uh, wutch nutôntanehtuongash, nukketeahogkou nauwáeu: wônteaop ut ne áyoi, uppetshóneau nagumau ut nôeu. Selah.
57.7 Nuttah menuhkohteau woi God, nuttah menuhkohteau, nukketꝏ̄homom kah nuttabuttantum.
57.8 Tꝏ̄kish nussohsumꝏ̄onk tꝏ̄hkeg psaltery kah harp: nen nompoéeu nuttꝏ̄hkem
57.9 Kuttabuttantamoush woi God, ut kenugke missinninnuut: kukketꝏ̄homoush ut kenugke wutohtimmóneat.
57.10 Newutche kummonaneteaonk missi, ut kesukqut, kah kꝏ̄nomwáonk ut matokqsit.
57.11 Ken misháhenunaj ut ongkoue kesukqut woi God, kussohsumoonk ongkoue ohtaj wame ohkit.
58.0 {Nohtumpuhpequodt Altaschith michtam} David.
58.1 SUN wunnamukut kussimwꝏ̄ wuñomwayeuonk woi mukkinnéonk? sun kꝏ̄newussittumumwꝏ̄, kenaau wosketompaog wunnaumonaoh?
58.2 Nux, kuttahhouóut kututussemwꝏ̄ matcheseonk: kukquokquadhûmumwꝏ̄, kenutcheganu ꝏ̄wo[skh]uaonganꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash ut ohkeit.
58.3 Matchetówog penuwohteoóog wutch wompequainneat, wô[o]nuog quenanneekhettit, pannꝏ̄wayeuog.
58.4 Wutonkquosketúeuonk[X] ogqueneungquodt wutonkquosketúeuonk askꝏ̄k: ogqunneunkqussuog mo nanꝏ̄tamꝏ̄k Addar, kobhog wehtáuog.
58.5 Nnoh matta nꝏ̄tauonk wuttaúatongquss[ú]oh padchummúau, tohkonogque waantamwu padchummúadt.
58.6 Pohquetáhash weepittúash woi God, wuttꝏ̄nꝏ̄wóut pohquetahash ukkehtomputteau wskoshshumwe qunn[ó]nꝏ̄og woi Jehovah.
58.7 Sobpáshettich onatuh nuppe pamutchúwog nagwutteaeu: sonteq[h]ohhꝏ̄adt ukkôunkquodt, ogqunneunkquodtich tohmetohho[ó]mꝏ̄ug.
58.8 Onatuh askéquttum mahtupáit: onatuh poékheunt mittumwossis, woh mo nauôꝏ̄og nepauzoh.
58.9 Ohkꝏ̄k asq aumattamꝏ̄kup nꝏ̄sippasqunaonk, pish wunneemunuh nahog onatuh pémsquoh, aspomantamwéhhettit, káh musquantog.
58.10 Sampweusseaen pish weekontam nag annꝏ̄taonk: pish kutchishitteau wussetash ꝏ̄squehheonganꝏ̄ matcheetowog.
58.11 Nemehkuh pish wosketomp nꝏ̄wau, wunnamuhkut na wutonkquatunk wunnomwausseaen: wunnamuhkt nnoh God wussittuk ut ohkeit.
59.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt Altaschith Michtam} David, {Saul anooteamwut, kah wutaskuhwouh, ut weetuomut wunushonaont.}
59.1 Pohquohwusseh wutch nummatwomut, woi num-Manittꝏ̄m, wadchaneh nag wutch waabehtunkquéaneg.
59.2 Pohquawusseh wutch ánakausitcheg matcheseonk, kah wadchaneh wutch nushehteaenuog
59.3 Newutche kusseh, nag askuhw[a]og nukketeahogkôunoh, mas[u]gkénugig wuttôéog nuhhog, mátta wutch nuppanneseonk asa nummatcheseonk woi Jehovah.
59.4 Nag quogquéoge nanashwehtamwog, wanne wutch nummatcheseonk: tꝏ̄kish aninnumah, kah naish.
59.5 Newutche, woi Jehovah, ummanittꝏ̄mꝏ̄wóh ayeuhteáog um-Manittꝏ̄mwoh Israel, tꝏ̄kish natauwaheoneat wame penuohteaog: ahque monanum matchetowog matcheseaenúog. Selah.
59.6 Nag qushkeog wunnonkꝏ̄áe, nisketonkqussuog onatuh anum, kah quñupshaog otan.
59.7 Kusseh, kóhkonneauwáog ut wuttꝏ̄nꝏ̄wout, togkodteganash wussissetꝏ̄nꝏ̄wout: newutche (nꝏ̄waog) howan nꝏ̄tunk?
59.8 Qut ken woi Jehovah, kutahanehtauôog nnag: wame penuwohteaog kuttôontuhkonôog.
59.9 Newutche ummenuhkesuonk, kuttannôonsh, newutche God nuttusphꝏ̄waonk[.]
59.10 Nummonaneteae Manittꝏ̄m nukqushoi monánumuk: God pish nunnohtinuk nukkodtantamoonk en nummatwomut.
59.11 Ahque paguas nagok, ishkont nummissinninnumog wunántamwog, kummenuhkesuonk suswohwonch nahog, nꝏ̄kôhteash naghok, woi Jehovah nutogqunnéganun.
59.12 Newutche ummatcheseonganꝏ̄ ut wuttꝏ̄nꝏ̄wóut, kah ukkuttꝏ̄wongash ut wussissetꝏ̄nꝏ̄wout, tohqunach ut pittuánumꝏ̄onganit, kah newutche matchenaneteáonk kah pannꝏ̄waonk ne anꝏ̄wahettit.
59.13 Machukis naghok kummusquantamunat, machukis, matta woh wuttinniéneau: kah wahteauhettich God nánaunnau Jakoboh, en aongkouohkomuk. Selah.
59.14 Kah wunnonkꝏ̄ꝏ̄k qushkehettich, kah nehnehteáhettich onatuh anumwut, & qunnupwsháhettich otan.
59.15 Nanwódtinneahhamwohettich meetsuonk, kah mꝏ̄hmꝏ̄skouáhettich asquam wamepꝏ̄hetteg.
59.16 Qut nuttinnꝏ̄homom kummenuhkesuonk, nux nummishontꝏ̄waꝏ̄homom kummonaneteaonk nompoáeu: newutche ken nutusphouaonk, kah nꝏ̄wonkônous wuttammepunnáon.
59.17 Kukketꝏ̄homoush woi nummenuhkesuonk, newutche God nutusphowaonk, nummonaneteae Manittꝏ̄m.
60.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut Shushan Eduth michtam} David, {kuhkootommuhkou ayeukonont Aram Naharaim kah Aram Zobab: Joab quashket, paguanau Edomitsoh oonaohteaouut salt, nabo neesit muttannonganogkussuoh.}
60.1 Woi God kuppogkesumun kussisw[à]uhkôsumun: kummusquanumimunnonup, woi qushkish wonk en nuhhogkanonut.
60.2 Kukquéquanehteam ohke, kussokshadtaun: neetskehtaash nishnoh ut pohqui, newutche nunnukshau.
60.3 Kenohtin kummissinninnumog siôgokish: kꝏ̄tattamhimun quoshkussippâmꝏ̄we wine.
60.4 Kuttinnumauoog nag quashhukqueaneg muttâag: onk woh pôpômush[á]numun newutche wunnomwaonk. Selah.
60.5 Noh wômônat woh pohquohwhunau: kuttinnôhkou pohquohwussitch, kah nꝏ̄tah.
60.6 God unnꝏ̄wop ut ꝏ̄neetupanatamꝏ̄onganit, nꝏ̄wekontam: nuppaushinnuꝏ̄ Sechem, nukquohquodhumun ꝏ̄nꝏ̄wohkói Succoth.
60.7 Gillead nuttaihe, kah Manasse nuttaihe, onk Ephraim ummenuhkesuonk nuppuhkuk: Judah ayeuont naumatuongoh.
60.8 Moab nukkutshitunk ohkuhquoh: nuttánuwohkou nummohkis ut Edom: Philistia weekontash ken newutche neen.
60.9 Howan woh pasꝏ̄wit menuhki ꝏ̄tanit? howan ásꝏ̄wussit Edom?
60.10 Sunnummatta ken woi God, sohwhôkôseógkup? kah ken woi God, matta kꝏ̄chaiyeúmunnónup ut nutayeuwohkonnanoweenut.
60.11 Aninnumaiinnean wutch wuttammepunnaonganit: newutche wutannoôsuonk wosketomp tohnꝏ̄cheyeuꝏ̄.
60.12 God aninnumungqueog pish nukquehtâèmun: newutche nnoh pish tashkuhkonau nummatwomunônoh.
61.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut Neginoth ukketoohhomaonk} David.
61.1 NOOtah nummauonk woi God: kukkeihtash nuppeantamowonk.
61.2 Wutche aongkouohkomuk kummauunnitteoush, nuttah kꝏ̄shkoshunk: ussꝏ̄wusseh qussukquanit, ne anuwohqussꝏ̄mukqueh.
61.3 Newutche ken nutonkꝏ̄wohquassꝏ̄, kah menuhki wonkonous wutche matwâut.
61.4 Pish nuttay keekit micheme: nuppabahtanum wutonkaúhtomuh kenuppawhunnog. Selah.
61.5 Newutche ken God kenꝏ̄tam nukquoshômuaongash: kuttinninnumah wutahtaonganꝏ̄ neg quóhtukeg kꝏ̄wesuonk.
61.6 Ken kusepepomantamwah ketassꝏ̄t: kah ukkodtummꝏ̄mash neane monatash pometeongash.
61.7 Pish appu anaquabit God micheme: woi nanashwunush monaneteaonk kah wunnomwaonk ne woh wodchanukquit.
61.8 Nemehkuh nuttinnꝏ̄homom kꝏ̄weesuonk micheme: onk woh asekesukokish nutussen nukquoshómuaongash.
62.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut Jeduthun ukketoohhomaonk} David.
62.1 Webe nukketeahogkou annoôneau Goduh: noh wutch nꝏ̄wadchanitteaonk.
62.2 Noh webe nukqussukquanum, kah nꝏ̄wadchanitteaonk: noh nutusphouaonk, matta pish nummꝏ̄cheke ontsappu.
62.3 Toh uttꝏ̄che kenatwontamwꝏ̄ woskehuwaonk wutch wosketomp? pish wame kenushitteamwꝏ̄: onatuh qussukquaneneutunk kodnꝏ̄kompskemꝏ̄uk: kah onatuh kuhqushqueneutunk.
62.4 Webe weétuotuog penuhkonat wutche quttiánumaonganit, tapeneaumwog pannꝏ̄wayeuongash: wunnaneteamꝏ̄ wuttꝏ̄nꝏ̄: qut anomut matchenaneteaog.
62.5 Nukketeahogkou webe anôous God, newutche nutannoôsuonk wutchayeumó wuhhogkat.
62.6 Nagum webe nukqussukquanum, kah nꝏ̄wadchanitteaonk, nagum nutusphꝏ̄waonk, matta pish nutontsappu.
62.7 Ut Godut nꝏ̄wadchanitteaonk kah nussohsumꝏ̄wonk, ukqussukquanum nummenuhkeseuonk, nutusphuaónk ut Godut.
62.8 Pabahtanumꝏ̄k nagwutteaeu kenaau missi[n]ninnuog: sokanumꝏ̄k ketahhouwoash ut anaquabit, God kuttusphouaonganun. Selah.
62.9 Wu[ñ]amuhkut matche[k]eog tahnꝏ̄chéyeuog, kah wuttꝏ̄wosketompaog pannꝏ̄wayeuog: quogquodwhut naghok, wamu môeu, ánue nunkinwog onk ne tahnꝏ̄cheyeuꝏ̄uk.
62.10 Ahque pabahtantamꝏ̄k ut mukkꝏ̄kinnuaonganit, ahque tahnꝏ̄cheyeúꝏ̄k kummꝏ̄towonganit: monak weenai[é]etuonk, ahque kuttahhꝏ̄woog appehettich.
62.11 God wussinnu pasukqut, neesit nunnꝏ̄tamun yeu, menuhkesuonk wutchaiyeumꝏ̄ Godut.
62.12 Kah wonk ken Jehovah wutchayeumꝏ̄ monaneteaonk: newutche kuttinongquodtauon nishnoh wosketomp neane anakausit.
63.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David {ait touohkomukqut Judah.}
63.1 WOi God ken num-Manittꝏ̄m, nompoaeu kenatinneawhush: nukketeahogkou kúhketꝏ̄n kuhhog, nꝏ̄weyaus kukkodtaânumuk, nunohtae kah kuhketꝏ̄nꝏ̄e ohke toh mo adt nuppênꝏ̄g.
63.2 Naumunat kummenuhkesuonk kah kussohsumóonk neane mahche nau[u]nop ut kekit.
63.3 Newutche kꝏ̄womoausuonk mꝏ̄cheke wunnegen onk ne pomantamoonk: nusissittꝏ̄nash pish kꝏ̄wâwu[ss]umuk.
63.4 Yeu kittinne waussumunun ash pomantam: nuttahshinum nunnutcheganash ut kꝏ̄wesuonganit.
63.5 Nukketeahogkou pish tâpepꝏ̄h onatuh nashpe wein kah weesuuk: kah nuttꝏ̄n pish kꝏ̄wâwussumuk nashpe weekontamwe nussissittꝏ̄nash.
63.6 Nehquanumunnon ut nutappinneat kah natwanumunnon nishnoh uttꝏ̄che nukonáeu.
63.7 Newutche ken kutáninnumaiip: newajeh kenuppawhunog wutonkaohtomꝏ̄ nꝏ̄wekontam.
63.8 Nukketeahogkou kummenuhkodti neóhhuk: kuttinnohkou nukkogkôónuk.
63.9 Qut yeug natinneawhoncheg nukketeahogkôunoh nahunnushônat, pish auog wutchómuhqut.
63.10 Pish nushôog nashpe togkodtega[n]it: pish ummôwhôoh wonkqussissog.
63.11 Qut ketassꝏ̄t pish wekontam ut Godut, pish wame waeénomaog chadchekeyeuánit nashpe wuhhogkuh, qut pannꝏ̄wahettit wuttꝏ̄nꝏ̄ash pish kuppohhôsuash.
64.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ukketoohomaonk} David
64.1 NOOtash nꝏ̄wàdtauatonkqussúonk woi God, ut nuppeantamꝏ̄wonganit, wadcha[u]sh nukketeaonk wutch qushonat matwau.
64.2 Adtasheh wutch kéme ukkenꝏ̄nittuonganꝏ̄wout matcheetꝏ̄wog: nꝏ̄waabetunkqu[n]naóont anakausitcheg matcheseonk[.]
64.3 Nah kehtattóog weenannu onatuh togkodteg, pꝏ̄tonkunáog wutahtompeuh quosh[ô]hqunnumwog weesogkeyeuwongash.
64.4 Onk woh pumwáog kéme panuppu wunneetꝏ̄oh: teanuk uppumwóuh matta wabesuog.
64.5 Nag wuttꝏ̄máog wuhhogkauh wutche machik; kenꝏ̄netuog wutch wunashónat kému appehanog nꝏ̄waog, howan woh nógqueog?
64.6 Nag natinnehamwog matcheseongash usseog pannuppe natinneteaonk: nag wame né anomut ohtag, kah wuttahhou mꝏ̄nói.
64.7 Qut god pish uppumwoh kôuhquodt, teanuk pish wutchadchetahwoh.
64.8 Nemehkuh pish nehenwonche weenannu uppenushátauneau ut wuhhogkaout: neg wame nauoncheg pish wussemꝏ̄og.
64.9 Kah wame wosketompaog wabesuog, kah pish wahteauwahuwaog wutanakausuonk God: newutche pish waantamwe natwontamwog wutusseongash.
64.10 Sampweussecheg pish weekontamꝏ̄unaog Jehovahoh, kah pish uppabahtanumouh: kah wame s[á]mpwutteahoncheg pish waeenoáog.
65.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt: Ukketoohhomaonk} David.
65.1 Waeenomuwaonk kutannóonukqun woi God, ut Sion: kah quoshauaonk pish kittinhittean.
65.2 Woi ken nꝏ̄taman peantamoonk, wame weyaus pish kuppeyaónukqun.
65.3 Matcheseongash nutaumskunkqunash: qut nummatcheseonganash pish kutjiskhomunash.
65.4 Wunnanumau noh pepenauadt, kah noh pasꝏ̄adt, onk woh kꝏ̄weetomuk ut keekit: pish nꝏ̄wamepumun kꝏ̄neetuonk ut keekit kꝏ̄neetupanatamwe Temple.
65.5 Nashpe uhqunneunkquokish sampweusseonganit, kenampꝏ̄ho[m]aiimun, woi God nꝏ̄wadchanitteaonganun: uspuhhꝏ̄waonk pajeh wame aongkouohkomukquash: kah neg aitcheg nôadtit kehtahhanit.
65.6 Nahspe ummenuhkesuonk manuhkehteunk wadchuash, puttukquo[b]ussit menuhkesuonk.
65.7 Chequnehteau wadtauatunkqussuonk keitoh: ꝏ̄wadtauatonkqussuonganꝏ̄ tukkꝏ̄og, kah ꝏ̄wogkâeonganꝏ̄ missinninnuog.
65.8 Kah nag wadohkitcheg onkouohkomuk, wabesuontamwog kuhkinneasuongash: mohtompanaeu, sohhamunah, kah wunnonkwaeu kꝏ̄weekontamwahuwám.
65.9 Kenatauohtóh ohke, kah kutogquechittauun: kꝏ̄nogquehtaun nashpe wussepeum God ne numwohtau nippe: kukquoshaeihtau[ó/o]og weatchimiñeash, mahche yeuin quaquashweihtaman.
65.10 Mꝏ̄cheke kutogquechitoh wonitchuhhongash, kutasetahteanum ohke, kenꝏ̄keteauun nashpe sókanon, kꝏ̄nantamun ne noh adt sonkuk.
65.11 Kutchetuhquabenoh kodtummꝏ̄ nashpe kꝏ̄neetuonk, kummayut padtippashin wunnogkꝏ̄onk.
65.12 Padipashin maskehtuash ut touohkomuk: kah wadchuemesash weekontamꝏ̄mꝏ̄ash waéenu.
65.13 Wunnádtuppꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash wunohkukkomunnáoash monacheg floksog, kah ꝏ̄naohkôaouash pashanahteau weatchiminneash, mishe weekontamwog, kah ketꝏ̄hhomôog.
66.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ketoohmaonk}
66.1 WEeketongqusseg ut Godut, wame muttaók.
66.2 Anꝏ̄hamunk quttianatamꝏ̄onk ꝏ̄wesuonk: sohsumwahtauꝏ̄k tabuttantamauaonk.
66.3 Unnꝏ̄k God, toh kittinne uhqueneunkqus ut kutánakausuonganit? newutche missi kummenuhkesuonk, kummatwomog woskeche kuttit kꝏ̄namptunkquog.
66.4 Wame muttaok pish kꝏ̄wowussumuk, kah pish kukketꝏ̄homungquog, pish unnꝏ̄homoog kꝏ̄wesuonganit. Selah.
66.5 Peyunk naumꝏ̄k wutanakausuongash God, noh ohqunneongquotash wuttinheaongásh wosketompaog wunnaumonaoh.
66.6 Kehtoh ayim nu[n]obohteai: pomushopanneg tomogkonit wusseetꝏ̄wout; na nuttit weekontamꝏ̄unnanónúp.
66.7 Noh nanawunnum nashpe ummenuhkesuonk micheme, wuskesukquash naumꝏ̄ꝏ̄ásh wutohtimoneash: ohquontogig nananuaonk ahque misheheahettich wuhhogkauh. Selah.
66.8 Woi wunnanumok num-Manittꝏ̄mun kenaau missinninnuog, ayimau wuttauatongqussue tabuttantamoonk nꝏ̄tamounnat.
66.9 N noh kókônunont nukketeahogkóunnunꝏ̄noh ut pomantamꝏ̄onganit: kah katta unnantamꝏ̄ ontohtaj nussetinonash.
66.10 Newutche ken woi God, kukqutchhimunnonup: kukqutchhimunnonup onatuh silver quajteomuk.
66.11 Kuppasꝏ̄umunnonup hashabput, kupponumaiimun nuppisquaninnonut ohquommomꝏ̄wonk.
66.12 Kutayeu wosketompaog wunnayeumukqunnaoont nuppuhkukqun, nuppannupwushaumun nꝏ̄htau, kah nuppanupwushaumun nuppekontu qut ken kuppasꝏ̄ꝏ̄mun weenaeetuohkomukqut.
66.13 Nuttom keekit weeche chikohtae magꝏ̄ongash kuttâadtuhkaush kukquoshaumunnꝏ̄wongash.
66.14 Nish nussissitꝏ̄nash anꝏ̄wohpash, kah nuttꝏ̄n anꝏ̄wohpash wadtamehpunaon.
66.15 Kittinninnumaush chikohsue magꝏ̄ongash wees, kah ramse weekemungquok: kittinnumaush oxinog kah goatsog. Selah.
66.16 Nonche nꝏ̄tamꝏ̄k wame kenaau quoshogish God, kah nussampꝏ̄am uttoh asehtauomp nukketeahogkounoh.
66.17 Nummauunnitteau nashpe nuttꝏ̄nut kah mishsheheop nashpe neenan.
66.18 Womontamon matcheseongash ut nuttahhut, matta God woh nunnꝏ̄tunkꝏ̄h.
66.19 Qut wunnamuhkut nunnꝏ̄tunk God: kuhkeihtam nꝏ̄wadtauatongqussue peantamꝏ̄onk.
66.20 OOnanumunach God: matta quashkenumaeg en nuppeantamꝏ̄onganit, asa ummonaneteaonk wutch nuhhogkat.
67.0 {Nohtumpuhpequodt ut Neginoth ukketoohomaonk.}
67.1 GOD monanuminnean, kah wunnanuminnean: wuskesuk wôsumungquttuh. Selah.
67.2 Onk woh wahteoun kummay ut muttaohkit, kah kꝏ̄wadchanumꝏ̄onk kenugku wame wutohtimóneash.
67.3 Missinninnuog waeenomugqush woi God, wame missinninnuog waeenomugqush.
67.4 Woi wutohtimoneunk weekontamohettich, weekontamꝏ̄homahettich, newutche pish kꝏ̄sum missinninnuog sampwe: kah pish kenanaa[n]num wutahtimoneash ut muttaohkit. Selah.
67.5 Missinninnuog waeenomugqush woi God: wame missinninnuog waeenomugqush.
67.6 Neit pish ohke mishummeechummu: kah God kum-Manittꝏ̄mun pish kꝏ̄nanumugqun.
67.7 God pish kꝏ̄nanumugqun, kah wame aongkouohkomuk pish ukqushóoh.
68.0 {Nohtumpuhpequodt ukketoohomaonk} David.
68.1 Neepauitch God, ummatwomoh seahwhonch: kah wonk neg sekeneaoncheg wussemohettich wutch anaquabit.
68.2 Onatuh pukit ptꝏ̄hog, neinne nenꝏ̄hkau naghog: onatuh wax mohtupohtag ut nꝏ̄taut, nein paguanehettich matcheetowog ut anaquabit God.
68.3 Qut wunnomwaenuog weekontamwehettich: weekontamohettich ut anaquabit God, nux, mꝏ̄cheke weekontamohettich.
68.4 Ketꝏ̄hamok God anꝏ̄hamunk waeenomꝏ̄ongash ut ꝏ̄wesuonganit: mishehheuk n noh naꝏ̄mukqut kesuk, nashpu ꝏ̄wesuonk JAH: kah weekontamꝏ̄k ut anaquabit.
68.5 Mowadtꝏ̄sheg na ꝏ̄shoh, sekousquaog ꝏ̄sumugkouoh, God ꝏ̄neetupanatamwu ayeuonganit.
68.6 God ponamauau nonsiyeuꝏ̄oh weechinnumonát sohhꝏ̄wunau wehweepapissumutcheh mꝏ̄wóhshogquohtogquosh, qut ohquoantogig nananuwaonk wutohtuog nunnobohtéaouut.
68.7 Woi God sohhꝏ̄wunnat negonohkouadt kummissinninnumog: panupwuhaan touohkom[u]k. Selah.
68.8 Ohke quequanup, kesukquash punnemoash ut anaquabit God, Sinai, ut anaquabit God um-Manittꝏ̄moh Israel.
68.9 Ken woi God kuttannꝏ̄n mishe sokanon, uttoh adt menehketeauop kutohke sauunumꝏ̄mꝏ̄ug.
68.10 Kummukineonk ꝏ̄tohkinneaop: ken woi God kukquoshaeihtau mátcheeku, wutche kꝏ̄neetuonganit.
68.11 Jehováh unnꝏ̄wau kuttꝏ̄wonk: monaog wunnꝏ̄tamwahuwoneau.
68.12 Kehtassꝏ̄tamwog wutayeuwehteomꝏ̄woh kenuppe wussemꝏ̄og: káh mittumwussis nꝏ̄titteadt, chadchapenum máchehteaumuk.
68.13 Mukkꝏ̄kône nꝏ̄wetsumꝏ̄moneau ahkukquog, qut pish kutogqunneunkqussimwꝏ̄ wunnuppawhunnit wskꝏ̄wanon aqut Silver, kah ummequnoh wesôag gold.
68.14 Wamemanuhkesu soswohwhont kehtassꝏ̄timwoh na ut wompiyeup onatuh kꝏ̄unit ut Salmon.
68.15 OOwadchum God, onatuh wadchu Bashan, kussohkoi wadchu onatuh wadchu Bashan.
68.16 Tohwutch quesháog kenaau kussohkoaeu wadchuog? yeu wadchu God kontantog ꝏ̄tohkinneat, nux Jehovah ummicheme wutohkin.
68.17 Wuttatuppequanumukquaash God neesneechagut muttannunganuꝏ̄ash,mꝏ̄cheke mattanunganogkussuoh Angelsog: God ꝏ̄weamukshanoh ut Sinai: wunneetupanatamwe weekit.
68.18 Kuttuspeup en ongkouwu, kummisinohteam missinnohkonunk, kutattumunumup ummagꝏ̄onganooash wosketompaog, nux, wutch ahquoanitogig nananuwaonk, onk woh Lord god weechayeumoh.
68.19 OOnanumunach God asekesukokish kꝏ̄nꝏ̄washhikqun, Manit nꝏ̄wadchanitteaonganun. Selah.
68.20 N noh wâmanittꝏ̄meog, n noh wadchanuwae Manit, kah God Manit wutchayeumꝏ̄ pohquohhamoongash wutche nuppowonganit.
68.21 Qut pish God chadchetahhom uppuhkukkꝏ̄ ummatwomoh: kah quánonuhquoánt n noh aiont ummatcheseonganit.
68.22 God nꝏ̄wau pish nukqushkeaheoog wutch Bashan, nuppasꝏ̄woog wutch monaiyeuut kehtahannit.
68.23 Kusseet woh mussishin ꝏ̄sheaonganꝏ̄out kumma[t]womog, kah wenannꝏ̄ kuttiog [nunan].
68.24 Naumwog kutauonganash, woi God, wutauonganash num-Manittꝏ̄m, nukketassꝏ̄timꝏ̄m ut wunneetupanatamwe weetuomut.
68.25 Ketꝏ̄homwaenuog negonshauog, puhpequaenuog wutasukauouh, kenugku nag penompaog puhpequahtog timbrelsash.
68.26 Wunnanumꝏ̄k God ut mukkinneaonganit, Manit wutch tohkekomuwu Israel.
68.27 Na wuttappen peississit Benjamin, weeche wunnananuaeneumꝏ̄uh, wussontimosumoh Judah, kah kônꝏ̄sꝏ̄acheg, wussontimomoh Zabulon, kah wussontimomoh Naphthali.
68.28 Kum-Manittꝏ̄m kenꝏ̄tamup kummenuhkesuonk: menuhketeaush, woi God[,] ne aséansheagup.
68.29 Newutche kuttempleum ut Jerusalem ketassꝏ̄timwog pish kuppaudtunkquog magꝏ̄ongash.
68.30 Auskom quáqunnontugqutcheg, monacheg bullsog, kah kalfse missinninnuog, nonchemaghettit silver: siswah missinninnuog, weekontogig mattompog.
68.31 Sontimoog wutch sohhomwog wutch Egypt, Ethiopia teanuk pish summagunnumwog wunnutcheganooash en Godut.
68.32 Ketꝏ̄homok God kenaau asꝏ̄tamꝏ̄ongash muttaohket, woi ketꝏ̄hamꝏ̄k waeenomꝏ̄ongash Jehovah. Selah.
68.33 Noh naꝏ̄mukqut ongkoue ohohtag kesuk, na negonneyeuꝏ̄gkup, kusseh mishontꝏ̄wau, kah ne mishe mishontꝏ̄waonk.
68.34 Sampꝏ̄ak ummenuhkesuonk God, ꝏ̄netuonk waabappehtauau Israel, kah ummenuhkesuonk matohkqsut.
68.35 Woi God, kutohqunneongqus wutch kꝏ̄netupanatamwe appuonganit; um-Manittꝏ̄moh Israel noh anumaont ummissiñinnumoh menuhkesuonk kah tapenumꝏ̄onk, wunnanumunach God.
69.0 {Notompuhpequodt ut Shoshannim ukketoohomaonk} David.
69.1 Wadchaneh, woi God: newutche nippeash petutteaumꝏ̄ash nukketeahogkounut.
69.2 Nupwohkehchꝏ̄am mónói pissohquanuhtu, matta woh neep[a]u[ôú]muk, nuppeam mꝏ̄nompagwut uttoh adt nukkokqsin.
69.3 Nusauanum wutch nummauonk, nukquttunk nunnohteau, nuskesukquash sauunumꝏ̄mꝏ̄ash, ánoónog num-Manittꝏ̄m.
69.4 Nag sekeneaitcheg tahnꝏ̄che, monaog onk ne nummeesuonk ahtahshik: nag kodnushikqueoneg, nummatwomog tahnꝏ̄che, menuhkesuog: neit nunnompinnumun wonk ne matta neemanummoup.
69.5 Woi God kꝏ̄wahteoh nummattammagweseonk; kah nummatcheseongash matta kutassompatammꝏ̄.
69.6 Nag anóonukquéaneg woi Lord Jehovah ayeutaunit, ahque akodchhettich newutche neen: nag natineóhukquéaneg ahque quequenaúanumwehettich newutche neen, woi um-Manittꝏ̄moh Israel.
69.7 Newaj, newutche ken, nukkekómukquog, akodchuonk puttaghum nuskesuk.
69.8 Nuppenowohteau ut neematut, kah nu[ppp]enowohteau ut nokas wunneechanit.
69.9 Newutche nuszelum ut keékit nummꝏ̄hhuk: kah ukkekomuwaonganꝏ̄ neg kekomukquéaneg nꝏ̄chepunaùmukqunnau.
69.10 Mauon, kah áhhohpadt nukketeahogkou nashpe mat meetseonk, ne nukkekomitteáonk.
69.11 Nummanꝏ̄tiónakin hogkꝏ̄unam hogkꝏ̄: kah nuttehinohkunukqunneau.
69.12 Nag apitcheg anómsquoant nummamatchenukquog: kah nashpꝏ̄humꝏ̄og nuhhog kogkeissippamwaenuog.
69.13 Qut neen kuppeantamoush woi Jehovah tapeneamanish: woi God ut monakish kummonaneteaongash nꝏ̄tah, ut wunnamuhkuteyeúe kꝏ̄wadchánuwáonk.
69.14 Pohquohwusseh wutch wunnumwiyeuut, kah ahque kuttauweti: pohquohwusseh wutch nag sekeneaitcheg, kah wutch nꝏ̄nompagwut.
69.15 Ahque anéuhkauitch tomogkon, kah ahque mꝏ̄nôi misseaashquoasit, kah páhsahtheg ahque kupwamwitch ut wuttꝏ̄nut.
69.16 Nꝏ̄tah woi God, newutche kꝏ̄womoausúonk wunnegen, qushkish en nuhhogkat neane monak kukkitteamonteaneteáeu monaneteaongash.
69.17 Kah ahque puttogwhush kuskesuk wutch kuttinninneumut, newutche nꝏ̄tamehpunam, teanuk nꝏ̄tah.
69.18 Pasosukau nukketeahogkou, kah pohquáwhus: pohquawusseh newutche nummatwomog.
69.19 Kꝏ̄wahteoun nukkekómitteaonk, kah nutakodchúonk kah nummishauanumitteaonk, wame nummatwomog anaquábean.
69.20 Kekómitteaonk wutch pokshau nuttah kah nuhhogkat numwohteau onkquanumꝏ̄onk: kah nutôanóus howan woh nahtunkinneiit, qut wanne howan, kah mánetimmew[á]cheg, qut wane howan namheuh.
69.21 Kah nutassamukquog weswe noh nittin meechinneat: kah kúhkuttꝏ̄non nꝏ̄tattamhukquog sée wine.
69.22 Wuttablumꝏ̄ ahpehhanneuꝏ̄utch anaquabhettit: kah n[e]woh wanégikup ahpehhanne[á]ꝏ̄uach.
69.23 Pogkénumwóhettich, ut wushkesukkouwout onk woh monaumóog: kah nagwutteaeu nunnuksho[n]sh wusségonnohtogkꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash.
69.24 Sókanuttau kutjishánumaonk, kummuttae musuantamoonk tohqunukquéhettich
69.25 Wutáyeuonganꝏ̄ wanne howaununꝏ̄utch: wanne howaununnꝏ̄utch wek.
69.26 Newutche sasamakoúhwadt, ꝏ̄waskheouh: kah weattimáhettit, ummꝏ̄skheouh neh chadchetahwodcheh.
69.27 Ponamau sasamakuhhuwáonk wutch ummatcheseonganꝏ̄: kah ahque petutteahettich kussampweseonganit.
69.28 Nag jishkuhwunach ꝏ̄sukkuhwhonganꝏ̄ pamântogig: kah ahque wetsukwhoshettich sampweusseaenuwud.
69.29 Qut nummatchek kah nunneuantam: kꝏ̄wadchanuwaonk, woi God, qunnunkquappehikquttei.
69.30 Kꝏ̄woweenodtum ꝏ̄weesuonk God ketꝏ̄homaonganit: kah nummishsheh nashpe waeenomaonk.
69.31 Kah yeu en wussikkutteahukqut Jehovah, onk noh ox asa bullok noh wadaskonit kah wôhkassit.
69.32 Manunnissuog yeu pish wunnaumunneau, kah pish weekontamwog kah pish kuttahhou pomantamomou kenaau natinneawhog God.
69.33 Newutche Jehovah nꝏ̄tauau matchekuoh, kah matta jishánumoou kobshagkinausinutcheh.
69.34 Kesuk kah ohke waussumahettich neh, keitoh kah nishnoh teag naut momonchemoug.
69.35 Newutche God pohquohwuttau Sion, kah pish ꝏ̄tanahteau ut Judah, onk nag woh ꝏ̄tohkinneau, kah woh wutahtaunau.
69.36 Kah wunneech[a]nꝏ̄oh wuttinnúmꝏ̄oh, pish wutohtaunneau nahohtôeu ꝏ̄shuoh: kah wamontogig ꝏ̄wesuonk na pish ꝏ̄tohkinneau.
70.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt, ukketoohhomaonk} David. {koowaantamwahukqunnan}.
70.1 Teanuk pohquohwusseh woi God, teanuk aninnumah woi Jehovah.
70.2 Nag akodjhettich, kah quequenauanumwéhettich natinneawhoncheg nukketeahogkóunoh: qushkehettich, kah akodjhettich neg kodwoskéhukqueaneg.
70.3 Nah qushkéhettich, ne wutonkqu[a]tunkanꝏ̄ wutakodchuonganꝏ̄ anꝏ̄wacheg, Ho, ho.
70.4 Yeug wame natinneóhukqueaneg nag weekontammꝏ̄ónukqush, kah muskouanatammꝏ̄onukqush: kah neg womontogig kꝏ̄wadchanuaonk nagwutteaeu nꝏ̄wahettich God mishshehhenach.
70.5 Qut neen nummatcheek kah nukquenáhuk, kenupshash en nuhhogkat woi God; ken nutannósuéneum, kah nuppohquohwussueneum, woi Jehovah ahque sepohteash.
71.1 Kuppabahtanumush woi Jehovah, ahque quequenauanumitti.
71.2 Pohquawusseh ut kꝏ̄nomwauseonganit, kah pohquohhumwáhe: kuhkeihtah kah wadchaneh.
71.3 Ken menuhkaj nutáyeuonk, uttoh woh adt nagwutteáe wuñaiyee: kutannꝏ̄teamup kꝏ̄wadchaneat; newutche ken nukqussukquanum kah nꝏ̄wonkónous.
71.4 Pohquawusseh woi num-Manittꝏ̄m wutch wunnutcheganout matcheetowog: wutch wunnutcheganout mat wunnomwausseaen, kah nushehteaen.
71.5 Newutche ken nutannoósuonk woi Lord God: ken kuppabahtanumush, wutch nꝏ̄skenúunneat.
71.6 Kutashineup wutch ôontomukqut, ken wasꝏ̄wéan nokas wunnogkussit, nagwutteaeu kꝏ̄waeenomush.
71.7 Neen onatuh monchanatamꝏ̄onk wutch mꝏ̄nacheg: qut ken menuhki nutusphouwaonk.
71.8 Nuttꝏ̄nuit numwohtaj kꝏ̄waweenomutteaonk, kah kukquehtianumitteaonk qunnikesuk.
71.9 Ahque pohkeseh ut nukkehchiyeuunneat, ahque ohquanumeh nummenuhkesuonk mahchemꝏ̄ꝏ̄uk.
71.10 Newutche nummatwomog num̃atchenukquog kah nag askwhononcheg nukketeahogkôunuh kenꝏ̄nittuog.
71.11 Nꝏ̄waog, God wutahquanumoh: wunómohtuhkau kah tohqun, newutche matta howan uppohquohwhunoh
71.12 Woi God ahque nôꝏ̄sukah, woi num-Manittꝏ̄m, teauk ani[u]numah.
71.13 Quequenauanumwehettich, kah mohtuppaehettich matwahettit wutch nukketeahogkôunoh: kekontuonk kah mishananittuonk hogquehettich, kah woskehetcheg.
71.14 Qut nagwutteaeu nuttannous, & wonk nano kꝏ̄woweenomsh yauyatche.
71.15 Nuttꝏ̄n pish natitteau kꝏ̄nomwausseonk, kah kꝏ̄wadchanuwaonk qunnikesuk, newutche matta nꝏ̄wahteauꝏ̄h toh adtahshik.
71.16 Nuttom ummenuhkesuonganit Manit Jehovah: nꝏ̄wahteauwahuam kꝏ̄nomwausseonk ken webe.
71.17 Woi God kukkuhkꝏ̄tomah wutch nꝏ̄skenuunneat: kah toh yeu pajeh nꝏ̄wahteauwáhuwam kummonchanatamwanakausuongas[k].
71.18 Kah yeuyeu kohchiyeueh kah wompoquoi, woi God, ahque ohquanumeh nô pajeh wahteauwahuwaon yeu ut pometuonganit kummenuhkesuonk, kah kuttapenumꝏ̄onk neg wame paoncheg.
71.19 Kah kꝏ̄nomwausseonk, woi God, qunnuhquohteau noh mashanakausit: woi God, howan anunkquean?
71.20 Ken nátissean mishsheu kah onkquommommu wuttanmepunaonk*, wonk pish kukketeaheh, kah pish wonk kukkódtinne wutch mꝏ̄n[a]iyeuut ohke.
71.21 Pish kummishteoh nummissugkenuonk, kah pish kꝏ̄weekontamwahhe wéenu.
71.22 Kah kꝏ̄woweenomsh nashpe psaltery, nꝏ̄waweenodtum kꝏ̄nomwaonk: woi num-Manittꝏ̄m, kukketꝏ̄homoush nashpe harp, woi ken wunneetupanatamwaen ut Israel.
71.23 Nussissetꝏ̄nash pish mishe weekontamꝏ̄mꝏ̄ash, ketꝏ̄homaunon, kah nukketeahogkou pohquohwhunop.
71.24 Kah neenan pish keketꝏ̄kau kꝏ̄nomwausseonk qunikesuk: newutche nag quequenauánumôog, nag akodchuag kodwoskehetcheg.
72.0 {Ketoohomaonk wutche} Solomon.
72.1 Aninnumau ketassꝏ̄t kꝏ̄sittumꝏ̄ongash, woi God, kah kꝏ̄nomwausseonk ketassꝏ̄t wunnaumonuh.
72.2 Noh pish wussumau kummissinninnumoh en wunnomwausseonganit, kah kummatchekumog, wussittumꝏ̄onganit.
72.3 Wadchuash pish paudtoog wunnohteaonk en missinninnutu, kah wadchuwemesash nashpe wunnomwausseonk.
72.4 Pish wussumau matchekuoh ut missinninnutu, pish wadchanau wunnechanꝏ̄oh quenahukqutcheg, kah pish sokqshanau woskehuwaenuh.
72.5 Nag pish kukqushhukquog nishokke nuppauzsauk kah nanepaushadtoꝏ̄k, pannuppu wame pometuonganit.
72.6 Pish enunnꝏ̄keu onatuh sokanunk ut sashquonkanit: onatuh sokanon agwachippadtunk ohke.
72.7 Aspomantog wunomwausseog pish wunayeuogig; kah monat wunnogteaonk neanuhque nepauzsauk.
72.8 Kah pish nanauúnnum yeadt ketahhanuuk: kah yeawutch sepuut onk yeáen aongkouohkomuk.
72.9 Neg wadohkitcheg tóuohkomuk, pish nauaeog ut anaquabit: kah ummatwomoh nꝏ̄nꝏ̄squodtamog puppissai.
72.10 Tassꝏ̄tamwog wutch Tarshish kah munnohhannehtu, nag pish padtauog magꝏ̄ongash: tassꝏ̄tamwog wutch Sheba kah Seba pish magꝏ̄og magꝏ̄ongash
72.11 Nux wame ketassꝏ̄tamwog pish naaieog ut anaquabit: wame wutahtimoneunk pish ꝏ̄wowussumouh.
72.12 Newutche pish pohquohwunau quenahukqunutcheh maunitteungqut: kah wonk matcheku, kah noh matta wodtannunneumwonkaneg.
72.13 Noh pish wohqônumau matchekuoh kah quenahukqunutcheh: kah pish wadchanau ukketeahogkonꝏ̄oh quenahukqutcheg.
72.14 Pish pohquohwunau ukketeahogkounꝏ̄oh wutch asꝏ̄k[e]kodteamowonganit, & woskehuwaonganit: kah ꝏ̄squeheonganꝏ̄ mishoadtu ut anaquabit.
72.15 Kah pish pomantam, kah gold wutch Sheba pish aninnumauun: kah nag pish úppeantamwonshauh nagwutteaeu, kah asekesukokish waeenomau.
72.16 Na pish yeonitchamunyeuꝏ̄ ohkeit ut woskeche wadchuohkontu, ummeechummuꝏ̄onk pish nunnukshau onatuh Lebanon: kah neg otanit pish wushketuog onatuh ashkoshqut, ut ohkekontu.
72.17 OOwesuonk michémoheau: ꝏ̄wesuonk nagwutteohteau neane nepauzsauk: kah wosketompaog ꝏ̄nanumóog ut wuhhogkat, kah wame wutohtimoneash pish wuttussowenouh ꝏ̄nanumau.
72.18 OOnanumau Lord God, um-Manittꝏ̄ noh Israel, noh webe asit monchanatamꝏ̄ongash.
72.19 Kah ꝏ̄nanittamunach wussohsummꝏ̄angane ꝏ̄wesuonk micheme; kah muttaohket numwohtaj wussohsumóonk. Amen kah Amen.
72.20 Uppeantamꝏ̄ongash David wunnaumonuh Jesse, neit wohkukquohshin.
73.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} Asaph.
73.1 WUnnamuhkut God wunneneheau Israel, neg pahketeahoncheg.
73.2 Qut neen, nusseetash ômog tꝏ̄nequshinneash: nutontannehtuongash omog tꝏ̄nequshaash.
73.3 Newutch nutishkôônomp asꝏ̄tuog, naumon ꝏ̄naiyeuonk matchetowog.
73.4 Newutche wanne wehwhepappisseog ut wunnuppꝏ̄onganꝏ̄out: qut ummenuhkesuonganꝏ̄ menuhki.
73.5 Matta nag wuttammepunoog onatuh onkatogane: asuh matta wesauashauoog neane onkatogane.
73.6 Newutche pittuanumoonk ꝏ̄wéenuhkouh onatuh móoshagquohtogqut: ꝏ̄woskhuaonganꝏ̄ hogkꝏ̄og onatuh hogkꝏ̄onganit.
73.7 Mogquskesukquaog wutche wunnogkꝏ̄onk anuweetuog onk woh ne kodtantog metah.
73.8 Nag aninwog, kah matcheyéuog papaume woskehuwaonk, pittuwaog.
73.9 Wuttꝏ̄nꝏ̄ ayeuuhkônittue ponauwog kesukquéhtu, & wenañu pannupshaumꝏ̄ ohkit.
73.10 Newajeh ummissinninnumoh yeu en qushkenit: kah nippe numwohteau sénumauoneau naghok.
73.11 Onk nag nꝏ̄wàog, uttoh God wuttinwahteaun? kah wahteauonk sun wuhhogkat ohteau quanonkqappit?
73.12 Kusseh yeug matta anauongig Godoh, nag wunnaiyeuog ut muttaohkit, nag onchenaietuog.
73.13 Wunnamuhkut nuppaketeoh nuttah tahnꝏ̄che, kah nukkussenitcham matwoskhu[a]onganinnꝏ̄g.
73.14 Newutche nꝏ̄wesauwusham qunnikesuk, kah nussasamakouwhit as[m]ohtompogish.
73.15 Nꝏ̄waon, yeu woh nussin, kusseh woh nummatchenehteoh uppométuonganꝏ̄ keneechanog.
73.16 Yeu kodwahteauon, yeu siogkanakausuonk ut nuskesukqut,
73.17 Onk nô pajeh aoon ꝏ̄neetupanatamwe weekit God, nenutit wohtamunat ꝏ̄wohkukquoshinnꝏ̄onganꝏ̄,
73.18 Wunnamuhkut nag kupponóog tꝏ̄nequohteaouut: nag kuppinuhko[n]unk en paguaninneat.
73.19 Uttoh wuttin teanuk paguaninneau? pannuppu mohtuppaeog nashpe quequenauanumꝏ̄ongash.
73.20 Onatuh anukquonk tꝏ̄hkeit: woi Manit, tꝏ̄hkean pish kutohquanittam wuttinnussuonganꝏ̄.
73.21 Yeu nuttah wuttinneuánatamun; kah nukanukehteáwhutteap ut nuttꝏ̄unussit.
73.22 Yeu nuttin asꝏ̄kinneáh, kah mat nꝏ̄wahteauꝏ̄unáh: nutogquinneunkqussip puppinashimwut, ut anaquabean.
73.23 Qut nagwutteaeu kꝏ̄weetomsh: kenutcheg nuttannuk nuttinohkôunit.
73.24 Kussomsháseh nashpe kuhkinnꝏ̄suwonk: onk pish ompetagk kutattamunneh en kussohsumꝏ̄onganit.
73.25 Howan wadtihee ut kesukqut webe ken? kah matta howan nutahchewonamoh yeu ut muttaohket webe ken.
73.26 Nꝏ̄weyaus, kah nuttah s[a]unumwog: qut God ukqussukquánumoh nuttah, kah nutchippiyeum micheme.
73.27 Newutche kusseh, nag n[o]ꝏ̄sukkongquéaneg, pish paguanúog: nag kuppaguanopanneg mamussitcheg wutch kuhhogkat.
73.28 Qut nen, wunnegen nuppasꝏ̄sukauónat God: nuppabahtanum Manit Jehovah, onk woh nꝏ̄tamwáhuwam wame kutanakausuongash.
74.0 {Maschil ut} Asaph.
74.1 WOi God tohwuch sohwóhkôseog micheme? tohwutch kummusquanittamꝏ̄onk ayeuhkonáe pukittauúok ut sheepsut kenadtuppꝏ̄wonganit?
74.2 Mehquontash kummikkinneonk, nôadt tabhumóp: souobpunk ne kutahtóonk ne manꝏ̄hhomóp, yeu wadchúwe Sion ne wodohkéop.
74.3 Tahshinish kusseetash en nagwutteáeu paguanuongash: wame ne matchese asit matwau ut kꝏ̄neetupanatamwu keekit.
74.4 Kummatwômog nishketunkqussúog ut nôeu kummukkinneonganehtu: tahshinnumwog ummittaákinnꝏ̄ꝏ̄sh wutch kuhkinneasuongash.
74.5 Wosketomp wáeenomp neane wuttogkunk tahshinuk ut metugkꝏ̄kontu.
74.6 Qut yeuyeu tummethamwog mamansukwhongane anakausuongash moáeu, nashpe togkungash kah hammersash.
74.7 Unnuhteáog nꝏ̄tau kꝏ̄neetupanatamwe kekit, wunnisketeaúunnéau wutahtuonk kꝏ̄wesuonganit, uppenuhkoneau en ohkekontu.
74.8 Nꝏ̄waog ut wuttahhꝏ̄wóut, nag paguanontuh moáeu: nag wame chikohsumwog uppeantamwakomukquash God ut ohkeit.
74.9 Matta naumꝏ̄mun nukkehkinneasuonganunnonash, wanne wonk manittowomp[a]no, asa matta howan kenugke nenawun, ꝏ̄wahteaouun uttoh uttꝏ̄che?
74.10 Woi God tohuttꝏ̄che pish matwau kekómꝏ̄wau? sun pish matwau blasphemau kꝏ̄wesuonk micheme?
74.11 Tohwutch wutóntinnumun kenutcheg, kuttinnohkou? wutontinush wutch kuppꝏ̄chenauóunut.
74.12 Newutche God nukketassꝏ̄timom nukkonneayeúꝏ̄, ayik wadchánuwaonk ut nóeu ohkeit.
74.13 Kutchachaubenamup keihtoh nashpe kummenuhkêsuonk: kuppohquetahham uppuhkukꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash pꝏ̄tahpaog ut nippekontu.
74.14 Kussukquohtahhom uppuhkuk Leviathan: kah kuttinnumau ummeetsuonganꝏ̄ missinninnúog wodohkutcheg touohkomuk.
74.15 Kuppohshittahham tohkékomuash kah tomogkon: kenunappéhteóh moge sepuash.
74.16 Kesukod kuttaihe, kah nukon wonk kuttaihe, kukquoshaeihtau wequai, kah nepauz.
74.17 Wame kupponum wunnashinniinnash ohke: kuttaiyim sequan kah popón.
74.18 Yeu mehquoantash, matwau kehkontuk, woi Jehovah; kah asꝏ̄tuog missinninnáog blasphemaog kꝏ̄wesuonk.
74.19 Woi ahque magish ukketeahogkôunoh turtle kꝏ̄skuhwhanannom en monácheg: ahque wanánum ummukkinnéonk kummatchekeum micheme.
74.20 Mehquantash kꝏ̄nꝏ̄wáonk, newutche pohkenáoash ut ohkeit, wunnumwohteau wutohtuꝏ̄ash mukkꝏ̄kinneaenuog.
74.21 Noh waskhit, woi ahque qushkeitch akodchinát: matchekuog, kah quenaihukqutcheg waeenodtummohettich kꝏ̄wesuonk.
74.22 Omkish, woi God, kenꝏ̄tamwóntash kuttinnaiyeúonk: mehquontash asꝏ̄tu kukkekomuk asekesukokish.
74.23 Ahque wanantash ꝏ̄wadtauatongqussuonganꝏ̄ kummatwomog: ꝏ̄wogkoueonganꝏ̄ nag ayeuuhkonittue waábetunkquéaneg náno missi nagwutteáeu.
75.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut Altaschith: Ukketoohhomaonk} Asaph.
75.1 Kuttabuttantamaúunumun, woi God, kuttabuttantamaúunumun, newutche kꝏ̄wesuonk paswôhteau, kummonch[á]natame anakausuonganash ne nahtitteaúmꝏ̄.
75.2 Attumunnumon mukkinnéonk, pish nussampwe wussitum.
75.3 Ohke, kah wame neg noh wodohkutcheg saupásꝏ̄og: nukkogk[ô]nnum ohkekonnumuk.
75.4 Nuttin asꝏ̄tuog, ahque asꝏ̄ke ussek, kah matcheetowog, ahque tohshinꝏ̄k askon.
75.5 Ahque qunnunkqueu tahshinꝏ̄k kutaskonnꝏ̄wóog: ahque ketꝏ̄hkunk nashpe chétaeu missittupuk.
75.6 Newutche wuttꝏ̄anatuonk matta wutch wutchepwâóu, asa mat wutchéksuau, asa mat wutch sôúnnâeu.
75.7 Qut God wussittumwáen, pasukꝏ̄h kepúhteau, onkatogu omohkinaau.
75.8 Newutche wunnetcheganit Jehovah, noh wuttattamwáitchúꝏ̄, kah wine musqui: numwaeu kenittepâunausu, onk ne wussékenumun: qut niskeneunkquok ohteau appésinit, wame matcheetowog ut muttaohket pish senuppânumauoneau, onk pish ꝏ̄tattamunneau.
75.9 Qut nen nunnaihtitteam micheme: nuttinnꝏ̄hhomon tabuttantamꝏ̄onk ut um-Manittꝏ̄mut Jakob.
75.10 Onk wame wutáskonꝏ̄oh matcheetowog nuttummetahwôog: qut wutaskonóuh s[a]mpweusséaenuog pish tohshinôog.
76.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut Neginoth: Ukketoohomaonk} Asaph.
76.1 GOD waheau Jodah: ꝏ̄wesuonk missi ut Israel.
76.2 Onk week ohtau Salem, kah wutohtu Sion.
76.3 Nawuttit póhquenumun kôûhquodtash kah ahtompeh, ogqunneg kah togkodteg, kah ayeuwuttuonk. Selah.
76.4 Ken kummꝏ̄cheke sóhsum onk n nash mukkꝏ̄kinnuwontamwe wadchúash.
76.5 Manúhketeahoncheg woskehéog, kouéog ukkoúeonganꝏ̄: onk matta howan menuhkesu namehteau wunnutcheash.
76.6 Auskómuwáan, woi um-Manittꝏ̄moh Jakob, tatuppequânumog kah horsesog moáeu nuppꝏ̄e kouéog.
76.7 Ken, ken woh kukqushit: kah howan woh neepau ut anaquabean musquánittamanish?
76.8 Kenꝏ̄tamwahuwam wussittumꝏ̄onk wutch kesukqut: muttaohke wabeseup kah chequnappúp.
76.9 Omohket God wussumont, onk woh wadchanau wame manunnissuoh ut muttaohkeit. Selah.
76.10 Wunnamuhkut ummusquantamóonk wosketomp pish kꝏ̄wôweekomuk: ne asqueiyeuꝏ̄g musquanittuonk ne kꝏ̄tammehtean.
76.11 Quoshaumꝏ̄k kah âadtúhkók Jehovah kum-Manittꝏ̄mꝏ̄: wame neg wéinapitcheg paudtok mágꝏ̄ongash noh woh quóhshit.
76.12 Noh pish tummehtahwhau wunnashauaonganꝏ̄uh Santimôog: noh uhqunneunkqussu ut ketassꝏ̄timwut ut muttaohket.
77.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut Jeduthun, Ukketoohomaonk} Asaph.
77.1 Nummaúunnitteau God nashpe nꝏ̄wadtaúatongqussúonk, en Godut nashpe nꝏ̄wadtaúatonkqussuonk, onk nukkeihketongkup.
77.2 Wadtamehpunnáan natwánam God: nukkehkechesuonk manéyeuꝏ̄k nukonáeu, kah matta ohqutchúwanunnꝏ̄: nukketeahogkou sekeneam pôanatamweheonat.
77.3 Nummequânumomp God, kah nꝏ̄tamánatamup: nꝏ̄tapóhsinneáh, kah nunnashaúonk nukkonchuwannup. Selah.
77.4 Kꝏ̄wôshwahtôh nuskésukquash: nꝏ̄wsaume wuttamánatam, onk woh wanne nuttápenumꝏ̄ ketꝏ̄hkon.
77.5 Nunnatwóntamup nôadt aquompákup, kah kodtumꝏ̄ash nóadt.
77.6 Nummehquantam nukketꝏ̄homaonk nukkonáeu, nukkéketꝏ̄hkau nehenwonche nuttah, kah nunnashaúonk menuhkodtinneohteau.
77.7 Sun micheme pish pogkesꝏ̄au Jehovah? & sun matta wonk woh kitteamonteanitteaou?
77.8 Sun ummonáneteaonk micheme ámaémouk, quoshaumuaonk sun micheme panushano?
77.9 God sun wanántam ukkitteamonteánikónat: musquantog sun kuppóhhom ukkitteamonteánitteáeu kitteamonteanitteáonk. Selah.
77.10 Kah nussin, yeu nunnꝏ̄chumwesuonk: qut nummehquantam wuttinnohkôunne ukkodtumꝏ̄mash quanunkquappit.
77.11 Nummehquantam wutanakausuongash Jehovah: wunnamuhkut nummehquantam kenukkonne kummonchánatammuongash.
77.12 Nunnatwontam wame kutanakausuonk: kah nꝏ̄weogquttum kutusseongash.
77.13 Kummay, woi God, en kꝏ̄neetupanatamwe kekit, howan newuttinnꝏ̄hqueu Manittꝏ̄in ne anukkenuk kum-Manittꝏ̄mun?
77.14 Ken God monchanatamwe usséan, kꝏ̄wahteauwahuwam kummenuhkesuonk kenugke missinninnúut.
77.15 Kuppohquohwhunomp kummissinninnumog nashpe kuppit, wunnaumonuh Jakob, kah Joseph. Selah.
77.16 Nippe kenaúkup, woi God, nippe kenaukup: nag wabesúpanneg, kah mônâouash wuttammepunnomꝏ̄pash.
77.17 Matokqus sokanumup nuppe, póhkok wunnontꝏ̄womꝏ̄p, kah kukkôunkquodtash wonk sohwusháash.
77.18 Ummishantꝏ̄wáonganꝏ̄ keneempómog ut kesukqut: ukkutshaumun kutjishamꝏ̄ꝏ̄, ut muttaohket, kah ohke quéquanup kah nunnuksháp.
77.19 Kummay en kehtahhannet, kah kummay en missiyeuut nippe: kah kutóntánehtuongash mat wahteauoúunash.
77.20 Kummonchanomp kummissinninnumog onatuh flockut nashpe wunnutcheg Moses kah Aaron.
78.0 {Um-Maschil} Asaph.
78.1 WOi nummissinninnumog nꝏ̄tiégk nuttinaumatuonk, ahchúsittamꝏ̄k nuttinnꝏ̄waongash ut nuttꝏ̄nut.
78.2 Nꝏ̄wôshinum nuttꝏ̄n ut kukkinneasuonganit nussim nupwóaongash negonne yeuꝏ̄gish.
78.3 Nish nꝏ̄tamágupash kah wahteauagupash: kah nꝏ̄shinnónog nuttogqunna[n]ónup.
78.4 Matta nutadtatꝏ̄unnanonash wutche wunneechânꝏ̄oh, nuttinnonânonash pometuonk paaúmꝏ̄uk waeenomaonk Jehovah, kah ummenuhkesuonk, kah ummonchántamwe anakausuongash nish asépash.
78.5 Newutche menûhketeau wauwáonk Jakobut, kah kehtimau naumatuonguh ut Israel, ne anunnꝏ̄nomp kꝏ̄shinnónoh, woh wunnohtinnáneau wunneechânꝏ̄oh.
78.6 Ne pometuonk paaúmꝏ̄ug woh ꝏ̄wahteaúunneau, mukkiog neg woh nekitcheg: nag kesukkéhettit onk woh wuttinnoneau wunneechánꝏ̄oh.
78.7 Onk woh anóunáog God, onk woh mo wanantamóog wutanakaúsuongash God: qut woh nanaihteáog wuttinnꝏ̄waongash.
78.8 Kah woh mo unnaúoꝏ̄og ꝏ̄shꝏ̄oh, qussittꝏ̄munꝏ̄h kah nanánuwaonk ohquoantamꝏ̄munꝏ̄h pométeonk, pometeonk matta sampwohtauógig wuttahhꝏ̄óash: wunnashauonganꝏ̄ matta menuhkenauꝏ̄og Goduh.
78.9 Wunneechanoh Ephraim tapáaméog nemahtompáog, quehchiphouwáog wutch ayeúwuttinneat.
78.10 Matta nanaihteáog ꝏ̄nꝏ̄wáonk God, kah jishantamwog usseenat wuttinnaumatuonk.
78.11 Kah wunanatamwog wutanakausuongash, kah ummonchanatamꝏ̄mash nahtinôhpash.
78.12 Monchanatamꝏ̄ongash asépash ꝏ̄shuoh ut anaquabhettit ut ohket Egypt, kah wutohteakonit Zoan.
78.13 Paúshinum kehtoh kah uppannupwushanon: wunnumwônkquáhteauun nippe onatuh nomwonkquag.
78.14 Kah kesukodteáeu ummonchanuh nashpe matokqs: kah nukkonáeu nashpe wequanáe nꝏ̄tau.
78.15 Passehtham qussukquanah ut touohkomuk, kah ꝏ̄tattamheuh, onatuh wutch mꝏ̄nôayeúut.
78.16 Kah kussitchuwanteau wutch qussukquanit kah ayim jnippe anitchewánut sepuu[t].
78.17 Qut nano ummꝏ̄cheke matchenehheouh, mꝏ̄hmꝏ̄squeáhettit quanunkquappinnutcheh ut touohkomuk.
78.18 Kah qutcheheaog Goduh wuttahouóut: kôkodtauwontamwe wehquetummꝏ̄hettit meetsúonk.
78.19 Nux ayeuuhkone kenꝏ̄naog Goduh, nꝏ̄waog, woh wunnahtau God ahhutashpimuk ut touohkomuk.
78.20 Kusseh togkodtamup qussuk, onk nuppe wuttitchuánup kah kussitchuan anuwutchuwan, sun woh assan wonk petukqunnunk? woh quoshaeihtam weyaus wutche ummissinninnumoh?
78.21 Newutche God yeu wunnꝏ̄tamunnap, kah musquantamup namehkuh nꝏ̄tau nashqunau ayeuuhkonae Jakob, kah musquanatamꝏ̄onk ayeuhkonae nuhkuhkongquog Israel.
78.22 Newutche mat wunnamptauwoꝏ̄og God: mat pabuhtantumꝏ̄og ꝏ̄wadchanuáonk.
78.23 Tohkónogque ukkenꝏ̄tamun matokqs wutch waabe: kah wohshinug kesukque squoantamash.
78.24 Kah sokanonteadt manna woh ummeechinnaoont: kah anumauont kesukque weatchiminneash.
78.25 Wosketompaog meechwog Angelsog ummeechumumꝏ̄ wuttabe assamoh.
78.26 Wutchepwashinehteau ut mamahchekesukqut: kah nashpe ummenuhkesuonk pasꝏ̄wau sowanishinneoh.
78.27 Kah ogque sokanonteau weyaus puppissaiyeuut kah ummequnne puppinshasoh onatuh kehtohhunnómukqut.
78.28 Kah uppenuhkon ut nôeu tuppuksinnꝏ̄wonganit quinnuppu weekuwóut.
78.29 Onk meetsuog kah wamepꝏ̄og: newutche wuttinnumauh nehenwonche kodtantamunit.
78.30 Matta penuantamꝏ̄og ukkogkodtauóntamꝏ̄onganꝏ̄: qut ash meechummuug wuttꝏ̄nꝏ̄wóash.
78.31 Ummusquantamowonk God nuhkuhkongquog, kah nushau késukkomunnutche: kah kepetahwau pepenaadcheh ut Israel.
78.32 Qut onch matcheséog: kah matta wunnamptamóog newutche ummonchanatamwe anakausuongash.
78.33 Newaj mohtupanuk ukkesukodtumꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash ut tahnꝏ̄cheyeuꝏ̄ut: kah ukkodumꝏ̄mꝏ̄ash ut onkuppunónat.
78.34 Nahnashont, neit wunnatinneawhouh: kah qushkeog, kah nompoaeu natinneahwhôog Goduh.
78.35 Onk mehquoantamwog God ukqussukquanumꝏ̄oh. kah qunnunkappet Manit uppohquohwussuenúmꝏ̄oh.
78.36 Qut onch ꝏ̄wawunáunukumꝏ̄ouh ut wuttꝏ̄nꝏ̄wout: uppannuwaheóuh wutch weenanuôut.
78.37 Newutche wuttahhou matta sampwanꝏ̄h néh weeche, onk matta menuhkenumꝏ̄og ꝏ̄nꝏ̄waonk.
78.38 Qut nomwahtunk ukkitteamonteanitteáonk, wutahquoantamauoh ummatcheseonganóash kah matta uppaguanuh, nux, mꝏ̄chekit nompu puttikkinum ummusquantamꝏ̄onk, kah matta wagkauonumꝏ̄ wame ummusquantamꝏ̄onk.
78.39 Newutche mehquantamup nag webe weyausog: waban pomushont, kah matta wonk peyauꝏ̄.
78.40 Tohhen nohnompu ummꝏ̄mꝏ̄sqheouh ut touohkomuk? kah wunnohheouh ut touweu?
78.41 Nux, qushkeog kah qutchheaog Goduh, kah wuttogimóuh ꝏ̄neetupanatamꝏ̄moh Israel.
78.42 Matta mehquantamóog wunnutcheg: asa kesukod adt pohquohwhunósoh wutch ummatwommꝏ̄out.
78.43 Uttoh anákausip ukkuhkinneasuongash ut Egypt: kah ummonchanatamꝏ̄ongash ut ohkit Zoan.
78.44 Kah quanuppinuk wussepumash en wusqueheonganit: kah wuttomogkonꝏ̄mꝏ̄ash, onk matta wane wuttattámwuhhettekkupash.
78.45 Anꝏ̄nop mꝏ̄cheke unnissuoh mꝏ̄suhquoh, nag woskhukhetticheh, kah mohmoskuhteasu, nah paguanukqhetticheh.
78.46 Kah assamau mꝏ̄poh wame ne noh adtanegik: kah wutanakausuonganꝏ̄ chansompsuh.
78.47 Matcheehteop ꝏ̄weenomwussippagꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash nashpe mussegonoh: kah ummehtugkummꝏ̄oash sycomore nashpe tꝏ̄hpu
78.48 Kah uppuppinashimꝏ̄mꝏ̄oh ukquashquttahwhonat musségon, kah flocksumoh ukkutshamun.
78.49 Wunnuhketahwhoh ummuttae musquantamꝏ̄onk wutchenauausuonk, kah wutjishontamóonk, ꝏ̄tamanatamꝏ̄onk: anꝏ̄nont matche angelsog.
78.50 Ayim may wutch ummusquantamꝏ̄onk, matta wohquanumóou keteahogkounah wutch nuppunnat: qut aninnumauau uppomantamwowonganꝏ̄ en wesaushaonk.
78.51 Nushau wame mohtammeginitcheh ut Egypt: negonne ummenuhkesuonganꝏ̄ ꝏ̄weetuómut Ham.
78.52 Qut nehenwonche ummissinninnúmoh ohque wussohhꝏ̄wunuh shepsoh kah wussompshánuh en touohkomuk onatuh floksut.
78.53 Kah ꝏ̄wadchanuwae sampshanoh, onk matta wábeseog qut kehtoh nohkuhkauau matwâoh.
78.54 Kah uppasꝏ̄oh nahog uhquaeu ꝏ̄neetupanatamwe weekit; yeuut wadchuut wuttinnohkou tabhukup.
78.55 Kah sohwhohteau penuwohteaoh ut anaquabhettit, kah wutchachabenumaoh wutahtuonganꝏ̄ nashpe kuhkohhamóonk: kah ayim wuttauadtuonganꝏ̄ Israel ꝏ̄weekittamunnaonut.
78.56 Onk onch qutchheaog, kah mꝏ̄mꝏ̄sqheouh quanunkquappinutche Manittꝏ̄h, kah mat nana[?]ihteaouog ꝏ̄wauwaongash.
78.57 Qut nag qushkeog, kah mat nunnukqusseog onatuh ꝏ̄shuoh: penshumaeog onatuh matsompwesekq ohtomp.
78.58 Newutche ummꝏ̄mꝏ̄sqheouh kussohkóaaúut: kah ummishemꝏ̄sqheouh ennunneuhkontunkane Manintꝏ̄konat
78.59 Yeu nꝏ̄tog God musquantamup, kah mꝏ̄cheke uhquânumau Israeloh.
78.60 Newaj ahquoantam wuttabernakleum ut Shiloh: weetu uttoh ponug nôeu woskétompa[u]htu.
78.61 Kah ponam ummenuhkesuonk missinnauhtu, kah wussohsumoonk matwaog wunnutcheganout.
78.62 Kah aninnumauau ummissinninnumohh togkodteg: kah musquanumau wutahtuonguh.
78.63 Nꝏ̄tau mahchekuswau ꝏ̄skeumꝏ̄uh: kah wutsquomꝏ̄oh matta weetaetteauꝏ̄oh.
78.64 Wussephausueneumꝏ̄oh penushaog nashpe togkodteg: wussekousquomꝏ̄oh matta mauémooh.
78.65 Neit God tꝏ̄hkeu onatuh howan tꝏ̄kit wutch kouenat: kah onatuh manuhkesit wosketomp toquessumwidt wutch wine.
78.66 Kah a[n]ehtahwau ummatwomoh wusseganit: ukkekontuwaheuh micheme:
78.67 Kah wonk wussekeneaumun wuttabernakleup Joseph, kah matta pepenamo wútchippanowonk Ephraim.
78.68 Qut pepenam wutchippanowonk Judah, wadchu Sion ne wâmontog.
78.69 Kah ayim wussanctuaryhum onatuh kâsuhkôag: onatuh ohke ne manuhketeunk micheme.
78.70 Kah pepenauau Davidoh wuttinnumoh, kah wunneemunoh wutch shepsog ohhappehettit.
78.71 Wutahque nanaushepsoneat ushquoshumwoh wompequauwoh, uppasꝏ̄oh sohkomꝏ̄nonat Jakov ummissinniñumoh, kah Israel wutahtoonk.
78.72 Onk wussohkomonuh nean sampwag wuttah: kah wussampshanuh neaunag wunnehtuhtauonk ut wunnutcheganit.
79.0 {Ukketoohomwaonk} Asaph.
79.1 WOI God, penuwohteaog peyauog kutahtoongánit, nishketeauog kꝏ̄neetupanatamwu temple: nanomunkquatoog Jerusalem.
79.2 Assamaog psuksesoh mamachekesukqut nuppꝏ̄eu hogkaoh kittinneumoh: ꝏ̄weyausu kꝏ̄neetupanatamomog ohkeit puppinnashimwog.
79.3 OOsqheonganꝏ̄ seahhamwog onatuh nuppe, quinnuppe Jerusalem: onk wame howan upposekinuh.
79.4 Nukkekomukumun neetatteamungkonunnonog: nummamanauwanumitteamun kah nutá[h]anehteunteamun nag weenuhkunkqueogig.
79.5 Toh uttꝏ̄che pish kummusquantam, woi God, micheme? sun pish nashqunnaú kummusquantamoonk onatuh nꝏ̄taut?
79.6 Sokanumau kummusquantamoonk penuwohteaog, matta wahukkꝏ̄unneg: kah ketassꝏ̄t[a]mꝏ̄onganit matta weehquetumꝏ̄gig kꝏ̄wesuonk.
79.7 Newutche mahchipwôog Jakob: kah matchehteauog ꝏ̄tahtuonk.
79.8 Woi ahque ayeuuhkonittue mehquoantamaiinnean nóadt nummatcheseonganunnonash, kukkitteamonteanitteae kummonaneteaongash teanuk quoshae aninnumungqutteuh: newutche ahche nukkuttamungeyeumun.
79.9 Aninnumaiinnea[u] nꝏ̄wadchanitteae Manittꝏ̄mun, newutche kꝏ̄weseuongane sohsumoonk, kah pohquohwussinnean, kah jishkhomainnean nummatcheseonganunnonash, newutche kꝏ̄wesuonk.
79.10 Tohwhuch woh nꝏ̄wahettit penuwohteaog uttiyeuh um-Manittꝏ̄mꝏ̄oh? noh wahhenaj ut penuwohteatu wutch anaquabeog; anꝏ̄toan nashpe wsqueheonganꝏ̄ kittinnumog ne sꝏ̄ksquashongup.
79.11 Ummishanamꝏ̄ongkanꝏ̄ nég kobshagkinitcheg peyaumꝏ̄utch anaquabean, néanummissag kummenuhkesuonk, wadchan naghog kohquttumauutcheg wunnuppꝏ̄onganꝏ̄.
79.12 Nesausuk tahshit tashongquttau neetatteamunganonog ut uppꝏ̄chenawounnꝏ̄wout, ukkekomꝏ̄aonganꝏ̄ ne ash punnamukque[â]n, woi Jehovah.
79.13 Nemehkuh neenawun kummissinninnumog, kah kuttisshepsumwog wunnatuppꝏ̄wonganꝏ̄, kuttabuttantamauunnumun micheme: pish nunnohtinnomun kꝏ̄waweenomitteaonk, wame pometuonganash.
80.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut Sh[o]shannim Eduth, ukketoohomaonk} Asaph.
80.1 NOOtash woi ken wunnanashepsaeneumꝏ̄oh Israel, ken sampwushshanop Joseph onatuh flockut, ken wadohkea[n] nôeu cherubimsut wohsish.
80.2 Anaquabit Ephraim kah Benjamin kah Manasseh wogkauunish kummenuhkesuonk, kah peyaush wadchanean.
80.3 Quinnuppewussinnan wonk woi Jehovah, kuskesuk wohsumwahtoush, kah pish nꝏ̄wadchanitteamun.
80.4 Woi Jehovah ken um-Manittꝏ̄mꝏ̄oh ayeuhteaog, toh uttꝏ̄che pish kummusquantam uppeantamꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ kummissinninnumog.
80.5 Nag kussohkommꝏ̄nôog missuppegunne petukqunnunk: kah kꝏ̄tattamheaog missuppequnnupog mꝏ̄cheku.
80.6 Kuttayimaimun penuanittuonk neetatteamunganunnonut: kah nummatwomunno nog ahanuog môeu.
80.7 Quinnuppeninnean wonk, woi um-Manittꝏ̄mꝏ̄oh ayeuteaog, kuskesuk wóhsumwahtoush, kah pish nꝏ̄wadchânitteamun.
80.8 Kussohhꝏ̄wuttóh weenómwussippog wutch Egypt, kussohwôhteam pénuwot, kah kutohkekôn.
80.9 Negonnu kukquoshaeihtamup ayeuonk, kum̃enu[h]ku wudchábitteuhkónap, kah numwáontukquinnukkodtup ohke.
80.10 Wadhcuash onkaohtópash, kah wuttuhqunash ogqunneunkquodtupash ut qunnu[h]que chikuppit.
80.11 Unóntukquinukod kehtohhannet, kah wuttuhqunnémesash en sepuut.
80.12 Neit tohwutch sohqunnuman uppummenutunkanash: nemehkuh neg wame pâmushácheg mayut wuttit mukkꝏ̄pwunneau?
80.13 Touohkomukque boare mahchipwun: kah touohkomukque puppinashim ummahchipwun.
80.14 Qunnupish kenanumpassumunnumun woi um-Manittꝏ̄mꝏ̄oh ayeuteaog, wómompish wutch kesukqut, kah naush, kah nátauwôhtaash yeu weenomsippog.
80.15 Kah weenominneohteuk adohkehteáán kuttinnohkôunit kah wudtuk ne mánuhkehteáán wutch nehenwonche ken.
80.16 Chikohteau ut nꝏ̄táut, tumméthamun: awakompanaog kuttinnussûonk auskomont náhog.
80.17 Kenutcheg missuhkongqutch noh wosketomp kittinnohkôunit: wosketomp wunnaumonuh wutch nehenwonche ken manuhkeheadt.
80.18 Nemehkuh matta kukqushkéhtauunómun: keteáhinnean, kah nꝏ̄wehquetumumun kꝏ̄wesuonk.
80.19 Quinnuppeninnean, woi Jehovah um-Manittꝏ̄mꝏ̄oh ayeuteaog, kuskesuk wôhsumwahtauush, onk pish nꝏ̄wadcha[n]itteamun.
81.0 {Nohompuhpequodt ut Gittith, Ukketoohomaonk} Asaph.
81.1 MIshontꝏ̄waꝏ̄hhamok God nummenuhkesuonkanun weekontamwe mishontꝏ̄wak en um-Manittꝏ̄moh Jakob.
81.2 Neemunnumꝏ̄k ketꝏ̄homaonk: kah paudtauꝏ̄k timbrel, wunnontꝏ̄wáeu harp, weeche psaltery.
81.3 Péquagk monopuhpeg nepâuz weske oguamwidt: án kuhkꝏ̄wámukup, moaeu tabuttantamwáe kesukodt.
81.4 Newutche yeu an kuhkꝏ̄wámukup wutche Israel: wuttinnaumatuonk um-Manittꝏ̄moh Jakob.
81.5 Yeu en kuhkꝏ̄wona ut Joseph wutch wauwaonk, panupwushadt ohkit Egypt, na nuutt nꝏ̄tamun unóntowaonk, matta nꝏ̄wáhtamꝏ̄un.
81.6 Nutóntahtoh ꝏ̄wéanun wutch wuttúkedt: wunnutchegash pohquohwuttaúunash wutch ayeuónat akuhquog.
81.7 Kꝏ̄wehquetumaiip wadtamehpunaan kah kuppohuohwununup, kenampꝏ̄hamaúunup ut asampamukquodtut neempau: kukqutchhenup nippekontu Meribah. Selah.
81.8 Nꝏ̄tamꝏ̄k woi nummissinninnumog, kah kꝏ̄wauwaonsh, woi Israel, nꝏ̄tiéan.
81.9 Wanne woh penôwe Manit kutappetunkꝏ̄h: kah matta woh kꝏ̄wowuss[u]móh pénowe Manit.
81.10 Nen Jehovah kum-Manittꝏ̄m, waj sohhűwunukuéup Egypt: wóhshinush mꝏ̄cheke kuttꝏ̄n, kah pish numwôhtaun.
81.11 Qut nummissinninnúmog matta nukkeiketunkꝏ̄og: kah Israel matta nuttápeneunkkꝏ̄og.
81.12 Nemehkuh nukkonôog nehenwonche wutahchewontamꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ ut wuttahhꝏ̄wóut: kah usseog nehenwonche ukkinnꝏ̄nittuongannóut.
81.13 Woi nummissinninnúmog kukkeihtáhettis: kah Israel áhettis nummayut.
81.14 Woh teanuk nuppéeheóog ummatwómꝏ̄oh: kah woh ayeuhkônittue nukqushkenumup nunnetcheg nag sokeneunkqhetticheh.
81.15 Sékeneauóncheg Goduh, woh wutogquehtáuóuh: qut wutaquompaiyeumꝏ̄ woh michemahtop.
81.16 Onk woh wutassumopah wanégikish wheatash: onk honey wutch qussukquanit woh kꝏ̄wámepwununup.
82.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} Asaph.
82.1 GOD neepau ummukkinneunganout manukkesitcheg: wussumau kenugke Manittꝏ̄oh.
82.2 Tohuttꝏ̄che matta kussampwe wussittumumwꝏ̄ kah kꝏ̄wohquanumomwꝏ̄ matchetou? Selah.
82.3 Wadchánꝏ̄k matchékuog, kah mô wadtꝏ̄shꝏ̄gig: sampwenehheuk, onkapunnát kah quenahukquit.
82.4 Pohquahwhun matcheku kah quenahukquit: sohꝏ̄wus wutch wunnutchéganuóut machetowog.
82.5 Matta wahteauóog, asa mat wahtamóog: pomushaog pohkênaoùat: wame quenohtag ohkeit ontohtaash.
82.6 Nussip kenaau manittoog: kah kenaau wame wunneechânoh quanonkquappit.
82.7 Qut pish kenupmwꝏ̄ neáne wosketompaog: kah pish kuppenushaumwꝏ̄ neáne howohsꝏ̄tum.
82.8 Omohkish, woi God, wussittish ohke newutche pish kutahtoh wame wutohtimôneash.
83.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} Asaph.
83.1 Ahque netashshùash, woi God, ahque ohkꝏ̄ash, ahue chéqunapsh, woi God.
83.2 Newutche kusseh, kummatwômog wogkouéog: kah neg sekeneunkqueaneg tohshinnumwog uppuhkukꝏ̄h.
83.3 Asꝏ̄kekodteamwe kenꝏ̄nittúog ayeuhkône kummissinninnumut kah ayeukóne wetuodtuok neg adtahshadcheg.
83.4 Unnꝏ̄waog, éhoh peyunk tummehtawhontuh, onk woh matta wutohtimm[o]éog: ꝏ̄wesuonganꝏ̄ Israel woh mat mehquoantamꝏ̄un wonk.
83.5 Newutche wetuodtuog pasukqunnú metah: ꝏ̄nꝏ̄waog áyeuhkonetue ken.
83.6 Wodohkitcheg Edom, kah Ishmaelitsog: Moab kah Hagarensog.
83.7 Gebal, kah Ammon, kah Amalek, Philistiansog kah wodohkitcheg Tyre.
83.8 Wonk Assur ꝏ̄weetuómoh; aninnumauwóog wunnaumonuh Lot. Selah.
83.9 Unnehheuk onatuh Midianits neánheáp, Sisera, neanheup Jabin, up sepuut Kishon.
83.10 Neg pagwanehhettit ut Endor: ohqueneunkqusseuppanneg ánohkeit.
83.11 Wuttꝏ̄wosketompaog ogqunneunkqusséhettich Oreb, kah Zeeb, kah wame wussantimómꝏ̄oh ogqunneunkqussehettich Zeba, kah Zalmunna,
83.12 Nag nꝏ̄waog, neemunnumuttuh weekash God wutch kutahtauonganun.
83.13 Woi num-Manittꝏ̄m nag énneh onatuh wheelut, onatuh sequssunkanash ut wabanut.
83.14 Onatuh chaugohtag touohkomuk, kah onatuh kogkussompuneau nashqussuk wadchuash;
83.15 Ne woskeh nashpe kummehshittashshinneum: kah wabuwus nashpe kummehshittashshineum.
83.16 Numwohtaash akodchuonk wuskesukkꝏ̄wout, onk woh natinnehamwog kꝏ̄wesuonk, woi Jehovah.
83.17 Akodjhettich, kah wuttammepunâhettich micheme: nux, akodjhettich kah pagwanehettich.
83.18 Onk woh wosketompaog wahteauog, ken webe kꝏ̄wesuonkan JEHOVAH: kukqunnunkquap yeu ut wame ohkeit.
84.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut Gittith: ukketoohhomâonk wunnaumonuh} Korah.
84.1 Toh nuttinnu tápeneum keekash, woi wut-Jehovah áyeuhteáunit!
84.2 Nukketeahogkou nontweánumwꝏ̄, nux sauantam wutch uppeantamwahkomukqut Jehovah; nuttah kah nꝏ̄weyaus mishantꝏ̄waog wutch pomantamwae God.
84.3 Nux maméshasquish namehteau wetu, kah papaskhas ꝏ̄wadshayeu, uttoh woh apinit wunneechansuh, ut kut-altarumit woi wut-Jehovah ayeuteaunit, nukkehtassꝏ̄tamom, kah num-Manittꝏ̄m.
84.4 Wunnanumoog neg keekit apitcheg: nag nano kuttabatta[n]tamunkquog. Selah.
84.5 Wunnanumau wosketomp ummenuhkesuonk apehtunkquean, ut wuttahhꝏ̄wout ummayash.
84.6 Neg panupwushahettit ꝏ̄naohteai Baka ꝏ̄thamunkanuhkónneau: kah sókanon numwohhagwutteau nuppissepagwos.
84.7 Nag auog wutch menuhkesuonganit onk yean menuhkesuonganit: wame nogqussuog ut Sion anaqu[à]bit God.
84.8 Woi wut-Jehovah áyeuhteaunit, nꝏ̄tash nuppeantamꝏ̄onk, kuhkeihtah: woi um-Manittꝏ̄moh Jakob. Selah.
84.9 Naish woi Manit nutogqunneganun: kah monunneash wuskesuk sasequnukquean.
84.10 Newutche pasuk kesuk keekuwót negonne wunnegen onk nequt mutannunganogkodtash: ain woh negonne nunnanaeihteóh squont num-Manittꝏ̄m week, onk neit ꝏ̄weeketamon matchetꝏ̄wog wekuwout.
84.11 Newutche Jehovah Manit nepâuz kah ogqunneg: Jehovah magou wunneetupanatamꝏ̄onk kah sohsumoonk, wanne wunnegenninnꝏ̄gk woh ukqushkinnumauh wutch nah sampwshanutcheh.
84.12 Woi Manit ayeuteaunit, wunnanumau wosketomp nnoh pabahtanumukquean.
85.0 {Nohtumpuhpequodt ukketoohomaonk wunnaumoauh} Korah.
85.1 IEhovah, ken kuttápeneamup kutohke, kukquihchuwunnomp ummissinnóonk Jakob.
85.2 Kutahquontamauóp ummatcheseonk kummissinninnumog, kupputtagkuhum wame ummatcheseonk. Selah.
85.3 Kutamaunumup wame kummusquanatamꝏ̄onk: kukqushkep wutch kummishe musquanatamunat.
85.4 Quinnuppinninnean Woi Manit kꝏ̄wadchanuwonganun: kah kummusquanummuonganun netahshehteoush.
85.5 Sun micheme kummusquanumimun? sun kukqunteoh kummusquantamꝏ̄onk ut wame pometuonganit?
85.6 Sunnummatta wonk kuppomantamwahumun: onk kummissinninnumog woh kꝏ̄weekontamꝏ̄wônukquog?
85.7 Nahtussinnean kummonaneteaonk, woi Jehovah, kah aninnumaiinnean kꝏ̄wadchanuwaonk.
85.8 Nukkéhkitam ut toh ánꝏ̄wodt Manit Jehovah, newutche unnau wunnóhteaonk ummissinninnumoh, kah ꝏ̄neetupanatamꝏ̄moh: qut ahque nag qushkéhettich wonk asꝏ̄tuonganit.
85.9 Wunnamuhkut ꝏ̄wadchanuwaonk uppasꝏ̄sukongqunneau nag qushóncheg: onk woh sohsumꝏ̄onk ayeumꝏ̄ nutohkinnonut.
85.10 Monaneteaonk kah wunnamuhkuteyeuuk nogkiskôittuog: sampwesusséonk kah wunohteaonk chipwuttꝏ̄nápwuttúog,
85.11 Wanummuhkuteyeuꝏ̄k pish sonkun wutch ohkekontu, kah sampweusséonk pish womómpu wutch kesukqut.
85.12 Nux, Jehovah pish magou ne wanegik, kah kutohkin pish mogkékin.
85.13 Wunnomwausseonk pish wunnegónoh[-]kouoh, kah pish kupponukqun ummayu[t] wutántanehtuonganit.
86.0 {Uppeantamoonk} David.
86.1 Achꝏ̄sittah, woi Jehovah, nꝏ̄tah: newutche nummachek, kah nukquená[h]ik.
86.2 Wadchan nukketeahogkou newutche nen kodtumonteanuméan: woi num-Manittꝏ̄m, wadchan kittinneum n#noh pabahtánumugquean.
86.3 Monanumeh, woi Jehovah, newutche kummauunnitteaush asekesukokish.
86.4 Weekontamwáh ukketeahogkôunnouh kittinnum, newutche woi Jehovah kuttuspinnumaush nukketeahogkou.
86.5 Newutche ken Jehovah kꝏ̄neetum, kah teanuk kutahquoantus: kah mꝏ̄chekehteau kummonaneteaonk, nag wame wehqutumunkqueaneg.
86.6 Ahchúsitash, woi Jehovah, nuppeantamóonk: kah kukkeitash nꝏ̄wadtauatongqussuonk nanompasumunon.
86.7 Wuttammepunnaon kꝏ̄wéquetumoush, newutche pish kenampꝏ̄homah.
86.8 Kenugke manittꝏ̄wog, matta pasuk kuttinnongkꝏ̄, woi Jehovah: asa anakausuongash matta ogqunneongquodtinnowash kutanakausuonganit.
86.9 Wame wutahtimóneash nish kesteauupash, nag pish peyauog, pish kꝏ̄wowussumukquog anaquabean woi Jehovah: onk pish sohsumꝏ̄wóntamog kꝏ̄wesuonk.
86.10 Newutche ken kummissugken, kummonchanatamwe ussem: ken webe Manit.
86.11 Kuhkꝏ̄tomah kummay, woi God, nuppomusham kꝏ̄nomwaonganit: pasukquinteaush nuttah quihtamunnat kꝏ̄wesuonk.
86.12 Kuttabuttantamoush, woi Jehovah num-Manittꝏ̄m ut mamusse nuttahhut: onk nussohsumꝏ̄wontam kꝏ̄wesuonk micheme.
86.13 Newutche missi kummonanumúonk: onk kuppohquohwhun nukketeahogkou, wutch chepiohkomukque omohqut.
86.14 Woi Manit, pittuanumóog nꝏ̄ápetunkquog: kah mukkinéog onkkuppunnáhteaénúog kodtinneanâog nukketeahogkôunoh, matta kuppónukkꝏ̄og anaquabhettit.
86.15 Qut ken, woi Jehovah, Manit num-wohtea[u] kitteamonteanitteaonk, kah womoausu: kah sepe pahtsu, kah monat ummonaneteaonk, kah ꝏ̄nomwaonk.
86.16 Woi qushkish en hogkadt kah monanumeh, aninnumau kummenuhkesuonk kittinnúm: kah wadchan wunnaumonuh mittumwossisse kittinnúm.
86.17 Nahtusseh kukkinneasuonk wanegik, neg sekeneunkqueaneg woh wunnaumunneau, kah woh akodchúog newutche ken Jehovah kutannumaup kah kꝏ̄weekontamwáhip.
87.0 {Ukketoohomaonk wunnaumonuh} Korah.
87.1 Ukquenohtagóm ohteau ut ꝏ̄neetupanatamwu wadchukóntu.
87.2 Jehovah womantam squoantamash ut Sion, mꝏ̄cheke onk wame ꝏ̄tahtuonganit Jakob.
87.3 Sohsumꝏ̄ongash unneapash papaume ken woi wutꝏ̄tan God. Selah.
87.4 Nꝏ̄weeadtim Rahab, kah Babylon, neg wahukquéaneg, kusseh Philistia kah Tyre, weech Ethiopia, yeuoh wosketomp nawuttit neekit.
87.5 Papaume Sion pish nꝏ̄waog, yeuoh kah n$noh nawuttit nekinneah, kah quanunkquappit nagum pish ummenuhkeheuh.
87.6 Jehovah push wutogkétamun wussukwhóut missinninnuh, yeuoh wosketomp nawuttit nekinneau. Selah.
87.7 Naut nahtôꝏ̄hhomóncheg matta webe nohtompuhpequodcheg: wame nuttohkékomeúmash kutahtaunash.
88.0 {Ukketoohomaonk wunnaumonuh} Korah, {nohtumpuhpequodt ut Mahalath Leanoth um-Maschil} Heman {Ezrahite}.
88.1 WOi Jehovah nꝏ̄wadchanitteae Manit, nummauh ut anaquabean kesukodáeu, kah nukonáeu.
88.2 Nuppeantamóonk peyaumꝏ̄utch ánaquabean ahchúsitash nummaúonk.
88.3 Newutche nukketeáhogkounit numwohteau wuttammepunnaongash: kah nukketeaonk pasꝏ̄sukom weenohkeet.
88.4 Nꝏ̄wetogkeemit nag aô[n]cheg weenohkeet: onatuh neen wosketomp matta manuhkesit.
88.5 Nutchippéhtau kenugke nuppꝏ̄og, onatuh náhshitcheg apitcheg weenohkeet, neg matta waánummóacheg wonk: kah nag tummehtahwhôog wutch kenutchéganit.
88.6 Kussépsumeh quanónogok pasohtheonk: pohkénaoúut, ut mꝏ̄naiyeúut.
88.7 Kummusquantammꝏ̄onk nukquensummꝏ̄wónukqun: kah kꝏ̄taméhpunáseh nashpe wame kuttugkꝏ̄mog. Selah.
88.8 Kutamaunumah neetatteamunganuk nôadtit: kenehchánittamwâheneunk naghok, nukkuphâs, kah matta woh nussohhomꝏ̄h.
88.9 Nuskesuk mau, newutche nꝏ̄taméhpunnáonk, Jehovah, kenanampassumush asekesukokish, kuttushpunnumaush nunnutchegash.
88.10 Sun kenohtin monchanatamꝏ̄wongash nuppꝏ̄og? sun pish nuppꝏ̄og omohkeog kah kꝏ̄wowussumukquog. Selah.
88.11 Kꝏ̄womoausue kitteamonteanitteaonk sun pish wateauwaheau nnah wenohket? kah kꝏ̄nomwausseonk paguanuonganit?
88.12 Kummonchànatamꝏ̄ongash sun pish wohteauunash ut pohkenaouut? kah kussomweusseonk ut wanantamwae ohket.
88.13 Qut kummauunnitteaush, woi Jehovah kah nompoaeu nuppeantamoonk teanuk peayumꝏ̄.
88.14 Jehovah tohwutch sohwohteaon nukkete[á]hogkou? tohwhutch puttoghuman kuskesuk wutche neen?
88.15 Nutonkkuppunnam kah nahen nunnup, wutch nꝏ̄skenuuñeat yeu pajeh: waamattamon kussaiaskishohteaongash nukkogkeam.
88.16 Kummishe mꝏ̄squantamꝏ̄onk nunnuhkukongqun: kussaiaskishohteaongash nuttummetohuk,
88.17 Nꝏ̄weenuhkongquog asekesukokish onatuh nippe, nꝏ̄weenuhkongquog moaeu.
88.18 Nꝏ̄womoneg, kah neetatteamong kenaꝏ̄tashaog: kah yeug waanumogig kupponaog pohkenaouut.
89.0 {Um-Maschil Ethtan Ezrahit}
89.1 Nuttinꝏ̄homom ummonaneteaongash Jehovah micheme: nuttꝏ̄n pish wahteauwahuau kꝏ̄nomwausseonk ut wame pometuonganit.
89.2 Newutche nussip monáneteaonk pish micheme weekuhkon, kuppaubuhtanumitteaonk pish kummenuhkehteoh ut kesukquehtu.
89.3 Nꝏ̄nꝏ̄wamunnonup n$noh pepenꝏ̄ogkup, nutchadchekeimomp David nuttinnum.
89.4 Nummenuhkeh kꝏ̄skannemeneog micheme: kah nꝏ̄weketeam kutappuonk ut wame pometuonganit. Selah.
89.5 Kah kesukquash waeenodtumwog kummonchanatammuongash, woi Jehovah, kah kuppaubuhtanumitteaonk ummukkinneonganꝏ̄wout kꝏ̄neetupanatamꝏ̄mog.
89.6 Newutche howan woh ut kesukqut tatuppinit Godoh? howan masukkenuk kenugku nah wunnaumonainneunk woh tatupinat Jehovah$noh?
89.7 Manit mishu wabesuonou ummukkinneonganꝏ̄wout wunneetupanatamwog, kah ukquehtianumonaout wame nag quanupapitcheg.
89.8 Woi Jehovah, um-Manittꝏ̄moh ayeuteanit, howan manuhkesit Jehovah agquinne[n]gqussit kuhhogkat asa kꝏ̄nomwausseonganit weenuhkongquean?
89.9 Kenanaunum kehtohhane mishontꝏ̄waonk tukkꝏ̄og waapehettich, kutchequnashaog wonk.
89.10 Kussukqtahwhomp Rahab, neane noh nohshit: kusseoh kummatwomog nashpe menuhke kuhpit.
89.11 Kesukquash kuttaiheash, ohke wonk kuttaihe, papaume muttaok, kah ne adtahshimmeechumik, nish kummenuhkohtinash.
89.12 Nanumit kah soanish, neg kukkezheoog: Tabor kah Hermon nag pish weekontamwog ut kꝏ̄wesuonganit.
89.13 Kutahto menukhesue muhpit: menuhki kénutch, kah kuttinnohkou qunuhquodt.
89.14 Sampweusseonk kah wussittumoonk menehketeauꝏ̄mꝏ̄ kꝏ̄sittumwe appuonk: monaneteaonk kah wunnamuhkuteyeuuk pish negonshaumꝏ̄ ut kuskesukqut.
89.15 Wunnanamoog missinninnuog neg wahteunkeg wekontamwae wuttauatonkqussuonk: nag pomushaog, woi Jehovah ut wequaiyeue kuttinnussuonganit.
89.16 Ut kꝏ̄wesuonganit weekontamwog nehteagu kesuk: kah ut kussampweusseonganit mishsheheoog.
89.17 Newutche ken wussohsumoe menuhkesuonganꝏ̄: kah ut kukkitteamonteanitteaonganit nutaskonun pish tohshinau.
89.18 Newutche Jehovah nutushpuhhꝏ̄waonganun: kah ꝏ̄neetupanatamꝏ̄moh Israel, noh nukketassꝏ̄tamómun.
89.19 Neit kukkinnꝏ̄nomp wunneetupanatamweyeuit, ut monamansinneat, kah kussip, nupponamau aninnumóadtuonk noh manuhkesit: nummisheh noh pepenauit wutch missinninnutu.
89.20 Nummiskau David nuttinninnúm: kah nussusséqun nꝏ̄neetupanatamwe pummee.
89.21 Ut wuhhogkat nunnutcheg pish menehkhik: nuhpit wonk pish menuhkesuáhik.
89.22 Matwau matta pish wuttóadtéhtáheuh: kah wunnaumonuh matcheetowonk matta pish wutunkquanumwáheuh.
89.23 Kah nunnꝏ̄ketah ummatwomoh ut anaquabit: kah nussasámatahwhóog neg sekeneauoncheg.
89.24 Qut nuppaubatanumitteaonk, kah nummonaneteaonk pish weetomuk: kah ut nꝏ̄wesuonganit, wutaskonoh pish tahshin[ó]ninneuh.
89.25 Kah nupponam wunnutcheg ketahhannit: kah wuttinnohkou sepuwehtu.
89.26 Noh pish nummauunnitteunk, ken nꝏ̄sh: num$Manittꝏ̄m, kah qussukquanue nꝏ̄wadchanitteaonk.
89.27 Kah noh nummohtommégitteaeh: ánuunkqussúmau muttaohku ketassꝏ̄timwoh.
89.28 Nꝏ̄wadchanumau nummonaneteaonk micheme: kah nꝏ̄nꝏ̄waonganun pish menuhkohteau.
89.29 Kah ꝏ̄skannemunneoh nummichemappeheóog: kah wuttappuonk neane kesukque kesukodtash.
89.30 Wunneechanuh ohquánumáhettit nuttinnaumatuonguh, kah matta pomushaontamwahetteg nꝏ̄sittumꝏ̄ongash.
89.31 Nag pohquenummohettit nukkuhkꝏ̄waongash, kah matta nánauwehteauwéhetteg nuttinnaumatuongash.
89.32 Neit nátauohtóh uppanneseonganoash nashpe sasamatáheg, kah ummatcheseongash nashpe tattogkodtuongash.
89.33 Qut onch matta nuppápaquanne amaunumauoh nukkitteamonteanitteae womoausuonk: kah nuppaubuhtanumukqussuonk matta panushógkꝏ̄.
89.34 Nꝏ̄nꝏ̄waonk matta nuppohquenumꝏ̄, kah matta nutontcheteáꝏ̄ ne sohhamꝏ̄mꝏ̄ wutch nussissetꝏ̄nit
89.35 Pasukqut nutchadchekeyeuop nashpe nꝏ̄neetupanatamꝏ̄onk, matta nuppannꝏ̄waheoh David.
89.36 OOskannem pish michemohteau, kah wutappuonk onatuh nepâuz ut anaquabeh.
89.37 Pish michemenuhkohteau onatuh nanepauhshad, kah onatuh paubuhtanumukqussue wauwaen ut kesukqut. Selah.
89.38 Qut kuppogkenop kah kutjishanumop: kummusquanumau sasequnadt.
89.39 Kuttahnꝏ̄cheéhteoh ꝏ̄nꝏ̄waonk kittinnúm: kenishketeoh wutchetuhquab, unnohkónat ohkeit.
89.40 Kussukquetahham wame uppummenutunkash: kummahchumwéhteoh ꝏ̄manskash.
89.41 Wame neg paumshacheg mayit ummukkꝏ̄kinóuh: noh ushpunnomâonk weetatteamunguh.
89.42 Kuttohshinum wuttinnohkôunꝏ̄ ayeuuhkonukqutche: kꝏ̄weekontamwah wame ummatwomoh.
89.43 Kah kꝏ̄wehqueteoh en kenag wuttogkodteg, kah matta keneepauweheuh ayeuwuttinneat.
89.44 Wussohsumoonk ne kutteahsheáhto: kah kuttinnuhteam wutappuonk ohkeit?
89.45 Kuttiohquehteóh ꝏ̄skenue kesukodtash: kupputtogꝏ̄h akodchuonk[.] Selah.
89.46 Tohuttꝏ̄che, woi Jehovah, pish kupputtogquem? micheme? sun pish kummusquantamꝏ̄onk ogqunneau nꝏ̄taut?
89.47 Mehquoantash nutaquompiyeum uttoh[in] tióhqui: tohwaj tahnꝏ̄cheáheadt wame wosketompaog?
89.48 Howae noh wosketomp pomantog matta woh naumꝏ̄g nuppꝏ̄onk? sun woh pohquohwhunau ukketeahogkôunoh wutch wunnutcheganit weenohke. Selah.
89.49 Lord uttiyeush negonnáe kꝏ̄womoausuongash, nish chadchekeimuhpash David ut kꝏ̄namuhkuteyeumut?
89.50 Mehquoantash, woi Lord, kehkômaonganꝏ̄ kittinneumog: uttoh nuttin nashpe[u] ut nupꝏ̄chenauóunit, nukkehkómukꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ wame matikkenukeg.
89.51 Nish nashpe kummatwomog, woi Lord, ashpunáadtummoh[e]ttiche: nish nashpe ushpunnumáhetticheh wutontanehtuongash sasequnadt.
