89.52 Wunnanumunach Jehovah micheme. Amen, kah amen.
90.0 {Uppeantamooonk} Moses {Manittoowomp}.
90.1 WOi Lord, ken nutayeuonganun ut wame pometuonganehtu.
90.2 Asquam wadchauash neekininnꝏ̄g, kah asquam kahkénauwehtéauouan ohke kah muttaok, wutch micheme onk yaan micheme ken kum-Manittꝏ̄.
90.3 Kukquinnuppin wosketomp en paguanuonganit, kah kussim, quskeek kenaau wunneechanꝏ̄oh wosketompaog.
90.4 Newutche nequt muttannongane kodtummꝏ̄ tatuppeyeuꝏ̄, ut anaquabean, wunnonkou, pamshunk, kah onatuh nukkonáe askuhwheteaonk.
90.5 Kutogque moncheaheoog tommogka[u]it, nag onatuh kaémuk: nompoaeu tatuppeyeuꝏ̄og m[á]skit sonkuk.
90.6 Nompoáe nꝏ̄nꝏ̄han, kah neekin: wunnonkꝏ̄uk tummehthamun, kah uhpꝏ̄teau.
90.7 Newutche nummohtuppaémun nashpe kummusquanittamꝏ̄onk, kah nashpe kummishe musquanitteaonk nꝏ̄taméhitteamun.
90.8 Kupponum nummohtuppaémun nashpe kummusquanittamꝏ̄onk, kah nashpe kummishe musquanitteaonk nꝏ̄taméhitteamun.
90.9 Newutche wame nukkesukodtumunnonash mahtshaash ut kummishe musquanitteaonk: nutogque mahtshadtomun nukkodtumꝏ̄munnonash aunchemꝏ̄enuut.
90.10 Nukkesukodte nukkodtumꝏ̄munonash nesausuk tahshinchagkodash: kah shwosuk tahshinchagok, nashpe menuhkesuonk, onch ummenuhkesuonk sauámamꝏ̄onk kah onkquomomꝏ̄onk: newutche teanuk tummehthamun, kah nuttꝏ̄wemun.
90.11 Howan wahteunk kummusquantamꝏ̄e menuhkesuonk? neaunak kukqushitteaonk, ne nnih kummusquanitteaonk.
90.12 Ne$ne kuhkꝏ̄tomaiinnean ogketamunat nukkesukkodtumunonash, onk woh nupponamumun nuttahhunnonash waantamꝏ̄onganit.
90.13 Qushkish, woi Jehovah, toh uttꝏ̄che? kah aiushkiantash papaume kittinnneumog.
90.14 Woi tapeneauoshussunan teanuk nashpe kummonaueteaonk, onk woh nꝏ̄wekontamumun, kah nummuskauanatamumumun ut wame nukkesukkodtumunnonut.
90.15 Weekontamwáhinnean neáe kesukodtash onkkuppunnanéog, kah kodtumꝏ̄ash ne adt naumog machuk.
90.16 Kutanakausuonk pahkémꝏ̄utch ut kuttinnumut: kah kussohsumóouk en wunnechanꝏ̄wout.
90.17 Kah ꝏ̄neetuonk kum-Manittꝏ̄mun God nukkuhkongqutteuh, kah menuhketeaiinnean wutanakausuonk nunnutcheganunnonash: nux, wutanakausuonk nunnutcheganunnonash menehketeaush[.]
91.1 NNoh wadohkit asampâmukquadtit quanunkquapit, pish appeu wutonkauhtomut wame manuhkesit.
91.2 Nussim papaume Jehovah, noh nutusphouwaonk, kah nꝏ̄wonkónous: num-Manittꝏ̄m, noh nuppabahtanum.
91.3 Wunnamuhkut pish kuppohquohwhunuk wutch wutappéhanoh adchaénit: kah wutch wutannꝏ̄e wesausháonk.
91.4 Kupputtagkúhhup umméqunoh, kah agwu wunnuppawhunnit kuppabahtantam: ꝏ̄nomwayeuonk kutogqunnégonóhkom kah kutóngkouwóhquossꝏ̄.
91.5 Matta pish kꝏ̄wábesuontamꝏ̄h sauskshánittuongash nukkonáeu: asa kôúhquod pomushonk kesukodáeu.
91.6 Asa wesausháonk ne pomushaúmꝏ̄uk pohkenaouut: asa paguanuonk paguateaumꝏ̄ug puhshahquái.
91.7 Nequt muttánnonganogkussuog penushâhettit ut kishke ken, kah piukqut muttannonganogkussuog ut kuttinnohkôunit: qut pish matta kuppasꝏ̄sukkongkꝏ̄un.
91.8 Webe kuskesukqut pish kꝏ̄che naumun, kah pish kenaum wutonkquatunk matcheetou.
91.9 Newutche kuttaiimup Jehovah, noh nuttuspꝏ̄waonk, quanunkquapit, kutayeuonganit.
91.10 Matta pish kummáchoppino: asa pish matta wesaushaonk pasꝏ̄sukkꝏ̄mmꝏ̄ kꝏ̄tahtuonk.
91.11 Newutche ahtuhshau wut-angelsumoh wutche ken: woh kenanaaihhukquog nish noh kummayut.
91.12 Nag kutahshinukquog ut wunnutcheganꝏ̄out: ishkont kuttogkussittassun qussuk.
91.13 Pish kuttashkukau qunnônou kah adder: wuskoshimꝏ̄m qunnônou kah dragon pish kuttashkukau agwe kusseetut.
91.14 Newutche ꝏ̄womoausuonk nupponamungqun, newajeh pohquohwhunog: nukqunnunkqueh, newutche wahteoun nꝏ̄wesuonk.
91.15 Nꝏ̄weequetummunk, onk nunnampꝏ̄hamau: nꝏ̄weetom ut wuttammepunnónat, nuppohquohwhun, kah nukquihtiánum.
91.16 Pish nuttápe sepepomantamóonk: kah nunnaumwah nꝏ̄wadchanuwaonk.
92.0 {Sabath dayeu unnꝏ̄homaonk}.
92.1 Wunnegen tabuttantamauun Jehovah, kah unnꝏ̄homun kꝏ̄wesuonk, woi quanunkquapean.
92.2 Nahtikon kꝏ̄womoausue kitteamonteanitteaonk nompôáeu: kah kuppabahtanumitteaonk ásenukóhkish.
92.3 Ut puhpequoánit piukquómposik pémuneóhtanash, kah ut psaltery, kah ut harp wônóntꝏ̄wag.
92.4 Newutche ken Jehovah kꝏ̄weekontamwáhe nashpe kutanakausuonk: nummishe muskouanatamóntam nashpe wutanakausuongash kenutcheg.
92.5 Woi Jehovah, uttoh en missi kutanakausuongash, kah kuttenantamꝏ̄ongash mꝏ̄nâiyeuꝏ̄ash.
92.6 Puppinashimwe wosketomp matta ꝏ̄wahteauoúun: asuh mattammog matta wahtamꝏ̄un.
92.7 Matchetou sonkutche onatuh moskétuut, kah wame anakausitcheg matcheseonk adtanneghettit, ne onkwoh micheme pagwanôog.
92.8 Qut ken Jehovah quanunkquappean micheme.
92.9 Newutche kusseh kummatwómog, woi Jehovah, newutche kusseh kummatwómog pish paguanúog: wame anakausitcheg matcheseonk pish séahwhôog.
92.10 Qut nutaskon kutáshin onatuh wutáskonit nequtyeuwun; nussussequnit wuske pumme.
92.11 Kah wonk nuskesuk pish naum nukkodtantamóonk ut nummatwomut, kah nuttaúogash pish nꝏ̄tamwog ne kodtantamon papaume matchetowog neg waabetunkquéaneg
92.12 Sampweusseaenúog kussétuog onatuh palme mahtug: pish unneetu onatuh musquohtugkusseit ut Lebanon.
92.13 Yeug ahkuhteámukeg ut weekit Jehovah, nag pish dtannetuog wutchippenutunkanit num-Manittꝏ̄mun.
92.14 Nag pish yeayatcheh dtannegen meechum, mahtantamwáhettit, nag pish wunnogkꝏ̄og, kah ashkoshkꝏ̄ꝏ̄og.
92.15 Onk woh nahtitteáog Jehovah sampwésu: noh nukqussukquánum, kah matta penoweseonk ahtóou.
93.1 IEhovah wutassꝏ̄timun, hogkꝏ̄ wohquáunissónk, Jehovah hogkꝏ̄ menuhkesuonk, puttugquábussu: kah muttaok menehketeauun, onk woh matta ontohtano.
93.2 Kutappuonk meneketeauun nôadt; ummicheméyeu.
93.3 Tommogkon mishontꝏ̄wau, woi Jehovah, tommogkon mishontowau wuttauatongqussu, tommogkon mishéheau wuttugkꝏ̄moh.
93.4 Jehovah quanunkquappit mꝏ̄cheke missugken onk ꝏ̄wadtauatonkqussuonkanꝏ̄ monaog nippéog, onk kehtóntukquog ut kehtahhannit.
93.5 Kꝏ̄wauwâongash ahche wunnamuhkutéyeuꝏ̄ash: wunneetupanatamꝏ̄onk tapeneunkquod ut kekit, woi Jehovah micheme.
94.1 WOi Jehovah Manit noh annꝏ̄táonk wadchiyéuꝏ̄k, woi Manit noh annꝏ̄táonk wadchiyéuꝏ̄k, wôhsish.
94.2 Tahshin kuhhog woi ken wásittuman ohke: onkquattau pittuánumꝏ̄.
94.3 Woi Jehovah toh uttꝏ̄che matcheetowog, toh uttꝏ̄che matchetowog pish weekontamwog?
94.4 Toh uttꝏ̄che pish kuttꝏ̄og, kah keketꝏ̄kóntamwog woskehittuongash: kah wame anakausitcheg matcheseongash pish waéenowaog?
94.5 Nag sokqshanáog kummissinninnumoh, woi Jehovah, kah onkkapunnataúog kutahtáuonk.
94.6 Nusháog sekousqua, kah penowóhteuh: kah nusháog mowadtꝏ̄shꝏ̄neg.
94.7 Qut onch nꝏ̄waog, Jehovah matta wunnaumꝏ̄un: asuh um-Manittꝏ̄moh Jakob matta ꝏ̄tꝏ̄wóntamꝏ̄un.
94.8 Wohtamꝏ̄k kenaau puppinashimwe wosketompaog kenugke missinninnuut: kah kenaau mattammágwog aquompak pish kꝏ̄waantamumwꝏ̄.
94.9 Noh áhkitteadt mehtaúog, sunnummatta woh nꝏ̄tamꝏ̄? noh áyig muskesuk sunnummatta woh naumꝏ̄?
94.10 Noh sasamatahwhont penuwohteuh, sunnummatta woh sansamatahwhôu? noh kohkꝏ̄tomauont wosketompuh wahtunteáonk, sunnummatta woh wahteauouun?
94.11 Jehovah wahteóh wuttenantamꝏ̄ongash wosketompoh nish tahnꝏ̄cheyeúꝏ̄gish.
94.12 OOnánumau wosketomp sasamakoúwhadt, woi Jehovah: kah kahkꝏ̄tomauadt wutche kuttinnaumatuonganit.
94.13 Onk woh kittinnumau anwôhsinꝏ̄onk wutch onkquommomꝏ̄onganit: nô pajeh pahsahthamadt matcheetowog.
94.14 Newutche Jehovah matta pogkenáou ummissinninnumoh: asuh matta nukkodtumꝏ̄ wutahtouonk.
94.15 Qut wussittumóonk qunnuppémo en wunnomwausseonganit, kah wame sampwutteahóncheg wutásukkomunneau.
94.16 Howan wáabehtamwanshit ayeuuhkonittue matchesécheg? howan neepaiéhtamwánshit ayeuuhkonittue anakausitcheg matcheseongash?
94.17 Jehovah matta áninnumaiégis: nukketeahogkou teanuk woh chéquneiyeu.
94.18 Anꝏ̄wáon nusseet tꝏ̄nequshin: kummonaneteáonk, woi Jehovah, nukkogkanukkup.
94.19 Mônak nuttenántámꝏ̄wongash nuttahut, kꝏ̄nenéhhuwaongash wuttáphukqunash nukketeahogkou.
94.20 Wutappuonk matcheséonk sun woh kꝏ̄weechayeúmukqun? ayik woskéhuwaonk nashpe naumatuonk.
94.21 Nag moéog ayeuuhkonittue ukketeahogkôunoh sampweusseaen: kah ꝏ̄sumaúoh en nuppunnat matta woskéhuwâe wsqueheonk.
94.22 Qut Jehovah nuttusphouwaonk: kah num-Manittꝏ̄m nuttusphouéongane qussuk.
94.23 Kah noh pish upputtagquehtáhwhôh nehenwonche ummatcheseonganoash, kah pish wuttúmmetáhwhoh ut nehenwonche ummatcheseonganꝏ̄óut: nux, Jehovah kum-Manittꝏ̄mun pish wuttummetahwhoh.
95.1 HO peyonk ketꝏ̄homauontuh Jehovah: weekontamwe mishontꝏ̄wohkôontuh qussuk kꝏ̄wadchanitteáonganun.
95.2 Peyontuh anaquabit nashpe sampꝏ̄waonk: kah weekontamwe mishóntꝏ̄wóhkôontuh nashpe ketꝏ̄homaongash.
95.3 Newutche Jehovah missugken God: kah missugken ketassꝏ̄t anuwe wame manitꝏ̄og.
95.4 Ut wunnutcheganit mꝏ̄nôeiyeuash ut ohkekontu ohteau: kah kodúhkâuágu madchúash wuttáiheash.
95.5 Kehtoh wuttaihe, kah wutáyimunap: kah wunnutchegash kestauꝏ̄p nunnóbohke.
95.6 Ho peyunk waussumóntuh, náaétuh, appésittukqussinuttuh ut anaquabit Jehovah kezhúkqueagup.
95.7 Newutche noh kum$Manittꝏ̄mun, kenaau ummissinninnumoh wunnadtuppꝏ̄wonganit, us-shepsoh ut wunnutcheganit: yeu kesukok nꝏ̄tamóg ꝏ̄wadtauatonkqussuonk,
95.8 Ahque manuhketeáágk kuttahhuwoash, onatuh penuánittuonganit, kah onatuh qutchehuwae kesukodtut touohkomukqut.
95.9 Kꝏ̄shhuwóog quajhukquéan, kah natinneakôshettit, kah naumohettit nutanakausuongash.
95.10 Yauuncháge kodtumwáeu yeu neuantamhukqunah pométeonk, kah nussip, neg missinninnuog panneaûoh wuttahhꝏ̄oh, kah matta wahteauog nummayash.
95.11 Nag musquanumog nutchadchekéimog: onk woh matta petutteauóog, nutanwôsinnꝏ̄onganit.
96.1 WOi ketꝏ̄homok Jehovah weske anꝏ̄homaonk: ketꝏ̄homok Jehovah ut wame ohkeit.
96.2 Ketꝏ̄homok Jehovah, ꝏ̄nantamꝏ̄k ꝏ̄wesuonk: nahtitteak ꝏ̄wadchanꝏ̄waonk kesukodáeu.
96.3 Pahketauok wussohsumóonk kenugke penuwohteatu: ummonchanatamꝏ̄wongash ut kenugku wame missinninnútu.
96.4 Newutche Jehovah missugken; kah mishe waásumâu: noh woh mꝏ̄cheke qushau ánue wame manittꝏ̄og.
96.5 Newutche wame manittóog ut wutohtimoneat neukontunkanog: qut Jehovah ayimup kesukquash.
96.6 Quttianatuonk kah wohquanissuonk anaquabit ohteau: menuhkesuonk kah ꝏ̄netuonk ohtaash ut ꝏ̄neetupanatamwe wekit.
96.7 Aninnumók Jehovah, woi kutauwadtuonganou missinninnuog, aninnumók Jahovah sohsumꝏ̄onk, kah menuhkesuonk.
96.8 Aninnumok Jehovah wussohsumꝏ̄onk newadchiyeuꝏ̄k ꝏ̄wesuonganit, paudtauꝏ̄k magꝏ̄onk, kah peyunk wutchippunnutunkanit.
96.9 Woi waasumok Jehovah ut ꝏ̄neetupanatamwe ꝏ̄netu[og]anit: wabesek ut anaquabit wame ohke.
96.10 Nꝏ̄wag ut kenugke penuwohteaut Jehovah assꝏ̄tum, kah muttaok menuhketeauun kah mat pish ontohtano: noh sampwe wussumau missinninnuh.
96.11 Kesukquash weekontamꝏ̄mꝏ̄utch, kah ohke muskouantamꝏ̄mꝏ̄útch: kehtóh mishontꝏ̄omꝏ̄utch kah ne noh ohtag.
96.12 Ohteuk muskouantamꝏ̄mꝏ̄utch, kah wame ne noh ohtág; neit pish wame metugquash touohkomukqut weekontamꝏ̄mꝏ̄ash.
96.13 Ut anaquabit Jehovah newutche peyau newutche peyau wussittumunat ohke: sampweusseae wusittum muttaok: kah missinninnuh nashpe ꝏ̄nomwayeuonk.
97.1 IEhovah wutassꝏ̄timun, muttaok weekontamꝏ̄mꝏ̄utch, monakish munnohhánash muskouantamꝏ̄mꝏ̄utch.
97.2 Mahtokqs kah pahkenai ꝏ̄weenuhkongqun: wunnomwausseonk kah wussittumoonk wuttappuongane menuhkesuonk.
97.3 Nꝏ̄htau wunnegonuhkongqun, kah chikohswau ummatwomoh neit weenu.
97.4 Ukkuts[n]aumunash wohsumꝏ̄mꝏ̄ash muttaok: ohke wunnaumun onk nunnukshau.
97.5 Wadchuash sabahtaash onatuh wax ut anaquabit Jehovah: ut anaquabit uketassꝏ̄tamꝏ̄moh wame ohke.
97.6 Kesukquash nahtitteomꝏ̄ash ꝏ̄nomwausseonk, kah wame missinninnuog naumwog wussohsumoonk.
97.7 Wame neg waasumoncheg neuhkontunkane Manittꝏ̄ akojhettich, waeenomoncheg neukontunkane Manitto: n$noh waeenomꝏ̄k kenaau wame Manittoog.
97.8 Sion wunnꝏ̄tamun onk weekontamup, kah wuttaunoh Judah weekontamwog: newutche kꝏ̄sittumꝏ̄wongash woi Jehovah.
97.9 Newutche ken Jehovah kukqunnunkquap yeu ut wame muttaohket: ken kuttashinit anue onk nag wáme Manittꝏ̄og.
97.10 Kenaau womonogish Jehovah, sekeneamꝏ̄k matchit: noh wadchanau ukketeahogkouꝏ̄oh ꝏ̄neetupanatamꝏ̄moh, nah uppohquohwunoh wutch wunnutcheganꝏ̄wout matcheetowog.
97.11 Wequaj ohkehtaeu wutche wunnomwausseaenuog, kah weekontamꝏ̄onk wutch sampwutteahoncheg
97.12 Weekontamꝏ̄unok Jehovah kenaau wunnomwausseogish: kah tabattantamóg mehquoantamóg ꝏ̄neetupanatamꝏ̄onk.
98.0 {Ketoohomwaonk.}
98.1 WOI ketꝏ̄homok Jehovah wuske nꝏ̄homaonk newutche mahche nꝏ̄homaonk newutche mahche ussu monchanatamwe usseongash, wuttinohkou kah ꝏ̄neetupanatamwe wꝏ̄hpit ayimmꝏ̄ꝏ̄ wadchanuaonk.
98.2 Jehovah wahteauwahuwop ꝏ̄wadchanuwaonk: ꝏ̄nomwausseonk nahtitteop ut anaquabhettit penuohteaog.
98.3 Mehquántamup ummonaneteaonk kah ꝏ̄nomwayeuonk nogque en weekuwout Israel: wame aongkouohkumukquash naumwog ꝏ̄wadchanꝏ̄waonk kum-Manittꝏ̄mun.
98.4 Weekontamwaeu wuttauatongqussek en Jehovah wame ohke mishontowagk, kah muskouantamꝏ̄k, kah annꝏ̄hamunk tabuttantamoonk.
98.5 Ketꝏ̄hamok Jahovah mashpe harp: nashpe harp, kah wadtauatongqussue ketꝏ̄homaonk.
98.6 Weeche monopuhpequoanash, kah ꝏ̄wadtauatongqussuonk cornet: weekontamwae mishantꝏ̄wagk ut anaquabit Jehovah ketassꝏ̄t.
98.7 Kehtoh mishontꝏ̄waj, kah ne noh ohtag: muttaok kah neg noh wodtôhkutcheg.
98.8 Tommogkonog pohponkanitchahwohettich: wadchuog weekontamwuhhettich moaeu.
98.9 Anaquabit Jehovah, newutche peyau wussittumunat ohke: nashpe wunnomwausseonk wussittum muttaok, kah missinninnuog nashpe tatuppenehettuonk.
99.1 IEhovah wutassꝏ̄timun missinninnuog nunnukshahettich: appu ut cherubimsut, ohke kukkuhqushquemꝏ̄utch.
99.2 Jehovah missugken ut Sion: kah qunnonkquappu anue wame missinninnuh.
99.3 Nag wasittumohettich mohsag kah ohqunneungquok kꝏ̄wesuonk, newutche wunnetupanatamweyeuꝏ̄.
99.4 Ummenuhkesuonk ketassꝏ̄t womantam wussittumoonk, kummenuhkehteoh sampweusseonk, kummenuhkehteoh sampweusseonk: kutussen wussittumoonk kah sampweusseonk ut Jakob[]ut.
99.5 Tahshinꝏ̄k Jehovah kum-Manittꝏ̄mun, kah waussumok ut ukquensittassumꝏ̄unit newutche wunneetupanatam.
99.6 Moses kah Aaron ut kenugku wussephausueneumut: kah Samuel kenukku nag weequetukeg ꝏ̄wesuonk: weehquetumauaog Jehovah, kah noh wunnampꝏ̄homauoh nahog.
99.7 Ukkinnꝏ̄nuh ut qunnukque mahtokqsit nanaiteauog ꝏ̄wauwaongash, kah kuhkꝏ̄aongash nish anummaóhpash.
99.8 Nag kenampꝏ̄hhamauoog woi Jehovah kum-Manittꝏ̄mun: ken God nag aquoantamauadt, qut kussasamatahwhopanneg wunnatinnehamꝏ̄wongash.
99.9 Tahshinꝏ̄k Jehovah kum-Manittꝏ̄mun waussumꝏ̄k ut ꝏ̄neetupanatamwe wadchuut: newutche Jehovah kum-Manittꝏ̄mun wunneetupanatam.
100.0 {Tabuttantamoe ketoohomaonk}.
100.1 WEEkontamwae mishantowohtok Jehovah kenaau wame wutahtimoneunk
100.2 Weekontamwae waussumok Jehovah ketꝏ̄homꝏ̄e peyunk anaquabit.
100.3 Wahteauꝏ̄k, Jehovah n$noh God, n$noh kezhukqueagkup, qut matta kenawun kenawun n$noh ummissinninnumoh, kah wuttishepwussumoh wunnadtuppꝏ̄wonganit.
100.4 Tabuttautamoe petutteagk ꝏ̄squoantamut, kah ut wutchippinnutunkanit nashpe waeenomaonk tabuttantamꝏ̄k ꝏ̄nanatamꝏ̄k ꝏ̄wesuonk.
100.5 Newutche Jehovah wunneetou, ummonaneteaonk michemohteau: kah ꝏ̄nomwayeuonk nagwutteohteau wame pometeonganit.
101.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David.
101.1 Nuttinnꝏ̄homom monaneteaonk kah wussittumꝏ̄onk: ken woi Jehvovah ketꝏ̄homoush.
101.2 Nꝏ̄wáantammúun nuhhog en pahke mayut, woi aquompak kuppeyaauseh? pahketeaháe nuppompomusham nuttinnomukkomukqut.
101.3 Matta nupponamꝏ̄ matcheseonk anaquabeh: nussekeneam wutanakausuonganꝏ̄ nag pohchacheg, matta pissogqsháno nuhhogkat.
101.4 Musquantamwu metah nutamahkongqun: matta nꝏ̄waheau matcheetowaenin.
101.5 Howan kemeu matchénont wetatteamunguh, noh nuttummetoh: noh páhtuanumweanungqussit, kah pahtuánumwutteáhhont, matta nutchéqunehteauóh.
101.6 Nuskesukquash naum pabahtanumutcheg wutohtuout, onk woh nag nꝏ̄wetomukquog: noh pomshadt pahke mayut pish nꝏ̄tinnunnúmun.
101.7 Noh asꝏ̄k[i]komwe anakausit, matta woh nꝏ̄weetô[m]ukꝏ̄h: noh pannꝏ̄waégit, matta woh appeu anaquabeh.
101.8 Nompoáeu nuppaguanôog wame matchesecheg ut wutohtimóneat: onk woh nuttummetoh wame matchesecheg wutch wutꝏ̄tanit God.
102.0 {Onkkupinadt uppeantamoonk, kooshkoadt, onk sokanuk ummauunnittassuonk ut anaquabit Jehovah}.
102.1 NOOtash nuppeantamóonk, woi Jehovah: kah nummauonk peyaaúnukqush.
102.2 Ahque puttaghumah kuskesuk wutche neen wuttammepunnáon, ahchꝏ̄sittah, weehquetumauúnon, teanuk nampꝏ̄homah.
102.3 Newutche nukkesukkodtumash mohtupaémoash onatuh pukutáut, kah nuskonash chikohtaash onatuh kishkenau.
102.4 Nuttah togkodtamun, kah mussꝏ̄pohteau onatuh askoskqut: newaj wanántam nummeechinat nupputtukqunnunk.
102.5 Newutche nꝏ̄wadtauatongqussue chéquttummꝏ̄onk nummáhchekonáim.
102.6 Nutogqunneunkqus pellikanit ut touóhkomukqut: nutogqunneunkqus weésuut ut touóhkomukqut.
102.7 Nutaskwéteam, kah nutogqunneunkqus wameshashquésuut nonsieu ut woskéche kommuk.
102.8 Nummatwomog nummeech pukquée onatuh puttugquanunkanit: kah nukkinnetópánum nꝏ̄tattamꝏ̄onk nussippéquash.
102.9 Newutche nummeech pukquée onatuh puttugquanunkanit: kah nukkinnetópánum nꝏ̄tattamꝏ̄onk nussippéquash.
102.10 Newutche kutjishánitteaonk kah kummishe musquánitteaonk, newutche kuttáhshinip kah wonk kuppenuhkoneh.
102.11 Nukkesukkodtumash ogqunneunkquodtash onkaóhtaut amaeémꝏ̄uk: onk nummussꝏ̄pás onatuh ashkoshqut.
102.12 Qut ken, woi Jehovah, pish kummichemap, kah kummequanumitteaonk en wame pometuonganit.
102.13 Pish kutomohkem, kah pish kummonanum Sion: newutche ahquompi kitteamonteánumonat, nux kuhquttumꝏ̄e ahquompi peyaumꝏ̄.
102.14 Newutche kuttinninnumog tapeneaúmwog ukqussukquanumash: kah womantamwog uppuppiseiyeum.
102.15 Nemehkuh penuohteaog wabesuóntamwog ꝏ̄wesuonk Jehovah: kah wame tahsꝏ̄tamwog ohkeit, kussohsumóonk.
102.16 Jehovah weekehteadt Sion, nogqussu ut wussohsumꝏ̄onganit.
102.17 Wuttꝏ̄antam uppeantamꝏ̄onk noh nonsiyeuut, kah matta jishóntamꝏ̄ nag uppeantamꝏ̄onganꝏ̄.
102.18 Yeu pish wussukwh[ó]su ut paaúmꝏ̄ug pometuonk: kah missinninnuog neg kezheámukùppanneg, waeenomáog Jehovah.
102.19 Newutche womompu wutch quanunkquapit ꝏ̄neetupanatamwe week: wutch [kesukqut sukkut] Jehovah naum ohke.
102.20 Wunnꝏ̄tamunat wutchéquttummꝏ̄onk kopshagkunit: wutompinneónat yeug káhtimutcheg nuppꝏ̄onk.
102.21 Wahteauwáhuwonat ꝏ̄wesuonk Jehovah ut Sion: kah wasumáonk ut Jerusalem.
102.22 Missinninnuog mo[é]hettit, kah asꝏ̄tamꝏ̄ongash waussumónat Jehovah.
102.23 Noh nꝏ̄chumwéhteau nummenuhkesuonk ut mayut, tióhqutteau nukkesukkodtumash.
102.24 Nussip, woi num-Manitꝏ̄m, ahque amáuneh nôeu ut nukkesukkodtumut, kukkodtumꝏ̄mash pannuppóhtaash ut wame pometuonganit.
102.25 Nꝏ̄wadt kupponamup quenohtag ohke, kah kesukquash wutanakausuongash kenutchegash.
102.26 Nag pish mohtupaémoash, qut pish ken kummichemap, nux wame pish nekonneaiyeuꝏ̄og onatuh hogkꝏ̄onganit: nag pish kutôsꝏ̄wunnôog onatuh petúsqushaonk, kah nag pish ôsꝏ̄wunnôog.
102.27 Qut ken noh nan, kah kukkodtumꝏ̄mash matta pish wohkukqushinninnꝏ̄ash.
102.28 Wunnaumónneunk wutch kittinnumog pish nagwutteaéyeúog: kah wunneechannꝏ̄oh pish menuhkhéoog ut anaquabean.
103.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David.
103.1 Wunnanum Jehovah, woi nukketeahogkou kah wame ne apetunkqueh ꝏ̄neetupanatamwe wesuonk.
103.2 Wunnanum Jehovah woi nukketeahogkou: kah ahque wanontash wame ꝏ̄nenehhuongash.
103.3 Nnoh kutahquoantamunk wame kummatcheseongash n$noh neetskehteau wame kummahchinnaongash.
103.4 N$noh pohquohwuttau kukketeaonk wutch paguanuonganit: noh kutchetukquabunuk ꝏ̄womoausuwu womoausuonk, kah ukkitteamonteanitteae monaneteaongash.
103.5 Noh tapehteau kuttꝏ̄n nashpe wanegukish: kꝏ̄skenuꝏ̄onk wuskehteáuun onatuh wompsukukquáut.
103.6 Jehovah wunnehteau sampweusseonk, kah wussittumoonk wame neg was[h]hitcheg.
103.7 Wahteauwaheau ummayash Mosesuh, wutusseongash ut wunnaumonat Israel.
103.8 Jehovah momaneteau, kah kitteamonteaneteau, chekeu musquantam, kah monat ummonanéteaonk.
103.9 Matta nagwutteáeu auskomuwau, asuh matta micheme musquanitteauou.
103.10 Matta kuttinhukkꝏ̄unan neane matcheseog asuh mat kuttinonkquatunkꝏ̄unnan neane panneusseog.
103.11 Newutche néane kesuk qunuhquok anue onk yeu ohke: nenukkukqun ummonaneteaonk nag quashoncheg.
103.12 Wutch wutcheksuau onk yeu pajeh wutchepwoou: na nꝏ̄hque kutontahtunk qunnan kummatcheseonganunnonash.
103.13 Onatuh wutꝏ̄shimáu kodtumonteanumont wunneechanoh, ne wuttinne Jehovah kitteamonteanumon neh quoshukqutcheh.
103.14 Newutche wahteau toh anhenogus: mehquoantam nuppuppissaiyeumun.
103.15 Qut wosketomp ukkesukkodtumash ogqunneonkquodtash moskehtuut: onatuh ohteakone uppeshaônit, ne wuttinnegin.
103.16 Newutche wabanuppamukaumun, neit mohtupaemo, kah ne ohtagkup matta wonk pish ꝏ̄wahteauouun.
103.17 Qut ummonaneteaonk Jehovah wutche micheme onk yean micheme nag quoshoncheg: kah wussampweusseonk wunnechaneunk onk wunnechanꝏ̄oh.
103.18 Neh nauaihteanutcheh ꝏ̄nꝏ̄waonk: kah neg mehquontogig wuttinnꝏ̄waongash woh wutussenaoash.
103.19 Jehovah quaquoshweetam wutappuonk ut kesukquehtu kah wutassꝏ̄tamoonk wunnanauwunumun wame.
103.20 Wunnanumo'k Jehovah kenaau wut-Angelsumoh mishimmenuhkeseog kah usseog wuttinnꝏ̄waongash, kukkehtámog ꝏ̄wodtauatonkqussue kuttꝏ̄wonk.
103.21 Wunnanumok Jehovah kenaau wame wutayeuwehteomuh kenaau wuttinnumoh usseog uttoh unnantog.
103.22 Unnanumok Jehováh kenaau wame wutanakausuongash[,] papannuppe wutassꝏ̄tamꝏ̄onganit: wunnanum Jehovah woi nukketeahogkou.
104.1 Wunnanum Jehovah, woi nukketeahogkou, woi Jehovah num[-]Manittꝏ̄m muttae missugken: kuthogq sohsumoonk kah wohquanissuonk.
104.2 Kupputhogkꝏ̄ kuhhog wequai onatuh hogkꝏ̄onk: kupishquáginum kesukquash onatuh wadchukemꝏ̄up.
104.3 Nohponum wuttabasseash wekit ut nippekontu, noh ayik matohqs wuttatuppequanumuk, noh pomushohkonau wunnuppuhwhunuh ut wabanit.
104.4 Noh ayeuau wut-Angelsumoh nashauauittꝏ̄in: wuttinnumoh nꝏ̄nꝏ̄wunnaeu nꝏ̄htau.
104.5 Noh wunnohtau quenohtag ohkeh, matta woh ontohtanꝏ̄h micheme
104.6 Kupputagguhhumun mônoi onatuh hogkꝏ̄wonganit: nuppe wohqutohteauonk nish wadchuash.
104.7 Nag auskomádche wussemowog: ꝏ̄wadtauatongqussuonganꝏ̄ keneempomog nag kenupshaog.
104.8 Nish kukkuhquemꝏ̄ash wadchuut nish wowussumꝏ̄ash en ꝏ̄nohteaouut, uttoh adt quoshaeihtamop.
104.9 Kꝏ̄nohtoh kuhkinneganash, matta woh anuushomunꝏ̄ash nish matta woh qushkemunꝏ̄ash nuhkuhkomunât ohke.
104.10 Annꝏ̄nau tohkekomeuh ut passohteaiyeuut, ne anitchuog wodchuuhkontu.
104.11 Wattattamwuhheaog nish noh puppinnashimwoh ut ohteakonit: touohkomukque assesog ontham ukkonkkuhtꝏ̄nꝏ̄onk.
104.12 Kishke nag puppinshasog mamachekesukqut ꝏ̄adshaiyeuog: nen kuttꝏ̄waog ut wuttuhquinnehtu.
104.13 Wuttattippadtaou wadchúash wutch quanunkquok week: ummeechummuonk kutanakausuonk tapehteau ohke.
104.14 Ayim moskéhtuash nékinit wutche puppinnashimwog: kah wunnépogquash wutch wutauwohteaonganit wosketomp: onkwoh paudtau meetsuonk wutch ohkekontu.
104.15 Kah wine ne weekóntamwáhteunk wosketomp wuttah, kah pummee ayimꝏ̄mꝏ̄uk wuskesuk wohsittàut: kah petugqunnunk mánuhkehteaháhont wosketompuh.
104.16 Ummehtugkumash Jehovah numwóhteau, utchikupog ut Lebanon neahketeahpoh.
104.17 Nawuttit wadjisheahkoneau psuksésuk: kah stork ꝏ̄wetu kꝏ̄wáoh.
104.18 Kussókôiye wadchuash, wutusphuaonganꝏ̄ touóhkomukque goatsoh: kah qussukquanuhtu wôhtuhquásog.
104.19 Kehtimau nanepâuzshádtuh uttꝏ̄cheyeúꝏ̄ut, nepâuz wahteau toh woh adt wayont.
104.20 Kutayim pohkenâi, onk nuhkon: neit wame puppinashimwussog touôhkomukqut uppimmaiinneau.
104.21 Wushkoshimwe qunnónouwemésog nehnehkóntamwog neawuttamwuhhettit: kah natinnehámwog ummeetsuonganꝏ̄ wutch Godut.
104.22 Pashpishonche, mohmoéog kah sepsinwog assampamukquodtut.
104.23 Wosketomp sohham en wutanakausuonganit, kah ꝏ̄tamanatamonganit na en wunnonkꝏ̄ꝏ̄wut.
104.24 Woi Jehovah tahshinnúꝏ̄ash kutanakausuongash? kutussénash wamu ut waantamꝏ̄onganit: ohket numwohteau kꝏ̄ween[a]ieetuonk.
104.25 Kah missi kah mishigski kehtoh, uttoh adt pumáhhomwúhhettit matta woh wôáun[un]kig, naneeswe papeississitcheg kah matikkénukeg puppinashimwog.
104.26 Na pomushaumꝏ̄g kuhtꝏ̄nogquosh, noh pꝏ̄tab kuttaiyimau, nawuttit pûhpin neat.
104.27 Yeug wame kutannaónukquog, onk woh n[a]g kutassamóog nish noh uttꝏ̄che.
104.28 Uttohassamadt ne mukkinnumunneau: kꝏ̄wôhshwunum kenukutcheg onk nag kuttáphéoog nashpe wanégik.
104.29 Kupputtagguhhum kuskesuk, nag wuttammepunnáog: kutamaùnumun wunnashauonganꝏ̄, onk nuppꝏ̄og, onk quinnuppéog en puppissiyeúunneat.
104.30 Kutannꝏ̄n kenashaúanit onk nag kezhéaog: kah kꝏ̄skéhteóh woskéit ohke.
104.31 Wussohsumꝏ̄onk Jehovah michemohteau: Jehovah weekontam ut wutanakausuonganéhtu,
104.32 Móninneam ohke, kah nunnukeshau: mussinnum wadchúash, onk nish qussóhtóouash.
104.33 Nukkuttꝏ̄homau Jehovah tisohkepomantam: nuttinnꝏ̄homau tabuttantamꝏ̄ongash num-Manittꝏ̄m, ash papomantamop.
104.34 Nunnatwânumáonk weetumungquot: nꝏ̄weekontam ut Jehovah.
104.35 Matcheseáenúog mohtupaéhettich wutch ohket, kah ahque wonk matcheetowaenúutch: wunnânum Jehovah woi nukketeahogkou waeenomꝏ̄k Jehovah.
105.1 WOi tabuttantamok Jehovah, wehquetumok ꝏ̄wésuonk: wahteauwahuwagk wutússeongash ut kenugke missinninnútu.
105.2 Ketꝏ̄hamok, anꝏ̄hamok ketꝏ̄hamaongash: wéogquttomꝏ̄k wame ummonchánatamwe anakausuongash.
105.3 Waeenomok ut wunneetupanatamwu ꝏ̄wesuonganit: wuttahhꝏ̄wóash weekontamꝏ̄mꝏ̄utch neg natinnewhóncheg Jehovah.
105.4 Natinnehꝏ̄k Jehovah kah ummenuhkesuonk: natinnehamꝏ̄k wuskesuk micheme.
105.5 Mehquontamꝏ̄k monchanatamwu wutanakausuongash nish asépash: ummonchanatamꝏ̄wongash, kah wussittumꝏ̄ongash ut wuttꝏ̄nut.
105.6 Woi kenaau Abraham ꝏ̄skannemuneoh: kenaau wunneechanoh Jakob pepénaômpuh.
105.7 Noh Jehovah kum-Manittꝏ̄mun: ꝏ̄sittumꝏ̄ongash yeuut wame muttaohkeit.
105.8 Mehquantam ꝏ̄nꝏ̄waonk micheme: wuttinnꝏ̄wáonk ne ánꝏ̄wop nequt muttannongane pometeongash.
105.9 Ne ꝏ̄nꝏ̄wáonk ayikup nashpe Abrahamoh, kah wadchadchekéimáonk Isaakoh.
105.10 Kah ummenuhkéhteaun ne nan Jakoboh, wutche naumatuonk: kah Israeloh wutch machemohtag wunnꝏ̄waonk.
105.11 Anꝏ̄wadt, ken kuttinnumaush ohket Canaan, kutahtaongane ohteuk.
105.12 Ohguhshettit wosketompaog: nux, kutohgussumwꝏ̄, kah kuppénuwohteamwꝏ̄ naut.
105.13 Aáhettit wutch wutohtimóneat onk yaan wutohtimóneat: kah wutch asꝏ̄tamꝏ̄onganit, en onkatogane missinninnûut.
105.14 Matta unnánumôou howáne woskéhuk naghok, nux áushkómau ketahsꝏ̄timwoh wutche nagumôu.
105.15 Ahque mussinh saséqunog, kah ahque woskéheuk nummanittowompomog.
105.16 Wonk weehquetum mashógqunneáonk ut ohket: póhquanum wame anwôhhꝏ̄unne petugqunnunk.
105.17 Noh anꝏ̄nau wosketompoh negonáeu nag wutche, Joseph noh magumukup wutche wuttinnúmun.
105.18 Noh wusseetash woskéhukꝏ̄mꝏ̄ mꝏ̄óshagquogtag: mꝏ̄ôhshog aúmꝏ̄ ukketeahogkôunit.
105.19 Onk nô pajeh wuttinnꝏ̄waonk paaúmꝏ̄uk: wuttinnꝏ̄waonk Jehovah qutchhukqun.
105.20 Ketassꝏ̄t anꝏ̄teámꝏ̄, kah wutómpinneuh: nanaanuaenin ut missinninnútu, kah wussohwhunoh.
105.21 Wutáyeuoh wunnánaunnumenin week: kah nanaánumun wame wutahtóonk.
105.22 Onk woh tahtágkuppinau wussontimaumoh unnantog: kah onk woh kuhkꝏ̄tomauau ukkéhchaiyeumoh waantamóonk.
105.23 Kah Israel peyau Egypt, kah Jakob penꝏ̄wahteao ut ohkeit Ham.
105.24 Kah mꝏ̄chekéheau ummissinninnumoh misheu, kah ummꝏ̄cheke menêhkheuh onk neh ummatwomꝏ̄oh.
105.25 Qunnuppinum wuttahhꝏ̄woash sékeneauonat ummissinninneúmoh, asꝏ̄kekomonat wuttinninnumoh.
105.26 Anꝏ̄nau, Mosesoh wuttinninnumoh: kah Aaronoh neh pepenaúmpoh.
105.27 Nag nahtitteáog ukkehkinneasuonganꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash kenugke nahoh: kah ummonchanatamꝏ̄ongash ut ohkeit Ham.
105.28 Anꝏ̄nau pohkenáiyeuoh, onk ayim pohkenái: kah matta pa[n]néusseog wuttinnꝏ̄waonk.
105.29 Qunnuppinnum nuppéash wusqueheonkanúꝏ̄ut, kah paguanau namohsoh.
105.30 Ohke pasꝏ̄au monaoh tenogkequasog: ut wutchamberumꝏ̄óut kehtassꝏ̄tamwog.
105.31 Ketꝏ̄kóp, onk monaog peyâog mꝏ̄sesúhquog, kah yeuhquog wame ne ohkit.
105.32 Sokanonteau mussegon wutche sokanoni kah nꝏ̄nꝏ̄unneau ohke.
105.33 Kah sóquetahham weenómesippaguash, kah figse mehtugquash, kah póhquetahham matugquash ne ohkeit.
105.34 Ketꝏ̄hkop kah quahquequéshontáog peyauog, kah mꝏ̄páog, matta woh wâômukeg.
105.35 Kah mahchepꝏ̄og wame wunnépaquash ne ohkeit, kah mahchepꝏ̄og ummeechummúonk wutohtuout.
105.36 Kah nushau mohtommégitcheh neit ohkeit: negonne wame ummenuhkesuonganꝏ̄.
105.37 Kah wussohhꝏ̄wu[n]oh ohtóog silver kag gold: kah matta pasuk nꝏ̄chemwése neadtashaùwadthettit.
105.38 Egypt weekontamup, nag monchéhettit: newutche wábesuonganꝏ̄ nag wunohkukkongqunneau.
105.39 Sepagnunum matokqs upputtagúhwhou: kah nꝏ̄tau ꝏ̄wôhsumauóh nukkonáeu.
105.40 Weehquetumohettit, uppaudtaoh pꝏ̄hpꝏ̄hqutteh kah ꝏ̄wamepwuhheuh petukqunnunk wutch kesukqut.
105.41 Wohshinnum qussuk, kah nippe wuttitchꝏ̄wan: nunnobpahteaouut pomitchuwan nippe onatuh Sepuut.
105.42 Newutche mehquoantam ꝏ̄neetupanatamwe ukquoshꝏ̄waonk: Abramoh wuttinneumoh.
105.43 Kah sohhꝏ̄wunau ummissinninnumoh nashpe weekontamꝏ̄onk pepenauonche nashpe ketꝏ̄homaonk.
105.44 Kah aninnumauau wutohkeiash penuohteaog: onk nompanumwog wutanakausuonganꝏ̄ missinninnuog.
105.45 Onk woh usseog ukkuhkꝏ̄aongash kah nanaiheaog wuttinnaumatuongash waeenomok Jehovah.
106.1 Waeenomok Jehovah: woi tabuttantamꝏ̄k Jehovah newutche wunnetou, newutche ummonaneteaonk michemeyeuꝏ̄.
106.2 Howan woh mahshontꝏ̄sog mogagish wutanakausuongash Manit? howan woh nahtitteadt wame tabuttantamoongash?
106.3 OOnanumoog nag nanaaihteunkig wussittumoonk, kah noh sampweusset nagwutteaeu.
106.4 Mequanumeh woi Jehovah, nashpe kukkitteamonteanumaonk kummissinninnumog: woi nattouwahhe náshpe kꝏ̄wadchanuwaonk.
106.5 Onk woh nunnaum ꝏ̄netuonk pepenꝏ̄wadt, onk woh nꝏ̄wekontam ꝏ̄wekontamꝏ̄onganit kutohtimoin: onk woh kꝏ̄woweenomsh weeche kutohtoonk.
106.6 Nummatchesemun weeche nꝏ̄shinnonog; nutussemun matcheseonk, nummahche neeskesemun.
106.7 Nꝏ̄shinnonog matta wahteauoog kummonchanatamꝏ̄ongash ut Egypt; nag matta mehquoantamoog monakish kummonaneteaongash, qut ummꝏ̄mꝏ̄sqheouh ut ketahhannit, msqui ketahhannit?
106.8 Qut uppohquohwhunoh newutche ꝏ̄wesuonk, woh wahteauwahuwonat ummishe menuhkesuonk.
106.9 Kah auskontam msque kehtoh, nunnobpauꝏ̄p: nemehkuh uppannuppuwunuh mꝏ̄noiyeuut onatuh touohkomukqut.
106.10 Kah uppohquohwunoh nahog wutch wunnutcheganꝏ̄out jishanumoncheg: onk pohquohwunoh wutch matwaog wunnutcheganꝏ̄wo[u]t.
106.11 Onk nuppe nogkuhkouau ummatwomꝏ̄oh, onk nag matta pasuk squinneanoun,
106.12 Neit wunnamptámwog ukkuttꝏ̄wongash: anꝏ̄homoog tabuttantamoongash.
106.13 Teanuk wananatamwog wutánakausuongash: matta pahtauꝏ̄og ukkenꝏ̄nuwaonk.
106.14 Qut mꝏ̄cheke matchekodtantamwog ut touohkomukqut: kah qutcheheaog Goduh ut touohkomuk.
106.15 Kah wuttinnumauoh ne weequetumungqut: qut ꝏ̄nausheau nag ukketeahogkounóuh.
106.16 Kah ishkounoog Mosesoh ut tuppuksinnꝏ̄onganit kah Aaron ꝏ̄neetupanatamꝏ̄moh.
106.17 Ohke wôhshweemꝏ̄ kah misheaskꝏ̄ Dathanuh: kah nuhkuhkauou Abiram weechauoncheh.
106.18 Kah nꝏ̄tau nashqunau naut weechaugwutcheh: nꝏ̄nꝏ̄neau chikkoswau matcheetꝏ̄woh.
106.19 Kezheaog Calfeoh ut Horeb: kah waussumaog mohtuppohtaeu nuñeukontonkoh.
106.20 Yeu wuttinne osꝏ̄wunnumunneau wussohsumoonk, agqueneungqussit ox noh meechik moskehtuash.
106.21 Nag wunnanumaog Goduh uppohquohwussunenumꝏ̄uh: noh mahche usseit mógagish ut Egypt.
106.22 Monchanatámwe ânakausuongash wutohket Ham: kah uhqunneunkquokish kishke msqui ketahhannet.
106.23 Newaje nꝏ̄wadt, nuppaguanoog: mat Moses neh pepenauoncheh neepauokis anaquabit adtauwunneusik woh ukqushkinnumunat ummusquantamꝏ̄onk iskont na[h] uppaguanuh.
106.24 Nux wutjishontamunnaop kohkodtantamuk ohke: matta wunnamptamoog wuttinnꝏ̄waonk.
106.25 Qut mꝏ̄mꝏ̄skꝏ̄waog ut weekuwout kah matta kukkehtamoog ꝏ̄wadtauatonkqussuonk God.
106.26 Newajeh ayeuuhkonittue tohshinumauont wunnutcheg: onk woh uppaguanonat ut touohkomuk.
106.27 Woh u[k]kepuhkonat ꝏ̄skannemunnuuh kenugke wutohtimoneat; onk woh náh wusseahwonat ut ohkeit.
106.28 Kah wunnꝏ̄waog weeche Baal Peoroh: kah meechwog magꝏ̄wongash nag napukeg.
106.29 Yeu wuttin mꝏ̄sqheonneau nashpe neane natwoantamohettit, kah wesaushaonk nah wunuhkuhkauoh.
106.30 Neit Phineas neepau, kah sampweussittumoonk wuttussen, neit wesaushaonk o[n]tappu.
106.31 Kah yeu wussittumauon wutch sampweusseonganit: ut wame pomet[o]onganit micheme.
106.32 Kah ummꝏ̄sqheouh ut penuanittue nippeit: onk nemehkuh Moses sasamakuhwhau nagwutchu.
106.33 Newutche mꝏ̄sqheaog wunnashauanitto, newaje koshkomme matcheunnont ut wussissetꝏ̄nit.
106.34 Matta pagwottauoog wutohtimoneash papaume nish anompash Jehovah.
106.35 Qut kenukshaog penuwohteaut, kah kodnetuhtoog wutanakausuonganꝏ̄oash.
106.36 Kah nag waussumaog, nag wuttinneuhkontunkaneu Manittꝏ̄mꝏ̄oh, neghog ahpehhanuꝏ̄og nagwutchu.
106.37 Nux, nag sephausꝏ̄og wunnaumonaoh kah wuttaunꝏ̄woh Mattannittꝏ̄h.
106.38 Kah soksquaheaog nah mo woskhuwanegeh, ꝏ̄sqheonganꝏ̄ wunnechanꝏ̄oh kah wuttaunꝏ̄oh: n$nag maghettiche en nunneuhkontunkanu Manittꝏ̄moh Canaan, kah ohke nishketeauun nashpe wsqueheonk.
106.39 Yeu wuttin nisketeauunneau nehenwonche wutanakausuonganꝏ̄oash: onk mamussuog wutch nehenwonche wunnatwontamꝏ̄ongánoóash.
106.40 Newajeh Jehovah ummusquantamꝏ̄onk ayeuuhkonittue nashqunna nashpe ummissinninnumoh: newajeh ohquontaog nehenwonche wutahtoonk
106.41 Onk noh ummagunoh ut wunnutcheganoout penuwohteaog: kah nag sekeneauuncheg nah wunanaunouh.
106.42 Kah ummatwomꝏ̄uh woskehukquog: onk agwappeheoog nag wunnutcheganꝏ̄wout.
106.43 Mꝏ̄cheket uppohquohwhunoh nahoh: qut ummꝏ̄mꝏ̄sqheouh nashpe ukkinnꝏ̄nittuonganꝏ̄: kah nꝏ̄chumweheoog newutche ummatcheseonganꝏ̄.
106.44 Qut ukkitteamonteanumoh ut wutonkapunnaoont, nꝏ̄tog ummauonganꝏ̄.
106.45 Onk mehquoantam ꝏ̄nꝏ̄waonk wutche naghog, kah auskoiantam neaunummonakish monanéteaonganash.
106.46 Kah wutayimauoh ukkitteamonteanummonaout nag wame masinohteacheg.
106.47 Wadchanean woi Jehovah num$Manittꝏ̄mun, kah mómounninnean wutch kenugke penuwohteaut, onk woh kuttabuttantamauunnumun ut wunneetupanatamwe kꝏ̄wesuonganit kah weekontamꝏ̄wontamunat kuttabuttantamonteaonk.
106.48 Wunnanumunaj Jehovah um-Manittꝏ̄moh Israel wutch machemohtag onk yean machemohtag: kah wame missinninnuog nꝏ̄wahettich Amen, waeenomók Jehovah.
107.1 Tabuttantamok Jehovah, newutche noh wunneetou, newutche ummonaneteaonk michemohteau.
107.2 Nag pohquohwhunoncheh Jehovah ne nꝏ̄wahettich: uttiyeuh pohquohwhunumpuh wutch wunnutcheganit matwau.
107.3 Kah n$nah ummagkinuh wutche wutohtimoneát, wutche wutchepwoáyeu, kah wutch wutchesúau kah wutch nannummau, kah wutch sôanaiyeu.
107.4 Wâônuog ut touohkomuk matta máanóg: wanne miskaumꝏ̄og otan ꝏ̄tohkónneaôont.
107.5 Kadtupwéhettit, kah konkuhtꝏ̄nohettit: ukketeahogkôunnꝏ̄oh sôunumwoh ut wuhhogkaóut.
107.6 Neit mauunnitteauwaog Jehovah wutche wuttammehpunnaonganꝏ̄: onk nah uppohquohwhunoh wutch ꝏ̄taméhpunnaonganꝏ̄out.
107.7 Kah wussagkompaganuh en sampwe mayut: onk woh nag aúog ꝏ̄tanit toh woh wodohkéhettit.
107.8 Woi waeenomáhettit Jehovahnoh, wutche ꝏ̄neetowonk: kah wutch monchanatamwe anakaúsuongash en woskeetompaog wunnaumónaóut.
107.9 Newutche tápheau kodtántamwe keteahogkôunoh: kah tâpupwúhheau kodtuppꝏ̄wu keteahogkôunoh wanégik.
107.10 Neg apitcheg pohkenaouut, kah wutonkauhtomut nuppꝏ̄onk: tohtogkupséhettit onkapunnaonganit, kah mꝏ̄óhshogwohtogwash.
107.11 Newutche ayeukóntamwog wuttinnꝏ̄wáongash God: kah mamánauwontamwog ukkinnꝏ̄nuwáonk quanunkquappit.
107.12 Newajeh ayig hohpómau metah nashpe anakausuonk: nag kepsháog, onk matta howane aninnumunkꝏ̄og.
107.13 Neit mauunnitteauáog Jehovah ut ꝏ̄tamehpunnonnaóont: kah uppohquóhwhunoh nahog wutch ꝏ̄taméhpunónaôout.
107.14 Wussohhꝏ̄wunoh wutch pohkenaooúut, kah wutch wutonkaóhtomut nuppꝏ̄onk: kah poskishadtau wuttohtogkuppissuonganóash.
107.15 Woi wosketompaog waeenomahettit Jehovah wutche ꝏ̄neetowonk: kah wutche um̃onchanatamwananakausuongash ut wosketompaog wunneechanꝏ̄wout.
107.16 Newutche pokshadtaúop wompûhshogque kuppuhhoúnash: kah póhquetahham mꝏ̄óhshogque neepatúhquonkash.
107.17 Mattammagwog onkapunnáog newutche uppanneseonganoash, kah ummatcheseonganash.
107.18 Ukketeahogkôunꝏ̄oh ôhquánittamwoh nish noh unummeechumogkod: onk pasꝏ̄sukkómwog ꝏ̄squoantamash nuppꝏ̄onk.
107.19 Neit mauunitteauâog Jehovah wadtamehpunáhettit: uppohquohwhunoh wutch ꝏ̄tamehpunanaóont.
107.20 Annꝏ̄nau wuttinnꝏ̄waonguh, onk nah wunneetskeheuh: kah uppohquohwhunoh wutch uppaguaninneaôont.
107.21 Woi wosketompaog waeenomáhettit Jehovah wutche ꝏ̄nene`hhuwáonk, kah wutche ummonchanatamwe anakausuongash ut wosketompáog wunneechanꝏ̄woont.
107.22 Kah nag maghettich tabuttantamwae magꝏ̄ongash kah muskauánatamwe, wahteauwahuwáhettich wutanakausuongash.
107.23 Nag áoncheg kehtahhannit, ut kuhtꝏ̄nogquehtu: wutanakausuonganꝏ̄ ohtag nuppekontu.
107.24 Yeug naumwog wutanakausuonganash Jehovah, ummonchanatamꝏ̄wongash ut mꝏ̄náiyeuut.
107.25 Newutche anꝏ̄teamꝏ̄, kah ayim mishshetahshin: noh tohshinont tukkꝏ̄oh.
107.26 Nag tahshéog en kesukqut: kah wômussúog en mꝏ̄náiyeuut: keteahogkôunꝏ̄oh mohtupaéoh nashpe wuttaméhpunáonk.
107.27 Kehkepshaog, kah kehkeétukquommog onatuh kogkeissippamou: kah wôwohquiànumꝏ̄og.
107.28 Neit mauunnitteauwaog Jehovah wadtamehpunáhettit: kah nah wussohhꝏ̄wunoh wutch ꝏ̄tamehpunnaonganꝏ̄ôut.
107.29 Aippanehteau mishittashineuh neit tuhkꝏ̄óg mánunappûog.
107.30 Neit weekontamwog newutche mánunappuog: nemehkuh uppâsꝏ̄oh ne ohke kodtantaminit.
107.31 Woi wosketompaog waeenomáhettit Jehovah wutche ꝏ̄netꝏ̄onk: kah wutche ummonchanatamwanakausuongash ut wosketompaog wunnaumonnaont.
107.32 Nag misheheahettich ut ummukkinneonganꝏ̄wout missinninnùog, kah waasumahettich ut ummukkinneonganꝏ̄óut nanaánuacheg.
107.33 Osꝏ̄wunum sépuash ut touohkomuk, ôsꝏ̄wunum tohkékomuash en nunnabohteaóuut.
107.34 Mahmusségik ohkée ahquékin: newutche ummatcheetowonganꝏ̄ neg noh wadohkitcheg.
107.35 Touohkomuk quinnuppinnum en nuppeyeuꝏ̄ut: kah nanabohteáagish tohkékomwúhteau.
107.36 Kah na ꝏ̄tohkéheun kodtupwunutcheh, onk woh ququashwehtamwog ayeuongane otánat.
107.37 Onk woh ohkehteaog ohteuhkónash, kah woh ohkehteáog weenominneohtekonash woh adtnegik mꝏ̄cheke meechummúꝏ̄onk.
107.38 Kah nah ꝏ̄nânumoh, onk nag monáog; kah matta unnánumaou wunnétasseumoh ohguhségig.
107.39 Wonk, ohguhshéóog kah nꝏ̄chumwehêoog nashpe woskehettúonk, ꝏ̄tammepunnaonganꝏ̄, kah auwohkontánumóonk.
107.40 Wussóhkanumauau ôhquanittuonk sontimoh: kah wauwónheuh ut touohkomuk uttoh mo adt mánꝏ̄k.
107.41 Qut onch qunuhquoshau matchekuoh wutch wuttammehpunnaonganash: kah wutayimauoh weetu mishôénat onatuh flokut.
107.42 Sampweusseaenuog pish wunnaumunneau, kah pish weekontamwog: kah wame matcheseonganog pish kupputtꝏ̄naéog.
107.43 Howan waantog kah yeushog káhkinneâsit: nag pish wahtamwog ukkitteamonteánitteae ꝏ̄womoausuonk Jehovah.
108.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David.
108.1 WOi Manit nuttah menuhkohteau: pish nukketꝏ̄homom, kah kꝏ̄woeenomush, nashpe nussohsumóonk.
108.2 Tꝏ̄hkish psaltery kah harp: nunnómpoáeu tꝏ̄hkem.
108.3 Kꝏ̄waweenomush, woi Jehovah, ut kenugke missinninnúhtu: kah kuttinnꝏ̄homoush tabuttantamꝏ̄ongash ut kenugke wutohtimóneat.
108.4 Newutche kummonáneteaonk missi ongkouwe kesukqut: kah kꝏ̄nomwaonk mussisshin ut mahtoksqut.
108.5 Anuunkqussehetteash, woi Manit, kesukquash: kah kussohsumòonk waábe ohtaj onk wame ne ohke.
108.6 Noh womónat woh pohquohwhunau: kuttinohkou wadchanukquttei, kah nampꝏ̄hamah.
108.7 God nꝏ̄wop ut ꝏ̄neetupanatamꝏ̄onganit: pish nꝏ̄weekontám, pish nutchippun Sechem: kah nukquogquádhum ꝏ̄nôuhkôi Succoth.
108.8 Gilead nuttaihe, Manasseh nuttaihe, kah Ephraim ummenuhkesuonk nuppuhkuk: Judah noh ayik nuttinnaumatuonk.
108.9 Moab nukkutshahkukquom, nutánuwôohteam nummokis Edom, nummuskouanatamꝏ̄won Philistiansog.
108.10 Howan pasꝏ̄queh menuhke ꝏ̄tanat? howan sagkompáginit en Edom?
108.11 Sun~ummatta ken woi Manit, noh sôhwhókônukqueógkup? kah sun~um̃atta ken woi God kꝏ̄weechaiómun nutayeuhkoñanónut?
108.12 Aninaumaiinnean wutch wuttammepunnónat: newutche tahnꝏ̄cheyeuꝏ̄ wutaninnôsuonk wosketomp.
108.13 Nashpeu God pish nummenuhkesénan, newutche noh pish tahtahskúshkoauont kummatwómunnonuh.
109.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ukketoohomaonk} David.
109.1 Ahque netashúash, woi Manit, ken wâussumun.
109.2 Newutche wuttꝏ̄nꝏ̄ matchetowog, kah wuttꝏ̄nꝏ̄ asꝏ̄keaodteaumꝏ̄og woshweemꝏ̄, ayeuuhkone neen nuttinunkquog ayeuuhkone nen nashpe pannꝏ̄wae meenan.
109.3 Kah nukquinupuhkongquog nashpe sekeneadtue kuttꝏ̄wongash: kah nutayeuquog tahnꝏ̄che.
109.4 Newutche nꝏ̄womoausuonk, onk nag nummatwomog: qut neen nuppeantam.
109.5 Kah nag nutunkquatunkquog máchuk wutche wanegik, kah sekeneáadtuonk wutch nꝏ̄womoausuonk.
109.6 Anuwe pon matcheetowaenu ut nagum, kah Satan neepaitch ut wuttinohkôunit.
109.7 Wussumit, wussumunaj nuppunnat: kah uppeantamoonk matcheseongannutch.
109.8 Ukkesukkodtumash ogguhsenꝏ̄utch; onkatuk neemunutch wuttanohsuonk.
109.9 Wunnechanoh mo wutꝏ̄shunnéitch kah ummittamwussoh sekousquaunitch.
109.10 Wunneechanꝏ̄oh nagwutteaeu nanwaihettich kah weenshaunitch, natinnehamꝏ̄hettich uppetukqunnunkanꝏ̄ wonk ut touwe ayeuonganehtu.
109.11 Woskehuwaenin amaunich wame wutahtauonk: kah penuwot matchehtaunitch wutanakausuonk.
109.12 Ahque howan monanumonch: kah ahque howan kitteamonteanumonch wuttouaesumoh wunneechanꝏ̄oh.
109.13 Wutontseonk tummetahhamunaj ne nahohtôohtag pometeonk, ꝏ̄weseuonkanꝏ̄ jishkhamunaj.
109.14 Ummatcheseongash ꝏ̄shoh mehquantamunaj ut anaquabit Jehovah: kah ummatcheseonk ohkasoh ahque jishkhomunaj
109.15 Nish nagwutteohtaj anaquabit Jehovah, onk woh tummehtham wàánumaonganꝏ̄ wutch ohkekontu.
109.16 Newutche matta mehquoantamop monánekon, qut woskeheau matchekuoh, kah quenáhukqunutche, onk woh nushonat pohqutteahonutcheh.
109.17 Neanꝏ̄womontog ummatchenáneteaonk, neneh peyaaunukqutch: neane matta tápeneaumꝏ̄g wunaneteaonk, nene nôꝏ̄sukkongqutch.
109.18 Neane hogqut matchenaneteaonk onatuh hogkꝏ̄onganit: nein peyaaunukqutch ut wunnogkussit onatuh nippeit, kah ogqunneungquodtich pummeit ut wuskonut.
109.19 Tatupontaj wuthogkꝏ̄onganit neagqut: kah upputtugquobis ne padtukquobussit nagwutteaeu.
109.20 Yeu wutonkquatunkanehettich nummatwomog wutch Jehovahut: kah neg machenóncheg ayeuuhkone nuketeahogkou[]noh.
109.21 Qut usseansheh woi Jehovah Manit, newutche kꝏ̄wesuonk: newutche kummonanteaonk wunnegin: pohquohwusseh.
109.22 Newutche nummatchek kah nukquenahik, kah nuttah nꝏ̄chumwetahwau nuttinnomhogkat.
109.23 Nutamaim onatuh onkohohteau aumaitcheh: nuppâpamunkônit onatuh quaquequéshont.
109.24 Nukkuttukquog nꝏ̄chumwesuog nashpe matmeetsein: kah nꝏ̄weyaus wannehteau wunnogkꝏ̄onk.
109.25 Nag nukkekomukuppanneg: moneaihettit, nunnukkukquosháog.
109.26 Naninnumah woi Jehovah num-Manittꝏ̄m, unnꝏ̄wadchaneh neaunag kummonaneteaonk.
109.27 Onk woh nag wahteauog yeu kenutcheg: ken Jehovah kutussenap.
109.28 Matchenánitteahettich, qut ken wunnanumiteash: nag neepaahettit akodjhettich, qut kittinneum muskouantaj.
109.29 Nummatwomog hogquehettich akodchuonk: kah hogquehettich nehenwonche wunnanwayeuonganꝏ̄ onatuh hogkꝏ̄onganit.
109.30 Nummishuwaussum Jehovah ut nuttꝏ̄nut: nux nꝏ̄wawussum ut kenugku monacheg.
109.31 Newutche pish neepau wuttinohkôunit matcheku: ꝏ̄wadchanonat wutch neh waussumónutche ukketeahogkôunoh.
110.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David.
110.1 Manit unnau num-Manittꝏ̄moh, apsh nuttinohkounit, nô pajeh nutayéuonaonk kummatwomog, kuttappannehtuonk.
110.2 Jéhovah pish anꝏ̄nau kummenuhkesue pogkomunk wutch Sion: nanaunh ut nôeu kummatwomut.
110.3 Kummissinninnumog pish wuttinanatamunneáu, ne kesukok menuhkesean, ut ꝏ̄neetuongane wunneetupanatamꝏ̄onganit wutch nompoae oontomukout kutahto kꝏ̄skenue neechipog.
110.4 Jehovah chadchekeyeuop, kah matta pish aiuskoianatamꝏ̄, ken sephausuen micheme, netatup ꝏ̄nohtoonk Melchizedék.
110.5 Manit ut kuttinnohkounit pish pannuppetahwhau kétassꝏ̄timwoh musquantog.
110.6 Noh pish wussittum ut kenugke penuwohteaut, pish mꝏ̄chekeheau nuppꝏ̄emuhhogkuh: pish nꝏ̄chumwehtham[.] uppuhkukꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash monatash wutohtimoneash.
110.7 Pish wuttattam ut sepuemesut ut mayut: newajeh pish tohshinúk uppuhkuk.
111.1 Waeenomok Jéhovah: nowoweenom Jehovah nashpe mamusse nuttahhut, ummukkinneonganit sampwesitcheg, kah ut moeonganit.
111.2 Wutanakáusuongash Jehovah missiyeuash: wunnatinnehamunaoash neg wame weekontogig.
111.3 Wutanakausuonk quttianatamun kah sohsumꝏ̄mꝏ̄: kah wussampweusseonk michemohteau.
111.4 Ummonchanatamwu anakausuongash mehquontamwáhuwau: Jehovah kitteamonteanitteau kah numwohtau kitteamonteanitteaonk.
111.5 Assamau neh quoshhukqutcheh: nagwutteaeu mehquantam ꝏ̄nꝏ̄waonk.
111.6 Nahtináu ummissinniñumoh ummenuhkanakausuongash, onk woh wuttinnumauoh wutahtauonganꝏ̄ penuwohteaog.
111.7 Wunnutchegane anakausuongash, wunnomwayeuonk kah wussittumꝏ̄onk: wame wuttinnꝏ̄waongash wunnamuhkuteyeuꝏ̄ash.
111.8 Menuhkohtaash micheme kah micheme: wunnomwayeue kah sampweusseae kesteauunash.
111.9 Annꝏ̄nau mánoúwhuttuonguh en ummissinninnumut, noh kinnꝏ̄nau ꝏ̄nꝏ̄wáonguh micheme: wunneétupanatamwu, kah quttianatamwu ꝏ̄wesuonk.
111.10 Qushauonk Jehovah neit kutchishin waantamoonk: wunne wahwahtamwog neg ne asecheg: waeenomaonk michemohteau.
112.1 Waeenomꝏ̄k Jehovah. wunnanumau wosketomp noh quoshont Jehovah, mishe tapinneog wuttinnꝏ̄waongash.
112.2 Wuskannemunnéoh pish matikkenwoh ut ohkit: uppométuonkanꝏ̄ sampwesitcheg pish ꝏ̄nanumꝏ̄og.
112.3 Ahtoonk kah weenaieetuonk pish ohteau weekit, kah wussampweusseonk michemohteau.
112.4 Sampwesecheg waabetunkquog wequai, wutch pohkenaouut: noh womoausu, numwohteau kitteamonteanitteaonk, kah sampweussu.
112.5 Wunneetou wunnenehuau, kah namohkaaihhuau: wunnohtau wuttinniyeuongash nashpe waantamꝏ̄onk.
112.6 Wunnámuhkut matta pish ontashau micheme: sampweussecheg micheme, pish waanumaog.
112.7 Matta quehtamꝏ̄ mataunchemꝏ̄kaongash wuttah menuhketeauun pabahtanumont Jehovah$noh.
112.8 Wuttah menehkteteauun matta pish wabesu: nô pajeh wunnaumunat ukkodtantamꝏ̄onk en ummatwomut.
112.9 Wunnenehhuop, aninnumauup matchekuoh, wussampweusseonk michemohteau wutáskonoh pish tahshinouh nashpe quttianittuonk.
112.10 Matchetowog wunnaumunneau, kah neauanatamwog, nunnukkuttꝏ̄ham, kah mohtupaeu, ukkodtantamꝏ̄onk matchetou pish awakompanaumꝏ̄.
113.1 Waeenomꝏ̄k Jehóvah: waeenomꝏ̄k woi kenaau wuttinneumoh Jehovah, waéenotumꝏ̄k ꝏ̄wesuonk Jehovah.
113.2 Wunnantamunach ꝏ̄wesuonk Jehovah, yeu wutch onk yean micheme.
113.3 Wajeh pashpishont nôpajeh waiont ꝏ̄wesuonk Jehovah woh waeenotumun.
113.4 Jehovah ánuunkquapputam wame wutohtimóneash, kah wussohsumóonk onkouwe kesukquéhtu.
113.5 Howan agqunneongqussit Jehovah kum-Manittꝏ̄munnonut, noh quanunkquappit.
113.6 Noh ohhohpáheont wuhhogkuh naumunat nish kesukqut kah ohkeit.
113.7 Omohkinau matchékuoh wutch puppissiyeuut, kah tohshinau quenáhukqunnutcheh wutch annohkéit.
113.8 Onk woh weetappeheuh sontimátu, wussontimaúmꝏ̄oh ummissinninnumoh.
113.9 Mittamwossis mehchéit wutáyimauoh nánauunnumun weetu; kah muskouantamwu okásuoh mukkiésog: waeenomꝏ̄k Jehovah.
114.1 Israel sohhomwúhhettit wutch Egypt, week Jakob wutch missinninnúut penꝏ̄wontꝏ̄ácheg.
114.2 Judahhoh wussanctuariumhoh: Israeloh wunnánumóonk.
114.3 Kehtoh nag, onk wussemop, Jordon quihchiphouómꝏ̄p.
114.4 Wadchuash quéhqueshóbash onatuh wushkoshimwemésit, kah wadchuwémesash ogqueneungqutash lambsut.
114.5 Toh kuttinnai, woi ken kehtoh waj wussemwean: ken Jordan quahchippúhhꝏ̄w[á]án?
114.6 Kenaau wadchúog quehqueshaóg onatuh wuskoshimwemésit: kenaau wadchuwemesog onatuh lambsut?
114.7 Nunnukshash ken ohke ut anaquabit God, ut anaquabit um-Manittꝏ̄moh Jakob.
114.8 Noh qunnuppenum qussuk ohtóbohtáe nippe, sogguhtonkanompusk ut tohkekommuꝏ̄.
115.1 Matta neenaan, woi Jehovah, matta neenaan aninnumaiinnean waeenomóonk; qut kꝏ̄wesuonk sohsumꝏ̄ontamunach, newutche kummonaneteaonk kah kꝏ̄nomwâyeuonk.
115.2 Tohwutch woh pénuwot unnꝏ̄wadt, yeuyeu uttiyeu um-Manittꝏ̄mꝏ̄oh?
115.3 Qut kum-Manittꝏ̄mun ut kesukquehtu: mahche usseu nish noh kodt[a]ntamun.
115.4 Wuttinnukontunkanu Manittꝏ̄mꝏ̄oh silvertùꝏ̄woh kah goldeúꝏ̄woh: wutanakausuonganꝏ̄ wunnutcheganꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash wosketompaog.
115.5 Nag wuttꝏ̄núog, qut matta ketꝏ̄hkauꝏ̄og wuskesukꝏ̄og, qut matta naumꝏ̄og.
115.6 Nag wehtauogꝏ̄og, qut matta nꝏ̄tamꝏ̄og, wutchanuog, qut matta munnóntatteaoúog.
115.7 Wunnutcheganúog, qut matta mussúnnumꝏ̄og: wusseetuog, qut mat pomushauóog assa mat ketꝏ̄hkauóog ut ukquttunkanouwóut.
115.8 Neg kezheoncheg wutógqunneunkqussinneáoh: kah nish noh pasuk noh nah pabahtanumont.
115.9 Woi ken Israel pabahtanum Jehovah: noh wutannohsueneumꝏ̄oh kah wutogqunneganꝏ̄oh.
115.10 Woi week Aaron pabahtánum Jehovah, noh wutannohsuenúmꝏ̄oh kah wutogqunnéganꝏ̄oh.
115.11 Kenaau quashógish Jehovah, pabahtanumok Jehovah: kah nnah wutannohsuenúmꝏ̄oh, kah wutogqunnéganꝏ̄oh.
115.12 Jehovah kummomehquánumugqun, kꝏ̄nanumugqun, wunnánittam weekuwóash Israel: wunnanittam week Aaron.
115.13 Nah wunnánumou quoshánutcheh Jehovah: mátekénutche kah papéississinitcheh.
115.14 Jehovah pish náno kumishhukou kah náno: kenaau kah keneechânuwóog.
115.15 Kenaau kꝏ̄na[n]umugkou Jehovah, noh ayikup kesuk kah muttaok.
115.16 Kesuk nux kesukquash wuttaihe Jehovah: qut ohket wuttinnunnumaun wunnaumonauh wosketompaog.
115.17 Nuppꝏ̄og matta waeenomauꝏ̄og Jehovah; asa mat neg wómussitcheg in chequnapinneat.
115.18 Qut neenawun nꝏ̄wáwussumomun Jehovah yeu wutche, onk yean micheme waeenomꝏ̄k Jehovah.
116.1 NOOwomon Jehovah, newutche nꝏ̄tamup nꝏ̄wadtauatonkqussuépeantamꝏ̄ongash.
116.2 Newutche nutachꝏ̄sittuongúp, newajeh weequetumauog tohsohke pomantam.
116.3 Onkquommomꝏ̄e nuppꝏ̄onk nꝏ̄wéenuhkunk, chepiohkomukque onkapunnaongash nuttohqunukqunash, nummiskom wuttamehpunnáonk kah onkquommomꝏ̄onk
116.4 Néit nꝏ̄weehquetumun ꝏ̄wesuonk Jehovah: woi Jehovah kenanampassumush pohquawhus nukketeahogkou.
116.5 Kitteamonteanitteau Jehovah, kah sampweussu nux, kum-Manittꝏ̄mun monaneteau.
116.6 Jehovah wadchanau pasukqunnúꝏ̄uk wuttah, nuttaiukquonkhetteap, onk nuttannumungup.
116.7 Qushkish en kutanwossinnꝏ̄onganit woi nukketeahogkou: newutche Jehovah nummishonkquatonkup.
116.8 Newutch kuppohquohwhun nukketeahogkou wutch nuppunnat, nuskesukquash wutch mussuppegwunehtu, kah nusseetash wutch nꝏ̄nequssununnát.
116.9 Pish nuppompomusham anaquabit Jehovah: ohkeit adt pomantamuk.
116.10 Nꝏ̄namptamup, newajeh kuttꝏ̄wóp, nummishe onkuppunap.
116.11 Mꝏ̄mꝏ̄skupunnaon nussip, wame wosketompaog papannꝏ̄waog.
116.12 Chaguas woh anummauog Jehovah, wutch wame nꝏ̄nenéhukꝏ̄ongash?
116.13 Pish nemunnum wadchanittue wuttattamwaitch, kah nꝏ̄weehquetum ꝏ̄wesuonk Jehovah.
116.14 Nutôadtuhkau Jehovah nukquashaumaongash, yeuyeu anaquabenit wame ummissinninnumoh.
116.15 Wunnuppꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ ꝏ̄neetupanatamꝏ̄moh mishôadtu ut anaquabit Jehovah.
116.16 Woi Lord, neen wummamuhkut kittinneum. neen kittinneum, wunnaumonuh mittamwossisse kittinneum, kutompinnum nukkinnepissuongash.
116.17 Kittinnummaush tabuttantamwae sephausuongash, onk nꝏ̄weequetum ꝏ̄wesuonk Jehovah.
116.18 Nutôadtuhkau Jehovah nukquoshaumaongash, yeuyeu anaquabenit wame ummissinninnumoh.
116.19 Chippinneutunkanit weekit Jehovah: ut nóeu ken woi Jerusalem. waeenomꝏ̄k Jehovah.
117.1 WAeenomꝏ̄k, Jehovah wame kenaau wutohtimoneunk: waenomꝏ̄k kenaau wame missinninnuog.
117.2 Newutche ummonáneteae womoausuonk missi en kuhhogkan[ó]nut, kah wunnomwaeonk Jehovah michemohteau, Waeenomꝏ̄k Jehovah.
118.1 WOi tabattantamok Jehovah newutche wunneetou, newutche ummonaneteaonk michemohteau.
118.2 Israel yeuyeu nꝏ̄waj ummonaneteaonk michemohteau.
118.3 Week Aaron yeuyeu nꝏ̄waj, ummonaneteaonk michemohteau.
118.4 Neg quoshoncheg Jehovah yeuyeu nꝏ̄wahettich ummonaneteaonk michemohteau
118.5 Nꝏ̄weehquetumaomp Jehovah wadtamehpuuáon, Jehovah nampꝏ̄hamungkup, kah nupponuk pabahchayeuonganit.
118.6 Jehovah neechꝏ̄h, matta nꝏ̄wabesu toh woh anhit wosketomp?
118.7 Jehovah nunnontamunk weeche neg weechꝏ̄humukqueaneg; newajeh pish naum nukkodtantamoonk, ut neg sekenaitcheg.
118.8 Ayn wunnegik pabahtanumon Jehovah onk pabahtanumonat wosketomp.
118.9 Ayn wunnegik pabahtanumon Jehovah, onk pabahtanumonat sontimóog.
118.10 Wame wutahtimóneash nukquinnuppuhkongquog, qut ut ꝏ̄wesuonganit Jehovah, nag nuppaguanoog.
118.11 Nag nꝏ̄wéenuhkongquog, nux, nꝏ̄weenuhkongquog, qut ut ꝏ̄weesuonganit Jehovah nag nuppaguanoog.
118.12 Nag nukquinnuppuhkongquog onatuh aohkéaumꝏ̄ussit: nag óntahwhóog onatuh nꝏ̄nꝏ̄hsipashqunnaumuk kóussog, newutche ut ꝏ̄wesuonganit Jehovah nag nuppaguanoog.
118.13 Kukkussónkkomeh woh nuttin penshonát: qut Jehovah nuttannumungkup.
118.14 Jehovah nummenuhkesuonk kah nukkuttꝏ̄homwaonk, kah noh nꝏ̄wadchanitteaonganun.
118.15 Wâdtauatonkqussue muskouanatamꝏ̄onk, kah wadchanittúonk, ut weekit sampwéseaen, wuttinnohkou Jehováh ut menuhkeusseu.
118.16 Wuttinnohkou Jehovah spunnumun: wuttinnohkou Jehovah menuhkeussémꝏ̄.
118.17 Matta pish nunnuppꝏ̄, qut pish nuppomantam, kah pish nꝏ̄wahteauwahuwam wutanakausuongash Jehovah.
118.18 Jehovah nummishe nâsámakouhuk, qut matta magou nuhhog en nuppunnat.
118.19 Wôhshinnumah sampweusseongane squoantamash onk pish nuppetutteaontamun kah nꝏ̄woweenom Jehovah.
118.20 Kꝏ̄waeenomsh, newutche kenꝏ̄tah, kah ken nꝏ̄wadchanitteaonganun.
118.21 Kꝏ̄waeenomsh, newutche kenꝏ̄tah, kah ken nꝏ̄wadchanitteauonganun.
118.22 Qussuk weeketeaenuog mat tapeneaumohetteg, ne adnahshik negonahtag qussuk.
118.23 Yeu wutusseonk Jéhovah, kah monchanatamweyeuꝏ̄ ut nuskesukqunnonut.
118.24 Yeu kesukod Jehovah kesteunkup, nꝏ̄wekontamꝏ̄ontamunnan kah nummuskouanatamꝏ̄ontamunnan.
118.25 Yeuyéu wadchaneh kꝏ̄wehquetumoush woi Jehovah, woi Jehovah kꝏ̄weehquétumoush, aninnumah nꝏ̄nesenat.
118.26 Wunnanumau noh paont, ꝏ̄wesuonganit Jehovah; kꝏ̄nanumunumunnonup wutch weekit Jehovah.
118.27 Jéhováh noh Manit, kuhkꝏ̄tomungqueog wequai, tohkuppunauꝏ̄k sephausuonk ut wutaskonit Altar.
118.28 Ken num-Manittꝏ̄m, kꝏ̄waeenomsh, num-Manittꝏ̄m, kuttahshinish.
118.29 Woi tabuttantamok Jehovah, newutche wuñeetou, newutche ummonaneteaonk michemohteau.
119.1 WUnnaánumog pannuppe pahkositcheg ut mayut, neg pomshacheg wuttinnaumatuonganit Jehovah.
119.2 Wunnanumoóg nag nanaáitunkig ꝏ̄wauwaongash: kah néh natinneohukqutche nashpe mamusse wuttah.
119.3 Nag wonk matta matcheseog: auog ummayut.
119.4 Kutussumunnonup, nánaaihteauꝏ̄k nuttinnaumatuongash menuhkeu.
119.5 Woi nummayash sampwuhteaumuk, nanawehteáuunat kukkuhkꝏ̄waongash.
119.6 Neit pish matta nutakodchu, quttiántamon wame kuttinnꝏ̄waongash.
119.7 Kꝏ̄wáeenomsh nahpe sampwutteaheáonk: mahche netuhtaon kussampwewussittumꝏ̄ongash.
119.8 Nen nanaáihteoh kukkuhkꝏ̄waongash: ahque papaquannu ohquanumeh.
119.9 Uttoh woh wuttin wusken pahketeauun ummayash: nashpe nunnukqussit neaunag kukkuttꝏ̄onk.
119.10 Nashpe mamusse nuttah kenatinne[a]whush: ahue wáónittei wutche kuttinnꝏ̄waonganit.
119.11 Kuttinnꝏ̄waonk nutadtahtauun ut nuttahut, onk woh matta kummatchenehenno.
119.12 Kꝏ̄nanumit ken Jehovah: kuhkꝏ̄tumah kukkuhkꝏ̄waongásh.
119.13 Nashpe mussissetꝏ̄nash nꝏ̄wahteauwahuwam wame kuttꝏ̄ne wussittumꝏ̄ongásh.
119.14 Nꝏ̄weekontamup ut kꝏ̄wauwaongáne mayut, neaudtashik wame weenaieetuongash.
119.15 Nunnatwoantam ut kuttinnꝏ̄waonganit, kah nanaomputtam kummayash,
119.16 Nuttapeneamwah nuhhog kukkuhkꝏ̄waonganit mátta nꝏ̄wananâtamꝏ̄ kuttinnꝏ̄waonk.
119.17 Mishonkquatau kittinninneum, onk woh nuppomantam kah woh nanaaihteoh kuttinnꝏ̄waonk.
119.18 Wohshinish nuskesukquash onk woh nunnaum monchánátamꝏ̄wongash ut kuttinnaumatuonganit.
119.19 Nuppenꝏ̄wóhteau yeu ohket, ahque adtohtah kuttinnꝏ̄waongashh.
119.20 Nukketeahogkou pokshau nontweontamon kꝏ̄sittumꝏ̄ongash nagwutteaeu.
119.21 Kutauskomomp pittuanumutcheg matchenanumutcheg, né pañeoncheg wutch kuttinnꝏ̄waonganit.
119.22 Ontohtah kekontꝏ̄wonk kah jishanittuonk newutche nanaaihteoh kꝏ̄wauwaongash.
119.23 Sontimoog wonk appuog, kah nutayeuuhkonittue weadtimukquog qut kuttinneum natwontamup kukkuhkꝏ̄waongash.
119.24 Kꝏ̄wauwaongash wonk nûttapeneaumꝏ̄ungash, kah neg kahtimitcheg.
119.25 Nuhketeahogkou pissógquomou papissiyeúut: quaquakqheh neaúnag kuttinnꝏ̄waonk.
119.26 Nꝏ̄wateauwáhuwop nummayaassh, kah kenꝏ̄taip: kuhkꝏ̄tomah kukkuhkꝏ̄waongash.
119.27 Wahtamwaheh kittinnꝏ̄waongane mayash, onk pish nꝏ̄weogquttum kumonchanatamwe anaksausuongash.
119.28 Nukketeahogkou mohtuppáeu nashpe neuantamꝏ̄onk: menehkheh neaunag kuttinnꝏ̄waonk.
119.29 Pannepꝏ̄uneh wutch pannꝏ̄wae mayut, kah aninnumah nanouwe kittinnaumatuonk.
119.30 Nuppepénum wunnomwayeue may: kꝏ̄sittamꝏ̄ongash nupponamunash anaquabeh.
119.31 Nummenhuhkinnum kꝏ̄wauwaongash: woi Jehovah akodjheh.
119.32 Nummittumasham kuttinnꝏ̄waongane may: mishshehtauan nuttah.
119.33 Kuhkꝏ̄tumah, woi Jehovah, kukkuhkꝏ̄waongane may, onk pish nánawehteauunash na ut wohkukquoshik.
119.34 Aninnumah wohwohtamoonk neit nunnanaih kittinnaumatuonk: nux, nosweetamun nashpe mamusse nuttah.
119.35 Ayeuweh nuttônat kuttinnꝏ̄waongane may: newutche nish nuttapeneaumunash.
119.36 Nuttah ussꝏ̄utaush kꝏ̄wauwaonganit onk matta en i[á]hchewontamunát.
119.37 Qunnuppunush nuskesukquash wutche naumunat tahnꝏ̄cheyeuꝏ̄uk: kah quaquakqheh en kummayut.
119.38 Menehketeau kuttinnꝏ̄waonk kittinninneum: noh quoshhukquean.
119.39 Quinnuppenumah nukkekomitteaonk ne quohtam, newutche kꝏ̄sittumꝏ̄wongash wu[n]negenash.
119.40 Kusseh, nummishshe kodtantam kuttinnꝏ̄waongash; quaquakqheh ut kꝏ̄nomwausseonganit.
119.41 Kummonaneteaongash wonk peyauunukquttei, woi Jehovah, kꝏ̄wadchanuwaonk neaunag kukkuttꝏ̄wonk.
119.42 Neit toh woh nuttinne nampꝏ̄hamau kehkómit howan: newutche nuppâbahtantam kuttinnꝏ̄waonk.
119.43 Kah ahque papaquanne amaunsh wunnamuhkutee kuttꝏ̄onk wutch nuttꝏ̄nut; newutche nutannous ut kꝏ̄sittamꝏ̄onganit.
119.44 Nemehkuh pish nanawaheoh kittinnaumatuonk yeauyatcheh, micheme kah micheme.
119.45 Kah pish nanouwe pomusham: newutche nunnátinneahham kukkuhkꝏ̄tomuhteaongash.
119.46 Kah nuttinnꝏ̄wam kꝏ̄wauwaongash anaquabhettit ketahsꝏ̄tamwog, kah matta pish nutakodchuh.
119.47 Kah nꝏ̄wekontamwah nuhhog ut kuttinꝏ̄waonganit nish womantamónish.
119.48 Kah wonk nunnetchegash nuttashinum ken kuttinnꝏ̄waonganit nish womantamónish: kah nunnatwontam kukkuhkꝏ̄waongash.
119.49 Mehquontash kuttinnꝏ̄waonk ut kittinneumut, uttiyeu annóoshikqueáp.
119.50 Yeu nꝏ̄niyeuonk ut nutonkapunnaonganit newutche kuttinnꝏ̄waonk nukquaquakqhúk.
119.51 Pittuanumꝏ̄og mꝏ̄cheke nutahánehtunkquog: qut onch askq nunnukonoh kittinnaumatuonk.
119.52 Nummehquoantam nukkône kꝏ̄sittamꝏ̄ongash, woi Jehovah, káh nꝏ̄weekontamwah nuhhog.
119.53 Nunnukshaonk nunohkukonk, newutche matchetowog ohquânumaog kittinnaumatuonguh.
119.54 Kukkuhkꝏ̄waongash nꝏ̄ketꝏ̄hommaonganinneash ut weetuomut adt penuwohteaeomp.
119.55 Nummehquoantamup kꝏ̄wesuonk woi Jehovah nukkonaeu, onk nunnanaweh kuttinnaumatuonk.
119.56 Yeu nuttinahtauun newutche nanaéhteap kukkuhkꝏ̄tomuhteaongash.
119.57 Ken nutáhtauonk woi Jehovah, nussip, woh n[á]nauwehtauun kuttinnꝏ̄waonk.
119.58 Nanómpassum kꝏ̄womoausue nussuonk, nashpe mamusse nuttah, monanumeh neaunag kuttinnꝏ̄waonk.
119.59 Nunnatwontamup nummayassh, onk nukquinnuppinnumup nusseetash en kꝏ̄wauwaonganit.
119.60 Nukkinnuppeusséip matta nuppitchinwoeh nanauwéhteauunat kuttinuꝏ̄waongash.
119.61 Wutchippiyeuonganꝏ̄ matcheetowog nummukkꝏ̄kinnukquog: qut matta nꝏ̄wanánumoh kittinnaumatuonk.
119.62 Nôuttipukok nutomohkem woh kuttabuttantamoush, newutche sampwe kꝏ̄sittamꝏ̄wongash:
119.63 Nꝏ̄weéchaiyeumóog neg wame quoshhúkkꝏ̄aneg: onk neg nanawéhtunkeg kukkuhkꝏ̄tomuhteaongash.
119.64 Ohke woi Jehovah numwohteau kummonáneteaonk, kuhkꝏ̄tomah kukkuhkꝏ̄waongash.
119.65 Kꝏ̄nenéhheump kittinneum, woi Jehovah, neaunag kuttinnꝏ̄waonk.
119.66 Kuhkꝏ̄tomah wunnegen wussittumóouk, kah wahteauonk; newutche nꝏ̄namptamup kuttinnꝏ̄waongash.
119.67 Asquam onkapunnaan nꝏ̄wauwónip: qut yeuyeu nanauwéhteóh kuttinnꝏ̄waonk.
119.68 Ken kꝏ̄netum, kah kꝏ̄nésem: kuhkꝏ̄tomah kukkuhkꝏ̄waongash.
119.69 Pehtuanumóog nutayeuuhkone ayimunkquog pannꝏ̄wáonk; qut nanauwéhteuh kukkuhkꝏ̄tomuhteaongash nashpe mamusse nuttah.
119.70 Wuttahhꝏ̄woash wunnogkꝏ̄mꝏ̄ash onatuh pumméit; qut nuttapeneau kittinnaumatuonk.
119.71 Nꝏ̄nehkongqun nꝏ̄tamehpunaonk onk woh nunnetuhtóh kukkuhkꝏ̄waongash.
119.72 Kuttꝏ̄ne naumatuonk ne nutánue wunnenehikqun onk muttañonganogkodtash gold kah silver.
119.73 Kenutchegash nukkezhukqunapash kah nukkuhkenaihikqunapash: aninnumok wahwáhtamꝏ̄onk, onk woh nunnehtântoh kuttinnꝏ̄waongash.
119.74 Neg quoshhúkouanneg, pish weekontamwog nógquean: newutche nutannoóntam kuttinnꝏ̄waonk.
119.75 Nꝏ̄wahteoh, woi Jehovah, kꝏ̄sittamꝏ̄wongash sampwâouash: kah kutonkapúnausup wutch wunnamuhkut kꝏ̄womoausuonk.
119.76 Kꝏ̄weehquetumoush, kummonaneteáe womoausuonk taphúkquttei, neaunag kuttinnꝏ̄waonk ut kuttinneum ut.
119.77 Kuttumungke kummonaneteaonk peyaaûnukquttei onk woh nukkete[à]m: newutche kittinnaumatuonk nuttapeneam.
119.78 Pittuánumꝏ̄og akodchehettich, newutche tahnꝏ̄che nummusquanatamwe matchenetunkquog, qut pish nunnatwontam kukkuhkꝏ̄tomuhteaongash.
119.79 Yeug quashkꝏ̄unneg, quinnuppéhettich en nuhhogkat kah neg wahtunkeg kꝏ̄wauwaongash.
119.80 Mussaj nuttah ut kukkúhkꝏ̄waonganit: onk woh mat nutákodchúh.
119.81 Nukketeahogkou sauwunnum wutch kꝏ̄wadchanuwaonk, qut nutannowóntam kuttinnowaonk.
119.82 Nukesukquash sauwunnumꝏ̄mꝏ̄ash wutche kuttinnꝏ̄waonk anꝏ̄wáon, aquompak kuttápheh.
119.83 Newutche nutogqunneunkqus nônohtag wisk ut pukuttaut: onch matta nꝏ̄wanantamꝏ̄h kukkuhkꝏ̄waongash.
119.84 Tohshinash ukkesukkodtumash kittinneum? aquompak kittinhéog kꝏ̄sittumꝏ̄onk neg woskhúkqueaneg?
119.85 Pittuanumꝏ̄og wônteaog wutche neen: neg matta ánussegig neánussit kittinnaumatuonk.
119.86 Wame kuttinnꝏ̄waongash paubuhtanumukquodtash: tohnunnꝏ̄che woskehukquog, aninnumah.
119.87 Nahen nummohtupánukquog yeu ut ohkeit: qut matta nutahquoantamꝏ̄h kukkuhkꝏ̄tomuhteaongash.
119.88 Quahquáhqkheh neaunag kukkitteamonteanitteae kꝏ̄womoausuonk, nemehkuh woh nanauwehteóh kꝏ̄auwaongash ut kuttꝏ̄nut.
119.89 Micheme, woi Jehovah, kuttinnꝏ̄waonk menuhkoh[t]eau ut kesukqut.
119.90 Kussampwenéhuwaonk en pometuonganit onk yean pometuonganit: kummenuhkeéhteau ohke, onk ahteau.
119.91 Nash nagwutteohtaash yeu pajeh neaunag kukkuhkꝏ̄waongash: newutche wame kittinneumog.
119.92 Matta tapeneauwôógus kittinnaumatuonk: woh nutauwakompáneaup ut nutonkquommomꝏ̄nganit.
119.93 Matta pish nꝏ̄wananatamꝏ̄h kukkuhkꝏ̄tomuhteaongash: newutche nish nashpe kukquogquahqhenneapash.
119.94 Neen kuttaihe, wadchaneh; newutche nunnatinneáham kukkuhkꝏ̄tomuhteaongash.
119.95 Matchetowog nutaskwhonuk nunnushhukqunnaóut, qut nunnatwontam kꝏ̄wauwaongash.
119.96 Nunnanaúmup adt wohkukquoshik wame pannuppe wanegik, qut kuttinnꝏ̄waonk mishsheski.
119.97 Woi nummꝏ̄cheke womontam kenaumatuonk, ne nummissantamꝏ̄wonk quinni kesuk.
119.98 Kummꝏ̄cheke waantamwahhe onk neg nummatwomog nashpe kuttinnꝏ̄waongash: newutche nagwutteae nꝏ̄weetomukqunash.
119.99 Nummꝏ̄cheke wohwohtám onk neg wame kohkꝏ̄tomaiitcheg: newutche kꝏ̄wauwaongash nummissantamꝏ̄wongash.
119.100 Nummꝏ̄cheke wohtam o[n]k neg kutchiog: newutche nanawehteoh kukkuhkꝏ̄tomuhteaongash.
119.101 Nukqushkinnum nusseetash wutch nishnoh matchee may: onk woh nanawehteoh kuttinnꝏ̄waonk.
119.102 Matta nutamꝏ̄h wutch kꝏ̄sittamꝏ̄onganit: newutche ken kukkuhkꝏ̄tomah.
119.103 Uttoh nukkukque weekonash kuttinnꝏ̄waongash wutch nukqutchtamunat, mꝏ̄cheke weekonash onk ne hony ut nuttꝏ̄nit.
119.104 Nashpe [u]kuhkꝏ̄tomuhteaongash nꝏ̄wohwotam: newajeh nussekeneam nish noh pannꝏ̄wae may.
119.105 Kuttinꝏ̄waonk wequananteg ut nusseetut kah wequai ut nummayut.
119.106 Nutchadchekeyeuwap, kah pish nutusseh, onk woh nánawehteoh kussampwe wussittumꝏ̄wongash.
119.107 Nummꝏ̄cheke onkupunam quaquakqhe, woi Jehovah, neaunag kuttinnꝏ̄waonk.
119.108 Kꝏ̄wequetumoush tapeneash nanouwe nummagꝏ̄ongash wutch nuttꝏ̄nut, woi Jehovah, kah kuhkꝏ̄tomah kꝏ̄sittumꝏ̄waongash.
119.109 Nukketeahogkou nagwutteapu ut nunnutcheganit: onch matta nꝏ̄wannanumoh kuttinnaumatuonk.
119.110 Matchetowog nupponamunkquog appehhanoh, qut matta nuppanneoh wutch kukkuhkꝏ̄tamwehteaonganit.
119.111 Nunneemunnum kꝏ̄wauwaongash onatuh nutahtꝏ̄onganit micheme: newutche nih nꝏ̄weekontamwahukqunash ut nuttahut.
119.112 Nutahchuwunnum nuttah ussen kukkuhkꝏ̄waongash nagwutteaeu naut wohkukquoshik.
119.113 Nussekeneam tahnꝏ̄che unnantamowongash, qut kuttinnaumatuonk nꝏ̄womantam.
119.114 Ken nutassampamukquodtꝏ̄m, kah nutogqunneg; nutannowontam kuttinnowaonk.
119.115 Amaeihtaek kenaau matcheseogish: newutche neen nunnanaweehteoh wuttinnꝏ̄waongash num-Manittꝏ̄m.
119.116 Unnemenuhkinneh neaunag kuttinnꝏ̄waonk, onk woh nuppomantam: kah ahque akodchitti wutch nuttannoosuonk.
119.117 Pabahtinéh onk woh nꝏ̄wadchanit: onk nagwutteaeu nꝏ̄tꝏ̄anatam kukkuhkꝏ̄waongash.
119.118 Kutahtashkuhkauomp nag wame panneaoncheg wutch kukkuhkꝏ̄aonganit: newutche wutasꝏ̄kekodteamꝏ̄wonkanꝏ̄ pannꝏ̄wayeuonk.
119.119 Kutamaun wame matchetowog apitcheg ohkeit onatuh nishkeneunkquok: newaje womontam kꝏ̄wauwáongash.
119.120 Nꝏ̄weyaus nunnukshau wutche kukqushinꝏ̄wonk: kah nꝏ̄wabissuwontam kꝏ̄sittamꝏ̄wongash.
119.121 Nummahche ussem ꝏ̄sittumꝏ̄wonk kah sampweusseuonk: ahque poneh nummatchenehitteanat.
119.122 Pabachteau kittinneum wutch wanegik: ahque pittuanumꝏ̄og matchenehettich.
119.123 Nuskesukquash sauunumꝏ̄mꝏ̄ wutche kꝏ̄wadchanꝏ̄waonk: kah wutche kussampweusseongane kuttinnꝏ̄waonk.
119.124 Enneh kittinneum neaunag kummonaneteaonk kah kuhkꝏ̄tomah kukkuhkꝏ̄waongash.
119.125 Nen kittinneum, aninnumah wawohtamowonk: onk woh nꝏ̄wahteoh kꝏ̄wauwaongash.
119.126 Uttꝏ̄cheyeuꝏ̄ woh neadt anakausean woi Jehovah: newutche tahnꝏ̄cheteaog kittinnaumatuonk.
119.127 Newajeh ánue womantam kuttinnꝏ̄waonganash onk ne gold, nux, anue onk ne wunnegik gold.
119.128 Newajeh nꝏ̄tꝏ̄wontam wame kuttiñꝏ̄waongash papaume wame teanteaquashinash sampwayeúut: kah nussekeneam nishnoh pannowáe may.
119.129 Kꝏ̄wauwaongash monchanatamoyeuꝏ̄ash: newajeh nukketeahogkou nanawehteunk nashog.
119.130 Petutteau nꝏ̄ug kuttinnꝏ̄waongash wohsumꝏ̄mꝏ̄ash: aninnumauau wahtamꝏ̄wonk asꝏ̄tuoh.
119.131 Nꝏ̄wohshinnumup nuttꝏ̄n kah nummehmehshanómup: newutche mꝏ̄cheke nutahchewontamup kuttinnꝏ̄waongash.
119.132 Monneah, kah monanumeh: neáhennehheadt yeug womontogig kꝏ̄wesuonk.
119.133 OOnahtaash nutóntanehtuongash kuttinnꝏ̄waonganit: kah ahqueh matcheseonk nanawunitch.
119.134 Pohquawhunch wutch ꝏ̄woskhuaonganit wosketomp, nemehkuh pish nanawehtaun kukkuhkꝏ̄tomuhteaongash.
119.135 Kuskesuk wohsumwahtoush ut kittinneumut: kah kuhkꝏ̄tumah kukkuhkꝏ̄waongash.
119.136 Sepúpog wuttitchuwan nukesukqut: newutche nag matta nanawehheauóoh kittinnaumatuonk.
119.137 Kussampweussem, woi Jehovah, kah sampwiyeuash kꝏ̄sittumꝏ̄ongash.
119.138 Kꝏ̄wauwaongash nish kussinneápash sampwáyeuash: kah ahche pabuhtanumukquodtash.
119.139 Nus[-]zealum nummóhtupanukqun: newutche nummatwomog wananatamwog kuttinnꝏ̄waongash.
119.140 Kuttinnꝏ̄wáonk mꝏ̄cheke pohki: newajeh kittinneum womóntog.
119.141 Nen nuppeissis, kah nutjishanumit: onch matta nꝏ̄wananittammꝏ̄ kukkuhkꝏ̄tomúhteaongash.
119.142 Kussampweusseonk micheme sampweusseonganúꝏ̄: kah kittinnaumatuonk wunnamu[h]kuteyeúꝏ̄.
119.143 Wuttammepunáonk kah wohwohkukquiánumꝏ̄onk nukkógkaanunuk: ônch kuttinnꝏ̄waongash nuttapeneaumunash.
119.144 Kꝏ̄wauwaongane nussampweusseonk michemohteau, aninnumah wahwahtamóonk onk woh nuppomantam.
119.145 Nummau nashpe mamusse nuttah: nꝏ̄tah woi Jehovah, nanawéhteuh kukkuhkꝏ̄waongash.
119.146 Kummaúunnitteanup, wadchaneh, onk woh nunnanauwéhteuh kꝏ̄wauwaongash.
119.147 Asquam mohtompannꝏ̄g nummaup: nutannꝏ̄wontam kuttinnꝏ̄waonk.
119.148 Negonne nuskesukquash woshweemꝏ̄ onk neg askuhwh[ó]sitcheg: onk woh nunnatwontam kuttinnꝏ̄waonk.
119.149 Nꝏ̄tash nꝏ̄wadtauatongqussuonk neaunag kukkitteamonteanitteáe womoausúonk, woi Jehovah, quhquahkqhe neaunag kꝏ̄sittumꝏ̄wonk.
119.150 Nag asuhkogig woskehuwaonk nuppasꝏ̄sukkongquog: nò[ú]ssukomwog kittinnaumatuonk.
119.151 Kuppaswop woi Jehovah: kah wame kuttinnꝏ̄waongash wunnamuhkuteyeuꝏ̄ash.
119.152 Papaume kꝏ̄wauwaongash, nôadt nꝏ̄wahteaueap, kummenuhkehteanapash micheme.
119.153 Natwontash nutonkapunáonk, kah pohquahwusseh: newutche matta nꝏ̄wananumeh kenaumatuonk.
119.154 Kenꝏ̄tamwansheh, kah pohquahwusseh: quahquahqhe neaunag kuttinnꝏ̄waonk.
119.155 Wadchanittúonk wunnôussukongqun matchetou: newutche nag matta natinnehamꝏ̄og kukkuhkꝏ̄waongash.
119.156 Mogkiyeuash kukkitteamonteanitteáe monanitteaongash woi Jehovah: quahquahqhe neaunag kꝏ̄sittumꝏ̄ongash.
119.157 Mꝏ̄naog woskhukqueóneg, kah nummatwomog: qut matta nuppanneoh wutch kꝏ̄wauwaonganit.
119.158 Nunnauomp matchetowog, kah neuanatamup: newutche matta nânaaihteauóog kuttinnꝏ̄wáonk.
119.159 Natwontash uttoh nuttinne womontamun kukkuhkꝏ̄tomúhteaongash: quahuahqhe woi Jehovah, neaunag kukkitteamonteanutteáe womoausuonk.
119.160 Kuttinnꝏ̄waonk wunnamuhkuteyeúꝏ̄ wutche weske kutchissik: kah nish noh pasuk kussampwe wussittumꝏ̄ongash michemohtaash.
119.161 Santimꝏ̄og tahnꝏ̄che nꝏ̄woskehukquog: qut nuttah quttianatam kuttinnꝏ̄wáonk.
119.162 Nꝏ̄weekontam wutche kuttinnꝏ̄waonk: neane howan maskog mishe woskehteauongash.
119.163 Nussekeneam kah nutjishontam pannꝏ̄wayeuonk; qut nꝏ̄womantam kittinnaumatuonk.
119.164 Nesausuk tahshit nompe pasukkesukqut kuttabuttantamoush: newutche kussampwe wussittumꝏ̄ongash.
119.165 Mishu wunnohteáog neg womantogig kittinnaumatuonk: kah matta pish teaug wuttamhukkꝏ̄og.
119.166 Jehovah nuttannoontamup kꝏ̄wadchanuwáonk: kah nummahche ussenash kuttinnꝏ̄waongash.
119.167 Nukketeahogkou nanawehteaóup kꝏ̄wauwaongash: kah nash nummꝏ̄cheke womontamunash.
119.168 Nanawehteauop kukkuhkꝏ̄tomuhteaongash, kah kꝏ̄wauwaongash: newutche wame kummayash anaquabeh ohtaash.
119.169 Nummauonk pasꝏ̄tshaumꝏ̄utch anaquabean, woi Jehovah: áninnumah wahwahtamóonk néaunag kuttinnꝏ̄waonk.
119.170 Nꝏ̄weequetumꝏ̄onk peyaumꝏ̄utch anaquabean: pohquahwusseh neaúnag kuttinnꝏ̄wáonk.
119.171 Nussissittꝏ̄nash yeumꝏ̄ash tabuttantamꝏ̄onk: mahche kuhkꝏ̄tomauean kukkuhkꝏ̄waongash.
119.172 Neenan pish yeumꝏ̄ kuttinnꝏ̄waonk: newutche wame kittinnꝏ̄waongash sampwiyeuash.
119.173 Kenutcheg aninnumaiitch: newutche nuppepenam kukkuhkꝏ̄tomuhteaongash.
119.174 Nummꝏ̄cheke kodtantam kꝏ̄wadchanuwaonk, woi Jehovah: kah kittinnaumatuonk nuttapeneau.
119.175 Nukketeahogkou pomantaj onk pish kꝏ̄waeenomuk: kah kꝏ̄sittumꝏ̄wongash aninnumungqutteuh.
119.176 Nꝏ̄auwóin onatuh shepsut waónit, natinneah kittinneum: newutche matta nꝏ̄wannantamꝏ̄ kuttinnꝏ̄waongash.
120.0 {Hohtoesohteae ketoohomawonk}.
120.1 WAdtaméhpunaon nummauunitteaop Jehovah, onk nꝏ̄tunkup.
120.2 Pohquohwus nukketeahogkou, woi Jehovah, wutch pannꝏ̄wae mussissetꝏ̄nut, kah wutch asꝏ̄kekodteamꝏ̄e meenannúut.
120.3 Toh pish kittinne aninnumont, asa toh pish kittinhit, woi ken pannꝏ̄wáe meenan?
120.4 Masugkenuk keénu ukkôúhquodtash, weeche kꝏ̄wáe mohkóssaash.
120.5 Missi nuttammepunáonk newutche nuttinneapeyon Meshek: onk nuttaiin Kedare weetuomehtu.
120.6 Nukketeahogkou wussépe weetómuh neh sekeneaumunutcheh wunnohteáonk
120.7 Nussim wunnohteagk: qut ketꝏ̄hkaon kodtantamwog ayeu wuttuonk.
121.0 {Hohtoesohteae ketoohomaonk}.
121.1 Nuttashinum nuskesukquash en wadchuuhkontu ne wꝏ̄mꝏ̄uk nuttannumonteáonk.
121.2 Nuttannumonteáonk ꝏ̄mꝏ̄ꝏ̄ wutch Jehovah, noh ayikup kesuk kah ohke.
121.3 Kusseet matta unnantamꝏ̄ ontattaunꝏ̄it: noh nanahukquéan matta woh kogkouequâou.
121.4 Kusseh, noh nanaúnont Israeloh, matta kogkoúequau kah matta kouewu.
121.5 Jehovah kenanaunuk: Jehovah kutonkaóhtom wutch kuttinohkôunit.
121.6 Nuppâuz matta pish kussa[u]ukissukꝏ̄h kesukodáeu, asa nanepaôhshad nukkonáeu.
121.7 Jehovah kenanauunuk wutche wame matchitit, wadchanau kukketeahogkôunuh.
121.8 Jehovah nanaaihteau kuppomusháonk, kah kuppeyaonk: yeu wutche onk yean micheme.
122.0 {Hohtoesahteae ketoohomaonk} David.
122.1 NOOweekontamup ashettit, óntuh weekit Jehovah.
122.2 Nusseetunonash pish ohtóash anóme kꝏ̄squontamut, woi Jerusalem.
122.3 Jersualem unnéhtaun onatuh otanit môsogquéhtag.
122.4 Wuttauadtuongangꝏ̄ na aumꝏ̄, wutchippannꝏ̄ongash Jehovah, ꝏ̄wauwaonganꝏ̄wóut Israel: onk woh tabuttantamwog ꝏ̄wesuonk Jehovah.
122.5 Newutche nâ ohteau wussittumꝏ̄we appuonganash, appuonganash weekit David.
122.6 Peantamwansh wunnóhteáonk Jerusalem: neg womônukqueáneg wunniyeuog.
122.7 Wunnohteáonk ohtaj kittinnómeneutonganehtu, kah wunniyeuonk kittinnomekomukqut.
122.8 Wutche neematog kah weechiyeumogig: yeuyeu nussim wunnohteáonk appehtunkqush.
122.9 Newutche week Jehovah kum-Manittꝏ̄mun, nunnatinneham kꝏ̄neetuonk.
123.0 {Hohtoesohteae ketoohomaonk}.
123.1 Kuttuspunnumoush nuskesukquash: woi ken apean kesukquehtu.
123.2 Kusseh, wuttinneumunneunk nean kenompatamꝏ̄hettit wussantimaumꝏ̄uh wunnutcheg, kah wuttinneumun mittamwussis nean kenompatog wunnutcheg wussonksquomoh: netatup nuskesukqunonnash kenompamágut Jehovah num-Manittꝏ̄mun nô pajeh monanumugqunnanonut.
123.3 Monanuminnean, woi Jehovah, monanuminnean: newutche ahche numwaméechimimun nutohquánumugkꝏ̄onganun.
123.4 Nukketeahogkôunnun ahche numwameechumeu ummamánꝏ̄wantamꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ saságeneogig: kah wutóhquánumꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ pahchuanumwutcheg.
124.0 {Hohtoesohtae ukketoohomaonk} David.
124.1 Matta Jehovah nunnꝏ̄gis wutche kuhhogkanonit, yeuyeu Israel woh nꝏ̄wau.
124.2 Matta Jehovah nunnꝏ̄gis wutche kuhhogkanonit, wosketompaog waabehtunkqueog.
124.3 Neit woh nag kummisseusquónukqunnonuppanneg, ummusquantamꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ ayeuuhkonittue nashqunag wutche kenaan.
124.4 Neit woh nippeash kenuhkekongqunnan, kussehtanup nukketeahogkôunnuñonoh nukkuhkau[ó]p.
124.5 Neit pittuanumwe nuppeash nukkuhkauop nukketeahogkounoh.
124.6 Wunnanumunaj Jehovah matta magꝏ̄unat kuhhogkanonuh meetsuonganꝏ̄ ut weepittuwout.
124.7 Nukketeahogkounnun pohquohham onatuh psukses wutch ukquomphonganit noh adchont: ohpe pokshau, onk nuppohquohhamumun.
124.8 Kutanninumonteaonganun ohteau ꝏ̄wesuonganit Jehovah, noh ayigkup kesuk kah ohke.
125.0 {Hohtoesohteae ketoohomaonk}.
125.1 Neg Pabahtanumoncheg Jehovah[,] ogqunneunkqussuog wadchuut Sion, ne matta woh ontuhtano, micheme ohteau.
125.2 Onatuh wadchuash nish quanupohtagish Jerusalem, neane Jehovah quinnuppekauont ummissinninneumoh: yeu wutche, onk yean micheme.
125.3 Newutche uppogkomunkanꝏ̄ matcheetowog matta pish sepohtano wutohtꝏ̄onganꝏ̄wout sampwesecheg: ishkont sampweseaenuog summagunnumwog wunnutcheganꝏ̄woash en matcheseonganit.
125.4 Wunne énne woi Jehovah, neg waneetukeg: kah nag sampwesitcheg ut wuttahhꝏ̄wout.
125.5 Qut neg áoncheg ꝏ̄wôóngke mayꝏ̄wout Jehovah pish nah ꝏ̄weechuwunuh matcheseaenutu: qut wunnahteáonk pish ohteau Israelut.
126.0 {Hohtôesohteae ketoohomaonk}.
126.1 JEhovah, quashkunont ummissinomuh Sion; nutohgqunneunkqussimunnonup neg anukquonkeg.
126.2 Neit nuttꝏ̄nonut numwohta ahanuonk, kah neenanuunnonut ketꝏ̄homaonk: neit nag nꝏ̄waog kꝏ̄wutche penuwohteaog, Jehovah ummishanakausuwehtaoh nahog.
126.3 Jehovah kummishanakausuwehtunkqun: newaj weekontamog.
126.4 Qushkinnean wutch nummissinnaneanonut woi Jehovah onatuh kussitchuwan wutche sowunnaeu.
126.5 Neg ahketeacheg wussippegꝏ̄woash, pish kepenumwog weekontamowonk.
126.6 Nnoh sohhog kah mauug nashpeit mahshoadtik wuskannem, wunnamuhkut pish peyau weeche weekontamowonk paudtunk ꝏ̄sheavsumash.
127.0 {Hotoesohteae ketoohomaonk wutche Solomon}
127.1 IEhovah matta ayimꝏ̄g weetu, tahnꝏ̄che an[a]kausuog neg ayikeg: Jehovah mat nanawehteaꝏ̄g otan askuhwheteáenin tahnꝏ̄che askuhwhosu.
127.2 Tahnꝏ̄cheyeuꝏ̄ kutomohkenau nompoaeu, kah cheke kukkoueneau, meechinat, neuanatamꝏ̄we petukqunnunk: ne wuttinne unninnumauun neh kaenutcheh womononcheh.
127.3 Kusseh mukkiesog wutahtoonk Jehovah kah wutóontomukae meechumuonk ne wut onkquatauuonk.
127.4 Onatuh kôuhquodtash wunnutcheganit manuhkesit wosketomp, neane keneechanog woskenuean.
127.5 OOnaiyeu woskeetomp not uppetanwonit nomwapenit, matta pish akodchuog, qut pish kenꝏ̄naog mátwaoh ut squont[ā]ut.
128.0 {Hohtoesohteae ketoohomaonk}
128.1 Nish noh quoshont Jehovah ꝏ̄nanumau: noh aont ummayut.
128.2 Newutche pish kummeech kenutchegane anakausuonk: kꝏ̄wuni, kah pish kꝏ̄nenehukqun.
128.3 Kummittumwus pish ogqunneungqussu mahshemeechumik we[n]omesippog ut kishke keekit: keneechanog pish ogqunneungqussuog Olive puntukquemesit, quinnuppe ahuttashpean.
128.4 Kusseh, yeu pish unne wunnanumon noh quoshont Jehovah.
128.5 Jehovah pish kꝏ̄nanumuk wutch Sion: onk pish kenaum ꝏ̄netuonk Jerusalem n[e]sahkepomantaman.
128.6 Nux pish kenaau keneechanog onk na wunneechanꝏ̄, kah ꝏ̄nohteaonganꝏ̄ Israel
129.0 {Hohtoesohteae ketoohomaonk}.
129.1 MOOcheke nompu nummatchenehukquog wutch nꝏ̄skenuunneat, Israel woh yeuyeu nꝏ̄wau.
129.2 Mꝏ̄cheke nompu nummatchenehukquog wutch nꝏ̄skenuunneat: onch matta nussohkunkꝏ̄og.
129.3 Anaskhomwaenuog anaskhamwog ut nuppi[s]hquanit: quohquonitchagquamwog.
129.4 Jehovah sampweussu: tummetham uppemunneohtonꝏ̄óash matcheetowog.
129.5 Wame akodjhetticheh[,] kah qushkehettich, sekeneog [g] Sion.
129.6 Ogqunneungqussehettich moskehtuuk woskeche komukqut: ne ahpohtag asq waummékininnokup.
129.7 Nish nashpe tisashquaenin matta nomwohtoꝏ̄g wunnutcheg: asuh noh woshpununk sheavesash uppꝏ̄chinnauwoonnut.
129.8 Asuh matta neg noh kishke paumushacheg unnꝏ̄wauꝏ̄og, ꝏ̄naneteaonk Jehovah apehtunkꝏ̄k: kꝏ̄nanum[u]numun ut ꝏ̄wesuonganit Jehovah.
130.0 {Hohtoesohteae ketoohomank}.
130.1 Wutche mꝏ̄naiyeut kummauunnitteanup woi Jehovah.
130.2 Jehovah, nꝏ̄tash nꝏ̄wadtauatongqussuonk: kehtaúogsh ahchusittamohettich nꝏ̄wadtauatongqussue weequeumꝏ̄onk.
130.3 Tohneit Jehovah kukkinneaséan matcheseongash, woi Jehovah howa woh neepauwit?
130.4 Qut kutahquoantausúonk kutahtaum: onk woh kukqushit.
130.5 Nuppaih Jehvah nukketeahogkou pahtussu: kah ut wuttinnꝏ̄waonganit nutannoóus.
130.6 Nukketeahogkou mꝏ̄chekeu páhheau Jehovah, onk nag askuhwhósicheg nompoáeu, onk nag askuwhósitcheg nompoáeu.
130.7 Israel annoónonch Jehovah, newutche Jehovah neit ohteau monaneteaonk, kh unnohmónat ummanꝏ̄hꝏ̄waonk.
130.8 Kah noh pish Israeloh mnꝏ̄whau wutch wame ummatcheseonganꝏ̄wóut.
131.0 {Hohtoesohteae ukketoohomaonk} David.
131.1 IEhovah, matta pittuanumꝏ̄ nuttah, asa matta nuskesukquash pittuanuwómpamukquodtinnꝏ̄ash: mat nꝏ̄wéog kehteóꝏ̄ ut nuhhogkat mogagish, asa nuwôhqussumugquéanish.
131.2 Wunnamuhkut nuttinneh nuhhog, kah nummanunnh onatuh ꝏ̄chininnat mukkies wutch okasit: nukketeahogkou oatuh ꝏ̄chininneat mukkies.
131.3 Israel annoónonch Jehovah, yeu wutche, onk yean micheme.
132.0 {Hohtoesohteae ketoohomáonk}.
132.1 IEhovah mehquantash David wame wuttuhquanumꝏ̄onganit.
132.2 Chadchekemop en Jehovahut, ukquoshaumuh menuhkesu um-Manittꝏ̄moh Jakob.
132.3 Wunnamuhkut matta nupetutteoh tabernakle neekit, kah matta nusseepsinnꝏ̄ nutappinneat.
132.4 Matta nuskesukquash koiémunꝏ̄ash, naneadtaskesukquash matta supweémunꝏ̄ash.
132.5 Nô pajeh mishkomon wutayeuonk wutche Jehova, wutayeuonk wutche menuhkesu um-Manittꝏ̄moh Jakob
132.6 Kusseh, nunnꝏ̄amûnan ut Ephrata, nummiskomúnan touohkomukqu ohkeit.
132.7 Nuppetutteamun wuttabernakluehtu, nꝏ̄wowussumoun utukquensit[]tassumꝏ̄unit.
132.8 Waabish woi Jehovah, en kutanwôhsinnꝏ̄wonganit: ken kah kummenuhke arkum.
132.9 Kussephausueneumg hogquehettich nashpe wunnomausseonk kah kꝏ̄neetupanatamꝏ̄mog muskouanatamwe mishontowáhettich.
132.10 Newutche kꝏ̄tinninneum David, ahque quinuppemau wuskesuk noh saséquinadt.
132.11 Jehováh adt wunnamuhkuteyeuuk chadchekeimop Davidoh, matta ukqushkinuumꝏ̄h: ummeechummúonk kuhhog nupponamun kutappuonganit,
132.12 Keneechánog nanauehteaúhettit nꝏ̄nꝏ̄waonk, kah nꝏ̄wauwáoash, nish woh kohkꝏ̄tomauogish nag: wunneechânꝏ̄oh pish wonk nanuk wutáppinneau kutappuonganit micheme.
132.13 Newutche hovah pepenam Sion: wutahchewontamun nohwuttin wutohkinnet.
132.14 Yeu nutanwôhsinꝏ̄onk micheme: yeu nꝏ̄tohkin, newute nukkodtantamun.
132.15 Nummꝏ̄chke wunnantamau ummeechumum: nuttápeteau ummatcheteumoh nashpe petukqunnunk.
132.16 Wussephausuéneumoh wonk nutogquannónineuh wadchânittuonk: kah ꝏ̄neetupanatamꝏ̄moh pish weekntamóe mishontꝏ̄wáoh.
132.17 Na nuttit ayeúon wutaskonoh David wussonkhékineat: nukkúhquttumaomp wequananteg wutche noh saséqunog.
132.18 Ummatwomoh pish nutogquodtumaónuh akodchuonk: qut nagum ut wuhhogkat wutchétuhquab pish wunnenégen.
133.0 {Hohtoesohteae ukketoohomaonk} David.
133.1 Kusseh, uttôh en wunnegen, kah uttôh en muskauantamenunkquodt, ꝏ̄weematittuog ꝏ̄weechaiyeútinneaout kah uppasukꝏ̄inneaóut.
133.2 Ogqunneungquot weetepumme ohtag muhpuhkukqut, ne anitchuagkup weeshetꝏ̄unit, Aaron ꝏ̄wishttꝏ̄unit, ne nanꝏ̄sitchuagkupuhquáe wutogkꝏ̄unit.
133.3 Onatuh tꝏ̄p ut Hermon, nꝏ̄kit wutch wadchuash Sion: newutche naut Jehovah unnꝏ̄wau wunnánetinneach, pomantamóonk micheme.
134.0 {Hohtoesohteae ketoohomaonk}.
134.1 Kusseh, wunnaumꝏ̄k Jehovah, wame kenaau wuttinnumoh Jehovah, nukkonaeu nepaéógish weeki Jehovah.
134.2 Spunnumꝏ̄k kenutcheganꝏ̄ash ut wunneetpanatamꝏ̄onganit, kah wunnanumꝏ̄k Jehovah.
134.3 Noh Jehovah kesteunk kesuk kah ohke, wunnanumukqush wutche Sion.
135.1 Waeenomok Jehovah, waeenodtomꝏ̄k ꝏ̄wesuonk Jehovah, waeenomonk, woi kenaau wuttinneumoh Jehovah.
135.2 Kenaau neepaué[a]gish weekit Jehovah, wutchippanutunkanit weekit kum-Manittꝏ̄mun.
135.3 Waeenomok Jehovah, newutche Jehovah wunneetou: waeenodtamꝏ̄k tabuttantamꝏ̄ongash ut ꝏ̄wesuonganit, newutche tapeneunkquot.
135.4 Newutche Jehovah uppepénau Jakoboh en wuhhogkat, kah Israeloh wutche nehenwonche ꝏ̄nenompakꝏ̄unoh.
