135.5 Newutche nꝏ̄wàhteauun Jehovah noh missugken, kah kum-Manittꝏ̄mun wame aneuhkauau manittꝏ̄h.
135.6 Tôh án wunnántog Jehovah ne wutussen, ut kesukqut kah ut ohkit: kehtahhannehtu kah wame mamꝏ̄noagish.
135.7 Oúwan waapunumwahtau wutch papogkodche ohkeit, ayim kutshaúmunnuꝏ̄ut wutch sókanonut: pásꝏ̄au mehshetahshinneoh wutch nô adt ummꝏ̄chekodchanont.
135.8 Noh tôgkomup mohtomméginitcheh ut Egypt, wosketompoh kah puppinashimwoh.
135.9 Anꝏ̄nau kuhkinneasuongash, kah monchanatamꝏ̄wongash ut nôeu ken woi Egypt, ut Pharaohut, kah wame wuttinninnúmut.
135.10 Noh tôgkodtogkup môgagish wutohtimóneash, kah paguanau matikkénutcheh ketassꝏ̄timwoh.
135.11 Sihon ketassꝏ̄t ut Amoritsut: kah Og ketassꝏ̄t ut Bashan, kah wame asꝏ̄tamꝏ̄wongash ut Canaan.
135.12 Kah magꝏ̄ nag wutohkéimꝏ̄ wutohkéinneat, ꝏ̄tohkéinnéaóut Israel ummissinninnumoh.
135.13 Kꝏ̄wesuonk woi Jehovah michemohteau, kah kummehquanumitteáonk papannuppu wame pometuonganit.
135.14 Newutche Jehovah wussumau ummissinninneumoh, kah aiuskoianatam papaume wuttinneumut.
135.15 Wuttinunneuhkontonkanꝏ̄oh penuohteá[o]g, nag silver kah gold, wutanakausuonganꝏ̄ wosketompaog wunnutcheganꝏ̄ꝏ̄ash.
135.16 Wuttꝏ̄nnúog, qut matta keketꝏ̄hkauꝏ̄og: wuskesukꝏ̄og, qut matta naumꝏ̄og.
135.17 Wahtauogꝏ̄og, qut matta nꝏ̄tamꝏ̄og: asa matta nashauóog wuttꝏ̄nꝏ̄wóut.
135.18 Nag kesheoncheg wutogqunneunkqussinneáuh, kah neyáne wame neg pabahtanumoncheg.
135.19 Wunnánumꝏ̄k Jehovah, woi week Israel, wunnanumꝏ̄k Jehovah, woi week Aaron:
135.20 Wunnanumꝏ̄k Jehovah, woi week Levi, kenaau quoshógish Jehovah wunnanumꝏ̄k Jehovah.
135.21 Wunnanumunach Jehovah wutch Sion, noh wodohkit Jerusalem: waeenomok Jehovah.
136.1 TAbuttantamꝏ̄k Jehovah, newutche noh wunneetou, newutche ummonaneteaonk michemohteau.
136.2 Tabuttantamꝏ̄k um-Manittꝏ̄mꝏ̄oh manittꝏ̄og, newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.3 Tabuttantamꝏ̄k wunnánaunnuaéneumoh nanaánuaénúog, newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.4 N noh nehtaue ásit misheu monchanatamꝏ̄wongash, newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.5 N$noh nashpu waantamꝏ̄onk ayim kesukquash, newutche ummonaneteáonk michemóhteau.
136.6 N$noh kodtunuk ohke wutch nippekontu, newutche ummonaneteâonk michemohteau.
136.7 N$noh ayikup môgagish wequaiyeuash, newutche úmmonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.8 Nepâuz onk woh nanaánum kesukod, newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.9 Nahnepaushad kah anogqsog onk woh nanawunumog nukon: newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.10 Nnoh nahshóp mohtommégitteomoh Egypt, newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.11 Kah sohꝏ̄wunnau Israeloh nahwutch kenugku, newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.12 Nashpe menuhkenitchónat, kah wussumógkinnumúnnat wuhpit, newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.13 N$noh pohshinugkup musque kehtoh: newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.14 Kah Israeloh pannupwushaheau pahshaúeu: newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.15 Qut kepúhteau Pharaohoh kah wame wutayuweehteomoh ut musque ketahhannit, newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.16 Nnoh ásꝏ̄wunuhp ummissinninneumoh pannuppu touohkomukqut, newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.17 N$noh nóhsheop mogkeketassꝏ̄timwoh: newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.18 Kah nushau tahsꝏ̄timwoh wáeenómutcheh: newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.19 Sihon ketassꝏ̄t ut Amoritsit: newutche ummonaneteaonk michemohteau.
136.20 Kah Og ketassꝏ̄t ut Bashan: newutche ummonaneteaonk michemohteau.
136.21 Káh wuttinnumaoh wutohkemꝏ̄ wutche wutáhtuonk, newutche ummonanéteaonk michemohteau.
136.22 Wutahtuonganꝏ̄ Israel wuttinneumoh: newutche ummonaneteaonk michemohteau.
136.23 N$noh kumméquanumukqunnonup tohukquonkqusseog, newutche ummonáneteaonk michemohteau.
136.24 Kah kup[p]ogquohwhunukqunnonup wutch kummatwomunnonut: newutche ummonaneteaonk michemohteau.
136.25 N$noh assamau wame weyausoh: newutche ummonaneteaonk michemohteau.
136.26 Woi tabuttantamꝏ̄k Jehovah kesukqut apit, newutche ummonaneteaonk michemohteau.
137.1 KIske sepuwehtu ut Bábilon, na nutapinnean, nux nummaumun, mehquontamog Sion.
137.2 Nutakꝏ̄chittomun nut-harpsumunnonash anumussukuppehtu, ut noeu.
137.3 Newutche nag monchanukqueagig en nummissinnanéanonut, na natꝏ̄tomungquñonog ketꝏ̄homaonk, kah nag paguánukqueágig nꝏ̄wáóg, unnꝏ̄hhomaiinnean pasuk Sione unnꝏ̄homaonk.
137.4 Toh woh kittinne ketꝏ̄hhomauonan Jehovah ukketꝏ̄homꝏ̄onk ut penuwohkomuk.
137.5 Wananumunan, woi Jerusalem, nummunadcheu wannehhikqutch nuhtompuhpequaonk.
137.6 Matta waanumunnꝏ̄on, neenan pissogqshonsh woskeche nuttꝏ̄nit: mátta anuwontammꝏ̄on Jerusalem negonohtag nꝏ̄weekontamoonk.
137.7 Mehquanum, woi Jehovah wunneechanoh Edom, ut ukkesukkodtumit Jerusalem, anꝏ̄wahettit nꝏ̄kinnumꝏ̄k nꝏ̄kinnumꝏ̄k anohteashik.
137.8 Woi ken wuttaunoh Babilon mos kenushit: wunnaiyeu moh onkquatunkquean, ne anheog.
137.9 Wunnaiyeu nnoh tohqunont kuppissesumoh, kah anóhkonont qussukquánit.
138.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David.
138.1 KOOwaweenomsh nashpe wame nuttahut: anaquabhettit Manittóog kuttinnꝏ̄namoushk ꝏ̄waweenomitteaonk.
138.2 Kꝏ̄wawu[s]sumsh unogqueu kꝏ̄neetupanatamwe Templeut, kah nuttabuttantam kꝏ̄wesuonk, newutche kꝏ̄womoausue womoausuonk, kah kꝏ̄nomwaonk: newutche kummishteop kuttinnꝏ̄waonk anue onk wame kꝏ̄wesuonk.
138.3 Ne kesukok mauon, kenampꝏ̄hamaiip; kummenuhkehip nashpe menuhkesuonk ut nukketeahogkounit.
138.4 Wame ketassꝏ̄tamog yeu muttaohkit pish kꝏ̄woweenomukquog, woi Jehovah, nag nꝏ̄tamwehettit kuttinnꝏ̄waongash wutch kuttꝏ̄nut.
138.5 Nux, pish ketꝏ̄homauog, ut ummayut Jehovah: newutche wusso[X]sumowonk Jehovah.
138.6 Tuhkonogque Jehovah ukqununkquapin onch monneauoh hohpautchekuoh: qut pitchuanumwehettit, nóutit wuttin waheuh.
138.7 Tuhkonogque nuppompamushon nashauwe wuttamepunonat, ken woh kukquaquakqheh, ken woh kussumogkunum kenutcheg ayeuuhkone ummusquantamꝏ̄onganꝏ̄wout nummatwomog: kah kuttinnohkou pish nꝏ̄wádchanuk.
138.8 Jehovah pannúppu kesteau ne wadtamaik nuhhogkat: kummonaneteaonk, woi Jehovah michemohteau: áhque ohquontash wutanakausuonk nehenwonche kenutchegash.
139.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ukketoohomaonk} David.
139.1 WOi Jehovah, kenátinneakôsip kah kꝏ̄wáheh.
139.2 Kꝏ̄wahteuh nummatappuonk, kah nutomohkeonk, kꝏ̄wahteuh nuttenantamoonk en nô adtit.
139.3 Kukquinnuppuhkom nummay, kah nussepsinnꝏ̄onk: kah kꝏ̄wahteuh wame nummayash.
139.4 Newutche matta kuttꝏ̄onk ohtáno neenanut qut kusseh, woi Jehovah, pannuppu kꝏ̄wahteauunash.
139.5 Kuppon kuhhog anaquabeh kah nuppisquanit, kah kenutcheg kupponamah.
139.6 Yeu wahteauonk wussaume monchanatamꝏ̄onganúꝏ̄ wutche neen, qunnuhquodt, matta woh nummissunnumꝏ̄un.
139.7 Toh nogqueu woh nutton wutch kenashauanittꝏ̄mut? asuh toh nogqueu woh nutussishon wutch anaquabean?
139.8 Aùon kesukqut na kuttappin, ayimon nutappin ut chepiohkomukqut, kusseh, na kutappin.
139.9 Neemunog umméqunoh nompoáeu, kah appeon aongkouwe ketahhannit,
139.10 Na kenutcheg nuttinsagkompagunukqun kah kuttinnohkou pish nukkogkôunuk.
139.11 Nꝏ̄waon, wunnamuhkut pohkenái pish nunnohkukkonk: nukon pish wequái quinuppe neen.
139.12 Nux, pohkéni matta kutassómpattammꝏ̄un qut nukon wohsumꝏ̄mꝏ̄ onatuh kesukok: pohkenái kah wequái naneeswe netatupeaúnak wutche ken.
139.13 Newutche kuppetukauomp nuttꝏ̄unnussog: kupputtogkꝏ̄hip ut nôkas wutoontomukqut.
139.14 Kꝏ̄waweenomsh newutche wabesúe kah monchanatamwe nukkezhitteup: kutanakausuongash monchanatamweyeuꝏ̄ash, onk yeu nukketeahogkou menuhke wahteoun.
139.15 Nuhhog matta mô puttogwhosu wutche ken, keme kezhimuk: kah wanehimuk ut agwe ohket.
139.16 Kuskesukquash naumwog nuhhog asquam pa[n]nuppe nꝏ̄nekezhett[e]aunk, kah kup[-]bꝏ̄kumut wame nuppompuhcháiyeumash tanussukkuhwhôsu, nish nano kake[na]áihteomukish mata pasuk ohtanꝏ̄g.
139.17 Uttôh mishôadtu kittenántamꝏ̄ongash en nuhhogkat, woi num-Manittꝏ̄m? toh ain muttâânit?
139.18 Nag ogkémog, nano monatash onk ne nágunt: tꝏ̄kshon ash kꝏ̄weétomsh.
139.19 Wunnamuhkut pish kuppaguan matcheetowog, woi num-Manittꝏ̄m, newutche amaéhtaegk kenaau nushshehteaenúog.
139.20 Newutche kummatchenukquog ayeuuhkône ken kah kummatwomog tahnꝏ̄che kenꝏ̄tamwog.
139.21 Sunnummatta nutjishanumꝏ̄og, woi Jehovah, jishanumugquéaneg? kah sunnummatta neuánumꝏ̄og yeug ayeuuhkonittue waábetunkquêaneg?
139.22 Nussekeneauóog nag nashpe pannuppe sekeneaittúonk: nag nutogquonumóog nummatwomut.
139.23 Natinnekôseh, woi num-Manittꝏ̄m, kah wahteaush nuttah: qutchéheh, kah wahteaush nuttenanatamꝏ̄ongash.
139.24 Kah naish uttiyeu matchemay ut nuhhogkat, kah sagkompaguneh en mayut máchemohtag.
140.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt, Ukketoohomaonk} David.
140.1 Pohquahwusseh, woi Jehovah, wutch matcheseanúut: wadchaneh wutch musquantamwe wosketompaut.
140.2 Neg mohmissóntogig woskehuwaonk wuttahhꝏ̄wóut: nagwutteáeu momoéog wutch ayeuwuttúonk.
140.3 Ayimwog weenannuꝏ̄ash kéniyeuash onatuh askꝏ̄kut: úhquoshket sesequáog agwu wussissetꝏ̄nꝏ̄wóut. Selah.
140.4 Wadchaneh, woi Jehovah, wutch wunnutcheganit matcheetou, nanaáihheh wutch musquantamwe woskeetompaut neg ahchewontogig kepuhkon nutauonganash.
140.5 Pitchuanumwog adtahsháog wutappehhannꝏ̄oh wutche neen, kah pémeneohtanémesash: sepagenáog wutashabpꝏ̄uh kishke m[a]yut; nupponamunkquog appehanah. Selah.
140.6 Nuttin Jehovah, ken num-Manittꝏ̄m, nꝏ̄tash nꝏ̄wadtauatonkqussue weequetumꝏ̄onk woi Jehovah.
140.7 Woi Jehovah Manit, nꝏ̄wadchanitteae menuhkesuonk: kupputtagguhhamup nuppuhkuk ne kesukok ayeuwuttimuk.
140.8 Ahque wéhtꝏ̄wom, woi Jehovah, matchetowog ne kodtantamóhettit: ahque kutchittánumau ummatcheetupanatamwe ompuwissuonk, ishkont mishehheáog wuhhogkaoh. Selah.
140.9 Yeug weenuhkoiitcheg, ꝏ̄woskehuwaonk ut wussissetꝏ̄nit nuhkeemꝏ̄utch ut nehenwonche uppuhkukkꝏ̄wóont.
140.10 Nashqunáe mokossaash nuhkuhkongkꝏ̄hettich, nohkónach nꝏ̄taut, en mꝏ̄nâeu passahthonganit, onk woh mo waápéog wonk.
140.11 Ahque menehkhénach mamatchenꝏ̄waenin ut ohkeit: woskehuwáonk pish ayeuau woskehuaenuh ukképôhkônat.
140.12 Nꝏ̄wahteóh Jehovah kenꝏ̄tamwonshheuh kuttummungeh wuttammepunnaeninneuh: kah wussampweteaumꝏ̄onk matchekuoh.
140.13 Wunnamuhkut sampweusseaenin pish tabuttantam kꝏ̄wesuonk: sampwesit pish ayeu anaquabean.
141.0 {Ukketooh[o]maonk} David.
141.1 JEhovah, kummauunnitteaush, kenuppe peyaauseh, kukkeitash nꝏ̄wadtauatongqussuonk mauunnitteáuunán.
141.2 Nuppeaantamꝏ̄onk sampwespeemꝏ̄utch ut anaquabean, onátuh incenseut kah nuttishpunnumunnat nunnutcheganash onatuh wunnonkwaeu sephausuonk.
141.3 Ponsh askuhwhosuonk, woi Jehovah anaquohtag nuttꝏ̄n: nanaaihtaash squontame nussissetꝏ̄nâsh.
141.4 Ahque nuttah kepech teague matcheseonganit, ussenat matcheseonganash weeche matcheseaenuog: kah ahque meechitti ꝏ̄weekitteamowonganꝏ̄.
141.5 Wuñomwausseaenuog togkomukquttei, ne womoausuonk: káh auskomitch, ne pish wunnegen pummee ne matta pish sꝏ̄quttahhamꝏ̄munꝏ̄ nuppuhkuk: newutché onch nuppeantamwansheoog onkapunahettit.
141.6 OOsittumwaenumꝏ̄uh kepuhteámuk ut qussukquanehtu, pish nꝏ̄tamwog nuttinnꝏ̄waongash, newutche weekonash.
141.7 Nuskonnonash nanwongquaash ut woskeche weenohkeet onatuh howan tâmettáhhog, kah nenekittâhhog mahtugquash ut woskeche ohkeit.
141.8 Qut nuskesukquash nogque en kuhhogkaou, woi Jehovah Manit: kuppâbuhtanumunnꝏ̄wonk kut[a]htaun: ahque nukkoz nukketeahogkou nussiyeuinneat.
141.9 Wadchaneh wutch appéhanit na ponamaihétticheh, kah wutch wutappehhanꝏ̄wóont neg anakausitcheg matcheseonk.
141.10 Matcheetowog penushahettich en nehenwonche wutappehanꝏ̄wóut: ash pame pishettit pohquohhamitti.
142.0 {Um-Maschil} David: {Peantamowonk apit puppuhkotteaouut.}
142.1 Nummauunnitteau Jehovah nashpe nꝏ̄wadtauatonkqussúonk: nashpe nꝏ̄wadtauatonkqussuonk nutayimup nꝏ̄weequetumꝏ̄onk en Jehovahut.
142.2 Nussokanum nummauunnitteáonk ut anaquabit: nunnahtin nꝏ̄tamehpunnaonk ut anaquabit.
142.3 Nunnashauonk quodtaogkomésit ut nuhhogkat, neit kꝏ̄wahteoh nummay: mayik ne âôump, kemu nupponamunkquog appehanah.
142.4 Nuttinnuhquaip nuttinohkôunit kah nuppabahsamputtamunah, qut mâtta howan nꝏ̄wahukꝏ̄, spuhhꝏ̄waonk nunnukkonnukqun: wanne howan tohhentupanumoou nukketeahogkounoh.
142.5 Kummauunnitteanup woi Jehovah, nussip, ken nuttusphouwaonk, nutahtoonk ut ohkit pomantogig.
142.6 Kukkeihtash nummauonk, newutche nuttiuhquonkqhit: pohquawusseh wutch nꝏ̄woskhuwaeneumut, newutche nag nutanuwunuhkesumukquog.
142.7 Sohhꝏ̄wush nukketeahogkou wutch kuppishagkinittuonganit onk woh nꝏ̄woweenodtum kꝏ̄wesuónk: sampweusseaenuog pish quinnupuhkongquog: newutche pish kumummisku wunneneheh.
143.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David.
143.1 NOOtash nuppeantamowonk woi Jehovah kuhkeitash nꝏ̄weehquetumꝏ̄wonganash: ut kussampwanumukqussinneat nampꝏ̄hamah, kah ut kꝏ̄nomwausseaonganit.
143.2 Kah ahque pasou ꝏ̄sittumꝏ̄onganit kittinneum: newutche anaquabean matta pish howan wósketomp noh pomantog sompweogquanumau.
143.3 Newutche matwau woskeheau nukkéteahogkounoh, unnehtham nuppomantamoonk ohkekontu: nꝏ̄tohkehhik pohkenahtu onatuh yeug sepe nuppukeg.
143.4 Newajeh nunnashauonk wuttaoukomesit ut nuhhogkat: nuttáh nuttinnomiyeumut nonsiyeumꝏ̄.
143.5 Nummehquontam nꝏ̄adt kesukkodtash, nunnatwontam wame kutanákausuongash, nummissantam kenutchegane anakausuongásh
143.6 Kussumogkunumoush nunnutcheganash: nukketeahogkou wutche ken, onatuh kunkohteatae ohke. Selah.
143.7 Nꝏ̄tah teanuk woi Jehovah, nunnashauonk sa[u]wunnum: ahque ahtohtah kuskesuk ishkont nutógqunneunkqus nag aoncheg possahtheganit.
143.8 Nꝏ̄tamwaheh womoausue kꝏ̄womoausuonk nompoaeu, newutche kuppabahtanumoush wahteauwaheh may toh wóh ayôi, newutche kutahshinnumaush nukketeahogkou.
143.9 Pohquawusseh woi J[é]hovah wutch nummatwomog: kuppogsinnꝏ̄wonsh noh kittin ahtahshinneat.
143.10 Kuhkꝏ̄tomah ussen kuttinanatamꝏ̄onk, newutche ken num-Manittꝏ̄m kenashauanittꝏ̄m wunnetu, sagkompaguneh en wutohtuwout sampwéusseog.
143.11 Quaquahqheh woi Jehovah, newutche kꝏ̄wesuonk: newutche kussampweusseonk sohhouwus nukketeahogkou wutch wuttammepunnonat.
143.12 Kah wutch kummonaneteaonganit tumméhtah nummatwomog, kah pagwas wame nnag onkapunnanoncheg nukketeahogkonuh: newutche nen kittinneum.
144.1 Wunanumunach Jehovah nummenuhkesuonk, noh kuhkꝏ̄tomwontog nunnutchegash ayeukonat, kah nuppahchanitcheash wutayeuuhkon[?]ôut.
144.2 Nꝏ̄neétꝏ̄onk kah nꝏ̄wonkonous, nukqunnunkqukkommuk kah nuppohquohwussuaenin, nutogqunneg, kah nnoh pàbuhtanumog: noh sohkauont nummissinninneumoh agwu neen.
144.3 Lord howan wosketomp nnoh ken waheadt? asa wunnaumonuh wosketomp onk woh kututtanantamau?
144.4 Wosketomp ogqueneunkqussu tahnꝏ̄cheye[n]ꝏ̄winneat: ukkesukodtumash ogqueneunkquodtash onkaohtaut, ne pamushaumꝏ̄uk.
144.5 Puskepukash kuskesukquash woi Jehovah, kah nꝏ̄kish: mussinush wadchuash, kah nash pish pukittauꝏ̄ash.
144.6 Sohwôhtaush ukkutshaumun kah nag séeah: pepumish kukkô[u]hquodtash kah nag pagwas.
144.7 Annꝏ̄s kenutcheg wutch waabe, sohhꝏ̄wuneh, & pohquohwusseh wutche mishe nippekontu: wutch wunnutcheganꝏ̄wout pénowe mukkiog.
144.8 N[o]h wuttꝏ̄n tahnꝏ̄che keketꝏ̄kómꝏ̄ug, kah wuttinnohkounꝏ̄wóut, pannꝏ̄wayeue wuttinnohkou.
144.9 Kuttinnꝏ̄hómoush wuske ketꝏ̄homwaonk woi Jehovah: ut psaltarehut, & puhpeg paukquompósik kuttinnꝏ̄homoush waeenodtuongash.
144.10 Noh aninnumauau ketahsꝏ̄timoh wadchanittúonk, noh pohquohwhunau Davidoh wuttinneumoh wutch woskehettue togkodteganit.
144.11 Sohwhuneh, kah pohquohwusseh wutch wunnutcheóont penowe mukkiog, noh wuttꝏ̄n tahnꝏ̄che anꝏ̄womꝏ̄uk: kah wuttinnohkonnꝏ̄woont pannꝏ̄wae wuttinohkou.
144.12 Naumonanonog woh ogqunneunkqussuog wuskontugkꝏ̄mesit sonkqhettit ut wuskenúunneat: nuttaununnonog woh ogqueneunkqussuog qussuk náshik wunneetatuppussumun onatuh wunne qussukquanekommuk.
144.13 Onk woh nutogqunakomukqunonash numwameechummuash, nishnoh teag ne woh wuttinnumun: nuttisshepsumunnouog woh ꝏ̄chekeneau muttannonganogkussuog nashomáogqunnonut.
144.14 Nutoxinumunnonog woh menuhkanakausuog, mattá woh howan uppetuhkontamꝏ̄un, asa mat sohhammꝏ̄: matta woh mauaonganinno nunnaushomaogqunnonut.
144.15 Wunnaiyeuog missinninnuog neg ne adtuhkég: wunnaiyeuog missinninnuog noh wamanittꝏ̄mut Jehovah.
145.0 {Waeenomuae ukketooohomaonk} David.
145.1 Kummishesh num-Manittꝏ̄m, woi ketassꝏ̄t: kah nꝏ̄nantam kꝏ̄wesuonk micheme kah micheme.
145.2 Asekesukokish kꝏ̄nánumoush: kah nꝏ̄wóweenodtum kꝏ̄wesuonk, micheme kah micheme.
145.3 Jehovah missugken, kah noh woh mahshe waeenomit: kah ummissugkenꝏ̄wonk, mat woh howan uppogkodadttinnekóntamꝏ̄un.
145.4 Pasuk pometuonk pish waeenodtum kutanakausuongash onk yean onkatoganit; kah pish wahteauwahuwau kummishanakausuongash.
145.5 Nꝏ̄wéogquttum wussohsumówe quttiánumáonk kummissugkenuonk, kah kummonchanatamwanakausuongash.
145.6 Kah pish keketꝏ̄hkontamwog ummenuhkesuonk kutunkquanuhkausuongash: kah pish nꝏ̄wahteauwahuwam kummissugkenuwonk.
145.7 Nag pish mꝏ̄cheke weogquttimwog mehquoantamꝏ̄onk kummishe wunneetowonk, & pish ketꝏ̄homaog kꝏ̄nomwausséonk
145.8 Jehovah monaneteau, kah numwohteau ukkitteamonteaneteaonk, cheke musquantam, kah mishe ummonaneteaonk.
145.9 Jehovah ꝏ̄neneheuh wame; kah ukkitteamonteanitteáe monaneteaongash nuhkuhkomwog wame wutanakausuongash.
145.10 Wame kutanakausuonganash pish kꝏ̄woweenomuk, woi Jehovah: kah kꝏ̄neetupanatamꝏ̄mog pish kꝏ̄nanumukquog.
145.11 Nag pish weogquttumwog sohsumóe kukkeassꝏ̄timóonk kah pish keketꝏ̄hkaog kummenuhkesuonk.
145.12 Onk woh wahteauwáheaog wosketompaog wunnaumonaoh, ummishanakausuongash, kah wussohsumóe missugkenue ukkehtassꝏ̄tamꝏ̄onk.
145.13 Kukketassꝏ̄timóonk micheme ohtag ketassꝏ̄timóonk: kah kenánaánumôonk pannuppe wame pometuonganash.
145.14 Jehovah pabahtinau wame panushonutcheh: kah tahshinau wame yeuh naausukompaunutcheh.
145.15 Wuskesukquash wame kukkenompomukqunash, kah nag kutassamoog nish noh uttꝏ̄che.
145.16 Kꝏ̄woshinum kenutcheg, & kuttapehteóh ukkodtantamꝏ̄onk nishnoh pamóntog.
145.17 Jehovah sampweussu ut wame ummayut, kah wunneetupanatam wame wutanakausuonganit.
145.18 Jehovah uppasꝏ̄sukauoh wame neh weehquttumungqutcheh: wame weequttumungqutcheh wunnamuhkut.
145.19 Noh tapeteaoh ukkodtantamoonk neh quashikqutcheh: kah wonk wunnꝏ̄tamauoh ummauonganꝏ̄, kah pish ꝏ̄wadchanuh.
145.20 Jehovah ꝏ̄wadchanuh wame neh womonukqutcheh: qut wame matchetowoh uppaguanuh.
145.21 Nuttꝏ̄n pish yeumꝏ̄ waeenomaonk Jehovah: kah wame weyaus wunnanatamohettich wunneetupanatamwe ꝏ̄wesuonk micheme kah micheme.
146.1 Waeenomok Jehovah waeenom Jehovah, woi nukketeahogkou.
146.2 As pamontam nꝏ̄woweenom Jehovah: nukketꝏ̄homau Num-Manittꝏ̄m tabuttantamꝏ̄wongash, as yeu apeh.
146.3 Ahque pabahtanumꝏ̄k santimoog, wunnaumonuh wosketomp, noh matta aninnohsuonk ohtoog.
146.4 Wunnashauonk amaemouk, quinnuppu en nuppuppissiyeumut: ne kesukok wuttenantamꝏ̄ongash monteagwuninnoash.
146.5 Wunnaiyeu n noh wodtanninnohsumit um-Manittꝏ̄moh Jakob, noh annoonont Jehovah um-Manittꝏ̄moh.
146.6 Noh aigkup kesuk kah ohke, kehtoh kah wame neg noh apitcheg: noh wadchanuk wunnomwayeuonk micheme.
146.7 Noh asit ꝏ̄sittumꝏ̄onk wutussehtaon waskhitcheh noh assamont kodtupwunutcheh: Jehovah ompinneau kobshagkinutcheh.
146.8 Jehovah wôhshinum wuskesukquash pogkenumunutche: Jehovah tohshinau neh nâuhsukompaunutcheh: Jehovah womonuh samweusseaenuh.
146.9 Jehovah wadchanau penuwohteuh: aninnumauau mat wodꝏ̄shꝏ̄nigeh, kah sekousquoh: qut ummay matcheetou ꝏ̄numuhkinumun.
146.10 Jehovah pish nanauunnuau micheme, kum-Manittꝏ̄m woi Sion ut wame pometuonganit: waeenomꝏ̄k Jehovah.
147.1 Waeenomꝏ̄k Jehovah: newutche wunnegen ketꝏ̄homauonat tabut tantamꝏ̄ongash kum-Manittꝏ̄mun: newutche weekontamweyeuꝏ̄, kah waeenomaonk tapeneunkquot.
147.2 Jehovah weekitteau Jerusalem: mukkinnau môaeu yeug sohwohteamukig wutch Israelaut.
147.3 Neetskeheau sohqutteahonutcheh: kah tohkupunau ꝏ̄woskesewonganꝏ̄ash.
147.4 Ogkemau neadtahsohettit anogqsog: nah wame ꝏ̄weseonganuhkauouh.
147.5 Missugken kum-Manittꝏ̄mun, kah mishe menuhkesu: ꝏ̄wohwohtamꝏ̄wonk matta wo[h]kukkoano.
147.6 Jehováh tahshinau manunnissuoh: unnohteau matchetuoh ohkekontu.
147.7 Ketꝏ̄homok Jehovah nashpe tabuttántamóonk: ketꝏ̄homok tabuttantamꝏ̄ongash ut harput en kum-Manittꝏ̄munnonut.
147.8 Noh pâdtahgúhhꝏ̄k kesukquash nashpe matokqs, noh quoshauwehtog sokanon wutche yeu ohke: noh ayig moskehtuash negkinut ut wadchuut.
147.9 Assamau puppinnashimwussoh, kah konkontuwémesoh mauunit.
147.10 Matta weekontamꝏ̄ ummenuhkesuonk horses: matta weekontamꝏ̄ wuhkontash wosketomp.
147.11 Jehovah weeteánumau neh quoshhukqutcheh, neh anoantamunutcheh ummonaneteáonk.
147.12 Waeenomꝏ̄k Jehovah, woi Jersualem: tabuttantamau kum-Manittꝏ̄m, woi Zion.
147.13 Newutche menehketeau neepattúhquonk kussquontamut: wunnanumau keneechanoh ut kuhhogkat.
147.14 Wunnóhteahuau ut wohkóeu: kah kenumwameechumuhkónuk nish wanegukish wheatash.
147.15 Annꝏ̄nau wuttinnꝏ̄waonguh ut ohkekontu: wuttinnꝏ̄waonk kenupshau.
147.16 Magou kꝏ̄nah onatuh wꝏ̄ll: seáhwhau tꝏ̄puoh onatuh pukquéit.
147.17 Sohwhohteau ukkuppádtinumoh onatuh kodchuhke petukqunneganit: howan woh neepauut wussónquayeumut?
147.18 Anꝏ̄nau wuttinnꝏ̄waonguh, kah nah wussâuppaswoh: mshéhtashinehteau, wonk tomógkon.
147.19 Kuhkꝏ̄tomauau Jakoboh wuttinnꝏ̄waonk, ukkuhkꝏ̄waongash, kah ꝏ̄wauwaongash Israeloh.
147.20 Matta wuttinteauun onkatuk wutohtimóin: kah ꝏ̄sittumꝏ̄wongash matta nah ꝏ̄wáhheóuh; waeeomꝏ̄k Jehovah.
148.1 WAeenomꝏ̄k Jehovah: waeenomꝏ̄k Jehovah wutch kesukqut: waeenomꝏ̄k ut quanunkquodtehtu.
148.2 Waeenomꝏ̄k kenaau wame wut-angelsumoh: waeenomꝏ̄k wame wutáyeuweéhteomoh.
148.3 Waeenomꝏ̄k kenaau nepâuz kah nepâuzshad: waenomꝏ̄k kenaau wohsumóeanogqsog
148.4 Waeenomꝏ̄k kenaau kesukquash kesuk, kah kenaau nippéog ongkouwe kesukquehtu.
148.5 Waeenodtumohettich ꝏ̄wesuonk Jehovah: newutche noh nꝏ̄wop onk nag kezheopanneg.
148.6 Onk noh menuhkeheuh nah micheme kah micheme: ayimup ukkúhkꝏ̄waonk, ne matta pish paumshaumúnꝏ̄g.
148.7 Waeenomꝏ̄k Jehovah wutche ohket, kenaau dragonsog, kah wame mꝏ̄nóagish.
148.8 Nꝏ̄tau, & musségon, kꝏ̄n, kah pukkuttaemes, mehshetahshin, usseog uttoh anꝏ̄wop.
148.9 Wadchuash kah wame wadchuemesash máhshemechume mahtugquash, kah wame chikupog.
148.10 Puppinashimwog, & wame neetassuog, neg pâpâmꝏ̄tacheg, & páhpumunont psukses
148.11 Kehtahsꝏ̄timwog ut ohkeit, kah wame missinninnuog: santimóog kah wame wussittumwaenuog ut ohkeit.
148.12 Naneeswe nunkompaog kah nunksquaog, kutchiog kah mukkiog.
148.13 Waeenodtumohettich ꝏ̄wesuonk Jehovah: newutche ne wesuonk webe muttáe wunnegen: wussohsumóonk aneukomꝏ̄ ohkeit kah kesukqut.
148.14 Noh wonk tashinau wutáskonꝏ̄oh ummissinninnuomoh, ꝏ̄waweenomuwaonganꝏ̄ wame ꝏ̄neetupanatamꝏ̄moh, wunnaumonuh Israel, missinninnúogpasꝏ̄sukauóuh: waeenomꝏ̄k Jehovah.
149.1 Waeeomꝏ̄k Jehovah: anꝏ̄homꝏ̄k Jehovah wuske anꝏ̄homáonk, kah wuttabuttantamꝏ̄onk ummukkinneonganꝏ̄ waneetupanatogig.
149.2 Israel weekontamꝏ̄wononch neh kezhikupoh: wunneechanoh Sion weekontamꝏ̄nàhettich wussantimaumꝏ̄oh.
149.3 Waeenodtúmwehettich ꝏ̄wesuonk nashpe puhpeg, anꝏ̄homauahettich tabuttantamꝏ̄ongash nashpe timbrel kah harp.
149.4 Newutche Jehovah weeteánumau ummissinninnúmoh: pish ꝏ̄néheau neh manunnissunutche nashpe wadchanittuonk.
149.5 Wunneetupanatamwog muskouanatamohettich ut sohsumoonganit: mishontꝏ̄wae ꝏ̄humahettich wutappinneáont.
149.6 Qunúhqueu tabuttantamauaongash Manit ohtaj wuttꝏ̄nꝏ̄wóut: kah togkodteg aéhtae kenag ohtaj wunnutcheganꝏ̄wout.
149.7 Ussenat wutannꝏ̄tauwaonk penuwohteuh, kah sasámakouwhittuongash ut missinninnùtu.
149.8 Tahtogkuppinnon kehtahsꝏ̄timwog mꝏ̄ôhshagquohtogquosh: kah wuttꝏ̄owosketompaog mꝏ̄ôhshagquohtogquosh.
149.9 Néhheoneau n nag neanussukwhosik wussittumóonk: yeu ukquttiantamꝏ̄onganꝏ̄ wame ꝏ̄neetupanatamꝏ̄moh: waeenomꝏ̄k Jehovah.
150.1 Waeenomꝏ̄k Jehovah, waeenomꝏ̄k Manit ut ꝏ̄neetupanatamwe weekit: waeenomꝏ̄k ut mamahchekesukqut ne ummenuhkesuonk ohtag.
150.2 Waeenomꝏ̄k wutch ummishanakausuongash: unnꝏ̄waeenomꝏ̄k neaunag ummissugkenuonk.
150.3 Waeenomꝏ̄k nashpe wadtauatonkqussue monopuhpeg; waeenomꝏ̄k nashpe psaltery kah harp.
150.4 Waeenomꝏ̄k nashpe timbrel kah puhpeg: waeenomꝏ̄k nashpe pemeneohtone pequonash kah organsash.
150.5 Waeenomꝏ̄k nashpe mishontowáe cymbalsash: waeenomꝏ̄k nashpe mishontowae cymbalsash
150.6 Nishnow oâus wuñahnahshonat waeenomonch Jehovah: waeenomꝏ̄k Jehovah.
